de bzhin gshegs pa 'dra'am mi 'dra blta yis/ ci'i phyir na 'dzam bu'i gling na de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal mthong ba nga min pa med pas phyis 'dra mi 'dra'i shan mi phyed
do/ /de skad zer nas bus sgo phye ba dang / bzo bo bi shwa karma rtsig phug na phar thal nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /der rgan mos bltas nas phyir byung ba la/ lha 'di bcom
ldan 'das dngos dang 'dra'am mi 'dra dris pas/ mas smras pa/ lha 'di bcom ldan 'das dgung lo sum cu so gnyis lon pa dang sku tshad mnyam ste/ sangs rgyas la 'od 'dom gang
yod pa dang / gcug tor ltar mi mngon pa dang / dbu skra bung ba ltar nag cing tshom bur 'khyil ba dang / smin mtshams na mdzod spu khru gang g.yas su 'khyil ba dang / gsung
gis chos 'chad/ na bza' gsol ba sku la sor bzhi mi reg pa dang / spyod lam gshegs pa/ bzhugs pa/ gzim pa la sogs pa sems can gyi don mdzad pa de 'di la med/ gzhan byin
rlabs la sogs pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang khyad par med do zhes zer ro/ /sku de'i zhal gyi dkyil 'khor la mi che tshad kyi brkyangs khru do dang / spyan dang zhal
la mtho gsum/ sku spyi la brkyangs khru brgyad yod do/ sku 'di la lta bas chog mi shes te/ bkres pa dang bskom pa brjed brjed du lta ba dang / mthong ba tsam gyis lus
ngag yid gsum ngal sos pa dang / sdug bsngal thams cad zhi ba dang / gdon bgegs dang bral ba/ yon tan dpag tu

maid pa byung ngo / /ye shes kyang rgyud la 'jug go/ /bltas te phyir 'gro ba na rgyab bstan nas phyir 'gro mi phod pa dang / phyi rol pa dang rten gang bzang 'gran pa na phyi
rol pa'i rten la nang pa sangs rgyas pa'i gang zag rnams phyag mi byed do/ /de lta bu'i dam bca' byed do/ /phyi pa mu stegs pa yang sku 'di la phyag mi byed pa'i dam bca'
ste bcas kyang mthong ba tsam gyis phyag byed do/ /lag pa lcags kyis bkyigs kyang rang grol nas phyag byed par 'gyur gyis zer nas rgan mo de de nub shi ste/ gdung ring
bsrel gyi phung por gyur to/ /bram ze mo de dpal lha mo'i sprul par grags so/ /de'i gdung la bus rdo rje gdan du mchod rten bzhengs te/ mchod rten ring bsrel gyi snying
po can du grags so/ / zhag gcig gis sgo dbye ba sngas pa la skyon ci yod bltas pas/ sku'i zhabs ya gcig gi mthe'u chung ma tshang zer bar 'dug ste/ nyan thos pa rnams na
re/ bdud lhas sbyin gyis bcom ldan 'das la rgyogs brgyab pas/ gnod sbyin dzam bha la dang / hi phus ma yod pas gab pas phyag na rdo rje rgyogs la rdo rje brgyab pas rgyogs
dum bu brgyar song / dum bu gcig hi pha la phog ste shi/ dum bu gcig dzam bha la la phog ste rma 'tshal btod/ des lan pa yin zer/ de ltar ma yin skad/ theg pa chen po'i
mkhas pa rnams ni/ de ma yin/ dbu skra tshom bur 'khyil ba de ma tshang ba yin skad/ rin po che inda?r ni las spyan 'bras byas 'dug go/ /de ni mthon mthing gi kha dog dang
'dra ba mthing ga 'od dang bcas pa'o/ /sku de'i mtshan ni ma hA bho dhi zhes grags so/ /gzhan rnams rgan mos ji skad smras pa bzhin no/ /bram ze spun gsum gyis rten bzhengs
pa'i sku tshad gsum ni/ rgya gar gyi gnas gsum na bzhugs nas sems can gyi don du bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing du bzhugs so/ /nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'i sku tshad ni/ sum
cu rtsa gsum na lha rnams kyi don mdzad do/ /dgung lo brgyad pa dang bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad des/ rgyal po gsal rgyal gyi macod gnas mdzad/ lo lnga bcu 'gro don rgya gar
du mdzad/ dgung lo bcu gnyis pa lo lnga brgya u rgyan du/ de nas srin po/ de nas kha che yi yul du lo lnga brgya/ de nas klus brkus nas/ klu'i rgyal po he man dha'i mchod
gnas shi le ta chu bhe ta bya ba phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa zhig dang / mkhan po skar rgyal bya ba 'phags pa byams pa'i grub pa thob pa gnyis kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi sku
de klu yul na yod par gzigs nas/ der skar rgyal gyis byams par sprul nas/ klu shing ghu dhe'i bdud rtsis klu rnams la bdud rtsi'i char bas brid/ shi le tas phyag na rdo
rjer sprul nas klu rnams sdigs gzir nas byams pa bskyangs te/ sku gzugs khrus kyi rdzing bu nas yar spyan drangs/ bstan pa nub tsa na/ sku des sna drangs pa'i rin po che'i
rten tsam mi yul na bzhugs tshad klu yul du spyan drang bar byas so/ /lo lnga brgyar ma ga dhar 'gro don mdzad do/ /'jam dpal gyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba/ sangs rgyas
mi bzhugs pa yongs mya ngan las 'das pa na/ 'gro ba rnams tshogs gsog pa'i rten gang la bgyi/ zhes zhus pas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhal nas/ sangs rgyas kyi rten la brgyad
de nyid las byung ba'i rten drug 'dra ba'i rten gnyis te brgyad kyis dkon mchog la bsod nams gsog pa'i rten

gyis zhes bka' bstsal to/ /dbu skra dang phyag sen gyi rten gnyis mnga' ba yin te/ dang po rab tu byung ba'i dus su dbu skra la mtho bcu dgu yod pa la/ rgyal bu rang gis mchod
rten rnams dag gi drung du ral gris bzhar ba sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyis khyer te/ mchod rten byas pa da lta yang lha rnams kyi gtsug phud kyis mchod pa'i dus
su ston zhes skad do/ /mi'i yul du yang / a po bdun pas mos pa'i mchod rten brtsigs nas/ gtsug phud blangs pa'i mchod rten zhes grags pa yod do/ /de ni byang chub sems
dpa'i dus yin pas byang chub sems dpa'i mchod rten yin la/ mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas dbu skra dang phyag sen bregs nas khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin la gnang pa
de la mchod rten byas te mchod do/ /gzhan yang lho phyogs mtha' 'khob tu yugs mo lnga brgya la sprul pa'i phyag sen gnang nas de la mchod rten bzhengs te mchod pa byed
do/ /rgyal po gzugs can snying po'i btsun mo'i tshogs kyang / dbu skra phyag sen zhus nas phyag sen gyi mchod rten mdzad do/ /rgyal po yul 'khor srung gis shAkya gyad chen
la srung ba'i don du sprul pa'i phyag sen gnang nas mchod pa chen po byas so/ /shAkya rnams bde la bkod do/ /lhung bzed kyi mchod rten byung ba ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
dka' thub las bzhengs nas/ bsod snyoms la byon pa'i dus su/ grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma la sogs brgyad kyis/ 'o thug bskol nas gser gyi snod du drangs pas 'o thug gsol
bas/ de'i gser snod chu bo nairanya?dzanar bor bas klu'i rgyal pos khyer bas/ lha yi dbang po brgya byin gyis bya khyung du sprul nas sdigs pas ma chun/ brgya byin rang
du byas nas bslangs pas byin nas mchod rten byas nas bzhugs so/ /sangs rgyas nang shing sgrol rgyu'i tshal na bzhugs pa la/ tshong dpon ga gon ta bzang po dang / bzang skyong
la sogs pa tshong phrug lnga brgyas/ 'o tsha dang sman dang mar gsum sbyar nas rin po che'i gzhong par blugs nas bcom ldan 'das la drangs pa'i dus su/ rgyal po chen
po bzhi yis rdo'i lhung bzed bzhi phul bas gcig tu byin gyis brlabs nas phyag tu bsnams nas bzhes te/ phyis rgyal po bzhi rang la gnang ste/ rang rang gi mchod rten byas
te mchod pa byed do/ /nyan thos kyi ched du mgar bas lcags la lhung bzed brdungs nas phyag na bsnams pa ni/ phyis nyan thos pa rnams kyis mchod rten mdzad de/ mchod par
byed do/ /mkhar gsil ni dngos su mchod rten yin la/ dkon mchog gsum gyi rten yin pas/ lha mi kun gyis mthong na dad pa'i mchod rten yin no/ /tshems mche ba dang / ring bsrel
byon tshul ni/ thub pa'i dbang po mya ngan las 'das nas spur zhugs la bzhen pa'i dus su/ tshems mche ba bzhi bo ma tshig pa de la mchod rten re byas so/ /ring bsrel ni
sku'i khams bzhi ga gdung phra mo byas nas bram zera'i rigs bre bo dang mnyam pas/ sku gdung cha brgyad du bgos nas byin te/ gnas rang rang so so ru mchod pa mang po rgyas
par byas so/ /bram ze bre bo la/ gser sku bum pa gsum byin nas/ bre bo'i grong du mchod rten byas so/ /bram ze'i khye'u Na?yagro tas sku gdung bzhu ba'i sol ba la mchod
rten byas so/ /de dag ni sangs rgyas nyid las byung bas na/ sangs rgyas nyid dang mnyam mo/ /mi dang mi ma

yin kun gyi mchod pa'i rten yin no/ /sangs rgyas dang 'dra ba'i rten gnyis la/ sku gzugs ni sku 'dra ba'i phyir na sku ngo bo dang 'dra'o/ /sku'i rten yin no/ /mchod rten ni
chos sku 'dra ba'i rten no/ /sku gzugs sku'i 'byung tshul ni/ nangs kyi thog mar/ byang chub sems dpa' zhing la gzigs pa'i tshe/ shing 'dzam bu'i bsil grib la bzhugs tshe
byang chub sems dpa'i sku 'dra re bzhengs nas/ zhing pa'i lha mi rnams kyis mchod pa'i rten mdzad do/ /sing ga la pa'i bu mo'i don du/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ras ris la bris
nas bskur te/ dad pa can bsod nams gsog pa'i rten mdzad do/ khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin gyis/ byang chub sems dpa'i dus kyi sku ci 'dra ba zhig bzhengs nas de shing
rta'i steng du bzhugs nas grong khyer thams cad du spyan drangs nas/ skye bo kun gyi mos gus dad mos kyi rten mdzad do/ / ras ris kyi sku ji ltar byung ba ni/ bcom ldan
'das nyid sku bzhugs pa'i dus su rgyal po gzugs can snying po dang / mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po u tra ya na bya ba gnyis ngo bo ma 'phrad par skyes kyis 'grul pa'i grogs po
yin pas skyes bskur ras phar bskur tshul bskur byed pa las/ dus nam zhig na/ rgyal po u tra ya nas rin po che sna tshogs dang / khyad 'phags kyi ras sna tshogs skyes snga
nas ma bskur ba'i khyad par can mang po bskur byung ba la/ rgyal po gzugs can snying po thugs las cher skyes nas/ da de'i lan nga la med pas skyes lan khyad 'phags shig
bskur bsams pas/ sngon chad med pa'i nor ya mtshan can bskur rgyu med pas/ lan ci bskur zhes bcom ldan 'das la zhus pa/ bdag la grogs po u tra ya nas/ skyes mtshar po khyad
'phags mang po bskur byung ba la/ bdag dbul ba de 'dra'i khyad 'phags bskur rgyu ma rnyed pas/ ci bskur ba lags na zhus pas/ 'o na khyod rang skyes lan nga'i sku gzugs
la spyan ras gzigs dang / byams pa/ 'jam dpal/ phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / de skyes lan du bskur gsungs nas/ lha bzo bi shwa karma la
bri bar zhu zhus pas/ ras btul te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku'i gzi brjid kyis bris bar ma nus so/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das rgyab ngos su bzhugs te/ ras 'dul la 'od zer btang nas
byin gyis brlabs so/ /ji ltar 'od 'dug pa ltarata bris/ bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis rab gnas mdzad nas/ glang po che thal kha'i steng du bzhugs nas de la gdugs phub/ rol
mo sil snyan mang pos brgyan/ mchod pa'i bye brag bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas te skyes lan du bskur ro/ /der mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po u tra ya na 'khor dang bcas pas
rol mo 'phan gdugs rgyal mtshan ba dan mang po dang mchod pa sna tshogs pa mang pos bsus nas/ phyag dang mchod pa dpag tu med pa byas so/ /rgyal pos sku gzugs la brtags te
shin tu dad pa skyes nas mos gus byas pa dad pa drag po skyes te/ rgyal srid spangs nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi drung du rab tu byung nas dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu
thob po/ /ras ris kyi sku gzugs de ltar byin gyis brlabs nas byon no/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'da' khar rgyal po ma skyes dgra'i don du bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzad pa bcu
gnyis tshang ba'i sku bris nas/ rgyal po'i thugs dam du mdzad de/ dus phyis kyang mya ngan bsal lo/ /bris

sku'i rten de ltar ngo mtshar du byung ngo / /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das chos sku dang 'dra ba'i rten mchod rten byon tshul ni/ lum bi'i tshal du/ rgyal po don thams cad grub
par sku 'khrungs tsa na bzhugs pa'i khang par khang pa brtsegs pa gcig byung ste/ de'i tsan dan gyi phye ma bre zho gcig la yang / 'dzam bu gling pa'i nor thams cad kyis
de'i rin du mi chog pa yin la/ dbyibs ni gzhal yas khang du yod/ khang bu brtsegs pa ltar ming du grags/ bar lhag sor bzhis ma reg pa gsum rim du yod pa zhig byung ba
la/ de lha rgyal tshangs pa la gnang nas tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi mchod pa'i rten mdzad do/ kun dga' bos tsan dan gyi khang bu brtsegs pa de lta bar 'dod nas 'dzam bu
gling du thengs gcig yong ngo / /dang po grong khyer ser skya ru thub pa lum bi'i tshal du sku 'khrungs pa'i dus su/ phyogs bzhir gom pa bdun bdun bzhag pa'i dus su/ yid
bzhin lhun gyis grub pa dpal pad ma can gyi mchod rten byon/ ming pad ma khor yug can gyi mchod rten du grags/ de nas de ltar mdzad pa re re'i dus de la mchod rten re byon/
dang po la bde gshegs mchod rten zhes bya'o/ /gnyis pa byang chub chen po'i mchod rten ni/ ma ga dha byang chub rtan du gyur zhes bya ba'i mchod rten no/ /nub ba glang
spyod na/ dpe med bsam 'das zhes bya pa'i mchod rten yod/ gsum pa dpal bkra shis sgo mangs kyi mchod rten ni/ wa ra Na si'i ye shes mchod rten bya ba'o/ /bzhi pa dpal
cho 'phrul bstan pa'i mchod rten ni/ mnyan du yod par mu stegs pham mdzad kyi mchod rten zhes bya'o/ /lnga pa dpal lha las babs pa'i mchod rten ni/ grong khyer gsal ldan
du sum cu rtsa gsum lhas mchod kyi mchod rten du grags so/ drug pa dpal gser 'od can dge 'dun dbyen 'dum pa ni/ rgyal po'i khab tu byams sems mchod rten grags so/ /bdun pa
dpal ka ni ka ni/ sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs pa'i mchod rten zhes bya'o/ /brgyad pa dpal chos kyi 'khor lo bskor zhing chos rgyal mya ngan med pa sangs rgyas
mya ngan las 'das pa na/ grong khyer rtsa mchog tu mya ngan las 'das pa'i mchod rten zhes bya'o/ /rgyal mtshan ltar yongs su grags pa'i mchod rten brgyad kyis 'gro ba rnams
kyi bsod nams gsog pa'i rten mdzad do/ ring bsrel gyi mchod rten brgyad ni/ ra ma dra ma ki'i yul dang / sa la'i yul dang / gyad yul dang / yangs pa can dang / tsa na
tsa ka la pa'i yul dang / byi nu ra tsha'i yul dang / ser skya dang / rgyal po'i khab dang / brgyad na bzhugs so/ /nyi ma'i snying po'i mdo las bshad pa'i drang srong thub
pa'i bzhugs gnas mchod rten nyi shu ni/ 'dzam bu gling na/ drang srong thub pa dang dga' 'phel gnyis/ ba lang spyod na gnas skra dang 'od zer 'byung ba gnyis/ lus 'phags
na 'byung ba dang na kro lta bu gnyis/ sgra mi snyan na/ spos brtsegs dang 'od zer gnyis/ rgya mtsho'i gnas na nor bu'i snying po 'od 'phro ba'o/ /sum cu rtsa gsum na me
tog rab rgyas dang bcu'o/ /gzhan yang yangs pa can na shin tu brtan/ ser skya na gser sgrom dri zhim/ ma ga dha na rgya chen/ bcom lhag na stug po'i sbrin/ ko sa la na
rgyal dag pa/ phug gi pha rol na bde ba'i dri/ sa 'dzin na mthong ba'i lam rgyags/ kha che na gur gum rtse mo/

chu len na 'od zer snying po/ rgaya yul na sred bu'i 'od dang bcu/ kha sha li'i yul na mchod rten ghan dha'o/ /mchod rten de rnams ni/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas dang / byang
chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas/ drang srong chan po mngon
par shes pa mnga' ba thams cad gnas pa/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za rnams gnyer byed cing gtad pa'o/ /thugs phyag mtshan nam mchod rten rang byung du
bzhugs nas/ 'gro ba sems can rnams la byin gyis brlabs pa ni/ 'og min gsang ba mchog gi gnas su/ chos sku 'gyur ba med pa'i mardar/ rang byung gi mchod rten/ nam mkha'i
dkyil na/ pha lam rdzas kyi rdo rje'i lte ba la a dkar po yod/ rdo rje rtse lnga bai DUrya'i mdog can/ lha tshangs pa'i khru gang ba'i tshad gcig dbyings kyi bar snang la
bzhugs skad/ de la ye shes mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis skor ba byed pa zhig bzhugs/ nam mkha' klong yangs kyi rgyud las/ rdo rje a dang nam mkha'i dbyings/ /dngos su snang
yang mthong ba nyung / /skal med rnams kyi spyod yal min/ /zhes gsungs so/ /thugs kyi rten ma mthong ba yang / /rnam dag chos sku'i mchod rten ni/ /yongs la kyab bzhin ma
rig glo bur sgrib/ /rnam snang mdzad kyi byin brlabs las/ /rang bzhin longs sku'i mchod rten ni/ /zhing khams lnga na bzhugs nas kyang / /khams gsum phal pas ma mthong
ngo / /sprul pa'i mchod rten la/ rang byung du grub pa dang / bzhengs pa gnyis gsungs so/ /dngos po gling bzhi'i rgya mtsho'i ngos la/ rang byung gi mchod rten brgyad/ gnyis
gnyis phyogs na bzhugs kyang / spyan gyi mngon shes med pa rnams kyis mi mthong ngo / /mchod rten rnam dag gi rgyud las/ shar gyi phyogs su gnyis bstan pa/ /byams pa
rdo rje brtsegs pa gnyis gnyis dang / /lho ru snying rje rin chen brtsegs pa gnyis gnyis dang / /nub tu dag ba pad ma brtsegs pa gnyis gnyis dang / byang du btang snyoms
rgya gram brtsegs pa gnyis gnyis dang brgyad bzhugs so/ /zhes gsungs/ rang byung du grub pa'i mchod rten brgyad ni/ bdud rtsi mchog gi lung gi rgyud bdun rtsi bam brgyad
las gsungs pa/ dpal u rgyan dur khrod pad ma brtsegs pa gzi'i mchod rten/ de na dngos grub 'byor pa longs spyod yod/ yi yul dur khrod lo ka brtsegs pa/ rang byung mchod rten
'ge'u do shal/ rdzu 'phrul me chu'i dngos grub yod/ rgya gar dur khrod bsil ba'i tshal/ rang byung mchod rten bde byed brtsegs/ de na mkhas shing snying stobs che/ si
nga'i yul gyi dur khrod sku la rdzogs/ rang byung mchod rten ri bo ta la la/ de na dngos grub mthong thos can/ /kha che'i yul gyi dur khrod ho can brdal/ /rang byung mchod
rten ka ni ka/ /dngos grub bde skyid 'byung ba yin/ /sa la'i yul dur khraud gsang chen rol rang byung mchod rten 'ge'u bstan pa/ dngos grub mthu dang dbang yang che/ bal
po'i yul gyi dur khrod lhun grub brtsegs/ mchod rten bya kram ka sho ka/ dngos grub zas dang longs spyod che/ za hor yul gyi dur khrod lang ka brtsegs/ mchod rten bde
byed gzhon nu'o/ /dngos grub 'byor pa longs spyod che/ zhes gsungs te/ mchod rten de rnams dur khrod chen po'i

gnas brgyad na bzhugs kyang grub pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa 'ga' las gang rung rung gis lta bar mi spobs so/ /skal ldan rnams la mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub ster ba'i
gnas so/ /ci'i phyir na gnas brtan ma mo brgyad gnas pa'i phyir ro/ /dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten yang ma dag pa'i snang ba la phyi 'byung ba bzhi las grub pa/
dbyibs gru gsum pa gcig snang ngo / dag pa'i snang ba la chos dbyings gsung gi dbang phyug dang / dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi dkyil 'khor du snang ste/ lo skor re nas sgo rang
dbye nas lta bar 'dod skad do/ /las can rnams la byin gyis brlabs shing dngos grub ster ba'i rten yin no/ /mchod rten gyi bzhengs tshul rnams ni gong du bstan pa rnams
yin no/ /bsod nams kyi zhing 'di yang dad pas bzhengs pa/ sdig dang ma 'dres par bsam pa rnam par dag pas bsgrubs pa yin no/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan
'das nyid dga' ldan gyi gnas nas gzigs pa rnam pa lnga la gzigs nas byon te/ grong khyer ser skyar yum gyi lhums su zhugs nas/ dus la babs nas lum bi'i tshal du bltams
pa dang / gzhon nu rol rtsed mdzad cing skye rga na 'chi'i sdug bsngal gzigs pa yis/ de las thugs phyung nas skyo ba drag po skyes nas mchod rten rnam dag gi drung du rab
tu byung nas/ chu bo nairanya?dzana'i 'gram du dka' thub spyad pa'i gnas yod de/ de na lha'i sprul pa'i bzo bos byas pa'i bcom ldan 'das kyi sku rtsa rgyus dang rgal tshigs
la sogs pa gsal ba shin tu rid pa/ zhal gyi dkyil 'khor la mi 'bring po'i khru gang yod pa/ zhal nub tu gzigs pa bzhugs pa de la/ glang rdzis snyan khung du shing bu
bcug pa'i gzugs kyang rdo la byas pa yod do/ /de 'dra ba'i bzo shes pa da lta 'dzam bu'i gling na ye med skad do/ /de'i dus su yab rgyal po zas gtsang mas 'khor lnga brgya
btang ba na/ de'i mda' ru mchod rten yod do/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' de la pho nya ba de dag gis bskul nas/ dka' thub las bzhengs/ rdo rje gdan gyi lho nub tu rgyang
grags phyed tsam na/ dur khrod kyi ro ras bshus te dud pa la sogs pas kha bsgyur ba'i sa na mchod rten zhig bzhugs/ de'i shar phyogs rgyang grags phyed tsam na/ chos
gos dras pa'i sa yod de/ de na kan dha an dhe sha zhes pa'i mchod rten che ba zhig yod/ de dang nye ba na byang chub sems dpas gri dang / khab brdar ba'i brdar zheng du khru
do/ chur khru gsum pa yod de/ de la mi rnams da lta yang mchod par byed do/ /de nas byang phyogs su byon te/ rdo rje gdan gyi steng logs la sku khrus mdzad cing dbu skra
bzhar ba'i mchod rten zhig yod/ de la rdo'i them skas dang mchod rten yang bzhugs so/ /byang chub shing gi chag dum dang / me tog snying po thams cad 'dor ro/ /rab tu
byung ba thams cad kyang der khrus byed de/ der skra dang sen mo dor na gang zag de ngan song du mi 'gro zer/ de nas mtsho de'i nub na/ grong pa'i bu mo legs skyes ma dang
mjal te/ des 'o thug drangs pa'i sa na mchod rten drug phreng byas pa yod/ der 'o thug gsol nas rdo rje gdan gyi lho phyogs lcags ri'i nang na/ kho na dhe sha zhes pa'i
rdo ring khru do pa gcig yod pa la/ byang chub shing dang thub pa'i sku mtho gang tsam pa 'bur du dod pa yod/

de'i steng na mchod rten chung ngu byas pa zhig yod pa de shin tu snyan skad/ der rdo rje gdan gyi dkon gnyer rnams skra bzhar sar byed/ de nas bsdu ba yang byed do/ /de nas
'o thug gsol nas rdo rje gdan gyi shar phyogs chu bo neranya?dzana'i 'gram mchod rten zhig bzhugs pa der/ 'o thug gsol ba'i snod chur bskyur ste/ smon lam btab pa na/ nga
mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sems can gyi don grub na snod chus mi 'khyer par shog sangs mi rgya na snod chus khyer cig gsungs pa las/ lhung bzed rgyang grags
gcig tsam chus khyer nas/ de yar log ste/ yar bskyar bas/ 'ben gang tsam gyi gong nas byung ste/ lhung bzed de lhas spyan drangs/ sngar lhung bzed de bskyur ba dang / log
pa dang / phyis byung ba gsum na rdo ring 'dom re lhag pa yod pa'i steng na rdo'i mchod rten re re yod skad/ de nas sku gser gyi gtan pa phyis pa ltar gyur nas/ phar nub
phyogs su bzhud de rgyang grags phyed tsam du nye bar nub gcig gzim pa'i sar/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku gzigs nas bzhugs pa'i steng na mchod rten lha khang can gcig bzhugs
nas yod do/ /de nas tshangs pa dang brgya byin gnyis kyis byang chub sems dpa' bsu ba'i tshal na rdo ring 'dom re lhag pa'i tsa na mchod rten re bzhugs/ de nas nub byang
mtshams na phar bzhud pa na/ rma bya gcig dang 'phrad/ des byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal bas der rma bya lung bstan nas/ de'i sa na mchod rten re re bzhugs/ de nas
byang phyogs su bzhud de/ rdo rje gdan nas nyi ma phyed lam na/ ri ga ya mgo'i steng nas spyan ras gzigs dang / 'jam dpal gnyis mjal nas lha cig bzhugs te/ rdo rje lta bu'i
ring nge 'dzin mngon sum du mdzad gsungs nas/ spyan ras gzigs btang nas der lho phyogs rdo rje gdan gyi gzhir 'ongs te/ de ni sa phyogs nyams dga' bas ting nge 'dzin
skye ba'i sar gyur pas/ khong rang ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ma sbran pas/ spyan ras gzigs le lo can zhes grags te/ de'i sgom sa rdo rje
gdan gyi lcags ri'i lho phyogs sgo nang na spyan ras gzigs kyi sku zhal la mi 'bring po'i khru gang tsam yod pa zhig bzhugs/ mchod rten lha khang co ba ri zhes bya ba
gcig bzhugs so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' tshur byon pa rdo rje gdan gyi lho phyogs na bzhugs te/ bzhugs sa de na byang chub sems dpa'i rdo sku byin rlabs che ba bzhengs
pa zhig bzhugs so/ /de nas byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhud pa'i lam zhes grags pa zhig yod de/ de nas byang chub kyi shing la brtag pa bya ba dang / phyi rabs gdul
bya rnams yid ches par bya ba'i phyir byang chub shing nas 'dom bco lnga tsam du bzhud nas zhal shar du gzigs nas/ thugs ka nas 'od zer bkyes nas/ byang chub kyi shing ma
yin pa thams cad bsregs pa'i sol ba rnams spungs pa las a dkar bo de zhes bya ba'i byang chub kyi shing gcig yod do/ /de dang byang chub kyi shing dngos kyi bar 'dom bdun
tsam yod do/ /a dkar bo de yi byang phyogs na ra pa khu le zhes pa rgya mtsho la thug pa'i khron pa zhig yod de/ bcom ldan 'das kyis rngul chu'i rang bzhin du byin gyis
brlabs nas/ dgra bcom pa mang po'i gdung bzhugs skad do/ /der skra dang sen mo dor na ngan song du mi 'gro

zer ba yod pa'i steng na mchod gnas kyi rten gcig yod pa'i bum pa'i logs la/ skra dang sen mo skyur ba'i bu gu yod pa can gcig bzhugs so/ /sngar 'od zer bkye ba de na/ bcom
ldan 'das kyi sku tshad med tsam pa zhal shar phyogs su bstan pa bzhengs nas bzhugs te/ de'i steng na 'od zer 'gyed pa'i gan dho la zhes 'dom nyi shu tsam yod pa gcig yod
do/ /de nas byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te zhal nub tu bstan nas srod la bdud 'dul ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ bdud kyi dmag bye ba dung phyur phrag
sum cu rtsa gnyis byung nas mtshon cha'i char rab tu phab pa na/ lha mo hu lu ta ra'i zhal nas khyed rnams dmag ma 'dren/ drangs kyang byang chub sems dpa' mi thub ces
brjod pas/ khong rnams na re/ shAkya thub pa mi gcig po 'di nged kyis brlag par bya ba la tshegs med zer nas ma nyan te/ rgyob gsod kyi sgra chen po yang bsgrags so/ /de
nas ri bo dhe shan nam ldan 'das kyi sku gsung thugs las khro bo'i rgyal po gshin rje gshed nges par byung nas/ phyag na rdo rjer thub pa chen po'i bka' bzhin mi byed pa
la phyag na rdo rjer khyod 'di lta bu'i khro bo gshin rje gshed 'jigs pa'i gzugs bsgyur te/ bdud dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / lha ma yin dang / lha rnams chings
shig chom shig rdeg cig rgyob cig sgrol cig gsungs nas bdud dpung chen po las rgyal ba'i byams pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs so/ /der byang chub sems dpa' byams
pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs pas/ bdud thams cad pham par byas pa'i tshe/ lha mo hu lu ta ra gad mo shor bas/ de 'phags pa la mi 'tsham par dgongs nas phyag
gis zhal bkab po/ de'i shul na byang chub kyi shing nub byang mtshams nas 'dom nyi shu lhag tsam gyi tshod na yod de/ der rdo sku rang byon bzhengs pa zhal lho phyogs su
gzigs pa/ hu lu ta ra zhes grags pa zhig bzhugs so/ /de'i rtsa na rin po che'i char babs pa'i mchod rten rin chen spungs pa zhes grags pa zangs gling pas bzhengs pa zhig
yod do/ / 'jam dpal rnga sgra can gyi sku ni/ nub phyogs lcags ri'i nang na sku rang byung khru gang tsam zhig mchod rten gyi nang na bzhugs pa'i mdun/ rdo'i gan dho la
yod pas/ nang phyogs nyi ma dros tsa na/ rna ba gtad nas nyan pas/ rnga sgra 'u ru ru grags pa yod/ de'i rgyab kyi tho skor na rdo leb chen po la/ rgya nag gi yi ge bris
pa mang po yod do/ /de nas nam gyi gung la zag pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin brnyes nas zhal shar du gzigs te/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes brnyes te/ mngon par rdzogs
par sangs rgyas so/ /zhag bdun phrag bdun bzhugs pa la bdun phrag dang po la zhabs skyil krung ma bshig par bzhugs/ gnyis pa la bzhengs nas 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad
zhabs kyis nye bar bcags te/ rdo rje gdan gyi byang phyogs rdo rje'i ra ba'i nang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyis gom pa bcu gnyis bor ba'i sa na/ pad ma chen po phub tsam
bcu gnyis byung ba'i mtha' ma'i pad ma gnyis kyi rtsa bar mchod rten re yang yod do/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi rtsa'i gdan bsdus pa'i sa na/ mchod rten byas pa ni logs
re la 'dom brgyad brgyad yod pa la/ dpangs su 'dom nyi shu tsam yod pa gcig lho phyogs byang chub kyi shing

gi rtsa na bzhugs/ de nas bdun phrag gsum pa la stong gsum rings pa nas rings par zhabs kyis bcags pa'i dus kyi byang phyogs rdo'i ra ba'i rgyab/ 'dom pa bzhi tsam gyi mtshams
na mchod rten mi che ba bcu gnyis kyi 'phreng ba byas pa yod/ de nas bdun phrag bzhi pa la/ zhag bdun du spyan mi btsum par byang chub kyi shing la gzigs te/ byang chub
kyi shing 'di la brten nas 'das pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyang sangs rgyas/ ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba yang 'di la brten nas sangs rgya bas/ thams cad la drin
che snyam du dgongs nas rten cing 'brel bar 'byung bar byin gyahis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyang de ltar mdzad gsungs/ de'i sa na bcom ldan 'das kyi sku tshad
byang chub kyi shing la gzigs pa gcig bzhugs pa'i steng na gan dho la 'dom nyi shu rtsa lnga pa gcig yod/ de'i rgyab na bcom ldan 'das kyis dag pa'i skyes rabs lnga brgya/
ma dag pa'i skye ba lnga brgya ste stong bzhe pa'i sa na mchod rten lha khang yod pa'i nang na bcom ldan 'das kyi sku tshad sbrul gyi gdengs kas sku rgyab dang dbu la
bkab pa gcig bzhugs/ de na na?ya gro ta'i sdong po chen po gcig kyang yod/ de nas bdun phrag lnga pa la klu'i rgyal po btang bzung gis phyag byas pa'i sa na mchod rten zhig
yod/ de nas rdo rje gdan gyi nub phyogs su byon pa na/ shin tu grang ba byung ste klu'i rgyal po btang bzung gis sbrul gyi lus kyi bcom ldan 'das kyi sku la dkyis te/
gdengs kas sku la bkab po/ de'i shul na zangs gling pas bzhengs pa'i mchod rten gcig gi nang na/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku shin tu legs pa sbrul gyi gdengs kas dbu bkab pa bzhugs
so/ /mcho'i nang na rdo'i theb skas bcom ldan 'das kyi mdun du byung ba yod/ de'i shar phyogs mda' rgyang gang tsam gyi sa na/ rgyal po bzhis lhung bzed phul ba'i sa
na mchod rten 'dom gsum pa gcig yod pa'i rtsa na/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku khru gang tsam gcig la rgyal po chen po bzhis lhung bzed phul ba'i tshul du byas pa yod do/ /de
nas bdun phrag drug pa la byang gi phyogs rgyang grags gcig tsam la tshur byon pa'i sar mu stegs kun tu rgyu ba 'dul ba'i sa na/ na?yagro ta'i shing sdong yod pa'i sa na/
mchod rten gcig bzhugs/ de nas zhag bdun phrag bdun pa la tshur byon nas/ rdo rje gdan gyi shar phyogs kyi sgo 'gram/ lcags ri'i rgyab lam po che'i g.yas phyogs na tshong
dpon ga gon bzang skyong dang mjal te/ sbrang rtsi la sogs phul/ de dag la shis par brjod pa'i lung bstan pa na/ mchod rten 'dom gang tsam gcig gi logs la bcom ldan 'das
kyi sku dang / tshong dpon ga go na'i gzugs byas pa yod do/ /de nas yang byon te/ rdo rje gdan gyi lho nub kyi mtshams shing na?ya gro ta'i sdong po gcig gi drung na/
chos mi gsung bar brtson pa chung ba la thugs gzhol te/ zab zhi spros bral zhes gsungs te bzhugs pa la/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin gyis gsol ba btab pa'i sa na/ mchod rten
na?ya gro ta a de zhes pa 'dom lnga tsam pa gcig yod pa'i nang na bcom ldan 'das kyi sku mi 'bring po tsam gcig zhal nub tu gzigs pa'i rtsa na tshangs pa dang brgya byin
gyi gzugs byas pa yod/ mchod rten gyi lho byang na sgo gnyis yod/ de nas wa ra Na sir bzhud de chos kyi 'khor

lo dang po bskor/ gnyis pa rgyal po'i khab dang / bya rgod phung po'i ri la chos gsungs pa dang / gsum pa yangs pa can dang / grong khyer pad mo can du chos gsungs pa dang
/ gnas gzhan du yang bzhugs te chos gsungs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa'i mchod rten bzhengs tshul rnams so/ /de nas dpal nA len dra na dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad
bzhugs pa'i dus su bstan pa dar bas/ gtsug lag khang chen po gcu bzhi/ chung ngu dgu bcu go bzhi yod/ dge slong paNDi ta lnga brgya/ dge tshul paNDi ta lnga brgya/ sngags
kyi paNDi ta lnga brgya/ bha ling a tsarya la sogs pa gtor ma'i ku su lu lnga brgya bzhugs/ de'i dus su bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa dar bas/ mu stegs pas phrag dog byas
nas dmag chen po drangs pas/ sgrol ma brgyad dang mgon po brgyad kyi lha khang bshig nas dmas par byas so/ /de nas ring zhig na/ yul dbus su rnal 'byor pa zhig gis lha mo
'od zer can chu bo gang gA'i 'gram du bsgrubs pas zhal mthong nas/ dngos grub ci 'dod zer/ nga rgyal po gcig thob par 'dod byas pas/ ba glang rdzi'i grong zhig na ma mad
gsum ngu ba mthong / khyod ci la ma dga' zhes dris pas/ nga'i bu la rgyal po'i res mos babs zer nas/ de la ngu rgyu ci yod dris pas/ do nub 'chi ba yin zer/ nga yis khyed
kyi bu'i tshab bya'am byas pas/ 'o na rung ste zer nas grong khyer de nyid du rnal 'byor pa de rgyal por dbang bskur ro/ /de'i nub mo rgyal po'i mal du btsun mo klu ru
sprul pa des sbrul gcig tu byas nas za ru byung bas lha mo 'od zer can gyis rdo rje'i dbyugs pas sbrul de mgo bo bcom nas bsad do/ /nangs par skye bo thams cad rol mo dang
bcas te rgyal po'i spur 'byin du byung bas rgyal po cad ma nyes par bzhugs pa mthong bas/ de rnams na re/ nged kyi rgyal po res mos bab na nub re la 'chi ba yin na/ khyod
ma shi ba ji tsug yin byas pas/ des sngar rgyal po klus bsad 'dug mdang ngas klu btul yod pas/ da rgyal po mi 'chi yis khyed rang rnams rgyal por gang 'os pa skos shig
byas pas/ da khyod rang la rgyal po zhu zer nas/ der des rgyal po mdzad pa la btsun mo brgya tham pa khab tu blangs dbang bskur ro/ /de'i mtshan yang go ba pa la zhes bya'o/
/de'i btsun mo dam pa zhig gi rmi lam du dge slong zhig gnas g.yar zer bas de rgyal po'i snyan du gsol bas/ gnas g.yar du chugs shig rgyal bu btsa' ba'i brda' yin gsungs/
de'i dus su dge slong sbyangs pa'i yon tan dpal ldan pa/ grub pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ sa lu bya ba zhig yod pas/ de'i thugs dgongs la/ 'dzam bu'i gling du theg
pa chen po'i chos dar bar bya/ de la nga skye ba la/ 'dzam bu'i gling du theg pa chen po'i chos dar bar bya/ de la nga skye ba la dbang thob pas dbus gyur gyi tshal/ shar
phyogs kyi mu khyer ri pa ri zhes bya ba'i rgyud 'di la bsil ba gang gA chu bo/ lho na nags la sogs pa yon tan du ma dang ldan pa 'dir/ rdo leb 'di'i steng du dge 'dun
sde pa bzhi las gyes pa bco brgyad/ theg pa chen po gcig bsam gtan pa'i gcig ste/ nyi shu tham pa 'tsho ba'i gzhis gcig yod na dga' ba la snyam du dgongs so/ /de yang da
lta nga la nus pa mi 'dug pas rgyal po 'di'i sras su gyur na rung ba la snyam nas/ mu tig hab rtse gcig yod pa

de btsun mo dam pa la bcol bas/ rgyal po la zhus pas tshags bya gsungs so/ /der rgyal po la zhus pas/ zungs gsungs pas bzung ngo / /dge slong des dkon mchog la mchod pa phul/
rgyal po'i sras su skye ba dang / gtsug lag khang rtsig par smon lam rnam par dag pa btab po/ /de nas skye gnas bzang por 'pho ba byas so/ /der btsun mo lto ba sbrum mar
gyur to/ /sngar rgyal po la sras med pas shin tu dgyes te/ btsun mo'i lus po'i rim gro cher byas so/ /der sras rgyal bu zhig btsas pa dang / mtshan yang ra ma pa la zhes
btags so/ /de cher skyes kyang smrar ma 'dod nas/ dus lan gcig gi tshe btsun mo yum la/ bdag gi mu tig hab rtse de gsol zhes zer ro/ /der btsun mo ha las te/ rgyal po
la zhus pa/ sngon dge slong gis mu tig hab rtsa bcol ba de las gzhan 'os med do gsungs/ rgyal bu de mtshan dang ldan zhing blo sbyong la sogs lapa la tshegs med de/ mkhas
shing dran pa dang ldan par gyur to/ /de nas smon lam btab pa'i sar gnas brtsigs pas gnod sbyin gyis yang yang bshig go/ /de dmag mis bsrungs kyang ma thub par bsig go/
/yang slar brtsigs te rgyal bu rang gis bsrungs pas yang gnod sbyin de bshig tu byung ngo / /der gnod sbyin la 'thab pas rgyal po rgyal bar gyur to/ /der gnod sbyin na re/
rgyal bu khyod nga'i gnas 'phrog tu byung bas bshig pa yin/ da ngas khyod kyi sbyin bdag bya yis ming de nga'i ming dang mthun par thogs zer bas/ 'bri ka ma la si la bya
bar btags te/ tshul khrims kyi dri ngad dang ldan pa yin no/ /de'i rab gnas slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad do/ /de nas jo bo shAkya dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i
sku tshad de der bzhugs su gsol lo/ /rgyal po de yang rgyal phran brgyad cu rtsa bzi la dbang byed pa gcig byung ngo / /de la btsun mo mang du yod pa las/ de rnams la
mchod gnas dge slong ma re re yod pa'i dus su/ btsun mo gcig rgyal po de dang ye ma 'phrad pa la/ der mchod gnas mas rgyal po dbang du bsdu ba'i rdzas de 'bu'i sha khu'i
tshod mar bskyur bas rgyal po la 'dren ma nus nas mtshor bor nas/ der klu'i rgyal po dbang 'dus nas rgyal po'i cha byad kyis rtag tu btsun mo'i tsa na 'gro ba de rgyal pos
mthong nas/ klu khyod nga'i btsun mo la spyod pa ci tsug yin dris pas/ klu na re/ nga la ni dbang med de/ nga yod pa'i mtshor dbang du bsdu ba'i rdzas phog pas lan pa
yin/ da rdzas 'byin du chug dang / btsun mo la yang nga'i bu chags yod pas/ de yang khyed rang gi bu gyis shig zer ro/ /btsun mo la bu byung ba de'i ming yang rgyal bu de
ba pa la zhes bya ste/ de nas che ru phyin pa dang / gtsug lag khang bzhengs par 'dod nas rtsis byas pas/ stegs bu'i khar macod pa bshams/ mar me'i kong bu bzhag nas de
bya rog gis 'khyer te/ de gar song ba der lha khang rtsigs shig zer ro/ /de mtshor bskyur bas/ da skal ba med do zhes mya ngan byed do/ /'khor rnams kyis mtsho de bsho bar
bshams pas/ yab klu'i rgyal po des sdong grogs byas te mtsho de bskams so/ /der gtsug lag khang bzhengs pas ming yang o tan ta pU ri bya bar grags so/ /rgya mtsho sbas
pa'i lha khang bya ba yin no/ /der sman tsha ba gsum bor bas tra5à½² ka tu ka'i lha khang zer/ mu stegs rig 'dzin

grub pa'i g.yog pos ro langs gser du 'gyur ba'i las byas kyang zer/ der paNDi ta mang po bzhugs pas gtsug lag khang chen por grags so/ /der ngo bo shAkya dgung lo bcu gnyis
pa'i sku tshad spyan drangs nas sems can gyi don mdzad do/ /de'i dus na rgyal po de ba pa la la sras med nas dkon mchog la mchod pa phul/ ngan slong la sbyin gtong chen
po byas pas/ sras gcig btsas gtsas te ming dharma pa la bya bar btags/ rgyal po des dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad der mchod pa byed cing 'gro don rgya che ba mdzad do/
/de'i tshe nub phyogs bha len ta'i phyi rol pa mu stegs kyi rgyal pos yul dbus su dmag drangs te/ lha khang thams cad bshig glegs bam thams cad bsregs/ paNDi ta thams cad
bkrongs/ rgyal po dharma pa la pham palas bstan pa nyams te/ rgya nag gi rgyal por nga la rgyu sems cad la 'bras bu sangs rgyas 'byung ba dam pa'i chos bya ba yod pa la
phyis mu stegs kyi phrag dog byas nas dmag gis gtsug lag khang bshig bstan pa dmas par byas pas/ khyod rgya nag rgyal po dpung che la thabs mkhas pas nged la sdong grogs
dgos pas/ khyed kyi dmag dpung che ba gcig btang bar zhu bya ba'i 'phrin yig btang bas/ rgya nag gi rgyal pos za 'og gi gos srub med pa gyon pa'i thugs kar dpal pe'u brtsegs
ma'i khang bu yod pa gcig gis sna drangs pa'i gser/ dngul/ dar zab/ rin po che'i bum pa la sogs pa lo gcig gi nang du skyes chen po lan gsum brdzangs/ 'o cag gnyis
po grogs po bya'o zhes pa'i 'phrin dang skyes byung / rgyal po dharma pa las de rkyen byas nas mu stegs byed pham par byas so/ /lha khang mang du brtsigs/ paNDi ta'i grwa
mang po btsugs/ glegs bam mang pa bris pas bstan pa sngar gyi sor chud pas rgyal po thugs dgyes nas bsams pa/ blon po rnams spro nas yod/ 'di rnams rgya nag po'i drin yin
pas skyes lan chen po 'dod du yong snyam ste thugs las cher byung bas de nas dus lan gcig rgya nag rgyal pos pho nya ba btang nas 'phrin yig 'di skad du bskur ro/ /kye
rgya gar rgyal po chos skyong bstan pa'i bdag /sngon bsags bsod nams dam pa'i dpal gyur pas/ /rigs rgyud mtho la bzang ba chos rgyud 'khrungs/ /gnas bzang mchog tu 'phags
pa rgya gar yul/ /sngon bsags 'phro mthud chos skyong mnga' bdag mdzad/ /bsod nams khyad du 'phags pas dge tshogs spel la brtson/ /sku khams bde zhing chos 'khor 'phel bar
bdag gis 'khums/ /gnas dang yal gyis bskal nas zhal mjal ma gyur kyang / /las dang smon lam 'brel bas bzlas pa'i gtam la brten/ /phan tshun brtse sems skyes pas grogs
su skyes kyis 'grul/ /khyed ni yul dbus sangs rgyas byon pa'i gnas su 'khrungs/ /bsod nams gsog pa'i mchod gnas rten gyis phongs pa med/ /bdag ni sangs rgyas zhabs kyis ma
bcags rgya nag yul du skyes/ /sngon gyi bsod nams dman pas bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing med pas/ /longs su spyod nor gyis phongs par ma gyur kyang / /mchod pa 'bul ba'i rten
zhig dgos pas na/ /khyod kyi mchod gnas sangs rgyas zhal skyin de/ /dge slong bzhi dang bcas te gnang bar zhu/ /zhes springs nas byung bas/ mi bskur bar thabs med nas
'di skad du springs so/ /rgyal po khyed la zhu zhing gsol ba ni/ /bdag gi mchod gnas sangs rgyas zhal skyin 'di/

/'jig rten 'di na 'di dang mtshungs pa med/ /mchod gnas gzhan du bzhugs pa ma mchis kyang / gang zhig rkang gnyis gtso bo sangs rgyas nyid kyi lung / /sangs rgyas nyid kyis
rab tu gnas shing mnga' gsol ba'i/ /sku gzugs sangs rgyas nyid dang mnyam pa 'di/ /gang zhig de la phyag dang mchod byed pa/ /sangs rgyas nyid la mchod dang khyad par med/
/de phyir dad dang mos pas 'di mchod pas/ /sangs rgyas nyid nges par 'gyur bas na/ /khyed kyi bka' bstsal shin tu lci bas na/ /bdag gi mchod gnas khyed la dbul bar bgyi'o/
/khyed kyis sems can 'gro don spel bar mdzod/ /ces springs nas sku shing rta'i steng du bzhugs su gsol te/ dharma pa la dbul bas skyes dod sangasar rgyas 'grub pa'i
rten yod bya ba'i 'phrin springs pa yin pas/ da yang rgya nag rgyal po bya ba chos nyams chung chud pa yin pas chos skyes su bya'o gsungs nas o tan ta pU ri nas dgung lo
bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad de gyad mi bzhis spyan drangs nas de dang dge slong mngon pa 'din pa gcig mdo sde 'dzin pa gcig 'dul ba 'dzin pa gcig theg pa chen po ba gcig de
rnams 'khor dang bcas te rdzings chab kyi steng nas spyan drangs te/ rgya nag rgyal po'i yul du gshegs so/ /mtshan yang jo bo shAkya mu ne ru gsol/ gdan khri da lta o tan
ta pU ri na bzhugs so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung dang bcas pa rgya nag po drin che bas de rnams brdzangs so/ /der rgya nag po'i yul du lo lnga brgya bzhugs nas 'gro
don mdzad do/ / de nas rgya gar gyi rgyal po dang bal po'i rgyal po gnyis skyes phar bskur tshur bskur ba las bal po'i rgyal po dharma a sho bya bas rgya gar gyi rgyal
po dharma pa la zhes bya ba chos skyong ba'i rgyal po de la skyes su rin po che glang po che'i rgyab khal gcig brdzangs nas de'i skyes lan du sangs rgyas dgung lo brgyad
pa'i sku tshad jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje gnang bar zhu zhes 'phrin springs pas mi bskur pa'i thabs med nas gnang ngo / /de yang bal yul du lo lnga brgya bzhugs nas 'gro don
mdzad do/ /de ni macom ldan 'das kyi sku tshad jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje yis ji ltar 'gro don mdzad pa'i 'phro las 'phros pa'i lo rgyus lags so/ /sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab
bzhengs par snga ba dpal lha yul du tshigs su bcad pa rin po che la bris pa yod skad/ mi yul sangs rgyas kyi sku ras ris la bris pa'i gshan du spro ba bskyed pa'i tshig
brtsam par bya zhing 'jug par bya/ /sangs rgyas bstan la dad par bya/ /'dam bu'i khyim na glang chen bzhin/ /'chi bdag sde ni gzhom par bya/ /chos 'dul 'di la spyod gyur
pa/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rab spangs nas/ /sdug bsngal mtha' ma med byed par 'gyur/ /zhes pa la sogs pa bris/ ras ris kyi gsham du rten 'brel bcu gnyis dang / 'phags pa'i lam
yan lag brgyad pa bris nas yod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi gso sbyong dang / khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin gyi mchod gnas kyi glegs bam klog pa'i yi ge zhus
nas bris pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi gsung gis yi ge dang / ming dang / tshig dang gsum gyi tshogs bsdus la phyi glegs bam du bsdus shig gsungs nas yi ge bsdus pa lnga bcu
pa/ dbyangs kyi yi ge bcu drug la a li zhes pa dang / gsal byed sum cu rtsa drug la ka li zhes bya ba dang /

de ltar a li ka li'i mdo gsungs/ ming gi tshogs bsdus pa la 'khor ba zhes pa dang / lam zhes pa la sogs ming sum brgya drug cu ru bsdus te gsungs/ tshig gi tshogs la chos kyi
phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong du gsungs pa rnams lung du bris pa yang gsang sngags rnams lha gnas su/ rdo rje 'dzin don sdud pa po rnams kyis rin po che gser gyi glegs
bam la baiDUrya zhun mas bris pa dang / bka' sde snod gsum gyi chos rnams thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas bka' bsdu ba lan gsum byas pa'i phyi ma la nyan thos dang / byang
chub sems dpa' dang / so so'i skye bo paNDi ta mkhas pa rnams kyis bka' shog la snag tsha nag pos bkod nas bka' rnams lung du bris pa ni chos dkon mchog gi rten yin/ 'phags
pa'i dge 'dun dkon mchog gi rten ji lta bu byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi 'khor na nyan thos kyi dge 'dun/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun gnyis yod pa la nyan thos mang
yang nyis brgya lnga bcu dang brgya dang bcu drug yod kyang gtso bo lngar 'dus te/ sras sgra gcan 'dzin dang / shes rab can gyi mchog shA ri'i bu dang / rdzu 'phrul can
gyi mchog mo'u 'gal gyi bu dang lnga'o/ /de la 'od srung mya ngan 'das pa'i sku lus brag bya rkang can gyi ri'i zom du bzhugs so/ /ri'i rtse mo ru rgyal po ma skyes dgras
mchod rten brtsigs te phyis byams pa'i bstan pa la lta bar bshad pas 'od srungs kyi rten yin no/ /mo'u 'gal gyi bu ni dgra bcom pa bdun khrir bcas pa mu stegs kyi tshogs
kyis grong khyer shing thag can du dbyig pas bcom nas mya ngan las 'das/ ston pa mya ngan las 'das pa ni thos par yang mi bya na mthong ba ni lta ci smos zhes pas de'i
dus su shA ri'i bu yang dgra bcom brgyad khri dang bcas pa grong khyer ya ngar du mya ngan las 'das nas spur zhugs la bzhen nas ring bsrel bsdus te mchod pa byed lugs sangs
rgyas nyid la zhus nas mchod rten brtsigs so/ /sru skye dgu'i bdag mo gau ta mi dgra bcom pa lnga brgya yang grong khyer pad mo can du lus so/ /kun dga' bos bstan pa
rjes su bskyangs nas phyis bcu pa'i dbus su mya ngan las 'das nas de'i spur gnyis su mdzad nas cha gcig rgyal po ma skyes dgra la gnang nas mchod rten mdzad do/ /cha gcig
yangs pa can gyi li tsa byi rnams la gnang nas mchod rten brtsigs so/ /sras sgra gcan 'dzin 'khor dgra bcom pa stong dang bcas nub phyogs pri yam ku'i gling na da lta yang
zhal bzhugs so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo dang sgra gcan 'dzin gnyis phyag gis bzung nas kun dga' bo ni go re long / sgra gcan 'dzin 'di nga'i bu/ 'di gnyis phyogs
bcu'i sangs rgyas la gtad/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis skyongs/ dge 'dun rnams kyis khur cig gsungs so/ /mdo sde dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su 'dzin pa gsung ba'i dus su
nyan thos 'od srungs chen po sangs rgyas kyi gdan phyed la bzhag nas 'od srungs ni nga dang mnyam mo zhes gsungs pas tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs dang dka' thub dang tshangs
par spyod pa la gnas pa gang ci yang rung ba de dag ni 'phags pa dgyes pa'i tshul khrims mchog ces bya ste gnas brtan rgyal po'i thu bo dang 'dra bar rab tu byung
nas ring po ma lon pa/ tshangs par spyod pa/ mngon par spyod pa rnams kyi mchog 'di lta ste/ dge slong tshe dang

ldan pa kun shes ko'u di na ya dang / 'dod pa chung ba dang sbyangs pa'i yon tan la gnas pa dang / chog shes pa rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa 'od srungs chen po dang / shes rab
che ba dang stobs che ba rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu dang / rdzu 'phrul dang mthu che ba rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa mo'u 'gal gyi bu chen po dang / lha'i
mig dang ldan pa rnams mchog 'phags pa ma 'gag pa dang / mang du thos pa rnams kyi mchog tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo dang / 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa
nye bar 'khor dang / chos smra ba rnams kyi mchog byams ma'i bu gang po dang / bslab la gus pa rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa sgra gcan 'dzin dang / mal cha dang stan bgo ba rnams
kyi mchog gyad nor gyi bu dang / 'khor du seng ge'i sgra grags pa rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa bha ra dhwa dza bsod snyoms len dang / khyim bdag dad pa skyed pa rnams kyi
mchog 'phags pa nag po 'char ka dang / lha dang mi yis mchod pa rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa legs mthong dang / zhes gsang sngasags rjes 'dzin las gsungs so/ /nyan thos rnams
kyahi nang nas che ba rnams yin no/ /gzhan yang gtso chen brgyad dang bcu drug dang / dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcu la sogs pa rnams las phyis nyan thos kyi sde
bco brgyad du gyes pa ni kun dga' bo nas brgyud pa mang ngo / /lnga brgya tha ma'i dus na sangs rgyas kyi na bza' ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan gos gsum 'chang ba yan chod
nyan thos rnams kyi rten du byin gyis brlabs te bzhag go/ /shAkya seng ge'-i bstan pa yi/ byung tshul mdo tsam shes ldan grogs po'i ngor/ ma 'brel bab col spangs te tshul
bzhin bkod/ 'khor lo gsum dang bsdu ba gsum/ gtan la 'bebs byed bstan bcos rim gsum dang / /rnam dbye zhib mo chos 'byung rgyas pa 'dir/ /bye brag sde pa'i rnam dbye bstan
pa ni/ /bstan pa'i rtsa ba sde pa rnam bzhi ste/ /thams cad yod smra phal chen gnas bstan pa/ /mang pos bkur ba de yang mkhan pas dbye/ /de la sgra gcan 'dzin dang nye
bar 'khor/ /ka ta ya na 'od srungs rim bzhin no/ /de las gyes pas bco brgyad dag tu blta'o/ /gzhi'i dang po 'od srungs ste/ sa ston sde dang chos srung sde/ /mang thos
gos dmar slob ma dang / /rnam par phye ste smra ba dang / /yod par smra ba'i sde pa bdun/ /shar dang nub dang gangs ri gnas/ /'jig rten 'das par smra ba dang / /rtag par
smra ba'i sde dang lnga/ /phal chen po/ rgyal byed tshal gnas/ 'jig med gnas/ gtsug lag khang chen gnas brtan pa/ sa sgrogs ri dang srung ba pa/ gnas ma bu yi sde rnams ni/
kun gyis bkur ba rnam gsum/ de dag rnams kyi khyad par rnams/ yul ston slob dpon bye brag las/ tha dad rnam pa bco brgyad do/ /zhes pa thams cad yod smra'i sde/ sgra gcan
'dzin gyis kun dga' bo la/ sha na'i gos can nyer sbas dang / dhi ti ka dang nag po ba/ legs 'ongs 'phags pa blo mi phebs/ de yang sde pa'i gyes lugs rnam par bzhag pa
ni 'phags pa nyan thos la mdo sde pa dang / bye brag smra ba gnyis kyi grub mtha' 'dzin/ de gnyis las nyan thos kyi sde pa bco brgyad gyes/ de yang btsun pa lha chen po
zhes pas/ lha rnams ma rig pa yis bslus/ /lam ni sgra'i rgyun las byung / /the tshom can ni gzha' ru 'jug /'di

ni sangs rgyas bstan pa yin/ /de skad smras pas ma matun pas/ /rgan rigs gang zag tshig yin zer/ /gzhon pa rgyal bana'i tshig yin zer/ /smras nas dge 'dun phal chen dang /
/gnas brtan pa yi sde gnyis byung / /de las rtsa ba'i sde bzhir gyes/ /phal chen gyi sde dang thams cad yod smra'i sde/ gnas brtan pa dang legs dpon pa/ phal chen pa dang
lnga ru gyes/ shar gyi ri bo'i sde/ nub kyi ri bo'i sde/ gangs ri'i sde/ 'jig rten 'das smra'i sde/ rtag smra'i sde/ thams cad yod smra bdun du gyes/ thams cad yod par smra
ba dang / 'od srungs sde dang chos srung sde/ mang du thos pa'i sde/ gos dmar can gyi sde dang / rnam par phye ste smra ba'i sde/ gnas brtan pa dag gsum du gyes/ rgyal
byed tshal gnas kyi sde dang / 'jig med rigs gnas kyi sde dang / gtsug lag khang chen po'o/ legs dpon pa la gsum du gyes/ sar sgrogs rigs kyi sde pa dang / srung ba'i sde
pa dang / gnas ma bu'i sde'o/ /de las gyes pa bco brgyad do/ /'phags pa nyan thos la mdo sde pa dang bye phrag smra ba gnyis so/ /grub mtha' 'dzin pa de gnyis lam bco
brgyad du gyes lugs bstan pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun rnams kyi rten byung tshul ni/ byang chub sems dpa' bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod pa'i nang nas sangs rgyas bcom
ldan 'das dang mnyam pa bzhi yod de/ byams pa ni dam pa tog dkar pos dga' ldan nas 'dzam bu'i gling du byon pa'i dus su byams pa rgya gar lho phyogs kyi khrong khyer gser
ldan na yod pa la lha yul du ston pa'i rgyal tshab dgos nas dga' ldan du skye ba bzhes/ chos kyi rgyal tshab mdzad do/ /'jam dpal ni shar phyogs kun tu bzang po'i zhing
nas zab mo'i don zhu chen la byon pa yin no/ /spyan ras gzigs ni nub phyogs bde ba can nas gsung rab kyi mdzod 'dzin pa la byon pa yin no/ /phyag na rdo rje ni shar phyogs
mngon par dga' ba nas bdud dang ma rungs thams cad 'dul ba'i don la byon nas byang chub sems dpa' bzhis bstan pa skyong ngo / /tshul rnams ni gong du bstan pa rnams
so/ /de bzhin sku dang gsung dang thugs dang mchod rten rang byung du byon pa dang / bzo bos byas te yon gyi bdag pos bzhengs pa ni bsam las 'das so/ /de rnams kyi 'gro don
ni bsam las 'das so/ /gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams khyi'u dang / bu mo/ khyim pa dang / rab tu byung ba dang / rgyal po dang / bram ze dang / ded dpon gyi cha
byad rnams dang / dud 'gro'i lus blangs nas de'i gzugs kyis sems can gyi don mdzad pa yang bsam las 'das so/ /bskal bzang lnga brgya dang gtso chen brgyad mi'i yul na bzhugs
par bshad do/ /li yul 'dir ni sangs rgyas stong po thams cad kyi bstan pa 'byung bar lung bstan pa las sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi bstan pa nub nas der drang srong gnyis
kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen byas so/ /de gnyis kyang mi ngan pa rnams kyis gtses pas rdzu 'phrul gyis yul gzhan du song ngo / /der klu rnams kyis yul de mtshor btang ngo
/ /dus phyis sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa 'khaur mang po dang bcas pa nam mkha' la rdzu 'phrul gyis byon te/ ri glang ru la bzhugs nas mtsho de la pad mo sum brgya lnga bcu
rtsa gsum 'dug pa de sku gzugs dang bcas pa'i dgon pa dang gtsug lag khang ghan dhe brdungs pa'i sde dgon

de snyed 'byung ba'i snga ltas su gsungs so/ /mtsho de shA ri'i bu'i gseg shang gi yu ba dang rnam sras kyi gdung gi rtse mo gnyid kyi ral gris gshos gtsang po la pho ste li
yul snang bar byas so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen thob kyis sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi mchod rten drung du bzugs te yul de byung bar gyur pa'i tshe/ thub pa'i
sku gzugs byed par sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs so/ /nam mkha'i snying pos kyang gtsug khang 'jig tshogs spong byed ces bya ba grub nas/ sa gzhi mchod gnas su 'gyur bar byin
gyis brlabs so/ /spyan ras gzigs kyis kyang / gtsug lag khang 'od mdzes zhes pa mdzad nas/ dngos grub thams cad 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs so/ /byams pas kyang / gtsug
lag khang bi si no nya zhes bya ba bsgrubs nas bdag nyid bzhugs par byin gyis brlabs so/ /sa'i snying pos kyang gtsug lag khang ye shes ri zhes bya ba bzhengs nas byin
gyis brlabs so/ /phyag dang mchod pa bya bar byin gyis brlabs so/ /byang chub sems dpa' sman pa'i rgyal pos gtsug lag khang sa na rtse zhes bya ba mdzad nas dngos grub ma
lus par 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs so/ /kun tu bzang pos kyang gtsug lag khang dge 'dun skyong zhes bya ba bsgrubs nas dngos grub 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs so/ /de bzhin
du sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang dgra bcom pa rnams kyis li yul du gtsug lag khang dang skyed mos tshal dang dgon
pa'i gnas 'byung bar byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo brgya song nas rgya nag gi rgyal po cha nang zhes bya ba la bu stong
du gcig gis ma tshang ba rgyal po bya ngan med mchod rten go ma sa la ghan dha la mchod pa 'bul du yong ba na der sras gcig btsas pa na bram ze mtshan mkhan la mtshan
bstan pas yab kyi ring la rgyal po byed par lung bstan to/ /der rgyal pos rgyal bu bor bas bsod nams kyi mthus sa la nu ma byung zhing 'dug pa de rnam thos sras kyis rgya
nag rgyal po la byin no/ /der song ba dang rgyal bu'i zla bo rnams kyis khyod rgyal po'i bu ma yin no/ /der song ba dang rgyal bu'i zla bo rnams kyis khyod rgyal po'i bu
ma yin no/ /zhes smras pas/ 'o na nga gar skyes pa'i sa der skyol zer nas sdod du ma 'dod do/ /der rgyal pos kyang nub phyogs na sngon sangs rgyas rnams kyis byin gyis
brlabs pa/ mchod rten go ma sa la ghan dha yod pa der rgyal bu sa la nu lo bcu gnyis lon pa gcig blon po ja shos gtso byas pa'i dmag khri tsho gcig bcas li yul 'dzin du btang
ngo / /de yang lo bcu dgu pa la li yul btab ste li yul bzung / des lo bcu gnyis li yul gyi rgyal po mdzad do/ /sa la nu'i bu rgyal po byi tsa na sam bya ni 'jam dpal
gyi sprul pa yin no/ /de'i ring la li yul du dam pa'i chos byung ste dar bar byas so/ /de'i dus su byams pa'i sprul pa bai ro tsa na bya ba byon/ de'i phyir de la sa nu'i
yul li yul zhes bya bar grags so/ /de'i tshe rgya gang nub phyogs nas chos rgyal mya ngan med kyi blon po yag sha zhes bya ba dmag stong tsho bdun dang bcas pa der 'ongs
te 'dug pas yul de'i skad rgya gar dang mthun pa/ spyod tshul bzhi ni rgya nag dang mthun par yod/ mya ngan

med kyi btsun mo chung ba sa la nu'i ma khrus byed pa'i tshe rnam sras nam mkha' la 'gro ba mthong ba la chags pa skyes pa las byung ste de nas sa la nu'i bu'i yul du hor dang
/ gru gu dang / sog po dang / sum pa dang / bod la sogs pa'i dmag 'ongs pa na/ rnam sras kyis de dag dmag dpon nang 'khrug byed pa dang / dmag rnams tshe thungabar byed
do zhes bshad do/ de dag ni mdo sde du ma dang / glang ru lung bstan pa las bshad do/ /le'u then gyi sa tshigs mkhar dge ba can/ grong khyer chain po dngar ldan na/ sangs
rgyas kyi sku bzhugs pa'i mthus/ yul gzhan gyi tshong dpon mang po der 'ong bar bshad do/ /yul de ni ru thog gi rgyab na yod do/ /bstan pa'i snyigs ma la sngags pa lcang
lo can smon lam thebs nas/ grol lam bskyed rdzogs thun re bsgoms pa dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug rnam rtog la thog brdzis byed pa rnams byang chub sems dpa'i dge
'dun gyi rten du bzhag go/ /de ltar rten gsum byon tshul lo/ /de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/ slad ma'i dus na/ dkon macog gsum gyi rten gsum
dang / bstan pa dang / chos dang / gang zag rnams zhing sus bsrung bar 'gyur zhes zhus pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ bstan pa la dga' ba rnams
kyis khas longs shig gsungs pa las/ lha mo 'od zer can na re/ bdag gis dkon mchog gi pho brang gi sgo srung bgyi'o zhes zer ro/ dpal mgon byams pa na re/ bdag gis rten gyi
dkon gnyer bgyi'o zhes gsungs so/ gtsang ris kyi dpal mgon bdun cu rtsa lnga na re/ bdag cag gis chos skyong zhing srung ma bgyi'o zer/ dpal ldan mgon po legs ldan nag
po na re/ bdag gis gtsug lag khang thams cad skyong ngo / dkyil 'khor gyi srung ma/ dug gsum gyi sman pa/ rig 'dzin gyi srog shing / rnal 'byor gyi dgra lha/ bdud 'dul gyi
dbang phyug bgyi'o zer/ dpal ldan lha mo nag mo ri ma ti na re/ bdag gis dam tshig gis rjes gcod/ bstan pa'i srung ma bgyi'o zer/ zhes khas blangs so/ /sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa srung ba ni mi dang mi ma yin pa gnyis ka la bka' bsgos te mi la 'phags pa dang skye ngo gnyis su phye/ 'phags pa la dge 'dun sde gnyis/ nyan thos kyi nang nas 'od
srungs chen po la bstan pa gnyer gtad/ kun dga' bo la thos pa'i mdzod du byin gyis brlabs te gtad/ nyan thos chen po gnas brtan bcu drug la tshe lo bdun brgya na/ yul
shi bi'i grong du/ rgyal po rig pa'i mchod gnas dge ba'i bshes gnyen zhes bya ba yon tan du ma ldan pa sku 'da' ba na/ sangs rgyas kyi dam cos yun ji srid du gnas par 'gyur
zhes dris pas/ dogs par ma byed cig sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'da' ba'i dus su/ khyad par can gnas brtan bcu drug gi lag tu dam pa'i chos
gtad do/ /de yang gnas brtan dang po bha ra dhwwa dza bsod snyoms len ni dgra bcom pa stong dang lhan cig tu nub kyi ba glang spyod na gnas so/ /de bzhin du gnas brtan gser
be'u dgra bcom pa stong dang lhan gcig tu kha che'i yul na gnas so/ /gnas brtan bha ra dhwa dza dgra bcom pa stong dang bcas shar gyi lus 'phags gling na gnas so/ /gnas
brtan mi phyed pa dgra bcom pa bdun stong dang bcas 'dzam bu'i gling gi ri gangs can la gnas so/ /gnas brtan

shing shun can dpal ldan bha ku la dgra bcom pa drug stong da bcas byang gi sgra mi snyan na gnas so/ /gnas brtan bzang po chen po ni dgra bcom pa dgu stong dang bcas zangs
gling na gnas so/ /gnas brtan nag po rdo rje ni dgra bcom pa stong dang bcas sing ga la'i gling na gnas so/ /gnas brtan bad sa'i bu gling bzang po dgra bcom pa khri gcig
stong dang bcas chu bo ya mu na'i gling na gnas so/ /gnas brtan ba glang skyong btsun pa nags na gnas dgra bcom pa brgyad stong dang bcas ri spod kyi ngad ldan lo mi kun
ri la gnas so/ /gnas brtan lam pa dgra bcom pa khri gsum stong dang bcas sum cu rtsa gsum lha'i gnas na gnas so/ /gnas brtan sgra gcan 'dzin dgra bcom pa stong dang bcas
pri yang ku'i gling na gnas so/ /gnas brtan sdom brtson klu'i sde dgra bcom pa khri nyis stong dang bcas ri bo ngos yangs la gnas so/ /gnas brtan yan lag 'byung zur gyis
shes dgra bcom pa lnga brgya dang / sum khri dang / ri bo ti se'i gangs la gnas so/ /gnas brtan drang srong shel nags gnas dge slong ma pham lapa dgra bcom pa khri bzhi
stong dang bcas lus 'apags ri la gnas so/ /gnas brtan 'phags pa lam phran dgra bcom pa khri lnga stong dang bcas bya rgod phung po'i ri la gnas so/ /gnas brtan gtsug gi lam
pa sbed byed dgra bcom pa stong phrag drug cu dang bcas ri rgyal bhi hu la zhes te ri gnya' sing 'dzin la gnas so/ /gnas brtan chen po bcu drug po de dag ni mi shes pa
med/ dad pas bsod snyoms 'bul ba/ bsod nams kyis tshogs gang byed pa'i sbyin gnas/ sbyin pa'i zhing yongs su dag par byed pa/ mtshon gyi bskal pa 'das nas mi rnams de ltar
dge ba bcu spyad pas/ tshe slar yang 'phel te tshe lo brgya pa na/ dgra bcom pa dag 'dzam bu'i gling du byon nas chos ston cing tshe lo drug par gyur gyis bar du bstan
pa gnas te/ tshe lo bdun brgya pa na de dag gis thub pa'i bstan pa ji snyed pa rnams bsdus te rin po che sna lnga'i tshogs kyis mchod pa byas te/ phyag dang skor ba byas
te mya ngan las 'da' 'o/ /mchod rten yang nub nas 'og dbang chen gser gyi sa gzhi la gnas so/ /des thub pa'i bstan pa rdzogs pa'o/ /de'i rjes la rang sangs rgyas bye ba
phrag bdun 'byung ngo / /tshe lo brgyad khri bar gyur pa na byams pa byon te 'khor 'dus pa dang po la nyan thos bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug go/ /'dus pa gnyis pa la/ bye
ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa bzhi'o/ /'dus pa gsum pa la bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa gnyis so/ /de'i dus na sa bon lan gcig btab pa la 'bras bu lan bdun 'byung ba la sogs pa mnga'
thang dang 'byor pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'byung ngo / /zhes bshad do/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni gong du bstan pa skyong bar bskos so/ /skye bo'i nang nas rgyal
po dang / bram ze/ khyim bdag gsum la gtad de/ skye dgu'i nang na mi nor yul gsum la dbang che ba rgyal po yin pas/ des kyang bstan pa'i gnyer gyis shig smra bsam gyi rig
pa la dbang thob pa bram ze yin pas des kyang bstan pa'i gnyer gyis shig rdzas dang nor longs spyod la dbang ba khyim bdag gi rigs shing sa la chen po lta bu yin pas des
kyang bsod nams gsog cing bstan pa'i zhabs tog gyis shig gsungs so/ /gzhan mi ma yin par rang rang gis khas

blangs pa dam du bcas pa rnams kyi nang nas/ gtso bo lngas khas blangs so/ /dge slong rab tu byung ba rnams kyi gter lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis gyis shig ces gtad do/ /rgyal
po chain po bzhis phyogs skyong ba bcu la las bcol/ phyogs skyong bcus bar snang la spyod pa'i lha klu dri za rnams la bskos te gtad do/ /des sa 'og sa steng gi lha
klu rnams la bcol te gtad do/ /de dag ni nyan thos dang skye bo rnams kyis mthong ba yin no/ /'bras bu byang chub sems dpa' rigs ldan rnams dang / rdo rje theg pa'i rig
pa 'dzin pa la gnas pa'i skal ldan rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis nang gi dam can rnams la bka' bsgos te/ dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma/ ma mo dang / mkha' 'gro/ shugs 'gro/ dbang
mo dang / gying dang / pho nya dang / srin mo dang / srin po dang / 'bar ma dang / sa bdag mo dang / lang ka dang / bstan ma dang / skyong ma dang / g.ya' ma dang / ga'
ri dang / gangs ri mo nyi shu rtsa gcig dge bsnyen nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / phug bdag dang / se mo la sogs pa/ gzhan yang phyi thun mong pa sde brgyad yan chad la bskos te
bka' bsgos/ bstan pa srung bar gnyer gtad do/ dpang por gsang ba'i bdag po dpal phyag na rdo rje bzhag ste/ srung ma rnams kyi lag tu rdo rje byin/ brten gtor dang / gtsang
gtor dang / 'byung gtor ster bar khas blangs/ bka' bsgos te/ de thams cad dam tshig las mi 'da' bar mdzad nas bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' bsgo'o/ /bskal bzang po'i sangs
rgyas stong po'i bstan pa thams cad gsang ba'i bdag po dpal phyag na rdo rjes srung bar gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo las bshad pas/ srung ma rnams kyi gtso bo ni
mthu stobs kyi bdag po dpal phyag na rdo rje 'chang ba yin no/ /sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i bya ba gsum kas byed pa ni/ 'khor rnam bzhi yin la/ de'i nang nas kyang dge slong
gi dge 'dun 'dul khrims rnam par dag pa srung ba rnams yin/ 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud las/ sangs rgyas bstan pa rin chen sgron/ /'bar ba'i snod ni dka' thub can/ /ngur smrig
'dzin pa shAkya'i sras/ /dge slong rnams ni yin phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs pa las/ sangs rgyas kyi gdung 'tshob par 'dzin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams yin te/ lhag pa'i
bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i thugs kyis bdag pas gzhan gces par 'dzin pa'i gang zag khyad par can rnams yin la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa gnas pa'i yul ni/ 'di dag na yod
par bshad de/ 'dzam bu gling gi yul rgya gar dang / sing ga la dang / sa la dang / li'i yul dang / bru zha'i yul dang / gru gu dang / bod yul kha ba can dang / 'jang yul
dang / mi nyag dang / yu gur dang / ka mi log dang / gser zhes pa'i yul dang / grong khyer spre'i gnas dang / byang phyogs shamabha la'i yul dang / gling phran rnams las/
gser gling dang / za ba'i gling dang / kam ma tshe'i gling / ma la ya'i gling dang / zangs gling dang / sing ga la'i gling rnams la bstan pa yod do/ /ka ba le'i gling na
yang bstan pa yod do/ /gzhan yang dpal dus 'khor lo dang / bka' rdzogs pa chen po nas gling gsum dang / gling phran brgyad dang / lha dang klu'i gnas na yang bstan pa yod
par gsungs so/ /lung gi chos rnams 'chad nyan bris klog gis bar la byang chub phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun

gyi sgo nas lam bskyed rdzogs gnyis la dbang ba sgrub pa byed pa rnams kyis bstan pa 'dzin yin te/ dam chos mngon pa mdzod las/ ston pa'i dam chos rnam gnyis te/ /lung dang
rtogs pa'i bdag nyid do/ /de 'dzin byed dang smra byed pa/ /sgrub par byed pa kho na yin/ /zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /dus ring zhig nas kha ba can gyi sems can rnams chos
kyis 'dul ba la dus ji tsam zhig na/ sangs rgyas kyi nyan thos rnams ni/ phung po lhag med du sangs rgyas/ sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni zhing khams gzhan
du 'gro don la gshegs/ de'i phyi de'i dbyar a su ra'i brag phug tu dgra bcom pa lnga brgyas sde snod gsum du bsdus nas/ de rnams shog dkar la brjed tho yi ge ris su bkod
nas bstan pa'i bdag po ni dge slong gi dge 'dun no/ /de mi nub pa'i rgyal mtshan lo lnga lhag tsam na/ a su ra'i brag phug tu dgra bcom pa lnga brgya tsam 'tshogs nas/
bka' 'khor lo dang po dgongs pa 'grel pa byed brag tu bshad pa bam po sum brgya pa brtsams so/ /bstan chos la de snga ba yin no/ /de nas sangs rgyas sku mya ngan las 'das
nas lo bzhi brgya na/ slob dpon klu sgrub byon nas/ bka' 'khor lo bar pa'i 'grel pa/ dbu ma rtsa ba shes rab la sogs pa rig pa'i tshogs drug brtsams pa lags so/ /de nas
lo dgu brgya na/ slob dpon thogs med sku mched byon nas bka' 'khor lo mtha' ma'i dgongs pa 'grel pa nges pa'i don ltar bkral lo/ /gzhan yang mkhyen pas bstan pa rgyas par
mdzad pa ni/ klu sgrub yab sras/ thogs med sku mched/ phyogs glang chos grags te/ 'dzam bu gling gi rgyan drug dang / mchog brgyad du gnyis su grags pa'i gang zag mkhas
pa rnams yin no/ /dbang phyug gis bstan pa srung zhing rgyas pa ni/ chos rgyal mya ngan med pa la sogs pa chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' rnams so/ /nus mthus bstan pa srung
zhing rgyas pa ni/ rnam la 'byor gyi dbang phyug 'bir ba pa'am/ rgyal sras pad ma 'byung gnas la sogs pa grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor chen po grub chen brgyad cu rtsa
lnga la sogs pa yin no/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' mdo rgyud dri ma med pa'i po ti glegs bam rnams ji ltar rgyas shing / gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud
sde chen po rnams rig pa 'dzin pa mi dang mi ma yin pa rnam pa gnyis la ji ltar brgyud pa'i tshul ni/ dpal rdo rje gdan gyi shar lho'i mtshams na/ ri ma la ya zhes bya
ba gsang ba'i bdag po dpal phyag rdor gyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i sa/ chos 'dzin rigs kyi grub gnas/ rdo rje thabs kyi lta ba'i yul du gyur pa drag shul gnam lcags 'bar ba
yod pa'i rtse la/ sdong po dang / yal ga dang lo 'dab rgyas pa/ me tog dang 'bras bu smin pa/ ri dwags kyi rgyal po seng ge 'dug pa'i gnas su gyur pa/ 'dabs na gcan gzan
dpa' brtul stag gi gnas yod pa/ ngos la brag dkar seng gi 'gyings pa 'dra ba yod pa/ de'i shar ngos la a su ra'i brag phug ces bya ba rang byung gi sgo zla gam la/ ngo mtshar
gyi ri mo ya mtshan can yod pa/ phug tu rin po che zur brgyad ma la/ nyi zla'i gzugs brnyan rang snang ba/ yang thog rim pa gsum dang ldan pa/ rtse la bya ka lan dha
ka gnyis med gcig tu smra ba'i tshang yod pa/ ri dwags mdzes pa mang po sna tshogs rgyu ba/ ljon shing gar

byed pa 'dra ba dang / me tog sna tshogs dgod pa lta bu yod pa/ 'bab chu snyan pa'i sgra 'byin pa/ bsil ngad 'jam gyi phyogs na nas ser bu g.yo ba/ bung ba rgyang ring glu
len pa/ nyin mo skye bo'i rgyung 'grul gyis dben pa/ mtshan mo mi ma yin pa'i bar gcod med pa/ mi rgod kyi 'tshe ba med pa/ rgyal blon gdug pas tsor bar ma gyur pa/ skal
ba dang ldan pa ma yin pa ma dag pa'i skye bos bgrod par mi nus pa'i gnas/ bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyi thugs rjes bskul nas/ gsang ba'i bdag po rdo rje 'chang nyid/ ri ma
la yar mngon sum du byon te/ 'khor dam pa'i rigs can lnga la rdo rje theg pa gsungs so/ /lha'i rig 'dzin grags ldan mchog skyong / klu rgyal 'jog po/ gnod sbyin skar mda'
gdong / srin pa blo gros thabs ldan/ mi las skal ldan li tsa byi dri ma med par grags pa la sogs mi dang mi ma yin pa gdul bya snod ldan sha stag la gsang ba sngags kyi
rgyud sde rnams bstan to/ /de'i rjes la srin po blo gros thabs ldan gyis rgyud sde rnams bsdus shing yi ger bkod pa'i byin rlabs mi yul du snang bar mdzad pa ni/ dpal 'khor
lo sdom pa'i rgyud phyi ma las/ /nga ni 'di nas mi snang nas/ /lo ni brgya dang nyi shu na/ /bstan pa'i snying po dam pa zhig /lha nas gsum du grags pa de/ /'dzam gling
shar lho phyogs mtshams kyi/ /dpal zhes bya ba'i ri bo la/ /lag na rdo rjes snang ba byed/ /mi las bskal ldan dam pa rnams/ /byang chub mchog tu grub gyur pas/ /de la
rtag tu gus par gyis/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / mdo sde gdams ngag 'bog pa'i rgyal po las/ rgyu la mos pa rgyu'i chos kyi/ /'khor lo rab tu bskor byas nas/ /rdo rje theg pa'i
nye lam zhig /phyi tshe zhig na 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pas/ de'i don gyis byin gyis brlabs nas gnas lugs sems/ rig 'dzin rig pa nas gang zag snyan nas snyan khung
du brgyud pa ni/ phyag na rdo rjes rig pa 'dzin pa rnams la gsungs shing / rdo rje gsang sngags kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i byin brlabs kyis/ za hor gyi yul pra dha mu nya
zhes bya bar sku 'khrungs pa/ rgyal po dza zhes bya ba sangs rgyas dang byang chub/ chos dang dge 'dun la mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa de/ ma ga dha na bzhugs pa'i dus su/
'khor rnams la ngas bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa rnams rgyas par byed palas/ khyed kun gyis tshol cig ces bka' bstsal pas/ 'bangs rnams kyis rgyal po la zhus shing gsol
ba/ rgyal po nyid rang yang rgyal po chen po dharma a sho ka bzhin du byang chub kyi shing drung du mchod pa phul la gsol ba thob ces zhus pas/ de ltar byas pas lha rnams
kyis lung bstan te/ a su ra'i brag phug tu song zhig ces nam mkha' las sgra byung ste/ der rgyal po dzas byon te bzhugs pa'i dus su/ mnal lam du mtshan ltas bdun shar
te/ rmi lam ni srol la bag chags kyi rmi lam/ nam gung la bdud kyis bstan pa'i rmi lam/ tho rengs lha yis bstan pa'i rmi lam dang gsum yin pa la/ rgyal po da la tho rengs
kyi dus su/ dang po la ni ri'i rtse mo ru phyag na rdo rje byon te sku las 'od zer 'phros te/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad bsregs te mi snang ngo / /gsung rnga bo che 'brug
stong ldir ba'i sgras sgra skad gzhan thams cad mi grags palar zil gyis gnon/ thugs ka nas rdo rje 'od 'bar

ba zhig byung nas/ rgyal po dza yi spyi bor thim/ nyi zla 'od 'bar ba zhig byung nas zhabs mthil du thim nas snang srid thams cad lto ru 'phyo ba zhig rmis so/ /gnyis pa la
ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dam pa'i chos kyi bka' bgro ba mdzad cing nyi zla'i steng du seng ge la bzhon nas gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong zhig bskor zhing srid pa gsum
gyi ka lo gyen la bsgyur ba zhig rmis so/ /gsum pa la ni nam mkha' la sprin gser gyi mdog can ni 'thibs/ cho 'phrul gyi 'brug sgra gdangs snyan la go zhing tshems pa ni
grags/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi na bun ni 'thibs/ baiDUrya sngon po'i 'od ni sa la byung bas snang srid gsal/ glog ni 'khyug rin po che sna tshogs kyi char dragha po ni
babs pa rmis so/ /bzhi pa la ni 'jig rten pa'i snang ba thabs cad ni 'gyur/ rin po che 'bar ba'i 'od ni shar bas snang srid kyi mun pa thams cad sel/ bdud rtsi sman gyi
chu rgyun gyis skye 'gro thams cad kyi nad ma lus par bsal te/ 'gro ba thams cad rdo rje rnal 'byor chen po'i sgra di ri ri sgrog pa zhig rmis so/ /lnga pa la ni sprin gyi
gseb nas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor las/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od zer shar ba de'i dkyil na rin po che smug po'i dpal be'u me 'od dang bcas pa phyi nang thams cad gsal ba'i
nang na/ rin po che gser gyi glegs bam la baiDUrya zhun mas nan du bris pa skar mda' thang la lhung ba ltar rgyal po dza'i khang steng du ggas bam po ti'i char babs pa
zhig rmis so/ /drug pa la ni yangaglegs bam mang po de rnams la byang chub sems dpal dang / rig pa 'dzin pa dang / lha mi mang pos glegs bam de dag gi yon tan brjod cing
bsngags pa brjod do/ /la la ni chos 'don/ la la ni klog la la ni shod/ la la ni sems/ la la ni sgom/ phyag dang skor ba byed cing / mchod pa byed pa yang rmis so/ /bdun
pa la ni nam mkha'i sprin gyi gseb nas sgra byung ste/ las dang skal bar rab ldan zhing / /rgyal bas 'byung bar lung bstan pa'i/ /dpal 'byor ldan pa'i sngon bsags can/ /bsod
nams chen po'i gra ma khyed/ /dbang pos ji ltar bstan pa bzhin/ /da lta dus 'dir mngon shar gyis/ /'khor ba'i gcong nad sbyang ba'i phyir/ /nga yi cho 'phrul byin rlabs
kyis/ /bstan pa'i snying po dam pa zhig /skal ldan khyed la bstan par bya'o/ /zhes pa la sogs pa lung bstan pa rmis so/ /de nas mnal yang sad/ gung yang langs nas 'dug
pa la/ shin tu thugs spro zhing nyams kyang shin tu dga' dgyes pa dang spro ba'i bsam pas bzhengs so/ /na bza' gsol/ ske rag bcings nas phyogs bzhir gus pas phyag 'tshal
te/ ltas 'di dang sbyar na don chen po zhig 'grub nges pas/ dus phyi ma min par tshe 'di nyid la thob par shog cig ces gsungs nas 'bangs 'khor phyi nang thams cad bsags
nas nga'i mtshan ma 'di dang sbyar na don bzang po 'grub nges par 'dug pas/ ri 'di'i rtse mor 'deng gsungs te/ rgyal blon 'khor dang bcas pa rnams kyis khrus byas/ gos gtsang
ma gon/ rgyan mdzes pa rnams btags/ zas ngan pal spangs nas rje 'bangs rnams ri bo'i rtse mor byon pa dang / rgyu rin po che las grub pa'i gsang ba'i bdag po rdo rje
'chang sku khru gang pa 'od dang bcas pa zhig rnyed nas rab tu dgyes te/ thams cad kyis kyang phyag 'tshal/

mchod pa phul/ skor ba byas nas/ tshe rabs sngon nas bsgrubs pa'i lha/ /las 'phros 'brel ba'i yi dam khyed/ /bskal pa brgyar yang mi spong ngo / /e ma ho ngo mtshar mchog gi
sku/ /'dren pa mchog 'di bdag gi dpal/ /mos pa'i lhag pa'i lha ru 'din/ /zhes yi dam gyi lhar dam du bcas nas ri 'di sgrub pa'i gnas yin pas brag phug tu spyan drangs nas/
dgung bdun dang zla ba drug tu gsol ba btab pas/ rmi lam du byung ba'i glegs bam rnams phyag tu byung ngo / /las dang thugs rje'i 'brel ba yi po ti glegs bam rnams la
rab tu dgyes pala'i tshul gyis bltas pas yi ge 'bru gcig kyang ma shes te/ e ma sngar gyi tshul rtags dang sbyar na glegs bam 'di rnams la don chen po zhig yod par nges
te/ bdag gis klog ma shes pa cis lan snyam ste/ spyan chab phyungs nas snod dang skal bar ldan pa shes rab can su yod byas te/ phyogs kun tu dris shing btsal bas/ rgyal po
rang gi yab kyi slob ma za hor gyi rgyal po u pa ra dza bya ba rig pa'i gnas thams cad la mkhas pa dang / de bshes gnyen che'o zhes gsan pas/ lo rgyus rnams zhib tu smos
nas spyan drangs pas/ rgyal rigs gdug pa che bas ma shes na mi rung snyam nas ma byon te/ lan du bdag gi 'dir glang po che la gdan drongs la skyol cig brtag par bgyi'o
zhes gsungs nas/ pho nya bas de ltar bzlas pas/ bskyal te u pa ra dzas gzigs pas tshig 'bru gcig kyang brda ma 'jal nas 'di bdag gi spyod yul du ma gyur gyis/ rgyal po nyid
kyi thugs kyi dgongs pas dpag par zhu zhes springs nas slar yang bskyal lo/ /de nas mkhyen pa su che dris pas/ lho phyogs dpal gyi ri phug na yab ku ku'i rgyal po/ yum
skyes skra'i la ba can gyi sras dge slong ku ku ra dza zhes bya ba tshe lo stong thub pa/ sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen mang gi sprul pa/ rig
pa'i gnas lnga thams cad mkhyen pa de/ bshes gnyen che'o zhes gsan nas/ de nas spyan dras nas des gzigs nas brtags pas/ rdo rje sems dpa' zhal mthong gi le'ur shes nas/
rdo rje sems dpa' sgrub par rtogs te/ gsol ba btab pas zhal mthong nas/ rigs kyi bu dngos grub ci 'dod gsungs pas/ gnas skabs su po ti dang glegs bam 'di rnams shes pa
dang / mthar thug tu sems can thams cad sangs rgyas thob par 'tshal lo zhes gsol bas/ rigs kyi bu rang gi phung po khams dang skye mched sbyong dang gsang ba'i bdag pos lung
ston par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas dga' ba dang spro ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa skyes te/ sems rtse gcig tu bsgrubs pas/ sa yang cher g.yos
te/ de nas rdo rje 'chang mngon sum du byon nas zhal mthong ba de nyid kyi tshe/ phyag na rdo rjes brtul zhugs mdzad de rdo rje nam mkha' la bsor zhing gdul bya'i snod kyi
sgrib pa spyangs nas/ mdun gyi nam mkha' la sprul pa'i sku'i dkyil 'khor sasnang bar mdzad nas/ ku ku ra dza dang / rgyal po dza dang bcas pa la dbang bskur nas/ rjes
su gnang ba byin pas rgyud sade kun mkhyen par gyur to/ /dge slong ku ku ra dzas rgyud sde chen po bzhi dang / drug dang / bco brgyad du phye nas rgyal po dza la bshad do/
/des tshom bu 'bum dang bcas te tshogs bsgrubs pas dngos grub rnam gnyis brnyes nas/ i?dra na bo dhi la sogs

pa smin par byas te tshom bu brgya dang bcas te tshogs bsgrubs pas/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i sa thob nas/ gdul bya skal ldan rnams smin par mdzad do/ /de nas blo ldan rgyal po dza
yis 'gro ba sems can skal pa dang ldan kun/ yang dag pa'i lam zab rdo rje theg pa la 'god pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi bka' mdo rgyud rab 'byams dri ma med pa rnams gsung
gi rten du po ti glegs bam rnams dkar shog la bris nas/ rgyas par mdzad do/ /lo rgyus de'i don ni 'di yin te/ thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo nyi shu rtsa brgyad na/ ma
la ya'i ri bo la/ gsang ba'i bdag po mngon par gshegs nas/ lha klu gnod sbyin srin po dang / /mi las skal ldan 'dus pa la/ /dbang pos ji ltar lung bstan dus/ /rgyal po rig
can ltas shar pa/ /'brel bas snang la mngon brtags pas/ /thugs kyi sgrub pa mngon rtogs te/ /de nyid sgo nas de nyid 'grub/ /bstan pa'i dngos grub de nas thob/ /don dam
bcud kyis de nas rgyas/ /'dod pa'i bsam pa de ru 'grub/ /smon pa'i lha dang de ru mjal/ /de nas rdo rje gdan steng gi/ /'dzam gling shar gyi phyogs mtshams su/ /pho brang
dam pa rin chen nang / /bkra shis dam pa'i khang bu ru/ /ku ku ra dza i?dra bo dhi dang / /sing ha u pa ra dza dang / /sras mo go ma sa la sogs/ /sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i
dbang thob nas/ /tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor dngos grub ste/ /rdo rje 'chang bar sngon du gshegs/ /de nas re zhig na rgyal po dza ma ga dha na bzhugs pa'i dus su yab mes kyi yi
ge rnams gzigs pas/ mes dhar ma a sho kas sangs rgyas kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs par zhal gyis bzhes pa la/ mchod rten bye ba bzhengs pa grub ste/ gsung gi rten
ma grub pas/ de'i phyag rjes ngas gsob pa/ zhes gsungs pas 'bangs rnams kyi rharma a sho kas zhal gyis ci bzhes zhus pas de ngas bshad kyis khyed rnams nyon cig gsungs
nas/ sngon skye ba snga ma la mnyan yod du byis par gyur pa na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo gnyis rgyal po'i khab tu bsod snyoms la gshegs
pa'i tshe de na tshong pa'i rigs tha ga pa ma mad gnyis yod pa'i bus/ bye ma la 'bras kyi bang ba'i tshul du byas te rtse ba la/ sangs rgyas byon pa la byis pa rnams
dad nas/ bye ma khyor gang phul ba dang / gzugs kyis ma slebs te/ grogs gnyis sgur ba'i steng du 'dzegs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi lhung bzed smad pa la yar gtor bas/ bye ma
lhung bzed du song ba de ma yis mthong nas/ ma na re bu la/ 'phags 'di lta bu byon pa la/ kha zas kyi bsnyen bkur mi byed par rdul 'thor ba zer nas bu la thal lcag brgyab
pas/ de la bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' bstsal pa/ khyed kyi bus nga la dad gus kyis bye 'bras phul bas/ bye ma phul ba'i grangs dang mnyam pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gdung
bzhengs pa'i las bsags te/ de'i 'bras bu ni/ ma 'ongs pa na 'dzam bu'i gling la dbang ba'i rgyal por skyes nas/ byis pa rtse rogs gnyis kyang bcom ldan 'das la dad pas
gnod sbyin gnyis su gyur nas/ rgyal po de yi 'phong grogs byas nas shing rta bsgrubs nas nub gcig la mchod rten bye ba brtsigs te/ bka' bsdu ba'i bdag rkyen yang byed la/
bla mchod dgra bcom pa gnas brtan grags pas gtso byas pa dgra bcom pa lnga brgya 'degs/ sku gdung bye ba bzhengs

par 'gyur ro/ /gsungs nas lung bstan gnang ngo / /der bram ze mo de dga' nas bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba/ bye ma de la grangs su bdog bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ bye
ma'i grangs bye ba yod do/ kun dga' bo khyod bye ma 'di chos gos kyi grar thums la byis pa bsod nams 'phel ba'i phyir gtsang khang la khyod kyis zhal ba gyis shig ces bka'
bstsal te de'i shul na nA len dra na mchod rten 'dom bzhi tsam pa zhig la bcom ldan 'das kyi sku bzhugs pa gcig yod do/ /phyis sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas lo brgya
drug cu na grong khyer shing thags can ma/ rgyal po shing rta bcu pa zhugs pa'i tshe/ ma ga dha na rigs 'breg mkhan bza' tsho gnyis kyis tshong pa mang po'i phyir phyin
pas lam du khyo sbrul gyis bsad pa'i pas bud med cig deshing thags can gyi rdzing na 'dug pa na rgyal po skyed chos tshal du gshegs pas gzigs nas bud med de la khyed kyis
'breg pa'i bya ba shes na/ nga'i sen mo bregasashig gsungs nas bu mo des phyag sen bregs pas/ shin tu bregs pa mkhas pas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed kyis nga'i sen mo 'breg
mkhan gyis shig khyed kyi 'tsho ba ngas sbyor ro zhes pa dang / bu mo de shin tu mdzes pas dus phyis rgyal po'i btsun mo phyi mtshams mar gyur pas/ 'bangs kun na re/
rgyal po'i rigs khyod kyis bslad zer nas 'tshe bar byed pas/ bu mo de shin tu yid mi bde zhing mya ngan che bas/ de nas re zhig na/ bu mo de la yul dbus su grong khyer me
tog rgyas par rgyal bu zhig btsas pas/ 'khor 'bangs kun na re/ da ni rgyal sras yod pas btsun mo yin zer zhing kun byams par gyur/ bu mo yi sems ma bde ba zhi bas/ bu rgyal
bu de'i mtshan yang mya ngan med ces bya'o/ /de nas re zhig na yab rgyal po la 'chi ltas byung nas rgyal po de la sras bram ze mtshan mkhan la mtshan ston la/ rtsis gyis
shig ces bka' bsgo byas so/ /der rgyal bu che shos kun bram ze'i drung du song ngo / /bu mo'i bsam pa la/ nga'i bu rgyal bu 'di yis nam kyang yang ni/ rgyal srid mi thob
snyam nas/ 'breg mkhan ma'i bu bram ze'i gam du ma phyin pa dang / glang rdzis glang btul bas glang po che bzang shos 'dug nas/ mya ngan med khyed kyis thob zer/ blon
po che ba zhig na re/ bram zes mtshan ma shes/ rgyal srid sus thob nges pa med kyis/ mya ngan med la khyed rang yang song dang zer ba dang / der rgyal bu chu ba 'breg mkhan
ma'i bu mya ngan med kyis kyang phyin pa dang / bram zes mtshan bltas pas bu chung ba mya ngan med kyis rgyal srid 'dzin par shes nas ni/ der bram zes smras na/ rgyal
bu che ba rnams kyis de nyid du phrag dog byed du 'ong bar 'dug nas rgyal bu chung ba gsod par 'dug pas/ bram zes khyed rgyal sras rnams stan ches bzang bar 'dug pa/ zas
gos ches bzang ba gcig gis rgyal sa 'dzin no/ /zhes smras so/ /lung bstan pa der rgyal bu che ba rnams na re/ stan bzang po la 'dug pa/ zas gos kyi mchog ni nga'i 'di yin
zhes zer te song ngo / /bu chung bas ni 'bras chan zos/ ras rnying pa gon/ sa gzhi la bsdad do/ /der blon po gcig gis lkog tu dris pas/ bram ze na re/ stan mchog ni sa
gzhi/ gos mchog ni ras gos/ zas mchog ni 'bras chan no/ /zhes zer nas/ 'breg ma'i bu la lung bstan par rig go/

/de nas dus ring zhig na/ nub phyogs rnga sgra can gyi rgyal pos/ shing thags can gyi rgyal po la dmag 'dren du btang ba la/ dus btab nas rgyal bu mya ngan med de'i dmag dpon
du bskos te btang bas/ nub phyogs rnga sgra can gyi dmag thams cad bsad/ de'i rgyal srid phrogs/ rgyal khams thob nas yab la skyes dang stangs mang po phul nas bca' mang
po bskur nas btang bas/ phu bo rnams na re/ rgyal khams de shin tu bzang bas/ nged 'dod do zer nas khong phu bo rnams kyis khyer ro/ /mya ngan med yab rgyal po'i drung
