khrims kyis chad pa bcad la 'dul dgos pas/ de la yang dbang che dgos pas zhes yab yum la zhus pas/ thugs dgyes nas bod 'bangs thams cad bsdus nas/ rin po che'i khri la rgyal
bu bzhugs su gsol te/ yab kyis rgyal srid gtad nas/ rgyal khams thams cad kyi rjer mnga' gsol snyams nas/ dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la rgyal sar bton pas/ srod la byang chub
sems dpa' 'jam dpal byon nas/ khri'i g.yas nas rin po che'i prog zhu cod pan gyi thod rnams bskon/ g.yon nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ rin po che'i bum pas
khrus chab gsol/ a mi de ba'i phyag mnya?dzu dzi ka lta bur brkyangs nas/ rgyal bu'i dbu la reg pas/ rgyal po'i sku las 'od zer 'phros te/ 'od re re'i sna la rta'i rgyal
po bha la hwa rgyal bu'i chibs pa lags te/ de las 'od zer brjod du med par 'phros pas/ 'od re re'i sna la zhing khams re re chags/ zhing khams re re na bcom ldan 'das
rnam par snang mdzad gangs chen mtsho re re sprul/ de rnams kyi thugs ka nas 'od zer brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par 'phros/ 'od re re'i sna la zhing khams re re
chags/ zhing khams re re na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od kyi rgyal po re re sprul/ de dag gi thugs ka nas 'od zer brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'phros te/
'od re re'i sna la 'jig rten gyi khams re re chags/ 'jig rten gyi khams re re na bcom ldan 'das rgyal ba shAkya thub pa re re sprul/ de dag re re'i sku las 'od zer brjod
du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'phros pas/ 'od zer phyogs bcu'i nam mkha'i mtha' khyab par 'phros/ nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i sems can re re'i mdun na byang chub
sems dpa' phyag stong spyan stong re re sprul nas/ sems can gyi don byed do/ /sems can de dag gi snang ba ma dag pas bdag mthong bar ma gyur to/ /de rnams ni de bzhin
gshegs pa la bka' drin che bas te/ tshul de lta bu'i rgyud ris ni khra 'brug gi rgyal bu'i khang bu de nyid na gser gyis bris nas yod do/ /de nas snga phan yab rgyal po rngon
la dgyes pas/ byang gangs la rong la pho brang bcas te/ rngon gyi bya ra byed pa nas/ nang zhig thang mtha' zhig na/ na gu sran ma tsam gcig byung bas gzigs/ nangs ma
gnyis pa la bya rog tsam/ gsum pa dang bzhi pa la g.yag tsam/ nub lnga pa la bi'u gcig skyes nas/ de la khyi dang skye 'brel gyin ma bsad do/ /de cher skyes nas 'brong
na le bong zan du gyur nas/ rta dang / mi dang / khyi dang gang mdun du byung ba thams cad bsad pas/ phung g.yag thal kha ru rings su grags pa de 'dul ba la rta cang shes
dgos pas/ kong po'i yul bre sna nas/ rta bya ma zhur ru/ dmu te long bas rnyed do/ /de yang 'bras ljang phor

chus sos te/ byang gangs la rong du byon te/ rta zhon nas g.yag ded nas/ dgong mo mtsho khug gcig tu tshuud pas/ rta ka 'then pa'i drung du 'brong shor ba/ khyung po spu thang
gzung rtse langs nas/ rta ka la 'jus te rdza rar khrid nas/ rgyal po la rgod sha grangs drangs so/ /de la khyed kyis phung g.yag 'dul rogs gyis gsungs pas/ ngos kyi grogs
po 'bod zer nas song ste/ dmu dpung rgyang ring po bya ba'i mi gzugs chen po zhig khrid byung ngo / /de la phung g.yag 'dul nus sam dris pas rngo thogs lags zer nas/
rdo bsdus nas khyer song bas/ phung g.yag kham pa'i rwa ya gcig la phog nas rwa bog pa chu la bcug pas chu khol/ rwa ya gcig spang la gnyegs bsnyegs pas spang tshigs nas
dud pa 'thul du byung / rdo des g.yag bsad do/ /rwa la rwa mkhar byas so/ /'phan ri la g.yag thod mkhar bya ba yod do/ /sha sga la btags pas sha lhung nas/ sga la sha thag
btags te/ sha sgye'ur bcug dmu dpung rgyang ring po la rta 'gros su btang na ji tsam rtol dris pas zla ba phyed na rtol lo zer/ 'dur du btang na dris pas/ zhag bdun na
rtol zer/ rta bang du btang na dgong mo rtol zer/ kho'i thu ba snga log phyi log byas nas gam gam 'gro ba rta'i bang dang mnyam mo/ /de nas rgyal po chen po/ gangs pha gi'i
rtsa ba nas pho brang gzigs kyis/ der bzhud cig zer nas/ dmu dpung rgyang ring po phyir byang du log go/ /gangs kyi rtsar rta tshigs bub byung bas/ rta mgo la lcag rgyab
pas rta 'tsher zhing / lcags thag lcags phur la gtod pas ma thub par rta shi'o/ /rgyal pos rta'i mya ngan byas te/ mtsho 'gram du sha gsol bas/ sha sa la lhung ba zhal
du gsol bas shin tu tshwa bro bar byung nas lan tshwa de nas rnyed do/ /mtsho de rgyal po'i bla mtsho bya bar grags so/ /de nas rgyal pos sha ka gsol bas zhal shin tu skyems
te chu grang mo gsol bas bsnyungs te grongs so/ /bang so 'gu ri sog por mkhar brtsigs so/ /skye bo rnams la yang dga' ston chen po yang byas so/ / de nas rgyal bu de
shin tu sku dbang che bas mtha'i rgyal po thams cad kyis bca' dang / skyes lo dam gyis thang gi tshul du yong bas zhu ba yi 'phrin yig klog pa na/ bod kyi rgyal po la kha
'phrin las yi ge med de/ 'o cag bod la yang yi ge dgos par snang / bka' lung gsal nas der blon bcu drug rgya gar du yi ge slob tu btang bas thang 'bre gsum la gtugs/ rdugs
la la ni mtha'i la gcan gyis bsad/ la la tshad pas gum/ la la lce bul/ la la shes rab chung nas skad ma lobs te rgyal po'i thugs dgongs ma grub/ de na thon mi bsam bu
zhes pa blo gsal la yid gzhungs pas mi chung sam bho Da la gser phye bre gang byin nas de la 'khor ngo tsha shes shing khrel yod pa bcu drug mi re la rta re/ dre'u re/
gser srang bcu drug gser lings pa srang brgya tham pa bskur/ dpal nA len dra'i gtsug lag khang du brdzangs btang ngo / /tsan dra ba'i slob ma rin chen blo gros/ de yi slob
ma gang pa'i zla ba/ de'i slob ma ma na sam gha/ de'i slob ma paNaTi ta lha rig pa'i seng ge la sgra bslabs/ rgya gar lho phyogs kyi paNaTi ta bram ze li byin dang 'phrad
de yi ge zhus pas/ spyir rgya gar na yi ge'i rigs mi 'dra ba drug cu rtsa bzhi yod/ bsdu na gsum du

'dus te lan dza lha'i yi ge/ na ga ra klu'i yi ge/ bha gru ma mi'i yi ge'o/ dang po dbang phyug chen pas ka tsa ta Ta pa/ kha tsha tha Tha ba kSha sha ha a la sogs pa la gsal
yig bkod do/ /de sgra mkhan gyis 'byung ba lnga bkod de ka kha ga gha nga zhes la sogs pa'i gsal yig sum bu so gnyis la sogs pa'i sde tshan/ bod la sgra med pa/ gha'i
sde tshan yi ge lnga lces mi 'gyur bas bzhag dbyangs yig bcu drug na ro gu gu'i khongs su bsdus te bsgyur ro/ /i gu gur bsgyur/ u zhabs kyur bsgyur/ e 'greng bur/ o na ro/
a rtseg tu bsgyur te/ ka mad sum cu tham par bsdebs/ na ga ra ma dper blangs pas dbu can du byas/ bha gru ma la dpe byas nas dbu med du byas so/ /bod kyi gcig la rgya gar
e ka ces te bod la ma btub nas ca bcug rgya'i lo ka bod kyi 'jig rten ma btab pas ja bcug rgya'i dharma la bod kyi chos bya ba ma btub nas cha bcug rgya'i pri ta la bod
kyi zhu ba bya ba byung bas zha bcug bod kyi yi ge ring po med pas 'a bcug bod la rgya gar la med pa'i yi ge phyed drug yod do/ /rgya skad sor bzhag pa yin no/ /sgra dang
yi ge bsgyur te bris pas lhug pa dang tshigs su bcad pa yin no/ /a glang po che'i sna lta bu/ a shad kyi rnam pa lta bu/ a brgya byin gyi rnam pa lta bu/ a seng ge'i ral
pa lta bu/ a rgyal po gdan la bzhugs pa lta bu/ phral ba dang bri ba dang 'phul yig lnga dang / rten yig dgu la sogs pa yan lag drug gi skor mtshams steng dang / logs
dang 'og tu phyung / shad kyis bcad/ tshig gis smra bar bya'o/ /ka mad sum cu bcos bcos nas byung ngo / /der phyi blon rnams na re/ sam bho Da yis rgya gar gyi yi ge bzhi
bcu rtsa drug la spros pas/ bod yig nyi shu rtsa bzhi las ma rnyed nas smra ba bsdebs su ma 'dod nas skad ma khugs te khong dbu 'thoms te nyal nas 'dug pa mnal du song ba
dang mnal sad pa'i tshe rang gi rtsa na skyes bu rgan po phyag 'khar thogs pa zhig 'dug nas khyod gang nas 'ongs/ gar 'gro/ ci byed pa yin/ rigs gang yin/ nga'i sgo bsdams
pa la gang nas thar zhes smras pas/ rgad po de na re/ chos nyid gshis la gong 'og med/ /yang dag don la bya byed med/ /nam mkha' lam du byas pa la/ /sgo cha bsdams pas
ga la thub/ /zer ro/ /de 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa yin par rig nas yang yang du dris pas rgad po na re/ nga zhang zhung mi yul nas 'ongs/ za hor gyi yul du 'gro
zer/ thag ji tsam yod byas pas ci cha yod zer/ mi snang bar song ngo / /der sam bho Das bsams pas rigs 'a zha yin zer bas 'a rnyed/ zhang zhung nas yongs zer zha rnyed/ za
hor yul du 'gro zer bas za rnyed/ thag ji tsam byas pas ci cha yod zer bas ca dang cha rnyed do/ /rgyags ci yod byas pas ja yod zer bas ja rnyed/ der rgya gar la med pa'i
yi ge drug gis kha bskangs te/ ka mad sum cu tham pa byung ste da gzod bod skad du bsgyur btub nas rgya yig la las bod yig tu bris nas rgya gar skad las/ bod skad bstan
nas sgra bsgyur nas gtan la phab/ bshad nyan dang sgom sgrub kyi srol ni ma thod dod Da 'bri ba dang klog pa'i srol ni ma thod dod de/ mdo sde dkon mchog sprin dang / pad
ma dkar po dang / za ma tog bkod pa dang / rin po che 'phreng ba dang / mdo phran mang bsgyur ro/

/de nas lha chos dang mi chos kyi gdams pa mang bsgyur ro/ /de rnams mchims phu'i phyag mdzod du bzhugs so/ /lo tsA ba la rgyal po'i rtsis dang / bsnyen bkur ni phra men gyi
yi ge chen mo yig mkhan la dar gyi yol ba/ za 'og gi bla re/ gab rtse'i gdan/ spyan ras gzigs tshod dgu/ zang zing gi longs spyod bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang ngo / /dge
ba nyams bag tu spyod du chug mtshan mchod gnas zhes bya bar btags so/ /yi ge'i dpe gcig lha sa'i brag logs la btab pa ni sbal nag nag la rgyangs pa 'dra ba gcig byung ngo
/ /'bri klog dag par bya ba'i phyir du sgra'i bstan bcos dang / dag yig rgyas pa yang mdzad de rgyal po'i phyag tu phul bas mnyes so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba la snga ba de
thon mi sam bho Da yin no//de nas rgyal pos lo bzhi'i bar du yi ge bslabs pas/ blon po 'ga' na re/ rgyal po lo bzhi'i bar du sgo tsam du mi yong bas glen pa gcig 'dug zer
nas/ bod skyid pa blon po'i drin yin zer bas/ rgyal po'i bsam pa la bod kyi blon po glen par byed nas 'di rnams mi thul lo snyam ste/ khyod bod rnams ni rgyal po glen pa
zhig bod bde ba la blon pos bkod pa yin zer/ blon po nga yis bskos sam/ khyod kyis bskos/ ngas pho brang gcig tu 'dug nas 'pho skyas ma byas na/ 'bangs dal zhing skyid pa
yin/ da nga yis khrims bca' yis/ khrims ma byas na/ nyes pa kun gyis byed pas/ nga'i sras dbon blon gyi srid med par 'gro/ nga ni chos kyi rgyal po yin pas/ nga'i bka'
'khor du gtogs pa bod spyi mthun la chos khrims med na/ las mi dge ba bcu spyad pas/ ngan song gsum du song nas sdug bsngal las thar pa med pa'i gnas su skye ba yin/ da nga'i
mnga' ris su gtogs pas 'thab mo byas nas srog bcad nas bsad na stong 'dod do/ /phan tshun ma rku zhig ma byin par blangs na/ bdun 'jal dngos dang brgyad 'dod do/ /'dod
log gzhan gyi chung ma la byi byas na/ smad 'chal 'dod do/ /brdzun du ma smra zhig brdzun smras na/ lha klu gnyan dgu la yang bcol nas bro 'dor du 'jug go bya ba la sogs
pa'i dge ba bcu'i khrims bcas te/ bka' chems kyi yi ge mang po mdzad nas/ snga dro gcig tu khrims kyis bka' nan bstsal te/ bka' shog mang po bsgrags nas/ rgyal po des
'jig rten pa dang sgo bstun te/ sems can gyi don mdzad pas thams cad mgu ste/ rgyal po 'di thugs drang la sgam pa zhig 'dug go zhes zer nas mtshan yang srong btsan sgam pa
bya bar grags so/ /de nas bod blon po 'tshal ris de nas tsam yang ma bsgyur bas rgyal po'i thugs la/ ngas khrims bcas pa yang btsan par gyur pas/ de yis dam pa'i chos kyi
srol gtod do zhes grags bsgrags so/ /da ni chos kyis sems can rnams 'dul du btub par 'dug pas/ chos khrims dge ba'i las stabs dang chos bya snyam mo/ /chos byed pa la
rten lha gcig dgos te/ rgyu ci la byas na yong / sa la byas na ni sa rdo rgyu ngan/ sing la byas na ni 'gas/ rin po che gser dngul la byas na ni dus ngan gyi sems can blo
ngan rnams kyis brnab sems dang / gnod sems byas nas bshig na de rnams kyi sgrib par 'gyur zhing / dkor chen por 'gyur bas/ zangs dang ra gan la bya snyam pas/ tshes brgyad
kyi stod la nam mkha'i sprin/ gseb nas lha'i bu mo mang po lus phyed thon tsam byas nas lha'i me tog

dang / 'phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / na bza' dang / phye phur dang / gser dngul gyi me tog mang po dang / rnga bo che dang / rdza rnga dang /
dung dang / zangs rnga dang / cha lang dang / 'khar rnga dang / rol mo pi wang dang / sil khrol dang / gling bu dang / sgra snyan dang / gdungs dang / rgyal mtshan dang /
ba dan dang / bla re dang mchod mang pos mchod cing / dkon mchog gsum yid la byed cing / sems dang ba dang ldan pa mang pos rim gror byas/ bkur sti byas/ bsti stangs du
byas/ mchod pa mang pos rgyal po la mchod nas rgyal po khyed kyis thugs dam gyi lha ji lta bu zhig bya bar sems pa ni rgya gar lho phyogs mthar thug pa'i sing ga la'i gling
na rgya mtsho'i 'gram bye ma'i gling bcom ldan 'das kha sarpa Ni bzhugs pa'i sku rgyab na tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sdong po gcig la de'i nang arya lo ki shwa ra
zhal bcu gcig pa rang byung zhig bzhugs yod do/ /de spyan drangs na kha ba can gyi sems can rnams kyi don byed par 'gyur ro/ /zhes mgrin gcig tu brjod nas mi snang bar gyur
to/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs la lha de ji ltar byas la gdan drangs snyam pa dang / bar gyi lam na sa stong dang / brag dang chu 'thab dang / shing nags dang / chu bo che
dang / gcan 'phrang dang / mi rgod dang / gtum po byed pa rtsub pa'i mi dang / mi ma yin pa mang po yod pas lam la mi thar bar shes te/ rgyal po de la ngo mtshar skyes
so/ /de nas rgyal po da nga yid dam gyi lha dngos dang mjal bar bya dgongs nas mchod g.yog gi bu mo lo bcu drug lon pa lha'i bu mo 'dra ba bcu drug gis mchod pa rgyun mi
chad par byed do/ /rgyal po yang spyod lam bzhi thun bzhir mchod pa khyad par 'phags pa du mas mchod pa mdzad pas de nas rgyal po'i thugs kha nas sprul pa'i dge slong a
ka ra ma ti shi la bya ba zhig sprul nas dge slong la 'phags pa zhes bos nas rgya gar lho phyogs phyi'i rgya mtsho'i 'gram jo bo dang kha sarapha Ni'i sku rgyab glang po
nyal ba'i 'og bye ma'i nang na/ nga'i yi dam gyi lha yod kyis de spyan drangs las spyon zhes bsgo ba dang rgyal po'i 'od zer spros pa'i sna la sprul pa'i dge slong gi dbu
la de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med bzhugs pa zhig sprul nas/ sku de spyan 'dren du btang ngo / /der dge slong des rdzu 'phrul gyis skad cig yud tsam zhig la rgya gar shar
phyogs su grong khyer shing thags can bya bar byon te gdul bya dang 'dul bar shes nas dbu'i a mi de ba bstan te thams cad dad par byas/ byams snying rje'i chos bshad nas
smin par byas/ der yi ge drug pa rang byon zhig thon par byas/ yi ge drug pa chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i sa zhes grags so/ /sku de ni 'og min man chad na byin rlabs che
ba gcig yin no/ /de nas dge slong des rgya gar lho phyogs sing ga lar byon nas/ grong khyer ko tu zhes bya ba na rgyal po ud man ta ke sa ra zhes bya ba yab mes yar chad
kyi sku ring la nang pa'i chos kyi rgyal po yin la/ khong rang gi ring la chos lugs 'gyur nas phyi rol mu stegs pa'i chos lugs bzung zhing mchod pa na ma re re la ra lug
dang / ma he lnga brgya tsam re'i sge bregs nas de'i khrag gis dbang phyug chen po la mchod sbyin byed pa

de 'dul ba'i dus la bas par dgongs te/ grong khyer da'ei lho phyogs na sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyis rab gnas mdzad pa'i mchod rten chen po pad ma'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba yod
pa'i bum pa'i thad nam mkha' la dkyil krung gis skor ba mdzad pas/ grong khyer de'i dkyil na rgyal pau'i pho brang dgu thog yod pa'i phyogs bzhir lta ba'i skar khung yod
pa las/ re zhig lho phyogs kyi sgo chung gi nang na/ lan kan gyi 'og na phar rgyal pos dbu snyengs po byas nas gzigs tsa na/ sprul pa'i dge slong de mchod rten pad ma'i 'khor
lo la bar snang la skor ba byed pa mthong bas/ de la shin tu thugs dad par gyur nas/ sgo ba la mchod rten pad ma'i 'khor lo la skor ba byed pa'i dge slong zhig yod/
de bos shing / nga'i drung du khrid las shog ces bka' bsgo bas/ sprul pa'i dge slong la sgo ba des/ 'phags pa khyed rgyal po'i pho brang du byon par zhu zhus pas/ dge slong
de skyil krung ma bshigs par nam mkha' la gshegs nas/ rgyal po'i pho brang gi steng du bya bzhin babs nas byon no/ /der rgyal pos dge slong la phyag byas/ gdugs tshod
yon dang bcas pa zhig drangs nas/ de'i rjes la me tog snyim pa gang gtor nas/ ji ltar sangs rgyas la bsnyen bkur bya pa'i me tog nam mkha' la me tog gi gdugs su gyur pa bzhin
du/ me tog de dag sa la ma lhung bar sprul pa'i dge slong de'i dbu steng du me tog gi gdugs su gyur to/ /de nas dge slong de yang nam mkha' la gshegs pa las/ rgyal po
na re/ 'phags pa nyi ma re bzhin du bdag gi pho brang du gdugs tshod la byon par zhu zhes gsol ba btab pas/ dge slong gi zhal nas/ rgyal po khyod ngas ji skad zer ba nyan
na/ nga nyi ma re re bzhin khyed kyi pho brang 'dir yong / de ltar mi gsan mi yong gsungs pa las/ rgyal po na re/ 'phags pa ji skad gsung ba bzhin nyan par 'tshal lo zhes
zer nas/ nyi ma re re bzhin rgyal po'i pho brang du byon nas/ rdzu 'phrul du ma bstan nas rgyal po 'khor bcas thugs dad du bcug go/ /der dus la babs pa'i tshe dge slong
gi zhal nas/ kye rgyal po chen po zhes bos nas/ da phyi rol pa'i chos lugs ngan pa de thongs la/ nang pa sangs rgyas pa'i chos lugs yab mes kyi ji ltar bzung ba'i srol
bzhin mdzad pa zhu zhes pa dang / tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po dang / tsan dan go shirSha la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs la/ gtsug lag khang
brgya rtsa brgyad du bzhugs su chug mdzod ces gsol ba dang / rgyal po na re/ 'phags ji skad gsungs pa bzhin nyan pa lags te/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po 'og min gyi gnas
na bdog pa bdag la len pa'i nus pa ma mchis/ tsan dan ga shirSha ni/ ri bo ma la ya'i yul na sbrul gdug pa 'bar bas 'khril nas dkris yod pas/ de la len pa'i mthu med pas
bka' mi bstsal bar zhu/ gzhan ji ltar gsungs pa bzin bsgrub ces zhus pas/ sprul pa'i dge slong gi zhal nas/ rgyal po/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po ni lho phyogs kyi mtha'i
rgya mtsho'i 'gram jo bo kha sarpa Ni'i sku rgyab/ glang po che nyal ba'i 'og bye ma'i nang na yod/ tsan dan go shirSha ni/ ri bo po ta la'i byang phyogs na/ shugs pa'i
nags tshal zhig na yod/ de la ches bco lnga'i zla ba shar ba'i 'od zer phog pas me tog dmar chems kyis kha

bye nas yong ba yin pas/ de nas longs las sku gzugs gyis zhes gsungs/ de nas sprul pa'i dge slong la rgyal po na re/ 'phags pa 'o na bdag cag gis rnyed par mi 'gyur bas/ 'phags
pas de rnams len pa'i ded dpon mdzad par zhu zhes gsol bas/ de nas dge slong gis/ de dag len pa la bar chad mi 'byung bar myur du 'grub par bya ba'i don ched du/ mchod
rten pad ma'i 'khor lo la mchod par mdzad do/ /mchod pa rgya chen po mdzad pa'i phan yon ni/ byin rlabs shin tu che ste/ lo dang / zla ba/ zhag dang / za ma las byung
ba yin te/ de yang yon tan ni/ nad thams cad sos pa dang / yul gzhan du 'gro na yang bde bar phyin cing bde bar bzlog ldog par 'gyur ba dang / rin chen len du 'gro ba rnams
kyis kyang / de ltar mchod na gling gzhan nas/ bde bar ci bsam grub nas bzlog ldog pa'i byin rlabs mnga' 'o/ /de nas rgyal po srong matsan sgam po'i bka' lung gis kyang
/ phyi rabs kyi 'gro ba rnams kyis kyang / las dang bya ba ci byed pa thams cad kyi sngon du/ dkon mchog gsum la mchod pa gyis shig ci bsam pa 'grub pa yin no/ zhes gsungs
so/ /de nas rgyal po ud man ta ke sa ra dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi dang bcas pa sprul pa'i dge slong gi zhabs thog la phyin pas/ jo bo kha sarpa Ni'i sku rgyab na/
bye ma'i thang ka la glang chen nyal nas yod pa la/ rgyal po na re/ glang po che gang gi 'og na yod ces dris pas/ glang po che ma gi'i 'og na yod do/ /der rgyal pos dge slong
la tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po sing ga la'i gling du yod pa de ji ltar lags zhes zhus pas/ 'di ltar lags te/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig gis klu'i yul du chos gsungs
pa la/ 'og min gyi lha'i rig 'dzin phru gu pho mo rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa 'khor ba 'jig la mchod pa'i me tog 'khyer 'ongs pa las/ lam du jo bo kha sarpa Ni la yang
mchod pa byas pa'i tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i me tog sa la lhung ba de skyes te/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus su/ shing gi lo 'dab rgyas/ sangs
rgyas 'od srungs mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus su me tog rgyas/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das dus tsa na shing gi rtsa ba rul te sa la 'gyel nas/ bye ma rlung
gis bdas pa'i 'og tu nub pa yin te/ da lta glang po che mche ba drug pa zhig 'khun cing nyal ba de'i 'og na yod te/ 'du shes kyi mchog dag pa'i 'du shes yin/ rjes rnams
kyi mchog glang po che'i rjes yin te/ yon tan brgyad dang ldan zhing skyon brgyad sel ba'i phyir ro/ /de nas rgyal po dang / dge slong / dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi dang
bcas kyis rgya mtsho'i 'gram jo bo kha sarpa Ni'i rgyab glang po che'i 'og gi bye ma brus pas/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying pa'i sdong po byung / der tsan dan sdong po bcad
pas/ dal gyis chod bya ba'i sgra yang byung / de bcad pa'i nang nas tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku zhal bcu gcig pa rang byon lta bas chog mi shes pa/ dri bsung dpag
tshad bcu gsum tshun chad khyab pa khru gang ba zhig byon no/ /de yang glang po che'i nang na che ba kha shar du lta ba / sna dmar ba/ 'khun bu byed pa/ 'jing khung na
ghi hang gi zar khu yod pa/ mche ba drug pa'i 'og nas byung te/ 'og min nas lha'i rig 'dzin 'khor ba zhes bya

ba dang / rig 'dzin mang pos yar gyis tshes brgyad dang / mar gyi tshes brgyad la lha'i bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun 'bebs pa la mkha' 'gro ma rnams hab tob byed pa/ der mkha' 'gro
ma gcig gis bdud rtsa ma thob gyis dogs nas/ gcer bur byas mtshan ma gdangs nas phyin nas/ dpag bsam shing la snyim pa bzed pa las/ gzhan rnams gad mo shor bas/ mo skyengs
nas bred stabs su song bas/ bdud rtsi snyim pa gang 'thung / gang 'khyer la bros bsams pa las/ stabs te bo bas/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sgang bu'i nang du song
bas/ slad nas myu gu brdol te/ sdong po chen por gyur pa'i gtan tshigs de yin no/ /der tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po/ jo bo rang byon pa'i shing la bu ga phra mo nas/ shing
dal bus chos bya ba lan gsum byung ba de nas/ 'od zer kha dog sna lnga byung nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'od des snang bar byas shing / slar shing de la skor ba lan gsum
byas nas bu ga de nyid du thim par gyur to/ /rang byung tsan dan gyi sku de/ rtsa ba'i zhal gsum zhi ba/ (de'i steng khro bo'i zhal gsum bzhad pa/ ) de'i steng na khro zhal
gnyis brtsegs gtsigs pa/ de'i steng na zhal gnyis bzhad pa/ de'i steng na a mi de ba'i zhal bzhugs pa phyag bcu pa ste/ rtsa ba'i phyag gnyis thugs khar thal mo sbyar
ba/ de'i 'og ma g.yas na pad ma dkar po bsnams pa/ de'i 'og ma na 'khor lo bsnams pa/ de'i 'og ma na mda' bsnams pa/ de'i 'og ma sa gnon mdzad pa'o/ /g.yon gnyis pa na bgrang
'phreng 'dzin pa/ gsum pa na ril ba spyi blug 'dzin pa/ gzhi pa na gzhu/ tha ma na yid bzhin nor bu rin po che 'dzin pa'o/ /de yang glang po che rnams tshad pas gdung
ba'i tshe/ rgya mtsho che bags gyis gzhol ba la brgal te/ 'og nas 'ong ba'i tshe/ glang po che mche ba drug pa de la mngon shes cung zad yod pas/ 'du shes rnams kyi nang
nas 'chi ba mi rtag pa sgom pa yin/ glang phrug rnams khrid nas 'ongs te/ glang po che de tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i steng du nyal du 'ongs pas/ de la yon tan brgyad
yod pa ni/ 'jigs pa brgyad sel te/ chu'i sbugs su tshud nas phyir log mi shes pa'i 'jigs pa dang / sa'i sbugs su tshud nas 'chi ba dang / nags la me shor nas 'chi ba dang
/ gnam lcags lhung ba dang / yams nad drag po dang / seng ge dang / sa g.yo ba dang / mi rgod kyi 'jigs pa dang brgyad do/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku rang byon
ban 'du'i me tog ltar dkar ba de byon pas/ dge slong shin tu dgyes nas gus pa'i phyag bgyis/ phyag tu blangs nas tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku rang byon la ban 'du'i
me tog ltar dkar ba de snying po'i tshal pa gcig gi steng du bzhugs so/ /shing gzhan rnams rgyal po la byin no/ /rgyal pos lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs pa'i nang
du/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku re bzhengs nas bzhugs so/ /de nas rgyal po dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi dang bcas pa dge slong gi zhabs tog byas nas ri bo po ta lar
byon te/ tshes bco lnga'i zla ba'i 'od zer dang po phog pas/ shug pa'i sdong po zhig la me tog dmar phung ste byung ba mthong ba de la/ dge slong gi zhal nas/ tsan dan
ga shirSha ni 'di yin gsungs pas/ 'o na me tog thams cad nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis kha bye 'ong / zla ba'i

'od zer gyis kha zum nas 'ong ba yin la/ go shirSha ni zla ba'i 'od zer gyis kha phye ba 'di ji ltar yin/ de tsan dan go shirSha ni shin tu tu bsil bas/ zla ba'i 'od zer de'i
grogs su gyur bas zla ba'i 'od zer shar bas kha bye ba yin no/ /de nas go shirSha sdong po bcad pa'i rtsa ba'i cha las/ mchod sdong gcig sgrub pa dang / shing tshal pa
gcig dge slong gis phyag tshags mdzad do/ /gzhan rnams rgyal po ud man ta ke sa ra la byin pas/ der rgyal pos go shirSha'i sku brgya brtsa brgyad bzhengs nas/ sngar gyi
gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa der bzhugs su gsol lo/ /gzhan phyi rol pa'i lugs rnams dor/ yab mes kyi chos lugs dang po sangs rgyas pa'i chos la gus par byas pa nas bzung ste/
nang pa sangs rgyas par gyur to/ /gzhan yang sprul pa'i dge slong gis/ rgyal po ud man ta ke sa ra'i rgyal khams su rta pa'i nyin lam bcu gsum gyi khor yug tu/ sems can
thams cad rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud du dbang bskur nas/ dpag par dka' ba'i don zam mo thams cad dar zhing rgyas par mdzad do/ /de nas sprul pa'i dge slong gis mchod rten
pad ma'i 'khor lo'i bum pa'i nang byon nas/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig dang / sangs rgyas 'od srungs dang / shAkya thub pa dang gsum gyis gdung ring bsrel bre re re gser
gyi bang ba mig gsum yod pa la/ rgya rim bdun gyis btab nas bzhag go/ /de nas rten de rnams spyan drangs nas byon tsa na/ rgya gar yul dbus su byon pa'i tshe/ ma ga dha
rdo rje gdan gyi byang chub kyi shing drung du rgyal po'i lha lcam mang po lag pa sbrel nas shon rtse/ glu len gar byed pa la/ mi la la na re rgyal rigs kyi bu mo yin zer/
la la na re dmangs rje rigs kyi bu mo yin zer/ la la na re bram ze'i bu mo yin zer/ la la na re dmangs rigs kyi rgyud yin zer khong cag ma mgu ste/ nged dmangs rigs kyi
bu mo a ang zer nas lag sbrel ba btang ste/ bu mo gcig gis byang chub kyi shing la phyang mo yug byas pas/ shing gi yal ga gcig chag nas de sprul pa'i dge slong la phul
lo/ /sprul pa'i dge slong gis shing de'i rtsa ba la mchod rten gsum srub pa'i bum pa'i nang du/ de bzhin gshegs pa gsum gyi gdung dang ring bsrel gyi snying po der bcug
go/ /de nas gnas chen po brgyad du byon nas byang chub kyi snying po spyan drangs/ rgya mtsho'i gling gi 'jag ma la lha mang po rin po che'i lcug ma'i kha na 'dug pa gzigs
te/ 'jag ma phon po gcig kyang bsnams/ chu bo nairanya?dzana'i bye ma yang skad gcig la blangs te/ de ltar yul bcu gsum nas rdzas ngo mtshar can lnga ste/ byang chub kyi
shing gi mchod rten/ gnas chen po brgyad nas byang chub kyi sa/ chu bo nairanya?dzana'i bye na/ (tsan dan go shirSha/ )rgya mtsho'i 'jag ma'o/ /rgya gar lho phyogs nas
rdzas ngo mtshar can lnga ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa gsum gyi gdung dang / ring bsrel dang / tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'o/ /de ltar rdzas ngo mtshar can bcu po de rnams bsnams
byon nas/ sbra stod tshal na rgyal po srong btsan sgam po bzhugs pa'i drung du/ sprul pa'i dge slong gis/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku de tsan dan go shirSha'i
mchod sdong gi steng du bzhugs su gsol/ de'i mdun na phar byang chub shing gi mchod rten/ bde bar gshegs

pa gsum gyi gdung ring bsrel gyi snying po can gsum bzhugs su bcug nas phul/ rdza khyad par can gzhan rnams kyang rim gyis phul bas/ rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la da ni yi dam
gyi lha dang mjal bas sems can gyi don bya ba la tshegs med par dgongs nas thugs dges shing dang bar gyur to/ /de nas rgyal po srong btsan sgam pos tsan dan sbrul gyi snying
po'i sku dang / mchod sdong de gar bzhugs su gsol nas bu mo na chung ma mtshan dang ldan pa bzhis mchod pa rgyun mi chad par byed du bcug go/ /rgyal po de nyid dang
skad cig kyang mi 'bral ba mdzad do/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la/ yi dam gyi lha spyan drangs nas kha ba can gyi yul du skyes pa'i sems can la theg pa chen po'i chos
'byung bas/ sa phyogs gang nas sems can gyi don 'byung bya snyam nas sman lha'i thugs kha nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i sprul pa lha tho tho ri'i snyan shal
yin gyi/ de'i zhabs kyis bcags pa dmar po ri pha mes kyi ri shul du 'gro dgos pa bstan/ jo bo thugs rje chen po'i mchod sdong spyan drangs/ snon gyi sbra stod tshal nas
yab rgyal po'i re'u shal yod par dgung mnal/ sang nangs par gro btegs nas yar phrang gi brag bya khyung gi gshog pa 'dra bar sbra dang khal phog rta dang dre'u dang rnga
mo rnams rtsa la btang / gro btab/ rgyal po dang blon po sna chen pos chu khar khrus chab gsol du byon pa dang / chu'i nang 'od zer khra shig ge 'dug pa gzigs pas/ der
blon pos dris pa/ rgyal po chen po chab nang na 'od zer gda' ba ci lags/ bka' bstsal pa/ gzhan yang 'di'i sprul pa byang chub sems dpa' khyad par can re 'byung bar 'gyur
ro/ /sku gsung thugs kyi rten rang byung yang 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /ngas sngon sangs rgyas 'od dpag med kyi drung du khas blangs/ sangs rgyas des kyang kha ba can gyi sems
can gyi byed do zhes gsungs so/ /de nas dmar po ri'i rtse la pha mes kyi ri'u shal la pho brang zhig brtsigs nas bzhugs so/ /rgyal pos mchod sdong dang tsan dan sbrul
gyi snying po'i sku rang byon dang dasu skad cig kyang mi 'bral bar bzhugs so/ /rgya gar yul du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rang byung du byon
pa rnams sprul pa'i rgyal pos gsan nas/ de rnams spyan drangs par dgongs te/ dang po rgya gar gyi lho phyogs grong khyer skyid pa'i 'byung gnas bya ba na bram ze dga' ba'i
rtsal bya ba dang / bram ze mo bde skyid gnyis la/ bu bram ze mang rab dang / bu mo bram ze mo bde ba lcam bya ba mtshan dang dpe byad ldan pa bzang sdug la 'od chags
pa zhig yod pa las/ brag dmar bya skyibs can bya ba'i rtsar mdzo mo dkar mo gcig 'tsho zhing bsdan pas char pa byung nas brag bya skyibs su char yib byas pas/ bu mo gnyid
du song ba'i rmi lam du thugs rje chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa khre'u dar dkar gyi gos gyon pa/ shel gyi 'phreng ba khyer ba mdzes shing lta na sdug pa
zhig byung nas bu mo la khyed dang khyim thabs bya'o zer nas 'khrig pa spyod pa rmis pas bu mo'i lus thams cad bde bas khyab nas 'dug gnyid sad pa dang nga la khyo de 'dra
zhig yod na dga' ba la snyam pa zhig byung ngo / /bu mo de'i lus la srid pa zhugs te 'gul ba dang 'phrig pa

la sogs pa byung / lus shin tu bde ba dang / yang ba/ sems bde ba dang / yid gsal ba/ rnam par mi rtog pa dang ldan no/ /bu mo de'i bsam pa la nga skyes pa dang ni ma nyal/
lus ni sbrum pas bram ze'i rigs kyang smad/ yul mi kun yang gshe yong ngo tsha rnyed nas ming po'i chung ma mna' ma la 'di skad smras so/ /ngas skyes pa dang ni ma nyal/
lus ni sbrum/ srog 'dor ram snyam byas/ mna' mas ming po la smras pas/ ming po na re/ de la shi phod mi dgos/ de byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa sems can gyi don byed pa
zhig yong ba yin/ mo rang gi dpal du yong gyis shig de skad chung ma la bsrings nas/ ming pos ji skad zer ba bzhin du mna' mas bram ze mo la smras so/ /de nas zla ba tshang
ba dang khye'u zhig btsas par gyur to/ /byis pa shin tu legs pa mtshan dang ldan pa gcig byung ngo / /de bram ze mtshan mkhan la bstan pas/ mtshan shin tu bzang bas ming
yang bde mchog dus kyi snying po bya bar btags so/ /der byis pa shin tu skyed che ba/ dad pa dang ldan pa/ blo rno ba/ shes rab che ba zhig byung nas lo lnga la lon pa
na/ ma la nga'i pha'i las skal ci yin dris pas/ ma yis bu khyod la pha med pa yin/ las skal du chos byed dgos smras pas/ 'o na chos slob tu 'gro bas ma yis gnang bar mdzod
ces zer nas slob dpon dharma bho dhi bya ba paNDi ta mkhas pa zhig la chos zhu bar phyin pas khye'u lo lnga pas chos sde snod rgyud sde mi go gsungs nas chos sgrung dang
/ lde'u dang / drang don gyi chos bshad pas bram ze mo'ibu blo ma khengs nas da slob dpon gzhan zhig 'tshol snyam nas yul gzhan zhig tu song bas/ lam khar khye'u mdzes
pa rig pa dang ldan pa gnyis dang 'phrad de/ der khyed gnyis gar 'gro zhes dris pas khye'u gnyis na re/ nga rgyal po'i bu yin/ khong blon po'i bu yin/ nged gnyis 'khor la
ba skyo ba skyes/ yang dag pa'i chos shig 'tshol bas/ o rgyan gyi yul na dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thugs kyi sprul pa slob dpon chen po yang sprul dga' rab rdo rje zhes
bya ba da lta nyid du rang grol du 'gro ba'i chos ston pa zhig bzhugs zer/ de'i drung du chos zhur 'gro zhes smras pas/ 'o na nga yang bram ze'i bu zhig yin/ khyed gnyis
dang 'grogs nas 'gro zhes smras nas der khye'u gsum gyis slob dpon dga' rab rdo rje'i drung du phyin pa dang mjal nas gser gyi pa Ta phyag rten du phul te/ slob dpon chen
po lags nged cag gsum la tshe 'di nyid la sgyu lus kyi phung po 'di lus ngag yid gsum ma spangs par 'bras bu phung po lhag med du 'gro ba/ lta dgongs thams cad kyi phul
du byung ba sangs rgya ba'i chos shig zhus 'tshal zhus pas rgyal bu la dgongs pa klong chen rab 'byams kyi rgyud gnang / bram ze'i bu la star kha gegs sel gyi rgyud gnang
/ blon po'i bu la lta ba shan 'byed kyi rgyud gnang ngo / /bram ze'i bu la khyod 'phags pa'i sprul pa yin pas lha 'phags pa thugs rje chen po sgoms/ snying po yi ge drug
pa zlos/ 'gro ba rigs drug gi sgrib pa sbyong ba yin no/ oM ni ye shes lnga ma 'gag cir yang 'char/ /lta ba mtha' bral rten dang bral/ /ma ni ma bcos rang lugs rtsol dang
bral/ /spros bral mnyam pa nyid kyi ngang / /ma btsal rang bzhag sgom pa yin/ /Ni ni rigs pa sems kyi gzhi/

/rtogs pas ma rig sangs te ye shes spangs/ /'tha' bral rten med chos kyi ngang / /ma bsgrubs 'bras bu rang byung mchog /me ni ye shes 'od gsal ba/ /rnam rtog mtshan ma rang
sar bsreg /rang sar grol ba chos nyid yin/ /hUM ni thugs kyi snying po ste/ /chos nyid rtogs pa ma sbas gsal/ /rang byung ye shes 'gyur med gnas/ /bram ze'i khye'u khyod
kyis sems can gyi don rgya chen po 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /gsungs nas bka' rdzogs pa chen po bram ze skor du grags pa gsungs so/ /de nas bram ze'i khye'u brag phug lha zhal
can bya bar sgom zhing sgrub pas brag de shel gyi mchod rten rdo rjes brgyan pa zhig tu gyur nas/ bram ze'i khye'u lus ma bor bar phung po lhag med du mkha' spyod du gshegs
so/ /brag shel gyi mchod rten de la sus skor ba lan gsum byas na ngan song gsum du mi 'gro ste/ byang chub kyi lam du zhugs par 'gyur la bram ze'i khye'u ni 'phags pa
spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa yin pas sems can thams cad la thugs rjes dus drug tu 'gro ba'i don mdzad do/ /thugs rang byon du byon pa'i lo rgyus so/ /gsung rang byon du
ji ltar byon pa'i lo rgyus ni/ de yang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa la/ 'phags pa klu sgrub nyid/ lang kar gshegs pa'i mdo las/ so so rang rig
ye shes ni/ /rtog ge rnams kyi ma yin te/ /phyi ma'i dus su gyur pa na/ /bstan pa su yis 'dzin par 'gyur/ /tshul gnas 'dzin par gyur pa ni/ /blo gros chen pos khyod byos
shig /bde gshegs mya ngan 'das gyur nas/ /lo ni nyis brgya lon pa na/ /lho phyogs bhe ta'i yul du ni/ /dge slong dpal ldan zhes grags pa/ /de min klu zhes 'bod pa ni/ /yod
dang med kyi mtha' rdzogs shing / /nga yi bstan pa 'jig rten 'dir/ /bla med theg pa theg pa rab bstan nas/ /bde ba can du de 'gro'o/ /zhes gsungs so/ /'phags pa sprin chen
po'i mdo las/ li tsa byi gzhon nu sems can thams cad kyis mthong na dga' ba 'di/ nga mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og dge slong klu zhes bya bar bzung nas nga'i bstan pa rgyas
par byas te/ rim gyis 'jig rten gyi khams dwangs pa'i 'od ces bya bar de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes 'byung gnas 'od ces bya bar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgya'o/ /zhes
lung bstan to/ /rngo bo che'i mdo las kyang bstan/ 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud chen po las/ de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan las 'das nas/ lo ni bzhi brgya lon pa na/ /dge slong klu
zhes 'bod pa 'byung / /bstan pa la ni dad cing phan/ /rab tu dga' ba'i sa thob nas/ /lo ni drug brgya dag tu 'tsho/ /rig pa rma bya chen mo yang / /bdag nyid chen po de yis
grub/ /bstan bcos don ni mata' dag dang / /skye ba med pa'i don yang rig /de nas mthar gyis sangs rgyas nyid/ /kho na thob par 'gyur gsungs so/ /zhes so/ /yang mdo sde
sku gsung thugs kyi sgron me bltams pa zhes bya ba sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhes bya ba nas/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi rgyan lung bstan/ /nyi ma zla
ba lta bu ru/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa gsal byed pa/ /'jig rten khams 'dir 'dzam bu yi/ /gling gi rgyan drug 'byung bar 'gyur/ /gnyis kyis sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrungs/ /gnyis
kyis yid ches lung don 'grol/ /gnyis kyis thugs kyi sgron me lham/ /gnyis ni rgyud pa'i slob dpon te/ /gnyis

ni dngos kyi slob ma'o/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de rnams kyi nang nas klu sgrub mchog tu bstan te/ rin chen phung po bkod pa'i mdo sde las/ 'gro lding zhes bya'i grong khyer du/
/rgyal po ki ta ka dang ni/ /bram ze gha ta ma yi sras/ /klu sgrub ces bya 'byung 'gyur te/ /klu rnams kun gyi slob dpon no/ /zhes gsungs so/ /gzhan yang dpal mgon po dang
/ dpal lha mo'i rgyud la sogs pa dang / yongs su grags pa'i mdo rgyud mang po nas klu sgrub lung bstan pa brgya rtsa brgyad gsungs skad/ de ltar bde bar gshegs pas lung
bstan pa'i ston pa gnyis pa lta bu'i slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub des gdul bya'i las can gyi nang nas thugs rje chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis 'dug thugs
mngon par shes pas gzigs pas khye'u ma he'i rdzi bo byed pa gcig 'dug nas de las dang skal bar ldan par gzigs te/ slob dpon gyis byis pa ma he'i rdzi bo byed pa de'i
rtsar byon nas/ khyed ma he gtan du 'tsho ba yin nam zhes gsungs pas/ gtan du mi 'tsho/ 'khor ba'i chos la snying po mi gda' chos shig byed smras pas/ slob dpon gyis de
la/ chos byed na ngas bslabs sam/ gsungs pas/ de gnang na shin tu legs pas bdag lha gcig sgom pa dang / snying po gcig zlos pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa phyin ci ma
log pa yang dag pa'i don zhig zhu zer nas/ slob dpon gyis khyod kyi yid dang mig sngar ci yong gsungs pas/ byis pas smras pa/ bdag la yid yul dang mig sngar ma he'i phru
gu gcig yong zhus pas/ slob dpon gyis khye'u de la gdams pa/ ma he'i phru gu de jo bo thugs rje chen po'i skur sgoms/ rang yang thugs rje chen por sgoms la/ snying po yi
ge drug pa zlos shig 'phags pa'i thugs ka nas 'od zer byung rang la phog rang gi snying kha nas byung / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs la phog ma he dang snang ba thams cad
thugs rje chen por sgoms shig rang sems spros bral bdag gzhan gnyis su med/ /cir yang mi rtog rtsol med lhug par zhog /snang sems chos nyid skye ba med pa yin/ /ma rtogs
'khrul pa'i sems can byams dang snying rjes skyongs/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / khye'u des slob dpon gyis ji ltar gdams pa bzhin bsgoms bzlas byas shing nyams su blangs pas ma
he bdud rtsis 'tsho zhing nyin re bzhin rtsa brngas te dgong mo ma he la rtsa phon re bkal nas 'ongs/ sang phod lo dus su song ba dang ma he'i phru gu'i snying kha nas
tshur grod pa lta bu zhig byung / de'i nang nas khye'u dkar po shel ltar dag pa lag na gser gyi phyag shing la mu tig gi yi ge drug pa 'bur du dod pa thogs pa zhig byung
nas/ ma he'i rdzi bo la phyag shing gtad de dbang bskur byin gyis brlabs nas dngos grub ci 'dod gsungs pas/ ma he'i rdzi bos phyag 'tshal skor ba byas nas bdag gi lus 'di
'phags pa'i skur gyur/ ngag byin gyis brlabs te yi ge drug pas 'gro ba rigs drug gi don byed par 'dod ces nas gdams ngag zhus pas sprul pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i zhal nas
yi dam gyi lha rang gi sems su shes par gyis shig snying po gsal dag chos kyi rang sgra la shes par gyis/ sems rig pa stong gsal du shes par gyis/ stong pa chos sku skye
med du shes par gyis/ sems can thams cad kyi don la mi skyo bar gyis/ gsungs nas lha de nam mkha' la 'ja'

yal ba ltar mi snang bar gshegs so/ /de nas ma he'i rdzi bos dgong mo de bzhin ma he ded nas 'ongs pas yul mi rnams kyis thugs rje chen po 'od sgor re byon par mthong nas/
kun gyis ma he'i rdzi bo la phyag 'tshal me tog gtor/ skor ba byas pas ma he'i rdzi bos smras pa/ khyed yul mi kun su dang nor/ nga ni ma he'i rdzi bo yin zhes smras pas/
yul mi kun na re/ khyed ni 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i skur snang ngo / /bdag cag gi phyag dang mchod pa'i gnas yin no/ /zhes smras nas/ de mchod gnas su zhus pas ma he'i
rdzi bo de lus ma spangs par phung po lha'i skur gyur nas dag pa mkha' spyod du gshegs te zhag re la 'dzam bu gling dang 'gro ba rigs drug gi gnas lan gsum bskor zhing
/ skal ldan rnams dngos grub su 'dod mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub nga la longs zhes gsung zhing byon pa yin te/ sems can las kyi sgrib pa ma dag pa rnams kyis mi
mthong ba yin no/ /phyag shing la snying po 'bur du dod yod do/ /nub phyogs par pa ta na'i gtsug lag khang gi slob dpon klu sgrub kyi dgon pa gser gyi brag bya skyibs can
bya ba na da lta yang bzhugs so/ /de ni gsung rab byung byon pa'i lo rgyus so/ /spyan ras gzigs kyi sku rang byung du byon du byon nas 'gro don ji ltar mdzad pa ni/ rgya
gar ma ha dha'i nub phyogs na tshong dpon mdzes pa'i blo gros zhes bya ba thugs rje chen po la mos pa/ chos la dad pa/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dka' ba dang
du len pa zhig yod pas/ rgya mon gyi ri khrod na tsan dan gyi sdong po gcig la skor ba byed cing 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs la yang gsol ba 'debs shing / oM ma Ni padme
hUM/ zhes yi ge drug pa'i snying po 'di bzlas nas kho tshe'i dus byed khar sman lam btab/ tsan dan gyi sdong po 'di thugs rje chen po'i skur gyur nas nga sems can gyi don
byed par gyur cig ces smon lam btab po/ /tshe'i dus byas te 'das gyur to/ /sdong po de'i rtsar kho'i phung po bsregs pa dang sang phod lo dus su phung po bsregs pa'i shul
na tshur shing gi lba ba chen po zhig skyes so/ /lba ba de gas pa dang de nas 'od zer kha dog sna lnga 'phros pas/ thugs rje chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug sku rang
byung du byon te/ dbus na budha lo ki shwa ra zhes bya ste/ sku mdog dkar po zhal bcu gcig pa phyag bcu pa zig byon te nam mkha' la gshegs skad do/ /shar phyogs su badzra
lo ki shwa ra zes bya ste/ rdo rje'i rigs sngon mo byon/ lho phyogs nas radna lo ki shwa ra zhes bya ste rin chen rigs gser po byon/ nub phyogs nas pad ma lo ki shwa ra
zhes bya ste/ pad ma'i rigs dmar po byon byang phyogs nas karma lo ki shwa ra zhes bya ste las kyi rigs sku mdog ljang khur byon no/ /de'i dus su rgyal po byang chub sems
dpa' srong btsan sgam po'i thugs dgongs la/ da rung rgya gar dang lha bal na mchod gnas ngo mtshar can 'dra yod yong bas spyan drangs la sems can gyi don bya snyam nas
tsan dan gyi sku la gsol ba btab nas mchod pa byas pas/ lha'i sku las 'od zer byung nas lho bar du song ngo / /der 'od zer gang song gzigs pas rgya gar dang bal po'i yul
gyi phar ngos na tsan dan ha ri'i sdong po la 'phags pa'i sku lnga byon nas bzhugs pa gzigs pa 'od zer gyi sna

la dge slong a ka ra shi la ma ti sprul nas spyan 'dren du btang bas sprul pa'i dge slong gis mang yul gyi rong du byon tsa na mdze nad kyis thum bur 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal
'dug pa gzigs so/ /de nas bal po'i mthil du byon pas yam bu yam 'gal na lo skor re re la mi rims cad kyis bcom nyen du 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa 'dug de nas bal po'i mthil du byon
pa dang / rgya gang dang bal po'i mtshams na zla ba gsum gsum la tshong dpon re re gnod sbyin chen po zhig gis khyer nas snga dro re la sbos grir 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa 'dug
pa gzigs so/ /de nas tsan dan ha ri'i gnas su byon pa dang / tsan dan gyi sku rigs lngar 'dug pa gzigs so/ /mtshan mo yang mun pas mi sgrib par nyin mo bzhin du snang
ngo / /de nas sprul pa'i dge slong gis spyan drangs pas gsol ba btab nas sku de rnams las dri bsung dpag tu med pal dpag tshad bcur khyab pa byung ngo / /sku de rnams lta
bas chog mi shes pa mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa'i 'od zer nyi ma shar ba lta bu 'dra ba snang nas spyan drangs pas/ 'phags pa lo ki shwa ra bya ba'i 'od zer sngon po
'phros pa de ma ga dhar zhog gsungs nas gshegs su ma gnang / byis lapa lo bdun lon pa tsam sku mdog dkar po byas pa zhig rgya gar rdo rje gdan du bzhugs so/ /de nas 'phags
pa lba ti bya ba sku mdog dmar po can 'od zer dmar po 'phro ba byis pa lo brgyad pa tsam zhig bal bod kyi mtshams mang yul gyi rong du byon/ /mdze nad chad do nga 'dir
zhog cig gsungs nas gshegs su ma gnang ngo / /de nas bya'aphags pa 'jwa ma li bya ba sku mdog ser po 'od zer ser po 'phro ba byis pa lo lnga lon pa'i tshad tsam zhig bal
yul yab bu'i shar phyogs su rims nad chen po sel ba'i don du 'gro don la dgongs nas bzhugs so/ /de nas 'phags pa dbu khang bya ba sku mdog dmar ljang 'od zer ljang khu 'phro
ba zhig bal yul gyi khrong khyer ye rang gi lho phyogs na bzhugs so/ /gzhan du spyan drangs du ma btub ste yul der sbos grir 'chi ba chad do/ /yul de rnams kyi sdug
bsngal ba de rnams sku de rnams kyi byin brlabs kyis grol zhing zhi bar mdzad do/ /sprul pa'i dge slong gis de rnams kyi lo rgyus rgyal po'i snyan du gsol bas/ rgyal po'i
zhal nas sems can gyi don logs na med do/ /de shin tu legs so gsungs nas thugs shin tu dges par gyur to/ /de nas sprul pa'i dge slong la mchod pa sna tshogs kyis mchod nas
mnyes par mdzad de rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i mdzod spur thims par gyur to/ /da ni kha ba can gyi sems can rnams la theg pa chen po'i chos shig 'byung bar bya dgongs
pas/ de yang bal po'i yul nas sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i bcom ldan 'das jo bo mi skyod rdo rje dang / byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo dang / tsan dan
go shi rSha'i sgrol ma rang byung gsum bzhugs so/ /rgya nag po'i yul na bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i sku tshab bzhugs pa bstan pa'i phyir/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po
la byon pa'i jo bo thugs rje chen po'i mdzod spu nas 'od zer gnyis 'phros te/ gcig nub tu song / gcig shar du song bas nub tu song de bal po'i yul yam bu yam 'gal na bal
po'i rgyal po gu na kA ma hA de ba ho sha khri pa'i sras bhi ham lo bi pa de ba zhes bya ba la lha gcig khri

btsun bya ba bu mo lo bcu drug lon pa/ sku mdog dkar la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa/ kha byad lta bas chog mi shes pa grong pa'i chos kyis ma
phog pa/ kha nas uta?pal sngon po'i dri bro ba/ rin po che'i bang mdzod la mnga' ba zhig yod pa de 'od de la brten nas/ bal po'i yul dang rgyal po rata?n de ba yang tshul
de ltar byas/ rgyal pos kyang de kho na bzhin gzigs so/ bu mo de bod du spyan 'drongs pa na sku de gsum yang bod du byon nas/ lho bal na bzhugs pa'i chos dang yi ge 'bru
gcig kyang ma lus par 'byungs par gzigs so/ /shar du song ba'i 'od zer des rgya nag po'i yul ke'u shing khri sgo na kong rtse 'phrul gyi rgyal po'i sras rgyud rkong rtse
'phrul chung btsan pa zhes bya ba la/ lha gcig ong jo bya ba bu mo lo bcu drug lon pa sku mdog sngo la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ uta?pal sngon po'i mdog 'dra ba/ mtshan
dang dpe byad du ldan pa/ kha byad lta bas chog mi shes pa/ kha nas tsan dan ha ri'i dri bro ba/ ber chung chu zhing gab pa bdun brtsegs gon pa/ rig pa'i bstan bcos la
mnga' brnyes pa zhig yod pa/ rgya nag gi yul dang rgya rje btsan pa yang / rgyal pos 'od byung ba de la brten nas de kho na bzhin du gzigs so/ /bu mo de spyan 'drongs na
sku de dang rgya nag po'i yul na yod pa'i chos dang / rig pa/ gtsug lag ma lus pa bod du 'byung bar gzigs so/ /sang nangs par snga dro blon po rnams rgyal po la phyag bya
bar phyin pa la/ rgyal po rgya phor na ja gsol zhing yengs ma gtam du ma da/ mdang gsum nga'i rmi lam na nub phyogs bal po'i yul na bu mo dkar mo gcig 'dug pa rmis/ shar
phyogs rgya nag po'i yul na bu mo sngon mo gcig 'dug par rmis/ zhes rmi lam du byung ba gsungs pa dang / blon po thon mi sam bho Da mi chung gis g.yon ngos nas phyag byas
nas/ bu mo de gnyis ngos kyis gdan 'drongs par byed do zhes zhus so/ /yang g.yas ngos nas blon po mgar stong btsan yul bzung gis 'bras chang rgya phor gang 'dren zhing
phyag byas te/ rgyal po'i rmi lam de gzhan su la yang mi bzlas par zhu/ bu mo de gnyis bdag gis gdan 'dren par bgyi'o/ /zhes zhus so/ /de nas blon po gnyis kyi bsam pa la
rgyal pos bu mo gnyis rmi lam du byung gsungs pa de/ de gnyis nga'i btsun mor khug bya ba yin nges snyam nas grong khyer gyi gtso bo rnams la yang / sang nangs par grong
re re nas lha sa'i na thang dang nags kyi mtshams 'o thang gi mtsho 'gram/ gla ba'i tshal chu mig gi 'gram/ shing star ka'i bsil grib la 'dun ma la tshogs shig 'dun rkyen
re yang khyer las shog cig ces bsgo'o/ /der nangs par grong khyer gyi gtso bo bdun tshogs pa na 'dun rkyen bsdus pas gnyis kyis sha rkang pa re re byung / gnyis kyis sha
lag pa re re byung / de tsho bsgrigs pas sha khog ma nyams pa gcig tshang bar byus bas/ de la shis pa brjod cing 'dun rkyen legs/ bkra shis pas da smon ne kha/ 'dun ma
yang rgya ma chung zhig zer bas/ de la blon po mgar stong btsan yul bzung na re/ 'o na rgyal po'i zhal nas/ shar nub gnyis na bu mo lha gcig sngon mo gcig dang / dkar mo
gcig rmi lam du byung gsungs nas rje lha gcig kyang nar song 'dug pas 'o skol lha gcig mo de gnyis spyan drangs

zhes pa dang / de la blo mthun par blon po rnams na re de shin tu legs so/ /blon po chen pos rje la de skad zhus shig ces nas/ blon po mgar stong btsan gyis sha de rgyal po
la drangs legs pa dang shis pa brjod/ rmi lam gyi bu mo de gnyis spyan drangs par 'tshal na de len pa'i thabs ji ltar bgyi zhes zhus pa dang / rgyal po'i zhal nas 'o na
de legs so/ /dang po nub phyogs kyi bu mo spyan drongs shig de ston zla ra ba'i tshes brgyad kyi skar ma nabs so'i rjes la rgyal gyi nyi ma ri rtse la ma shar ba/ bya thi
ba'i skad kyis mnon pa'i dus su rta pa brgya tham pa chas las song zhig gser gyi dong rtse brgya po 'di 'khyer la/ bal po'i rgyal po la phyag rten gyi shig gser bang ba
bdun po 'di 'khyer las zhu rten gyi shig gser gyi dra ba la lha'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi phra btab pa glang po che g.yogs pa 'di phul la zhu rten gyis la lha gcig zhus
shig gsungs nas btang bas/ de tsa na bal po'i rgyal po khros nas mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal pos nga la brnyas re che na/ gnyen bya ba mnyam po la 'doms pa la khyod pas nga bzang
/ nga la chos yod de khyod la med/ khyod kyis gtsug lag khang dang dkon mchog gsum gyi rten bzhengs nus na nga'i bu mo ster/ de mi nus na mi ster/ de'i lan khyer la shog
zer yong / de tsa na sgrom bu 'di phul cig de nas nged la chos la brten pa'i rgyal khrims yod de khyod la khrims med/ khrims 'cha' nus na bu mo ster/ mi nus na bu mo
mi ster zer yong bas de tsa na sgrom bu 'di phyag rten du phul cig de nas yang khyod dang nga gnyis mi mnyam/ khyod mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po la zas nor longs spyod med de
dbul/ nga la sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi ring nas deng sang bar du thab kyi du ba rgyun mi 'chad/ nor longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa yod de khyed la med pas bu mo mi ster
zer yong / de tsa na zangs kyi sgrom bu 'di phul cig 'di rnams phul la phar lam dang tshur lam la jo mo khro gnyer can la gsol ba thob cig de'i mtshan nas brjod la song
zhig der lha gcig spyan drangs nas 'ong gi gsungs nas thabs bslabs nas gtang ngo / /der rta pa brgya tham pas bal yul du phyin nas 'phrin pa la dong rtse rngan par byin te/
rgyal po dang mjal bar zhu zhes phyag byas pas/ rgyal po dang zhag bdun du ma mjal/ de nas rgyal po dang mjal ba'i tshe blon po mgar gyi sna drangs nas phyag gral byas
te zhe sa rdzogs pa dang / rgyal po na re/ khyed rnams rtags dang dpa' lugs sam/ (can/) su yin gang nas yong gsungs/ blon po rnams kyis lo tsA ba bar du bcug nas zhus pa/
nged mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i pho nya ba lags te gser gyi dong rtse brgya tham pa phyag rten byas/ gser gyi bang ba rnams zhu rten du phul nas/ der
rgyal pos khyed ci byed gsungs pa la/ blon pos zhus pa/ nged kyi rgyal po la btsun mo med pas khyed bal po'i rgyal po la gnen 'dogs/ lha gcig khri btsun 'di rgyal po srong
btsan sgam pos gzigs pas btsun mor zhu 'tshal zhes zhus nas/ de nas dra ba dra phyed glong po che khebs pa de yang rgyal po'i spyan sngar bzhag der dra ba dra phyed 'di
yon tan du ma dang ldan te mi nad dang phyugs nad byung ba'i tshe 'di gon nas grong khyer gyi mtha' bskor

bas nad chad nus/ sad dang ser ba byung du dogs pa'i tshe 'di gon nas grong khyer gyi mtha' bskor na de dag mi 'byung bar 'gyur/ g.yul du zhugs pa'i tshe 'di gon pas g.yul
las rgyal nus so/ /de ltar ngo mtshar che zhing 'dzam bu'i gling 'di na 'di la gong thang gdab tu mi btub pas 'di yang rin du 'bul bas/ lha gcig gnang bar zhu zhus pas/ bal
po yi rgyal pos khrel dgod byas te/ rgyal po na re/ a pa brnyas pa re che/ gnyen bya ba mnyam po la 'dogs pa yin pas khyed bas nga bzang / nga'i gnyen zla khyed ma yin
mod kyi/ 'on kyang khyed yong zin 'dug pas phar la song la/ khyed rang gi rgyal po la rgyal po bya ba la mchod gnas dgos pa yin/ khyed la chos med/ nga la sangs rgyas 'od
srungs kyi sku ring nas sku gsung thugs kyi rten yod pas bzang / khyed kyi mchod gnas sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs pa dang / de bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs
nus na ngas bu mo bkas gnang / de bzhin mi nus na bu mo mi ster gyis la de'i lan khyer las shog gsungs pas/ de la blon po mgar gyis khyed bal po dang bod kyi bar sa thag
ring po la/ 'phrin phar skyel tshur skyel byas na nged kyi lha gcig spyan 'drongs pa'i dus mi yong / de la rgyal pos gser gyi sgron bu 'di bskur ba lags byas te phyag tu
phul bas/ phyag tu bzhes nas kha phye nas gzigs pas/ bal po'i yi ge ru byung nas bklags lapas rgyal po bya ba la mchod gnas dgos pa yin khyod zer te/ khyod stod kyi rgyal
po sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi ring nas sku gsung thugs kyi rten yod de nga la med zer te/ khyod lha gcig gnang na ngas nyi ma gcig la sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul
nas lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs te/ sgo thams cad nub phyogs bal po'i yul la bstan la bzhag de ngo mtshar ram bya ba byung bas/ bal po'i rgyal po'i bsam pa la
'di rang bden nam mi bden/ mi bden na khyod pas nga bzang ba la brnyas bcos re che/ bden na ngas khyed mi thub ste thub par dka' ba gcig 'dug snyam nas/ yang khyed kyi
rgyal po des nga la khas len che bar gda' ste/ des kyang mi phan rgyal po bya ba la khrims dgos pa yin te khrims med pas/ nged la 'di na chos dge ba bcu'i khrims gtsang ma
chos dang mthun par yod de/ khyed la med/ khyed kyi chos dkar po dge bcu'i khrims 'cha' nus na bu mo sbyin/ de mi nus na mi ster gyis la lan khyer shog gsungs pa dang /
de nas blon po mgar gyis khyed bal yul dang bod gnyis kyi bar du 'phrin phar skyel tshur skyel byas na sa thag ring po la nged kyi lha gcig 'drongs pa'i dus mi yong bas
de la rgyal pos dngul gyi bka' sog sgrom bu 'di bskur ba lags so/ /zhes dngul gyi sgrom bu phyag tu phul bas/ phyag tu bzhes nas gzigs pas bal po'i yi ge byung bas/ rgyal
po la khrims dgos pa yin te khyed la khrims med zer te/ khyed dges shing lha gcig bkas gnang na ngas nyi ma gnyis la sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas chos dkar
po dge ba bcu'i khrims bca'/ de ngo mtshar ram bya ba byung / bal po'i rgyal pos snyam na/ nga bas kho thu ste lha gcig khri btsun kho la sbyin dgos/ de ma byin na khos
sku lus kyi bkod pa 'di tsam sprul nas dpag drangs nas nga'i rgyal khams thams cad 'joms/ grong khyer thams

cad bsreg lha gcig khri btsun yang rang dbang med par 'khrid do snyams nas/ thugs kyis ni lha gcig sbyin par thag bcad/ zhal du ni ma bton par blon po rnams blo brtan mi brtan
lta ba dang brtag par bya bas yang smras pa/ khyod las nga bzang ste/ khyod mtha' 'khob na zas dang longs spyod med/ nga la sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi ring nas da ltar
bar du thab tu du ba rgyun ma 'chad pa'i longs spyod kyi brel ba med pa yod pas khyed la med/ 'dod pa'i nor longs spyod la longs spyod du yod na lha gcig sbyin gyis/ de
med na mi ster gyis la lan khyer las shog gsungs pas/ de la blon po mgar gyis zhus pa/ sngar zhus pa bzhin du khyod bal yul dang bod gnyis kyi bar du thag ring po de la
'phrin phar skyel tshur skyel byas na/ nged kyis lha gcig spyan 'drongs pa'i dus mi yong bas de la rgyal pos zangs kyi sgrom bu 'di bskur ba lags so/ /zhes sgrom bu de phyag
tu phul lo/ /de rgyal pos gzigs pas bal po'i yi ger byung ste/ khyod bal po la sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi ring nas thab kyi du ba rgyun chad ma myongs pa nor longs spyod
kyis brel ba med/ nged mtha' 'khob rgyal po la med zer te/ khyod dgyes shing lha gcig khri btsun bkas gnang na/ ngas nangs gcig la sku lus kyi bkod pa brgyar sprul la
mig yul du gyur pa la gzugs kyi longs spyod mi 'dra ba stong / rna ba'i yul du gyur pa la sgra glu dbyangs dang rol mo sil snyan gyi longs spyod mi 'dra ba stong / sna'i
yul du gyur pa la dri'i longs spyod mi 'dra ba stong / lce'i yul du gyur pa la zas ro mchog gi longs spyod mi 'dra ba stong / lus kyi yul du gyur pa la reg bya'i longs spyod
mi 'dra ba stong / yid kyi yul du gyur pa la tshad med pa bzhi/ byang chub kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun la sogs pa stong du sprul/ gzhan yang skad cig thang cig yud tsam
gcig la 'dzam bu'i gling gi longs spyod kyi gter kha thams cad kha phye la sems can thams cad la brel ba dang / phongs pa thams cad bral ba'i longs spyod mnga' thang chen
pos sems can thams cad kyi don bya la bde ba la bkod la bzhag gi de ngo mtshar che 'am bya ba byung bas/ der bal po'i rgyal pa'i snyam pa la/ mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po'i
sku lus kyi bkod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab/ bka' sog sgrom bu yang thogs pa med/ snyam nas der lha gcig khri btsun bkas gnang ngo / /der yab rgyal
pos lha gcig la khyed bod kyi rgyal po'i btsun mo la 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ lha gcig gi zhal nas/ pha ma dang ming po dang mi 'phrad pa'i yul chos pa/ gnyen dang mi 'phrad
pa'i yul der nga mi 'gro zhes smras so/ /der yab rgyal po na re/ des mi phan/ khong sprul pa'i rgyal po yin par 'dug kho la sra brtan nas khyod khong la ma byin na/
khos sprul pa'i dmag mang po sprul nas khyed dbang med du 'khyer/ yul thams cad 'joms palas de bas da lta 'chams pa rung ngo gsungs te/ der yab rgyal pos lha gcig khri btsun
mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po la btsun mor gtong ngo gsungs pas/ mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po de dad pa shin tu che ba la lha rten med zer bas nga la rdzongs su lha gsum skur
cig rgyal po de dbul zer bas rin po che glang po che'i rgyab khal bdun skur cig ces lha gcig khri btsun gyis

zhu ba rgyal po la gsol bas/ rgyal pos lha gcig khri btsun la gnang bar dam bca' khas blangs pas/ de'i mchod gnas su sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyis rab gnas mdzad pa'i jo mo mi
skyod rdo rje dang / byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo/ rang byung tsan dan gyi jo mo sgrol ma gsum gnang ngo / /rin po che'i bang mdzod kha phye nas glang po che'i rgyab khal
bdun rdzongs su gnang ngo / /glang po che gcig smad du lha gcig khri btsun chibs nas tsan dan gyi sku phyag tu bsnams/ stod du jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje dang / byams pa chos
kyi 'khor lo bzhugs nas/ glang po che bdun la rin po che bkal te mang yul gyi shing sna tshogs skye ba'i yul zhig tu bskyal nas der glang po che brgyad po phyir log go/
/rin po che'i khal rnams rta mang po la bkal nas yi dam rnams dang lha gcig khri btsun dang / mi'i nor la dga' ba rin po che rata?n de ba dang / rtag sha rata?n de ba dang
baiDUrya'i lhung bzed gsum gyis gtso byas pa rnams blon po rnams kyis 'breng skyed byas nas sku gsum gyis brag dang chu 'thab kyi 'phrang la zhabs kyis byon/ mang yul
nas mdzo dang dre'u gsum gyis spyan drangs/ jo mo khro gnyer can gyi mtshan nas brjod cing gsol ba btab nas byon pas/ lha gcig khri btsun dre'u dkar po zhig la chibs nas
lha sa'i mthil la phyags phebs pa'i tshe/ rgyal po dga' ston gyi gdan sar spyan drangs/ dmar po ri'i pho brang du rgyal po dang zhal mjal ba'i tshe skye bo kun dang lha
mi kun la snang ba gsum du byung / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la arya pa lo rgyal por sprul pa dang / lha mo khro gnyer can lha gcig khri btsun du sprul nas mtha' 'khob tu
chos dar bar bya ba'i phyir zhal mjal ba'i sku las 'od zer 'phros pas phyogs bcu nam mkha'i mtha' khyab pa'i sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa thams cad skad cig la rgyun
gcod pa'i rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyis rnam par sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa gzigs so/ /byang chub sems pa rnams kyis bdag nyid chen
po 'khor byang chub sems dpa' 'bum gyis bskor nas/ theg pa chen po'i chos 'chad pa dang / nyan pa dang / 'dri ba dang / klog pa dang / sems pa dang / sgom pa dang / rnam
par grol ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'byung bar gzigs so/ /skye bo tha mal pa rnams kyis snang ba la bon po mang po dang bcas pa tshogs nas rgyal po dang lha gcig khri btsun
gnyis gdan gcig la bzhugs pa dang / dbu skra sbrel ba dang / sha khu thung res byed pa dang / mar khu'i skyu brje res byed pa la sogs pa'i snang ba byung bar mthong ngo
/ /de nas rgyal po tsan dan gyi sku bas 'ben tshad re ring du skad cig kyang mi 'bral bar bzhugs te/ de la lha gcig khri btsun gyis snyam pa na/ rgyal po 'di lha dang mi'i
spyod yul las 'das pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa ngo mtshar ba zhig 'dug pa la pho brang gi phyir mi 'gro ba cis lan snyam nas 'di 'dri rgyu yin pa la ngas ni bod
skad mi shes/ rgyal pos bal po'i skad ni mi shes pas/ 'di phal cher pha rol gyis dmag tshogs kyis 'jigs pa yod nges skrag yin te yong bsam ste/ de la thugs bde ba'i thabs
gcig bya snyam ste/ rin po che mang po'i rkyen sbyar nas gnod sbyin mang po bran du bkol te/ dmar po ri'i mtha'i

khongs stag ri seng ri rgya che ba khongs su bcug so phag gi lcags ri gyang rim sum cu rtsa gnyis dang mnyam pa'i mtho khyad tsam pa de la mda' yab dang / pha gu dang / skyed
pa dang / rta babs dang / rin po che 'bar ba dang / dril bu g.yer kha'i sgra 'khrol ba dang / mu tig gi dra ba dang dra ba phyed pas brgyan pa/ srin po lang ka mgrin bcu'i
grong khyer dang mtshungs pa/ de'i lho ngos lcags ri'i nang na pho brang sog po'i mkhar dgu thog dang / rgyal po'i rtsi mkhar mnyam pa/ de gnyis lcags thag gis 'brel
nas dngul dang zangs kyi sbubs kyi srang lam la 'og tu dril bu stong btags pa/ rgyal po dang btsun mo gnyis phar gshegs tshur gshegs pa la sil snyan gyi sgra 'byung ba la
phan tshun rgyu ba/ rtse mo la na bun 'thul ba/ nam phyed la char zim zim 'bab pa/ sgo rnams rang bzhin dam par byed pa/ lcags ri'i nang na grong khyer chen po yod pa de
la mkhar dgu brgya dgu bcu go dgu rtse mo nyag dang stong / rtse mo rnams nyag thag gis sbrel ba/ mkhar re la mdung ba dan dmar po can sked pa khra bo stong btsugs pa/
phyogs bzhi na sgo spe bzhis bsrungs pa/ gtso 'khor la bya ra ba mi lngas bsrungs pa/ pha rol gyi dmag gi 'jigs pas mi tshugs pa/ mthong na 'jigs pa dang skrag pa'i pho brang
de lta bu zhig brtsigs so/ /de'i dpe ra sa'i 'phrul snang gi klu khang gi logs la bris yod do/ /shar phyogs kyi 'od kyis gsal bar byas pa'i lha gcig spyan drangs bar
bya ba ni/ blon po chen po mgar gyis rgyal po la zhus pa/ rje lags/ rgyal nag po'i yul gyi lha gcig sngon mo de bdag gis spyan 'dren par zhu zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas
khyed rgya nag po'i lha gcig sngon mo de spyan 'dren na nga'i drung du shog cig thabs bslabs te gtong ngo gsungs nas/ de nas rta pa brgya tham pa 'gro bar chas pa dang
/ blon po chen po mgar stong btsan yul bzung gis rgyal po'i drung du phyin pa dang / rgyal pos gser gyi bang ba bdun zhu rten du bskur/ dong rtse bdun phyag rten du bskur/
rin po che baiDUrya sngon po'i rmog la pad ma ra ga'i phod btsugs pa/ de gon na lha dang lha ma yin 'thab pa'i g.yul du zhugs kyang rin po che'i mtshon cha 'khor lo dam
bca' bzhi ldan pas brgyab kyang mi 'phog rgyal po'i dbang bskur ba'i prog zhu yon tan dang ldan pa yin pas lha gcig gi rin du byed/ rin po che man shel mdog gsal ba mdangs
dang ldan pa nyin mo bas nub mo 'od gsal ba grong khyer gyi sgron me byed pa dang lha gcig gi phyag rten du chu shel bskur ro/ /'di rnams rgyal po dngos la phul la zhu
ba gyis shig ces gsungs so/ /bka' shog sgrom bu lnga gtad nas rgyal po des khyod la bka' lung mi 'thad pa gsung du 'ong gi de'i dus bka' shog sgrom bu 'di rnams rim pa bzhin
du phul la 'di ltar gyis bya ba'i zhal ta bslabs btang ngo / /glu dang / mchod tshig dang / snyan ngag dang / sdeb sbyor dang / bzhad gad dang / rtse mo dang / kha btseg
dang / gyad stobs 'gran pa la sogs rgya nag po'i spyod pa dang mi mthun pa yang bslabs te btang ngo / /mar lam dang yar lam/ jo mo sgrol ma'i mtshan nas brjod la song
zhig bya khwa ta'i skad kyis ma non pa la song zhig gsungs so/ /rgyal po dang khroms gyes/ dus de'i tshe blon

po chen po mgar gyis mgo byas snye bo rta pa brgya tham pa rgyal po rgya rje btsan po'i pho brang du lhags so/ /dus mnyam du stag gzig nor gyi rgyal po dang / khrom ge sar
dmag gi rgyal po dang / rgya gar chos kyi rgyal po dang / bod kyi rta pa brgya po thams cad 'dzoms so/ /de nas so so'i mjal ba'i phyag rten rnams phul nas bod kyi blon pos
rgya nag gi blon po la gser gyi bang ba bskur nas/ nged bod kyi rgyal po'i blon po yin pas/ rje lha gcig dang mjal ba'i zhu 'phrin bka' shog sgrom bu dang bcas pa yang
yod ces pas/ khong blon po gzhan pas dma' bar byas nas rgyal po dang zhag bdun du ma mjal lo/ /de nas mjal ba'i tshe blon po mgar gyis sna drangs pa'i blon po rnams kyis
phyag gral byas/ blon po mgar gyis dong rtse bdun phyag rten du phul/ rgyal po la phyag dang zhe sa dang rdzogs par phul te rgyal po'i mdun du baiDUrya'i rmog bzhag ste/
lo tsA ba bar du bcug nas zhus pa/ rje lags/ bdag cag mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i blon po lags/ rin po che baiDUrya'i rmog 'di gon nas g.yul du zhugs na
g.yul las rnam par rgyal bar 'gyur/ nad yams byung pa'i tshe na 'di gon nas grong khyer gyi mtha' bskor na nad yams chad nus/ lo nyes kyis dogs pa'i tshe yang 'di gon nas
zhing mtha' bskor na lo legs par 'ong / ngo mtshar bas 'dzam bu'i gling na rin thang gzhal du med pa 'di rje la 'bul bar bgyi/ nor bu chu shel 'di yang lha gcig gi rin
du 'bul/ lha gcig 'phrul gyi kong jo bdag cag mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po'i btsun mor gnang bar zhu zhus pa la/ rgyal po 'khor dang bcas pa bzhad gad byed do/ /der rgyal po
na re/ khyed mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po spobs pa re mtho/ nga sangs rgyas 'od srungs nas rgyal po'i rgyud pa rgyun ma chad pa yin la/ nga la chos khrims dar gyi mdun pa 'dra
ba yang yod/ rgyal khrims gser gyi gnya' shing 'dra ba yang nga la yod/ khyed nga'i gnyen zla ma yin/ 'on kyang sa thag ring po nas yong zin pa yar song la khyed rang
gis rgyal po la dris/ rgyal po bya ba la chos dge ba bcu'i khrims dgos pa yin/ khyod bod la khrims med pas bod kyis chos dge ba bcu'i khrims bca' nus sam/ de 'cha' 'dod na
lha gcig sbyin/ mi nus na mi ster bas dris las shog gsungs pas/ slar yang blon pos phyag byas/ rje lha gcig lags/ nged 'phrin re re la rgya nag dang bod la yar 'gro mar
'gro byas na lha gcig spyan 'dren pa'i dus mi 'ong / nged cag gi rgyal pos bka' shog sgrom bu 'di bskur ba lags/ 'di gzigs su gsol zhes bka' shog sgrom bu phyag tu phul
lo/ /rgyal pos kha phye nas gzigs pas/ rgya nag stong 'khun gyi yi ge mthing shog la gser gyis bris nas/ mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgom pos/ rgyal nag rgyal po
seng ge btsan pa la bka' bstsal pa/ lha gcig btsun mo kong jo 'di nga'i btsun mor phul zhig khyed nged la khrims med pa la snyad byed na/ ngas sprul pa'i mi mang po sprul
nas bod yul du chos dge ba bcu la brten pa'i khrims nyi ma gcig la bca' bar bya yi de ltar byas kyang lha gcig mi ster na ngas dmag dpag tu maid pa sprul la khyed kyi rgyal
khams thams cad 'joms par 'gyur ro bya ba'i yi ge 'dug nas/ rgya nag rgyal po skrag cing dngas te 'on kyang

rgyal po thugs zab pas da dung blon po la/ khyed kyi rgyal pos nged la sdigs re gtong bar 'dug ste des mi phan/ rgyal po yod pa'i dus na chos dar dgos pas de la dkon mchog
gsum gyi rten dgos/ de bzhugs pa'i lha khang dgos pas khyed la med pas/ bod du gtsug lag khang brtsig nus pa yod dam/ de nus na ngas lha gcig sbyin te/ mi nus na mi ster
gyis la dris las shog gsungs pas/ blon po mgar gyis yang phyag byas te rje lags/ de la rgya nag dang bod bar sa thag ring po la 'phrin gcig la phar skyel tshur skyel byas
na lha gcig kong jo gdan 'drongs pa'i dus mi 'ong / de'i lan du bka' shog sgrom bu 'di bskur ba lags zhes sgrom bu phyag tu phul ba phye ste gzigs pas/ sngar ltar yi ge
byung bas khyed nga la gtsug lag khang med zer nas snyad byed na/ ngas sprul pa'i bzo bo bsam gyis mi khyab pa sprul la bod yul du lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs te
sgo thams cad rgya yi yul la gtad la bzhag bya ba byung / de ltar ma yin pa nga la lha gcig mi ster na/ ngas sprul pa'i dmag mi dpag tu med pa sprul la khyed kyi yul thams
cad gzhom pham byas ba byung nas/ rgyal po bred nas blon po rnams kyis brten te pho brang du gshegs so/ /phyi nas rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la/ bu mo mthar bod la gtang dgos
par 'dug snyam ste/ rgyal po dang / rgyal mo dang / rgyal bu dang / (lha gcig)tsho tshogs nas rgyal blon tsho gros byas pas/ yab na re/ rgya gar chos kyi 'byung sa yin
pas rgya gar chos kyi rgyal po la byin zer/ yum na re/ rgya gar la longs spyod med sprang po dang 'dra bas longs spyod dgos te/ stag gzig nor gyi rgyal por ster zer ro/
/ming po na re/ srid dgos pas khrom ge sar dmag gi rgyal po la sbyin zer/ lha gcig kong jo rang byad bzhin legs pa la dga' bas nga khrom la 'gro zer ro/ /de yang khrom gyi
rgyal po shin tu legs pas de la mo chags nas yong du re bas rgyal po la yang de bzhin du yod do/ /de'i blon po rnams na re/ bod la kong jo mi ster zer ro bod kyis rgya'i
gyen po thams cad bsad pa yin zer ro/ /bod la mos pa dang dga' ba gang yang med kyang khrims kyis nye ring byar mi btub pas/ rgyal pos nga'i lha gcig 'di khyed mi rigs
bzhi'i blon po rig pa gang rno ba la ster gsungs pas/ der rig pa 'gran du bcug pa las/ rgya'i rgyal po rje seng ge gtsan pa la g.yu bre zhabs tsam g.yu zhags 'khyil ba bya
ba yod pa de la dar thag sus tshud pa la lha gcig ster bas sus tshud 'gran pa las/ gzhan rnams kyis nyi ma mang por thabs ci byas kyang ma tshud pas/ khong tsho dbang
dang nor yang che/ rgyal po yang khong tsho la dga' yang thabs rdugs nas ma tshud do zhes/ der bod kyi blon po'i lag tu g.yu zhags 'khyil ba gtad pa las/ bod kyi blon po
mgar stong btsan yul bzung gis rgya'i grog ma che ba gcig bzung nas de zan gyis gsos te/ nyi ma tsha po la grog ma'i sked pa la dar skud btags te/ de la dar gyi thi gu btags/
de la dar yug btags nas mig nang phar dal bus phus btab palas phar ngos kyi g.yu'i mig nang rwa co snyong ste byung bas der thag pa je sbom thon te dar yug 'then nas
thag pa tshud pas/ g.yu'i thag pa nged kyis tshud pas nged la lha gcig ster dgos byas kyang ma ster/ da bya

ba bu brgya ngos sus shes pa la lha gcig ster ro zer bas shes kyang ma byin/ shing gzhog gru bzhi po rtse mo dang rtsa ba ngos zin pa la lha gcig ster zer ba la ngos zin yang
ma ster/ yang khang bzang bzhir g.yog mo bzhi bskos/ snye bo mi rair lug re/ cha tshos re drangs nas 'di rnams nyin re la bza' ba zin pa/ lpags pa mnyed tshar ba/ chang
'thung sus tshar ba la lha gcig ster zer bas gzhan rnams kyis sha dus gcig la yog zas byas/ chang yang btung byas kyang sha la sun nas bzas ma tshar/ chang gis kyang bzi
nas 'thung ma tshar ba las/ blon po mgar gyis gral rim gyis sha kham re zo/ chang hub re byas nas rim gyis btung bas sha yang bzas tshar/ chang yang btung tshar/ rje chang
gis ma bzi ba dang / sha rnams legs par zos zin/ pags pa yang gral rim gyis mnyed tshar bas/ lha gcig nged la ster dgos byas pas/ der rgyal pos bod la lha gcig bkas gnang
ba las/ nged la lha gcig mi ster zer bas/ stag gcig na re/ nged la mi ster na yul mes bsreta zer/ khrom na re/ nged la lha gcig mi ster na yul du chu 'dren zer/ de la
sogs pa'i 'phrul 'gran pas sus kyang bod kyi blon pa'i rig pa ma thub po/ /da nged la lha gcig zhu byas pas nub gcig gi tshe rnga zhig brdungs pa dang snye bo rnams la
spyod lam ston pa'i g.yog mo rnams na re/ rgyal po'i pho brang du snye bo rnams la shog bya ba'i rnga yin pas da chas zer/ der snye bo rnams rgyugs nas song ste/ bod kyi
blon po'i bsam pa la rnga 'di skyon can zhig yin snyam nas kho rang gi 'dug sa'i sgo yi ya them la mtshal gyis rdo rje gcig bris/ ma them la g.yung drung ris gcig bris te
sgo rnams bgrangs shing song / sgo re la mtshan ma re btab ste phyin no/ rgyal po'i pho brang du phyin pa'i tshe dga' ston chen po gnang nas thams cad bzi ba dang / rgyal
po na re/ da rgya srang ma 'dzol bar phyin pa la lha gcig ster zer nas/ der blon po gzhan rnams chang gis bzi ba dang sgo 'chol te ma rnyed do/ /de nas blon mgar gyis bod
rnams khrid nas me sgron btegs te mtshan ma btab pa lta bzhin phyin pas/ rang gi khyim du tshud de mal du nyal yod pas/ phyi nyin nangs par blta bar btang bas gzhan rnams
kyi 'dzol nas lam yang ma rnyed par srang bar thams cad du nyal nas bsdad 'dug bod kyi blon pos khang pa ma 'dzol bar rnyed 'dug pas/ lha gcig bkas gnang 'tshal byas
pas/ rgyal pos da lha gcig kong jo bu mo brgya'i khrod du bcug la sus ngo shes pa de la ster ro ngos zungs shig gsungs pa la/ sngar gyi rnams ma nor bar byung ngo / /de nas
bod kyi blon po rig pa can des/ kong jo'i sngar nas kyi g.yog mo gcig yod pa la ci za ba'i phyed phyed byin te/ gzhan yang rngan pa phag tu byin nas sems bzung ba dang
/ sang kog jo bu mo brgya'i khrod du yong bar yod pas de khyod kyis nga la ma nor ston dgos byas pas/ 'bras kyi sog ma ske la byugs te chad pa yong bya ba'i brda' byas/
blon pos khyed la chad pa mi yong ba'i thabs yod bya ba'i brda byas pas/ de ltar yod na smra ba'i 'dzum byas te/ de nas blon po mgar gyis sgyed bu gsum gyi steng du zangs
chus bkang ba de kha bcad de rba bar g.yog mo bcug lcags kyi se ru'i nang nas mar smrar bcug pa/ kong jo la

g.yog bcu drug yod pa'i smra mkhas dam pa nga yin no/ /khyed bod dang las 'brel yod pas kong jo thob ste yong / bu mo lnga brgya song ba las phyed sum brgya song ba'i bar nas
'ong / cha lugs bzang ngan 'bring po tsam zhig yod de/ sha mdangs bag tsam sngo ba lus las tsan dan gyi dri zhim 'thul ba/ kha nas uta?pal gyi dri yang bro/ ha cang mi
ring mi thung ba/ ha cang mi skam mi rgyagags/ mdzangs shing legs la/ 'dzum mdangs che/ gom 'gros dal la sa chod che/ ha cang mi nag mi sngo la/ ha cang mi snga mi dmar
ba/ so tshags dam la so zho dkar/ rnyil mdung ring la rnyil khugags dmar/ mig dpangs dma' la mig rgyang ring / dpral ba'i dkyil na g.yung drung ris/ bkra shis phyag rgya
nas tsam yod/ mkhur tshos g.yas par pad ma ris/ mkhur tshos g.yon mar 'khor lo ris/ lkog ma'i dkyil na dpal be'u ris/ gdong pa g.yon pa'i gong rim na/ mtshal gyi g.yung drung
nas tsam yod/ lha mo klu mo yin pa'i rtags/ /g.ya yi sbrang ma khyad par can/ /bzhin la 'khor zhing yod pa yin/ /de ni lha gcig kong jo yin/ /khyed rang mda' bya rgod
ma gcig la dar leb rgan dmar lapo btags te lag pal ma 'ju bar na bza'i gong pa nas mda' ltong gis sgril la zungs shig zer ro/ /sang nangs par bu mo lnga brgya lam nas byung
/ snye bo tshan pa bzhi po yang sgo na bsgugs so/ /bod gzhan rnams khang bzang na yod do/ /blon po mgar gyis sgo yi rgyab nas mda' bya rgod ma bzung zhing thogs te nga
ni ltad mo blta'o zer te bsdad/ de nas bu mo phyed sum brgya po grangs ma nor bar brtsis nas bar na yar byon pa'i na bza'i gong ba nas mda' stong gis sgril zhing bzung
nas phyir 'then pas/ zhal phyir log byas te he zer ba'i zhal nas uta?pal gyi dri bro ba/ rtags dang mtshan ma rnams ji ltar zer ba zhin 'dug go/ /skra 'dab slog pas g.yung
drung ris kyang 'dug go/ /khang bzang du gdan drangs so/ /snye bo gzhan gsum po rnams kyis bu mo gzugs bzang ba/ kha byad legs pa dang / sha mdangs che ba/ gos gang bzang
/ rgyan gang legs rnams sus zin zin gyis thob sha byas nas khang par khrid do/ /kong jo ngas thob ngas thob zer zhing dga' ston so sor byas so/ /rgya rje'i thugs dgongs
la nga'i bu mo sus thob snyam nas gzigs su byon pas/ kong jo bod kyi khang bzang na 'dug pas 'di mi srid de smra mchu ba yod pas/ de mtshang che bas ngos bzung bar gros
byas pas spor thang sum brgya bting nas brtsis te ngos bzung ba la/ smra mkhan ni ri gsum gyi kha ba mtsho zhig yod pa/ de'i kha na thang zhig yod pa/ de'i steng na lus
po mig gis khengs pa mchu lcags kyis byas pa zhig gis smras so bya ba byung ba dang / 'di 'dra mi srid zer te spor thang sum brgya po mes bsregs so/ da lta rgya nag gi rtsis
drug bu skor yin no/ /yab kyi lha gcig kong jo la khyod mtha' 'khob rgyal po la ster dgos byas pas/ der kong jos yab la zhus pa/ kye ma yab gcig rgyal po gson/ /bod
kyi yul du bdag mchi na/ /kha ba can gyi sa phyogs de/ /grang la bser bus bsil bag che/ /lha klu 'dre srin gdug pa mang / /gangs ri gcan gzan mche ba 'dra/ /brag ri 'brong
po'i ru ltar 'dra/ /nyams mi dga' zhing bag mi gro/ /'bru chen mi 'khrungs mu ge'i sa/ /gdol pa sha zan byol

song rigs/ /spyod pa rtsing bas kla klo'i mi/ /mi grung bsrun srin po'i spyod pa mtshungs/ /mtha' 'khob ston pas zhabs ma bcags/ /'khor bzhi med pas rigs ngan yul/ /chos med
ma rig mun pa'i gling / /mchod pa'i rten dang gnas med pas/ bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing ma mchis/ /de 'dra'i yul du 'gro dgos na/ /yab kyi mchod gnas yi dam lha/ /shAkya
mu ne bdag la zhu/ /kha ba can ni bkres dbul yul/ /rin chen bang mdzod bdag la zhu/ /kha ba can ni grang la bsil/ /tshe gcig thub pa'i gos shig zhu/ /bod kyi mi ni mi grung
ste/ /rtsing spyod che bas spyod bag med/ /g.yog mo lnga brgya bdag la zhu/ /de lta'i mi lus yul phyogs der/ /mgo nag mi rnams 'dul byed du/ /bdag gi sems bskyed ji ltar
bgyi/ /yab kyis bdag la bka' bstsal zhu/ /zhes kong jos zhu tshig zhus pa las/ yab rgyal pos gsungs pa/ kye ma bu mo bdag la gson/ /bod ces kha ba can gyi yul/ /yul khams
khyad 'phags de yin no/ /gangs ri rang byung mtho ba'i gnas/ /mtsho bzhi g.yu'i maNDal 'dra/ /thang bzhi mchod pa bshams pa 'dra/ /chu bzhi yul gsum rang bzhin can/ /ri
mtha sa gtsang gangs ri'i ljongs/ /bkra shis nyams dga' g.yung drung bris pa 'dra/ /rgyal khams gzhan na mis rje byed pas ngo mtshar chung / /bod yul mi rje lhas byed
ngo mtshar che/ /mtha' bzhi'i rgyal po kun gyis legs par 'khur/ /chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po der/ /byang chung sems dpa'i sprul pa mi drug ldan/ /yon tan dpag tu
med pa'i rgyal po ni/ /'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po nyid dang mtshungs/ /khong gi mdzad spyod rgya chen mnga' bas na/ /bod khams kun kyang yul du gyur po yi/ /dge slong
dge 'dun dge bsnyen pha ma kun/ /khyed rang nyid kyis gsog par byas pas chog /de ltar yin pas bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing / /bdag gi mchod gnas shAkya mu ne 'di/ /sangs
rgyas ston pa'i zhal skyin yin pas na/ /sangs rgyas nyid dang khyad par med par gsungs/ /gang zhig gus dang dad pas kun blangs nas/ /sems can kun la byams dang snying rje
yis/ /de dag du:kha las sgrol bya ba'i phyir/ /bla med byang chub thob par bya ba'i phyir/ /rten mchog 'di la mos shing mchod byed na/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i grong khyer rab
zhugs te/ /dgra bcom rang rgyal thob par the tshom med/ /srid pa'i nyon mongs las dang bral bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig ngan 'gro srid pa'i sdug bsngal yongs su bcad byas nas/
/bde 'gro mtho ris thob par rgyal bas gsungs/ /gang zhig 'jig rten bde bar 'gro 'dod cing / /phyag 'tshal mchod pa phul zhing gsol btab na/ /yid la ji ltar bsam bzhin 'byung
'gyur ro/ /mi mthun gnod pa ma lus zhi bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig 'di la dad pas phyag 'tshal lam/ /shin tu gus pas mchod par byed pa dang / /lta zhing skor bar byed pa
thams cad kun/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni myur du thob par 'gyur/ /de phyir dad dang gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /de ltar yon tan khyad par can ldan pa/ /bdag gi mchod gnas snying
dang 'dra ba yang / /bu mo khyod la brtse bas bdag gis brdzang / /rin chen bang mdzod mang po dbyig gi gter/ /bdag gi gces pa'i rin chen gter chen yang / /brtse ba'i bu
mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /'phra men 'phrul zhal nyi zlas brgyan pa yang / /mdzes pa'i

bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /gser g.yu brtsegs pa'i yi ge chen po yang / /gtsug lag rtsis kyi yig cha sum brgya drug cu yang / /longs spyod rdzas kyi gser spyad dngul
spyad kyang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /zas kyi sbyor kha sum brgya drug cu yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /btung ba chang gi
sbyor thabs mang pa yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /sra ba go cha'i gon pa sum brgya yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /rno ba mtshon
gyi brdung thabs sum brgya rnams/ /rgyal po srog srid bsrung phyir bu mo khyod la brdzang / /gdags pa rgyan gyi rnam pa sum brgya dang / /gser sga g.yu sga 'khor can
la sogs pa/ /rgyal po rgyal srid mdzes par bya ba'i phyir/ /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /za 'og stan thul seng ge bya brgyad ma/ /nyi zla 'ja' mtshon ri
dwags bkra ba dang / /ljon shing shing lo nor bu'i ris su bris/ /rgyal po ngo mtshar bskyed phyir bu mo khyod la brdzang / /de ltar ngo mtshar che ba'i 'phrul cha sna tshogs
dang / /gtsug lag khang khrims bcu bzhi bcad pa'i thabs/ /tshig gi mdzod dang yi ge'i gter tshogs dang / /tshig gi phul dang tsam ka la sogs dang / /lugs kyi bstan bcos
mang po khyod la brdzang / /so tshigs sa yi 'dul thabs yi ge'i tshogs/ /legs sbyor spyod pa la sogs mang po dang / /bzhon she rdzi'u skyong phyugs kyi spel thabs dang
/ /grangs dang rtsis dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams dang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /rgya'i gab rtse sum brgya drug cu po/ /legs nyes ston pa'i las kyi me
long yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /so nam sna bzhi 'phrul gyi bya thabs sum brgya dang / /shing 'thag chu 'thag 'phrul gyi skor thabs dang / /thags
ran sgrim thabs 'phrul 'khor mang po dang / /'khar 'phar chen bya brgya ri mo me tog dang / /bya ris sprin gyis brgyan pa'i ldum ris dang / /thags kyi brnams snam pa
g.yu drung 'khor lo ris/ /pad ma stong ldan gsang chen rin chen 'ja' ba ris/ /thags skas len thabs khyung dang g.yu 'brug dang / /'phrul cha rnam pa sna tshogs kyang / /brtse
ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /bzo'i btsem thabs khyad par sum brgya dang / /bkod pa'i khyad par drug bu tham pa yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis
brdzang / /nad rnams bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi zhi ba'i sman/ /brtag pa brgyad dang spyad lnga sbyong drug dang / /sbyor sde bzhi dang sbyar thabs sum brgya yang / /brtse ba'i
