bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /nyon mongs brgyad khri bzhi stong zhi byed cing / /yon tan rgya mtsho ma lus rgyas byed pa'i/ /mdo sde rgyud sde mang po'i gsung rab dang
/ /mi dge bcu spangs dge bcu spyod pa yi/ /bstan bcos rig pa'i tshogs rnams mang po yang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /rol mo rtsed 'jo thag rgyug
gar mkhan dang / /sil khrol sil snyan dril bu cong rnams dang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /pi wang rgyud mang har chung snyan pa'i sgra/ /rtsed 'jo rol
mo mang po sna tshogs dang / /der gting mar me'i spar thabs dang / /chos yang reng bu spos kyi sbyor thabs

dang / /brtse ba'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzang / /de nas sang nangs par kong jos g.yog mo dam pa bzhi khrid nas pho brang du rgyal po la phyag byas so/ /blon po rnams kyis
lha gcig kong jo la phyag byas te gshegs par zhu 'tshal byas pas/ lha gcig kong jo'i zhal nas blon po rnams la gsungs pa/ blon po rnams la nga bod du 'gro ba la shing
se ba yod dam/ rtsa gres ma yod dam/ sa kham pa yod dam/ sngo lo ma yod dam/ rdo bzo nyan yod dam/ yon tan slob pa yod dam gsungs pas/ blon pos de rnams 'dug zhus pas/ 'o
na so nam byar rung gsungs te dges so/ /me tog dang rgya spos dang nyung ma'i gzhi dang / tsong sgog rnams gzhi bsnams nas byon/ jo bo shAkya mu ne shing rta'i steng du
bzhugs su gsol/ de'i phyi tshur lha gcig g.yog mo dam pa rnams dang byon no/ /de'i zebs sga'i sna dre'u dkar mo gnyis kyis 'then/ de'i phyi na g.yog mo rnams dang rol mo
pi wang dang bkod pa mang palo glu len rol mo byed/ bod kyi blon pos mtha' bskor nas shing rta dang / rta dang / dre'u dang / rnga mong dang / bong bu dang / glang gis 'then
te rdzongs dang bcas nas byon no/ /lha gcig gi 'khor na gyad pa dpa' bo lo nyi shu rtsa lnga lon pa lnga brgya dang / rigs bzang gi bu mo lo bcu drug lon pa lnga brgya
ste tsho dang bcas pa btang ngo / /de yang skar ma nabs so shar ba'i dus la babs pa na/ mkhar gyi phyir chas nas byon/ nyi ma shar ba tsam la gar slebs sar bsdad de thang
bde ba dang / shing dang me tog gi shing rtsa'i bsil grib la za 'og gi lding phub/ rin po che'i khri brtsigs pa'i steng du jo bo shAkya bzhugs/ de'i drung du lha gcig
gis g.yog mo dam pa bzhi dang / lha rol dang bcas nas jo bo la bsang bu 'dren/ lha gcig kyang bsang bu gsol/ se tog dang me tog mang pos mchod pa 'bul/ rnam dag sku lnga
mchog tu gzugs bzang ba/ /zhes bstod pa byed/ de tshar nas bsang bu'i lhag ma rnams g.yog pho mo dang blon po rnams za/ bod kyi blon palo rnams zas sna tshogs zos te/ glu
gar la sogs longs spyod byed/ la la ni mdun ma byed/ la la ni gyad stobs 'gran/ la la ni sho rtse/ la la ni khran rtse/ la la ni bod du 'di tshod tsam na slebs re dga'
zer zhing yong ngo / /slon po mgar ni bod blon gyi mi tshab tu bzhag der rgyal po rig pa che bas mgar mi gcig phung zer ba byung ngo / /rgyal pos mi skyin du bzhag nas/ blon
po rig pa can 'di'i rgyud 'dra 'phel lam zer nas rgya mo rigs bzang ma gcig grogs kyi dam par gnang ngo / /de ltar byas kyang blon po chen po rigs rgyud 'phel gyis dogs
nas 'brel bar ma gyur to/ /de nas blon pos thabs byas te zas ci byin pa ma zos par shin tu lus ngan par gyur/ nyi ma la rtag tu bsdad pas sha sngo bar gyur/ 'khur ba g.yas
dang g.yon du mtshal dang rams bcug te bsres nas lud pa bor bas lud pa sngon dmar du byung ngo / /mal 'og sa'i 'og ko rlon bting pa'i khar gdan bting pa la nyal bas
dri ma rgya mos tshor bar gyur/ blon po chen po sku lus dri mi zhim pa bro ba ci yin zer/ blon po na re/ nga la rgya'i tshad pa'i nad byung ba ma tshor ram zer/ der nyin
gcig tsam na rgyal po byon nas blon po chen po la nad byung ngam/ cu zhig bder song na 'o skol 'dun ma bya rgyu

mang po yod gsungs/ rje lags zhe sa zhu 'tshal/ bro 'tshal zhing gda' byas pas/ rgyal pos blon po de mi thub gzigs nas/ der lud pa bskyur ba yang rnag khrag tu byung / dri
mi zhim par song / tho phyi na yang rnag can gyi lud pa bskyur ba skam po mang pa gzigs/ rgyal po de blon po zhi dogs nas/ sang nangs par rgya nag na mkhas pa'i sman pa gsum
pos nas rtsa bstan pa la/ blon po'i zhal nas rgya mo khyod do nub khyim gzhan du nyol/ 'o cag lhan cig tu nyal na bud med bya ba dri ma che bas/ sang nangs par lha rje
rtsa lta ba mi mngon/ de ltar byung na/ sman pas dpyad log byas nas nga shi na khyod la yug za yong zer nas sgor bton/ gcan lpags la mal zlum lapo mthon po byas nas nang
logs thams cad srin bal gyis bkab ste mtshan mo der tshugs tshad nyal ba skyil krung byas shing nyal lo/ /des rtsa thams cad 'khrugs nas nangs par sman pa gsum gyis bltas
tsa na/ rgyal po la rtsa bltas pa'i lung byin pa/ blon po chen po'i snyung nad 'di rlung las gyur ba'i nad brgya rtsa gcig kya ma yin/ de bzhin mkhris pa las gyur pa yang
ma yin/ ban kan yang ma yin/ 'dus lapa las gyur pa brgya rtsa gcig kyang ma yin/ bgegs rigs stog phrag brgyad cu dang byis pa'i gdon chen bco lnga yang mi gnod/ de ma
yin pa'i nad tshabs chen po zhig 'dug ste nged rnams kyis bcos mi shes zer ro/ /der blon po rig pa tsan gyis shes te 'ong snyam nas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ blon po chen po
khyod rig pa can yin na khyod kyi nad 'di rang ci yin par 'dug ces dris pas/ 'di gzhan ma yin/ bod kyi lha gnyan ma dga' ba yin no zer/ 'o na cis phan dris pas gto byas
na phan zer bas/ de la yas thabs ci dgos byas pas/ rta mog ro mgo dmar gcig dang / za 'og gi thal ba sgro ba gang / lug gi mtsher khrag grod pal gang / sol pa'i mdung sing
gang chag med pa 'dom gsum/ mda' gsum/ khru gsum byas pa zhig dgos zer nas der nags ri thams cad bsregs te sol bar btang yang sol ba'i mdung shing ser ka med pa ma byung
/ dar zab thams cad bsregs kyang thal ba sgro ba gang ma byung / lug thams cad bsad kyang mtsher khrag grod pa gang ma byung / lug thams cad bsad kyang mtsher khrag grod
pa gang ma byung / de rnams gang te rnyed pa byung na yang rta mog ro mgo dmar ma rnyed pas/ der blon po na re/ lar nga 'chi zer ro/ nad 'drir byung ba la/ khyed rang snying
na sar skyol cig nga zhag bdun nas 'chi yi/ 'chi sar ltas ngan sna tshogs 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i mthus rgyal khams su mi phyugs thams cad nyes par 'gyur ro byas
pas/ der rgyal pos blon po shi dogs nas 'di skad gsungs so/ /blon po chen po khyed rig pa che ba yin pas nad 'dir phan pa'i thabs ci yod gsungs so/ /blon po na re/ lha nad
yin pas bod kyi ri mthong sar lha gsol na zhes zhus pas/ der rgyal po blon po shi dogs nas rta mtshal bu rngo nag la bskyon nas mdo smad tsong khar lha gsol du btang ngo
/ /blon po bod du shor gyis dogs nas gyad mi bzhi sku srung la btang / yar 'gro khar rgyal pos blon po la khyed rig pa can yin pas/ so nam gyi lugs ji ltar byas na bzang
gsungs pas/ sa bon spu ser tsam gyis la thob dang snye ma grung la legs pa smin sla ba 'ong byas pas/ khrims

kyi rnga brdungs nas zhing la sa bon thams cad spu ser tsam byas nas btab pas 'ong / de bzhin mi byed na chad pa gcod do byas pas/ rgya'i rgyal khams thams cad kyis blon po
rig can gyi kha ta byas pa bden nam bsam pa dang / rgyal khrims btsan pas thams cad kyis sa bon brngos nas btab/ de nas rgya nag gis bod kyi blon po yar btang lam du zhugs
nas/ gyad mi bzhi po la zas cung zad tsam las ma byin par khrid de rgya mo tsha ba'i rong du slebs pa dang / de'i tshe rgya yi stobs can bzhi po la chang mang po myos
myos blud nas ri la phyin tsa na rta rnams kyi rmig pa la skyon byas so/ /rta mog ro mgo dmar de gzhan gyi rta bang gis mi slebs pa yin pas/ de bzhon nas khong bzhi la chu
gtor dgra byung longs byas pas/ khong bzhis tho me tho me langs tsa na lcag brgyab shad kyis song ba dang / khong bzhi po na re/ bod kyi blon po chen po de 'dra byed pa
sngar nas dogs dogs pa der byas so/ /'o skol rnams log na ni rgyal pos chad pa gcod pas blonapo de rang gi phyir 'brangs zer nas song / blon pos kyang mi nye mi ring bar
khrid nas phyin tsa na/ lha gcig gi 'khor dang blon po mgar gyi srung ma las bod kyi mi'i rus rgya yin tshad de rnams las gyes pa yin no/ /der shul du rgya nag gi ljang
pa skyes pa na shin tu bzang bar byung ba la/ ston du song tsa na snye ma long bar song nas/ gcig na re/ bod kyi blon pos gdug pa byas pa 'dra/ snye ma thams can long bar
song 'dug zer/ der rgya thams cad kyis dar zab kyang rabs bcad/ shing thams cad kyang bsregs/ lug thams cad kyang bsad/ shAkya mu ne yang lha gcig gis khyer bas bod kyi
blon pos rgya'i yul khams thams cad phung bar byas so/ /zhes gleng bas gcig gis gcig tu brgyud nas rgyal po'i snyan song ngo / /rgyal po'i bsam pa la bden nam snyam nas/
ngan pa de bod song ba yin ded cig gsungs pas/ rta pa mang po 'ded du btang ngo / /blon pos nyin gcig mtsher rnying pa zhig nas gyad pa mi bzhi sbangs skam po 'thu ru bcug
nas gtsang po la bskyur bas rgya'i ded mis chu'i nang nas sbangs byung ba mthong bas/ der slebs kyang phan med kho la bsu ba'i dmag mang po byung bas rab la brgal ba'i
sar rta'i sbangs btang ba yang 'di tsam byung zer ro/ /gcig na re/ da dung ded cig zer nas bdas tsa na/ yang blon pos rta lcag gi rgyu'i spa nags dang 'phrad nas spa mang
po bcad de lcags mang pa byas nas chu la bskur bas/ rgya'i ded mis mthong nas 'o skol rnams kyis kho'i rjes slebs kyang phan med/ rta lcag chu la lhung ba yang 'di tsam
'dug pa la 'o skol thams cad thabs kyis khrid 'gro/ log pa legs zer nas mar log go/ /de nas blon po yang byon tsa na/ kong jo dpon g.yog nam zla dbyar kha'i nyi ma dros pa'i
dus su spang thang bde mo me tog khra yal le ba la/ dar dkar gyi gur phub/ rin po che'i khri bshams/ za 'og gi 'bol bting / lha shAkya mu ne gser khri la bzhugs/ de'i
drung du kong jos 'bras chang lhung bzed bkang nas/ mchod pa mang pa 'bul zhing me tog dang / bdug spos kyis mchos nas dngul gyi pi wang gi rgyud la brten nas bstod pa/
rnam dag sku lnga mchog tu gzugs bzang ba/ /ye shes rgya mtsho gser gyi ri bo 'dra/ /grags pa 'jig rten gsum

na lham me ba/ /mgon po mchog khyod la ni gus phyag 'tshal/ /ces bstod pa phul/ de nas lha gcig la bsang bu 'dren/ de'i lhag ma rnams g.yog mo rnams pham pham byed do/ /de
nas sgang bu shin tu mtho sa nas bltas tsa na/ gyad khal dang bcas pa slebs te/ la la ni phyag byed/ la la ni bstod pa byed/ la la ni rtsed dga' ste 'dod pa'i longs spyod
la longs spyod/ tshul de lta bus snga dro re la nyin lam bcu drug re gcod cing 'ongs so/ /der blon po mgar gyis nag shod du kong jo chas pa'i rjes slebs te/ dga' ston chen
po yang byas so/ /kong jo la blon po mgar gyi bu chags pas rgyal mo 'phrang lam 'chos shing dus 'gor zer ba sogs su gyur bya ba dang / sha ba la zhing rmod pa dang / glang
bu ngu thang du dus 'gor bar yang gyur to/ /shAkya mu nes bod kyi sa gzhi thams cad zhabs kyis bcags so/ /de nas rgyal po la pho nya bsrings nas rgya mo kong jo yang
gdan 'drongs nas yod/ gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne yang gdan 'drongs nas yod do/ gyad mi brgyad kyang yod bya ba'i pho nya ba bsrings nas/ bsu ba'i bkod pa dang lam 'phrang
yang legs par 'chos shig byas pas/ grong khyer ba rnams kyis shar phyogs mgar sna'i gdong du lam 'chos shig par bka' bstsal to/ /yang kong jo dang lha shAkya mu ne lho phyogs
nas 'ong bas/ grong khyer ba kun gyis lho bse sgrom gyi lam 'chos shig par bka' bstsal to/ /yang kong jo dang lha shAkya mu ne nub phyogs nas 'ong bas/ grong khyer
ba kun gyis nub phyogs dan 'bag nas lam 'chos shig ces bka' bstsal to/ /yang kong jo dang lha shAkya mu ne byang phyogs nas 'ong bas/ grong khyer ba kun gyis byang phyogs
sgo phug nas lam 'chos shig par bka' bstsal to/ /de nas yang phyogs bzhi ka nas kong jo dang lha shAkya mu ne byon par gyur to/ /shar phyogs rgya mo rab kha bya bar thogs/
lho phyogs bse sgrom gyi phu na 'khyags pa yod pas de la kong jo na re/ 'di dung dkar g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra zer/ nub phyogs phag sna'i gdong du sa sgo bye ba dang /
gnam sgo bye ba la mgon po mched lcam dral rdo la 'bur du dod pa yod zer ro/ /byang lha bsu gdong na bus ba byed pa yang gnang / lha sa'i nags kyi gseb ne chung gi stod na
chu mig gi 'dam du shing rta bying ba dang / gyad lha dgas sku btegs/ klu dgas shing rta btegs te 'dam nas bton pas/ shing rta 'gul bar ma nus so/ /bskyod par ga la nus/
gyad gnyis ngal sos nas gyad lha dgas sku btegs pas 'gul bar ma nus bskyod par ga la nus so/ /gyad lha dga' dang klu dga' gnyis ka log nas btegs pas kyang sku de shin tu
lci bar gyur nas der bzhugs te sa las bral ma nus so/ /kong jos snyam na 'di ji ltar yin/ ci'i rtags yin snyam te/ spor thang sum brgya'i gab rtse bting nas ju zhag brtsis
pas/ bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams 'di sa gzhi srin mo gan rkyal la 'gyel ba 'dra bar mkhyen/ lha sa'i 'o thang gi mtsho srin mo'i snying khrag tu mkhyen/ sa yul de
ni snying khar mkhyen/ thang 'di'i dkyil na ri bog chad de gnyis snying gi rus pa sems can thams cad kyi srog za ba'i gnod sems su mkhyen/ shar gyi ri sna nub tu zug nub
kyi ri sna shar du zug lho'i ri sna byang du zug byang gi ri sna lhor zug pa de/ mi spyod ngan pa/ sa gzhi thams

cad jag pa'i skye bos gang bar mkhyen/ de bas rgya cher brtsis te gzigs pas/ yul de'i shar na ri pad ma ra ga spungs pa 'dra ba yod/ lho na ri rin po che spungs pa 'dra ba
yod/ nub na ri mchod sdong btsugs pa 'dra ba yod/ byang na ri man ji'i khar dung chos chab kyis bkang ba bzhag pa 'dra ba yod/ de rnams ni sa phyogs der dad pa can gyi skye
bo mang po 'byung zhing 'du bar rang rang gi yon tan 'byungaba'i lung du mkhyen/ der dad pa can gyi skye bo mang po 'byung bas ngang gis dad pa che ba dang / chos byar
rung ba rang bzhin gyis yon tan 'byung ba'i gzhi 'phel zhing rgyas par bya ba'i phyir/ gtsug lag khang zhig bzhengs dgongs par mkhyen/ de la de'i dpyad mdzad pas sa'i dbye
ba sum brgyad dang drug cu/ sa'i dpyad nor re re bdun cu rtsa gsum/ de'i ngos bzung ba dgu bcu tham pa/ ngos bzung pa'i skyon zlog pa/ de'i 'bras bu chud mi za bar byed
pa/ de thams cad kyang bsdus na bzhir 'dus te/ skye bo mang po 'du ba'i sa/ rgyal po'i sa gtan la dbab pa dang / 'phags pa rab tu byung ba'i sa/ gtsug lag khang gi sa gtan
la dbab pa dang drang srong mang po 'byung ba'i gnas/ dgon pa'i sa gtan la dbab pa dang / re zhig bde bar spyod pa'i sa/ skye bo phal po che'i sa gtan la dbab pa'o/ /de
dag las kyang da res dang po gnyis kyi sa gtan la 'bebs te/ de yang yon tan rnam pa brgyad yod pa zhig dgos/ yon tan brgyad yod pa la skyon lnga tsam yang yong / yon tan
brgyad yod pa ni/ gnam 'khor lo rtsims brgyad du yod pa/ sa pad ma 'dab brgyad du yod/ bar bkra shis rtags brgyad kyis brgyan pa'i sa/ ju yag gi lha khang tshangs pa/
rin po che sna lnga yod pa'/ de'i nus pa 'don pa la skyon lnga sel dgos par mkhyen/ skyon lnga ni klu'i pho brang dang / 'dre'i 'dun phung dang / ma mo'i nyal sa dang / btsan
gyi rgyu srang dang / 'byung ba'i sa dgra de rnams rim gyis bzlog pa la/ klu'i pho brang gi khar jo bo shAkya mu nes mnan par mkhyen/ sku'i phyogs bzhir ka ba bzhi btsugs/
de la dar gyi yol ba bres nas gyad pa mi gnyis srung du bcug ste/ kong jo dpon g.yog rnams rgyal po'i pho brang gi shar sgor byon nas/ snye bo rta pa brgya tham pas
sgo ba gnyis la brda sbyar te/ khyed rgyal po'i spyaha sngar song las/ kong jo yang spyan drongs nas yod/ gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne yang spyan drongs nas yod/ dga' ston
chen po yang gyis shig rgyal po yang dga' ston gyi sar spyan 'drongs bya ba'i zhu 'phrin btang ngo / /der sgo bas dga' ston gyi rnga brdungs pas/ skye bo thams cad ci byed
na zer zhing lta/ dga' ston gyi rnga re brdungs pas a re dga'/ kong jo yang byon/ gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne spyan drangs zer nas/ grong khyer gyi mi rnams rgyan thams
cad kyi brgyan nas/ srang ka na phar tshur 'ur rgyangs dang chas nas 'ongs bas/ lha gcig khri btsun pho brang na bzhugs pa'i thugs dgongs la/ 'ur sgra de tsam ci yin snyam
ste gong khar byon te bltas pas/ kong jo dpon g.yog rnams shar sgo na 'dug pa gzigs/ lha sa bye ma'i gling chu mig kha na gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne bzhugs pa mthong ba
dang / 'di snyam du bsams te/ jo bo shAkya mu ne bzhugs pa'i sa ya kir lha khang bya bsam par 'dug ste ngas lha

khang ma brtsigs par mo lha khang rtsig mi gzhug dgos snyam na/ kong jo bos te/ ye kong jo khyod la lha dang dug ste/ lha nga la yang yod/ chen ma yang nga yin/ pho brang chen
po 'di tsam pa ngas brtsigs/ byas pa yang nga che/ ngas lha khang ma brtsigs par khyod kyis lha khang ma rtsigs shig/ ces a nan gyis bos/ kye ma kong jo khyod g.yog 'khor
mang po byas nas byon/ /dka' las byas nas snye bos bkug /tshegs med bod kyi yul du byon/ /nga ni them pa snga brgal yin/ /chen ma che ba che rgyu yin/ /chen ma btsun
pa btsun rgyu yin/ /chen ma gnyan re gnyan rgyu yin/ snga ma mi che mi btsun na/ /snga ma mi dge mi gnyan na/ /'jig rten chos lugs smad par 'gyur/ /de las thab ka nga snga
zhing / /rje'i sku mthong ba nga snga bas/ /nga la sngon du gus par gyis/ /lar ni 'jig rten lugs ltar na/ /slong bar byed na su zhig btsun/ /bran mo byed na su zhig btsun/
/dge bar mi byed su zhig 'khur/ /dam chos byed pa su zhig sdug /dkon mchog mchod pa su zhig 'bul/ /khrungs ma 'thung bar zhig zhim/ /btsun mo yong ba su zhig bzang /
/'on kyang rje la bstod pa la/ bstod pa thams cad 'gran pa yin/ /khyod dang nga gnyis 'gran pa yin/ /dkon mchog dbu 'phangs bstod pa 'gran/ /chos gzhi dkon mchog gsum gyi
gzhi/ /gtsug lag khang rnams bzhengs pa 'gran/ /de'i sa dgra bsub par 'gran/ /mchod gnas gnyis la mchod pa 'gran/ /mar gyi bu 'bangs skyong ba 'gran/ /long sprang sbyin
pa gtong ba 'gran/ /thad kar dkon nor gsog pa 'gran/ /zhing bcu'i so nam bya ba 'gran/ /kha thos tsig thos phan pa med/ /de bas dam chos spyod pa dang / /sdig pa thams cad
bshags pa ni/ dam pas dam chos spyad pa dang / sdig pa rgyab tu dor ba dang / de ltar 'gran par ma nus na/ /khyod kyang rje la re ma che/ /de ltar 'gran la chos skor bzhengs/
/nga ni chen ma yin pas na/ /lha khang sngon la nga rtsig go/ /zhes smras pa dang / kong jo na re/ khyod chen ma yang yin/ byas pa yang che/ grub cog kyang che/ lag
ris kyang che bar gda' yis zer nas/ dngul dkar gyi lcag 'o thang gi mtsho la gtad nas/ khyod 'di bsub nas de'i steng du lha khang rtsigs shig yang kong jos smras pa/ kye
ma khri btsun khyod gson dang / /'khor bar skyes pa'i sems can rnams/ /nad kyi ma gdungs su zhig yod/ /'phongs pa gang gis mthong ma gyur/ /'byor pa rtag tu sa la yod/
/sa steng nor skad su zhig grags/ /grags dang bral na su zhig yong / /su zhig khyim thab kyis ma smras/ /rtag tu rgyal po yod du 'ong / /shing rta'i yul du gang ma gyur/
/skyes nas byung dus su ma gyur/ /skyes bu bder bsam mthar phyin su/ /chen chun 'gran pa su zhig yin/ /de ltar yin na khyod mad de/ /khyod kyi che rgyu btsun rgyu de/ /khyod
la nyan par ngas lta yi/ /khyod kyis che bar shes par gyis/ /khyed la gus par ngas 'dud do/ /'gran pa'i 'gran sems med mod kyi/ /khyod kyis 'gran no zhes smras pa/ /them
pa snga brgal chen ma khyod/ /chos skor lha khang khyod kyis bzhengs/ /nga ni khad mnyam sa la bzhengs/ /chen mas dka' ba byed pas na/ /khyed la de skad bkur bar bya/
/khyed kyis 'gran rgyu de rnams la/ /rang las rang nyid byed pa la/ /de la 'gran rgyu ngas mi mthong / /zhes

gsungs so/ /dngul gyis lcag mtsho la btsugs nas/ khyod kyis lha kha 'dir rtsigs shig zer ro/ /khri btsun gyis kyang lcag jo bo shAkya la gtad nas/ sa thang khad mnyam po ya
gi 'dra ba la ngas kyang 'byongs mchi zer nas khri btsun skyengs te/ kong jo dang rgyal po mjal ba'i skabs ma ster ro/ /de nas blon po rnams kyis thabs byas nas rgyal po
dang kong jo zhal mjal bas/ 'di la snang ba gsum du byung ba ni/ skye bo tha mal pa rnams kyis 'bol brtsigs pa dang / bon po mang pos sna min sna tshogs byed pa dang / sna
sgron pa dang / 'gal ba brgyab pa dang / gdan gcig la bzhugs nas dbu skra sbrel ba dang / mar khu'i skyu brje ba la sogs pa'i snang ba mang pa byung ngo / /byang chub
sems dpa' rnams kyis snang ba la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang / rje btsun ma sgrol ma zhal mjal te/ 'gro ba sems can gyi don chen po byed par gzigs so/ /de
nas khri btsun gyis dngul zam la byon/ rgyal po rtse mkhar la bzhugs pa la bka' bgros so/ /kho mo lha khang gcig brtsig par 'dod na/ rgyal po sa la dbang ba yin pas/ lha
khang gi sa gcig zhu byas pas/ rgyal po'i zhal las/ khyod rang la legs pa gcig tu brtsig pas chog gi rtsigs shig ces gsungs so/ /khri btsun gyis rta pa mang po'i 'khor 'khrid/
gnod sbyin mang po'i 'khor gyis bskor nas/ dol dang / yar lungs sog kha la sogs pa'i yul dga' ba thams cad du lha khang gi rmang bting bas/ nyin mi brtsigs pa nub
mo zhig lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad brtsigs pa rnams zhig par gyur te/ da res ni lha gcig kong jo la gros gci ga'adri dgos/ mo rgya nag pal brtag pa dang / rtsis la mkha
pa yin snyam nas/ g.yog mo dam pa zhig la gser sel ma bre gang bskur nas/ khyod song la lha sa bye ma'i gling ne'u chung chu mig kha na/ dar dkar yol ba'i nang na/ jo bo
shA?kya mu ne'i drung du rgya mo kong jo mchod pa 'bul zhing yod kyi/ der song nas gser 'di phul la/ kha ning gi de 'dra ma zer bar/ da res lha khang brtsig pa'i sa legs
pa zhig ston cig nga'i lha khang 'byongs tsa na khyod kyang lha khang rtsig tu gzhug gi bya ba bsrings so/ /g.yog mos kyang de skad zhus pas/ kong jos kyang sa legs par bstan
no/ /de yang skye bo mang po 'du ba'i gnas 'dir yon tan brgyad yod do/ /'di'i phan yon 'byin pa la skyon lnga bzlog dgos te/ yon tan brgyad po 'di ni/ bkra shis pa'i
rtags brgyad kyis brgyan pa yod de/ gnam 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad kyi 'og sa pad ma 'dab brgyad kyi steng na/ 'phan dkar gyi ri la gdugs 'dra ba yod/ ra ka'i brag la spyan
gsum nya 'dra ba yod/ rdzong btsan gyi brag la bum pa 'dra ba yod/ grib bse sgrom gyi phur dung dkar g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra bas khyab pa yod/ grib mda' yug ma'i zur na
thugs rin po che dpal be'u 'dra ba yod/ shun gyi brag la sku rgyal mtshan 'dra ba yod/ shar rtsibs kyi ri la ljags pad ma kha phye ba'i ri yod/ de'i skyon lnga ni/ lho phyogs
gla ba'i tshal na 'dre'-i ngan phung yod pa de gtor/ lho nub mtshams su btsan gyi rgyu srang yod pa de khog nub byang mtshams kyi brag phug kha lho lta na ma mo'i nyal
sa yod pa de phrogs/ byang phyogs bye ma'i gling du klu'i pho brang yod pas/ de jo bo shAkya mu nes mnan yod

kyi/ gzhan yang 'byung ba'i dgra yod de/ shar phyogs bye ma'i lung stong du srin mo 'doms bzed pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra yod/ der dbang phyug chen po'i ling ga tshugs/ lho phyogs
yug ma'i ri la rus sbal nag po gzan la gzhungs pa 'dra ba yod/ de la bya khyung ga ru Da kha ston/ nub phyogs shun gyi brag bdun nag po bya ra byed pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra
yod/ de'i phyogs su mchod rten bse ru rtsigs/ byang phyogs nya ran nang bran gyi ri la glang po stobs can g.yul la zhugs pa 'dra ba yod de/ de la rdo'i seng ge dkar mo tshugs/
de ltar byas nas dbus 'o thang gi mtsho la/ ra skyes las sa bskyal nas/ mtsho bsrubs te lha khang byas na/ lho'i g.yu 'brug sngon mo dang / byang nub bya phu'i bya
dmar po dang / byang rdo rje'i rus sbal nag po dang / shar bye ma ri'i stag skya bo rnams la nus pa gdod byung / sgo phu'i lcags dang / ra ga'i zangs dang / la rtog gi dngul
dang / lcags ka ri'i gser kyang 'dod 'byung / khyod kyi lha khang yang gdod rtsig tu btub/ kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su legs dgu cog kyang gdod 'byuung / nyes so cog
gi skyon ni 'grib par 'gyur gyi bya ba'i lan bskur ro/ /g.yog mos mgo mjug nor nas/ 'phan yul nas ra la sa bskyal nas mtsho srub bya ba rnam la thos te/ de ltar byas pas
mtsho rnyog ma langs song bas/ kong jos nga la phrag dog byas 'dug snyam ste/ da res rgyal por zhu'o snyam nas/ rtse mkhar du phyin te/ rgyal po chen po lags/ ngas lha
khang gi rmang brgya rtsa brgyad bting bas nub mo zhig nas grub par ma gyur na ji ltar bgyi zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ nga la dri sa yod kyi gsungs so/ /rgyal pos kyang
bu mo bcu drug po mchod pa 'bul du bsgo ba rnams/ lha thugs rje chen po la mchod pa 'bul du bcug nas/ gsol ba btab pa'i rjes la/ tsan dan gyi sku zhabs g.yas pa las/ 'od
zer zhig byung nas/ 'o thang gi mtsho la phog go/ sang nangs par na ma re la/ rgyal po'i chibs 'chag pa'i shar phyogs gru do'i bar la chibs dkyus sa yod pas/ rta gcig
rgyugs pa 'ur ting khrol zhes pas/ rta drug cu rgyugs pa'i sgra byung / lan drug rgyugs pa dang / grong khyer ba rnams rta 'chag cing ltad mo byed pa dang / rgyal po thod
dmar 'phyur re pho brang du gshegs pa mi ltas mthong / de'i nangs par rgyal po'i zhal nas/ lha gcig khri btsun la chibs 'chags zhes gsungs te/ pho brang lho phyogs kyi sgo
nas/ 'o thang gi mtsho'i 'gram na mar zheng 'dom gsum/ dkyus su 'dom sum brgya yod pa/ zabs su 'dom do/ so phag dang spang leb la sogs pa dang / rgyal po'i chibs dkyus
sa 'dra ba zhig yod pa/ khri btsun gyis sne drangs te/ rta 'dur chen la btang nas byon pa dang / 'o thang gi mtsho 'gram du rtol ba las rgyal po na re/ nga'i sor gdub 'di
gar song sar khyod lha khang rtsigs shig gsungs nas sor gdub 'phangs pas/ nam mkha' ru song ste khri btsun gyi rta sga'i phyi ru la babs/ de yar nas 'o thang gi mtsho la
song ste/ khri btsun gyi snyam na/ rgyal pos kyang kong jo la gros dris 'dug snyam nas/ mig mchi mas gang ngo / /rgyal pos khri btsun la 'od 'di khyod kyis mthong ngam
byas pas/ ngas lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad kyi rmang bting yang zhig da yang mtsho 'di la lha khang mi btub lapas

mig mchi mas gang nas ma mthong ngo / /yang rgyal po na re/ ngas khyod lha khang rtsig pa'i grogs bya'o zhes gsungs pas/ der khri btsun rab tu dga' nas bsgo ba bzhin mnyan
te/ der rgyal po na re/ nga'i pho brang zhig 'o thang du rtsigs shig ces gsungs so/ /'o thang du pho brang gsum thog ma zhig brtsigs pa'i nang du mchod gnas bcu spyan drangs
te/ khri btsun gyis klong rdol dang / rgyun 'dul la sogs pa zul phug dbus rkyang bu tshal gyi klu de rnams la chos skyong bcol/ chu dkar chung sbu ba gdong du bsgyur
nas mtsho shing gla bas phub pas/ dkyil du shing gis ma slebs/ yang rgyal po la gros dris pas/ nga la 'dri sa zhig yod kyi gsungs nas/ yang lha la mchod pa phul bas rtsa
ba'i zhal 'od zer zhig byung ste/ 'o thang gi mtsho'i thad kar 'od zer las sprin 'khrigs pas/ 'od char lta bur babs so/ /de la khri btsun gyis bltas pas/ mtsho nang du dkar
po rim pa gsum mthong ngo / de la bal po rdo mkhan gyis rdo gsang phu nas drangs te/ bzo byas nas 'od zer la brgyab pas 'od zer dang rdo mnyam du zad tsa na/ mtsho'i dkyil
du mkhar bu zhig byung / de la shing rnams gtad de mtsho phubs so/ /de la shing klu'i yul nas rdo rje'i 'dag pa bye ma'i mes mi tshig pa/ chus kyang mi 'drul ba/ brkos
kyang mi phed pa/ rdo rje pha lam lta bus byugs/ de'i steng du khro chu'i pha gus bsgrigs/ srubs gsos 'khan pas byugs/ de'i steng du so phag dang / spang leb dang / rdo
leb dang / sa bzang dang / bye ma rdo hrug rnams rim pas bting ba'i khar/ skye bo dang bstun nas grub bzhir rmang bting / btsun pa dang bstun nas re'u mig tu bris te rmang
bting / bon po dang bstun nas g.yung drung ris su byas/ rgya'i rten dpe har la dpe blangs te gzings 'bring po dang tshad mnyam nas rmang bting bas zhig go/ /yang rgyal
po na re/ bal po'i lha bzo sprul pa de la/ khyod kyis nga'i 'bag cig gyis dang bsgo ba las/ bal po'i lha bzos kyang byang chub shing gi srog shing / tsan dan goshirSha'i
rus shing dang / rme ru lcags gzer dang / gnas brgyad kyi sa dang / chu bo nairanya?dza na'i bye ba dang / tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i lde gu dang / ba spos zan ma'i
'o ma dang / rgya mtsho gle'i 'jag ma dang / rin po che'i spyan 'bras dang / shing bal gyi thi gu dang / lde men la sogs sta gon byas nas rgyal po'i dbu sngas su bzhag go/
/sang nangs par dga' ston chen po yang byas/ lha bzhengs par yang chas pas/ de'i tho rangs rgyal po'i pho brang du mthongs na mar phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub
sems dpa' thams cad bkra lam gyis shar byon te lha'i rgyu la thim pas/ rgyal po'i thugs la/ nga'i lha 'di phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
kyis byin gyis brlabs pa 'dra ba zhig yong bar 'dug na/ phyag stong spyan stong zhig bya'am/ zhal bcu gcig pa zhig bya'am/ yi ge drug ma zhig bya'am/ ha ya gha?rib zhi
bya'am/ lo ki shwa ra zhig bya'am/ kha sarpa Ni zhig bya'am/ chu srin 'dzin khri zhig bya'am/ kro ta mgrin sngon zhig bya'am snyam pa dang / dgung langs tsa na/ rgyal po'i
dbu sngas na/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug zhal bcu gcig pa bzhengs pa/ rtsa ba'i zhal gsum spyan gsum pa/

da'ei steng du bzhad pa'i zhal gnyis/ de'i steng gtsigs pa'i zhal dmar po gnyis/ da'ei steng na 'dzum pa'i zhal mthing ga gnyis/ de'i steng na a mi de ba'i zhal dmar po gtsug
tor dang bcas pa/ phyag bcu pa/ dang po gnyis thugs khar thal mo sbyar ba/ g.yas kyi gnyis pa na pad ma dkar po'i steng na sprul pa'i sku 'od dpag tu med pa/ gsum pa ru
mda'/ bzhi po na 'khor lo/ lnga pa sa gnon mdzad pa'o/ /g.yon gyi gnyis pa na 'phreng ba/ gsum pa na nor bu rin po che/ bzhi par gzhu/ lnga pa na bum pa spyi blugs bsnams
pa/ ri dwags e na ya'i stod g.yogs dkris pa/ dar sna tshogs kyi sham thabs bsnams par gzigs so/ /de nas bal po'i lha bzo ba la/ sku ni shin tu legs na 'di'i thugs kar
mchod sdong 'di gsum dang / tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku rang byon 'di bzhugs pa yin pa la zhes bka' bstsal bas/ lha bzo ba na re/ sku 'di kho bos ma bgyis te dgung
langs tsa na rgyal pos dga' ston mdzad pa dang rgyal po nyid la dris la 'bag bya'o snyam pa mchis zer ro/ /sku de shin tu g.yo bar gyur pa dang / phyag dang po gcig gis/
zhabs g.yon ma'i sham thabs pus mo'i gong du brdzes te/ zhabs mthil nas 'od byung ste tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sku dang mchod sdong la phog pas/ de dag zhabs g.yas
pa'i 'og tu nub nas/ thugs khar song ste der chags pa dang sa g.yos par gyur ro/ /lha rnams kyis nam mkha' dang mar snang la mchod pa byed do/ /sham thabs kyang de nyid
du chags la sku de nyid shin tu sbram pa yin no/ /shin tu g.yo ba yin/ a mi de ba de g.yon du yo ba yin/ rgyal po thugs dgyes te ngo mtshar bar gyur to/ /kha ba can du sku
bzhengs pa la de snga ba yin no/ /rgyal pos 'byung ba sa'i dgra bzlog pa'i phyir dbang phyug chen po'i ling ga dang / bya khyung ga ru Da'i rten dang / gza' rnams kyi mchod
rten ser ru dang / rdo'i seng ge dkar mo yang mdzad do/ /de nas jo mo ru yong bzas brag phug ma mo nyal sar bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kun tu zhal bzhengs su
gsol lo/ /klu'i pho brang jo bo shAkyas mnan zin/ pho brang gi lho nub tu btsan gyi rgyu srang gcad par bya ba'i phyir mtshams bcad kyi mchod rten ke ru bzhengs/ de ma
bzhengs na kha ba can gyi sgrub pa po rnams kyi srog btsan gyis 'phrog pas/ mchod rten de bzhengs pas rab tu byung ba la btsan gyi gnod pa mi 'byung ngo gsungs so/ /de nas
gnam stong gi srod la rgyal po 'o thang gi mtsho 'gram du byon pa dang / lho phyogs gla ba'i tshal na lha 'dre rnams 'tshogs nas gros byed pa/ kha ba can 'di nged lha srin
'dre srin mi ma yin rnams kyis dbang ba yin pa la/ rgyal po srong btsan sgam po chos byed zer te/ sangs rgyas zer ba dang / chos zer ba la/ mi nad dang / phyugs nad dang
/ lo tog la btsa' dang / than pa dang / sad dang / ser ba dang / lo nyes gtong / 'jig rten du nyes dgu thams cad gtong / btsad po'i lha khang yang sngar bshig pa de legs
so/ /da yang bshig par bya'o/ /de la yang rdo'i char dbab par bya'o/ /zhes zer te gyes nas song ngo / /de nas rgyal pos 'dre'i 'dun phung bshig pa'i phyir du/ jo bo thugs
rje chen po la gsol ba btab pas jo bo bzhad pa'i zhal gnyis nas 'od zer byung nas rnam pa gnyis su song

bas/ 'od zer gcig gi sna la dpal rta mgrin byung / gcig la khro bo bdud rtsi 'khyil ba byung / de gnyis kyi thugs kha nas me dpung bskal ba'i le lta bu 'phros pas/ shing sdong
gi rtsa bar 'dre'i 'dun phung yod pa/ 'dre thams cad brgyal par gyur pa la/ rgyal po'i phyag song bas lho phyogs gla ba'i tshal na dug gi sdong po yod pa la phog pas/
dug thor phyag rgyas bcings te/ dus mtha'i rlung ngam/ bskal pa bsregs pa'i me btang bas 'dre rnams phyi'i rgya mtsho'i gle la bskyal bas/ 'dre rnams brgyal pa las sangs
te nyi zer la lag pas mig skyor nas kha ba can du lta'o/ /khro bo gnyis kyi me phung gi gla ba'i tshal gyi brag la bcom ldan 'das kha sarpa Ni/ dpal rta mgrin dang / a mi
de ba'i gzugs su chags/ de la rgyal po dges te thugs ngo mtshar bar gyur to/ /sang nangs par bal po lha bzos 'od zer ji lta ba bzhin du rdo la brkos te 'bur tu bton nas
bzhag go/ /rgyal po'i zhal nas bal po'i lha bzo ba la khyod kyi mdang gi jo bo thugs rje chen po'i zhal gyi dkyil 'khor las byung ba'i 'od zer gyi sna'i lha de gnyis mthong
ngam/ gsol ba/ mthong lags/ bka' bstsal pa/ 'o na lha de gnyis kyi gzugs gyis dang ces bsgo ba dang / bal po lha bzo bas rta mgrin dang / khro bo bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i
'od zer ltar bzo byas so/ /da rung gyis dang gsungs pas/ kha sarpa ni dang 'jig rten dbang phyug byas so/ /thugs rje chen po'i 'khor nyungs so/ /da rung gyis dang byas
pas/ don yod zhags pa dang / yid bzhin 'khor lo dang / a yu ta ra dang / lha mo 'od zer can te gtso 'khor dgu pho brang de nyid du/ rgyal po'i dbu sngas su bzhugs so/ /de
ltar sa dgra bzlog nas da lha khang brtsig tu btub par mkhyen te/ rgya'i dben khang dpe har la dpe byas/ gzings 'bring po la tshad byas nas kha ba can du dam pa'i chos la
sogs legs dgu cog dar bar bya ba dang / nyes dgu cog nub par bya ba'i phyir/ sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas gor phyed du btang nas/ la las sa skyas/ la las
rdo skyas/ la las shing bcad/ la las rtsig pa brtsigs nas gor phyed shing phyed du btang ngo / /skye bo phal pas mi mthong bar bya ba'i ched du na bun gyis sgrib par byas
pa'i gseb tu pha ya di ri ri brtsigs pas nyi ma gcig la rtsig pa rnams 'byongs par byas so/ /yang 'phro rtsig tu ma btub nas sprul pa mdzad de/ bod kyi sa gzhi srin mo
gan rkyal du 'gyel ba 'dra ba'i dpung mgo dang / dpyi mgo mnan par bya ba'i ched du ru bzhi'i gtsug lag khang chen bzhi bzhengs su gsol ba ni/ dpung pa g.yon pa la g.yung
drung g.yo ru khra 'brug bzhengs so/ /dpung mgo g.yas par dbu ru ka tshal bzhengs so/ /dpyi g.yas pa la gtsang 'gram bzhengs so/ /dpyi g.yon pa la ru lag grom pa rgyang
bzhengs so/ /yang rtsig tu ma btub nas bar tshigs rnams gnon pa'i phyir mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi bzhengs te/ gru mo g.yon pa la lho brag kho 'thing bzhengs so/
/gru mo g.yas pa la kong po bu chu thar legs bzhengs so/ /pus mo g.yas pa la dre'i ka brag pus mo g.yon pa la spra dun tse bzhengs so/ /yang rtsig tu ma btub pas nying lag
rnams gnon pa'i phyir/ lag mthil g.yon pa la khams kyi klong thang sgron ma'i lha khang bzhengs so/ /lag mthil

g.yas pa la byang tsha spe dpal tshad rlung gnon gyi lha khang bzhengs so/ /de'i rkang pa g.yas pa'i mthil la mang yul byams sprin gyi lha khang bzhengs so/ /rkang pa g.yon
pa la mon skyer chu'i lha khang bzhengs so/ /yang nyin mo brtsigs pal nub po zhig ste/ byang chub tshal gyi ka ba bzhi la mdo khams su klong thang dpal 'byung / lho phyogs
su rgya chu thog rngam/ nub 'a zha'i yul du ke'u ri gzigs/ sgro skyer du/ li yuul du 'dag sha inatra/ mtha' 'dul brgyad la/ kha che ru snang sbal chen brtsigs pa/ kong
yul du bu chu thar legs/ sba gro skyer chur dpal be'u rgyas pa/ yang 'dul brgyad la/ shar seng ge dkar mo'i mche ba'i steng du rdo mi 'gyur ba/ de'i 'chong du/ myang por
myang po ka chung / lho g.yu 'brug gi gshog steng du spa gro skyer chu/ de'i mchong du sma sha/ me lha'i nub bya dmar po'i mchu steng du mang yul byams sprin/ de'i 'chong
du byang can gyi lha khang / byang rus sbal nag po'i rgyab steng du spra dun tse/ de'i 'chong du gshen gsal gyi lha khang bzhengs so/ /ru mtshams gnon pa la byang shar
du li ti brgya rtsa brgyad/ shar lhor kong bu chu/ lho nub tu lho brag kho 'thing / nub byang du pad ma g.yung drung / de nas yang 'dul la/ gling chu skyer chu/ shar nyi
zla gnon pa'i phyir du bum thang dang / gling chu skyer chu/ shar nyi zla gnon pa'i phyir du bum thang dang / glong rtse gnyis/ me lha gnon pa'i phyir du gye re gyer chung
gnyis/ gnod sbyin gnon pa'i ched du/ gu langs la dpe blangs pa'i rdo shan lha khang dang / shing kun la dpe blangs pa'i hab sha gnyis/ mtsho ma pham gyi kha gnon la gangs
bar bzhengs so/ /gangs ti si'i kha gnon la 'phrang dum bzhengs so/ /sangs rgyas 'das pa'i rten du nub ri'i gnam sa gra zur gnon pa'i ched du khyung lung dngul dkar bzhengs
so/ /dbang phyug chen po sgrub pa'i gnas su mang yul shing sa/ sangs rgyas kyis rtag tu mi yul kyi rtags su li yul slangs lapa'i lha khang la sogs bzhengs so/ /de nas
ra sa dang rgya stag bzhengs su gsol lo/ /bal yul du bha ga bhe ba ri/ phu tro dhe ba ri/ shing kun lha khang / hab shang lha khang bzhengs so/ /de ltar mtha' 'dul yang
'dul bco brgyad bzhengs so/ /'chong dang bcas pa'i lha khang rnams so/ /bal yul du lo bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis rgyal sa mdzad do/ /de nas lha khang rtsig tu btub par mkhyen nas/
rgya'i dpe khang ha ra la dpe blangs nas gzings 'bring po'i tshad du byas te/ bal po'i rgyal po dang chad btsan par byas so/ /nyes dgu cog nub par bya ba'i phyir/ sku
lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas gor phyed shing phyed du btang / la las sa skyas/ la las rdo skyas/ la las shing bcad/ la las rtsig pa byas/ gor phyed shing phyed
du btang ngo / /skye bo phal pas mi mthong ba'i ched du/ na bun gyis bsgribs pa'i gseb tu yo yA yo yA di ri ri brtsigs so/ /nyi ma gcig la 'byongs par byas so/ /btsun mo
rnams kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dar dkar gsal ba'i me long dang / blon po rnams kyis byas pa'i yi ge zla ba'i 'dod 'jo na yang tshul 'di cung zad bris 'dug ste/ ji lta bzhengs
pa'i tshul rgyas par ma bris so/ /de nas ra sa'i gtsug

lag khang gi thog phub par 'dod nas/ rgyal pos sku'i bkod pal lnga stong du sprul nas bzhengs pa la/ la las shing bcad/ la las shing 'dren/ la las shing bzo byed pa las/ lha
gcig khri btsun bsang bu 'dren du 'ongs pa las/ na ma gcig lha gcig khri btsun dbu skru 'khru bas ma khom ste g.yog mo la/ dngul gzhong chen por sha gsar pa dang mar gsar
pa dang spod kyis sbran pa la sogs g.yos sna bcu gnyis 'bras chang dang bcas pa rgyal po la 'dren du btang bas/ sprul pa'i bzo bo sum brgya bzo byed kyi 'dug pas de'i
nang nas rgyal po ngo ma shes te/ pho brang du phyir log go/ /de nas lha gcig rang bsang bu 'dren du song ba las/ rgyal po dbus kyi de yin/ ber nag po gsol ba la thod dmar
po can de yin no zer bas/ de nas phyir g.yog mos bltar phyin tsa na/ lha gcig ra sa'i nang song nas dbus kyi de dkyil 'khor gyi kha na thig gu nag po'i sna la bzung ba'i
zer nag po gsol/ la thod dmar po dbu la bcings pa de la bsang bu 'dren pa dang / rgyal pos bsang bu blangs pas tig gu lhod song ba dang shing bzo ba thams cad 'gyel nas
'og na 'jag ma lhag ge 'dug pa bu mos sgo bar nas mthong bas/ 'o na lags thams cad 'phrul du snang byas pas/ rgyal po de la yengs bzhin du ste'u'i kha thal bas seng ge gcig
gi sna bcad pas/ bzo bo brgyas seng ge re'i sna bcad/ rgyal pos spang leb gcig la gzong kha thal nas/ bu gu gcig phug pas bu gu brgya phug rgyal pos log le kha thal bas/
ka ba gcig zur nyams pas/ ka ba brgya'i zur nyams par gyur to/ /der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ nga'i 'phrul pa 'bangs mi tshun chad kyis shes so gsungs nas/ 'phrul pa zhig
pas snang ba gsum du byung ngo / /skye bo phal ba'i snang ba la/ shing dang 'dag pa'i mi la ste'u ltag re brgyab pas zhig par mthong ngo / /blon po chen po rnams kyi snang
ba la sprul pa'i shing bzo ba rnams rtsig pa'i gseb na phar rkang pa gzhug nyug ge song bar mthong ngo / /rgyal po yab yum shing bzo'i dbur chag dang tson rtsi la sogs
tshar bar gzigs so/ /de nas shing rnams sngar gdung cher du bcer ba dang / sa srod/ blon po dag na re/ da sa yang srod/ sprin yang 'thibs/ glog kyang byung / char 'bab pa
'dra na/ rgyal po'i shing gi rtsi 'jig pa srung ba'i phyir grong khyer ba rnams kyi re ba dang phyar sle rnams bsdus la shing la g.yogs dgos pa/ las kyi rnga brdungs pas/
grong khyer ba na re/ sngar rgyal po gtsug lag khang gartsigs pa la las kyi rnga ma brdungs pas/ ngal gso na ci byed zer/ sgo ba na re/ shing gi char skyibs re ba rnams
kyis shing la bkab dgos pas bye ma'i gling du 'khyer la shog ces bsgo 'o/ /grong khyer ba thams cad phyar ba la sogs pa thams cad khyer nas ra sa'i 'gram du phyin tsa na/
srod la rgyal pos sprul pa byas pas/ ra sa'i thog phug zin nas/ steng nas sprul pa'i mi pha tshe thogs pa yud yud 'dug pa blon po rnams kyis mthong ngo / /blon po rnams
ngo mtshar du gyur ro/ /re ba rnams kyis ra sa'i rgya mthongs bkab po/ /de nas sang nangs par rgyal pos de na gang legs pa zhig la nga'i jo bo thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor
dgu po'i bzhugs sa bya dgos snyam nas gtsang khang ltar byon pas/ dbus kyi gtsang khang sgo phye ba dang /

de na de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'khrugs pa gtso 'khor dgu theg pa chen po'i chos kyi bgro ba mdzad cing bzhugs nas 'dug gtsang khang g.yas pa sgo phye tsa na/ de na de bzhin gshegs
pa 'od dpag med gtso 'khor dgu dang bcas pa theg pa chen po'i chos kyi bgro ba mdzad kyin bzhugs 'dug yang gtsang khang g.yon pa sgo phye tsa na/ de na de bzhin gshegs
pa byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo gtso 'khor dgu po theg pa chen po'i chos kyi bgro ba mdzad kyin bzhugs 'dug gtsang khang lho ngos sgo phye tsa na/ de na bcom ldan 'das mi
bskyod rdo rjes 'khor gnod sbyin pho mo rnams la bod kha ba can gyi 'dre srin 'dul pa'i thabs ston/ de nas arya dzam bha la gter gyi bum pa gtod kyin bzhugs/ gtsang khang
byang ngos sgo phye tsa na/ de nyams dga' ba sa gzhi gu yangs pa bya byed kyis mtho ba/ shing gi bzo legs par gzigs pa na nga'i lha'i bzhugs khang 'di la bya'o snyam ste
phyir byon tsa na/ sgo'i them pa'i rtsar/ klu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sku mdog dkar po spyan dmar po gsum sbrul mgo nyi shu rtsa gtsig pas rgyal po'i zhabs
la gtugs te phyag byas nas rgyal po chen po khyod kyi gtsug lag khang 'di stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams su rgyas par bskyang gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig
zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas 'ben tshad gang tsam phyir byon tsa na/ klu'i rgyal po dga' bo sbrul mgo bdun pa gcig byas te/ rgyal po khyod kyi gtsug lag khang
'di stong bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams su rgyas par bskyang gi nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas byon pa dang klu nye dga' bos rgyal
po la phyag byas nas khyed kyi gtsug lag khang 'di stong gsum gyi stong chen po 'dir ngas rgyas par bskyang gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur
to/ /de nas byon pa'i mdun du gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po na ga ku bhe ra mgo gsum pa zhig gis phyag byas te/ rgyal po khyod kyi gtsug lag khang 'di mi'i 'jigs pa las ngas
bsrung gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas byin pa'i mdun du srin po'i rgyal po lang ka mgrin bcu mgo dgu pa gcig gis rgyal po la phyag
bya te/ rgyal po khyod kyi gtsug lag khang 'di la me'i 'jigs pal byung na ngas bsrung gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas byon
pa dang dri za'i rgyal po zur phud lnga pas rgyal po la phyag byas te/ khyod kyi gtsug lag khang 'di la mi ma yin gyi gnod pa byung na ngas bsrung gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang
gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar song ngo / /de nas zhal lhor gzigs pas dpal lha mos lcags kyi bre ba so gcu gnyis pa gcig thogs nas rgyal po la phyag byas te/ khyod kyi
gtsug lag khang 'di la chu'i 'jigs pa byung na ngas bsrung gi/ nga'i gzugs gcig kyang gyis shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /gtsug lag khang mi ma yin pa rnams kyis
bsrung bar khas blangs/ de nas rgyal pos kyang nangs par nyi ma shar tsam la dga' ston gyi rnga brdungs/ lha gcig khri matsun gyis dga' ston gyis shig blon pa rnams kyis
lus rgyan dang chos las mchod pa rgyun mi chad pa spel zhing / ra sa'i gtsug lag khang du lha 'dren du shog cig

ces bka' bstsal pas/ 'breng zhags dang shing rta la sogs pa sta gon du byas so/ /sang nangs pa dgung sangs pa dang / mchod pa'i bu mo bcu drug dang / blon po chen po rnams
phyag 'tshal du yong tsa na lha gcig kyang mi bzhugs par/ rgyal po'i dbu sngas na spos dang me tog sngar med pa'i thor ba re snang bas bred pas rtab di ri byas pas/ khang
thog gi ne tso smra mkhan gcig na re/ khyed rnams ci'i phyir thugs rtab por byed zer ro/ /mchod g.yog gi bu mo rnams na re/ lha rnams gtsang khang du spyan 'dren bsams tsa
na lha rnams gcig kyang med zer/ ne tso na re/ mdang nam phyed tsam na lha rnams gcig gis gcig la phyag byas nas/ me tog gtor nas pho brang gi mthongs nas yar song bas/
byang phyogs bye ma'i gling na phar bltas te song zer ro/ /de bden nam mi bden snyam ste blon po de dag gis byang phyogs bye ma'i gling du phyin tsa na/ bye ma'i gling
la zhabs rjes pad mo 'dug pa mthong / der rlung 'tshub langs pas bye ma'i gle'i pad mo zum pas/ blon po dag gis mig rig rig phar tsab tshur tsab byed do/ /ra sa'i gtsug lag
khang du dre'u dkar mo skad 'don zhing sna shud nas song ba dang / de'i phyi la phyin tsa na/ lha khang sgo lhor lta ba byang ma de na jo bo thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor
dgu gdan med par gral byas nas 'dug pa grong khyer ba'i mi thams cad kyis mthong ngo / /rgyal po yang de la thugs dgyes te ngo mtshar che zer nas thal mo sbyar ro/ /de
nas rgyal pos bal po lha bzo ba la/ khyod kyis gtsang khang gi lho phyogs 'di la lha gcig bris dang zhes bka' bsgo ba dang / lha bzo bas kyang ka ba shing lo can gyi rtsar
kong bu dang pir dang tshon rtsi la sogs pa sta gon byas te sang nangs par 'bri bar brtsam mo/ /nangs par lha bzo bas rgyal po la phyag byas te/ lha ji lta bu bri zhus
pas/ rgyal po dang lha bzo dang blon po chen po rnams 'grogs te ra sa'i gtsug lag khang du byon pa dang / lho phyogs kyi rtsig logs la bcom ldan 'das kha sarpa Ni 'jigs
pa brgyad skyob bris nas 'dug go/ /de la ngo mtshar ro zhes smras pa dang / de'i 'phro la gang la ci 'dul de la der ston gling la 'phel bar gyur to/ /de nas sprul lapa'i
lha bzo des kyang de'i 'og gi rta mgron dkar po dang / lha mo sgrol ma la sogs pal lha lnga bris so/ /rgyal pos gdung ma rnams kyi bar bkag la chos mngon pa'i sde snod kyi
rgyud ris bkod/ gdung tshar rnams la phyi rabs dpon sras bla blon rnams kyi don du dam chos 'dul pa'i rgyud ris rnams bkod do/ /phyi rabs kyis rigs pa'i chos go bar bya
ba'i don du glo 'bur nub byang mtshams su lde'u bris/ lung gi chos go bar bya ba'i phyir du sgrung rgyud mang po yang bris so/ /bslab pa gsum la 'god pa'i phyir bon sha
ba nam mkha' la 'gro shes pa yang yod do/ /de nas rgyal pos lha gcig khri btsun la bka' bstsal pa/ khyod kyi yab rgyal po'i thugs dgongs skong ba dang chad btsan par bya
ba'i phyir dang / ba can gyi sems can gyi phyag dang mchod pa byed pa'i rten 'dzugs pa dang / nag po'i phyogs thams cad 'grib la legs so cog dar bar bya ba'i phyir lha khang
'di tshang bar gyis shig ces bka' bstsal ba dang / de la lha gcig khri btsun spro bas/ rgyal po la ji ltar

bgyi zhus pas/ rgyal pos bka' bstsal ba/ yab rgyal po dang nga'i bang chen blon po rnams chad byas khas blangs pa'i dus su/ mtha' 'khob kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su lha khang
brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs la sgo thams cad nub phyogs bal po'i yul du kha bstan/ gtsang khang dbus mar bcom ldan 'das a mi de ba gtso 'khor dgu bzhengs su gsol cig de'i
g.yon gtsang khang lho mar bcom ldan 'das mi bskyod rdo rjes gtso byas chos skyong ba'i gnod sbyin chen kapo gter gyi bum pa thogs pa bzhengs shig gtsang khang gi sgo
lnga tshar nas kha ba can skyes pa'i sems can de dag bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' la yid mi ches pa/ chos kyi bdud rtsi la 'thung du mi btub pa/ thar pa'i bkar bslab pa gsum
la mi slob pa/ rigs pa'i chos la blo mi 'gro ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdul byar ma gyur pa rnams ngas 'dul ba yin pas/ nga'i khrims btsan du byas pas/ chos kyi bdun rtsi
'thung ba yin/ nga'i rgyal khasam su chos bdud rtsir bya ba'i phyir ka ba shing lo tsan dang nye bar chos kyi gter sba bar bya'o/ /de bsrung ba'i phyir ka ba sbrul mgo can
du mthu'i gter sba bar bya'o/ /de nas mtha'i ngan sngags dang phra men gyis mi tshugs par bya ba'i phyir ka ba seng ge lag zan ma la phyir bzlog sba bar bya'o/ /de thams
cad kyi rkyen 'byung zhing kha ba can du char chu dus su 'bab pa dang / lo phyugs dus su smin par bya ba dang / sad dang ser ba mi 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir ka ba bum pa
can dang mi ring bar rin po che'i gter sba bar bya'o/ /ra sa'i zhig ral gso ba dang mchod pa rgyun mi chad par bya ba'i phyir/ dkyil 'khor gyi 'og tu rin po che dbang gi
rgyal po dang gser dngul la sogs pa'i khram thob cig gzhan yang mi la nad mi 'ong ba dang / pha spun rme mi 'chor ba dang / ya rabs nang 'khrug mi 'chor ba dang / spyir
rgyal khams gzhan gyi dmag mi yong ba dang / phyi rol mu stegs byed kyi chos mi dar ba dang / sgrub pa po la bar chad mi yong ba la sogs nyes pa thams cad mi 'gyur ba dang
/ legs dgu cog dar ba'i phyir du thabs rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad do/ /de yang ji ltar byas lugs dang / gar sbas pa dang / phyung nas ji ltar longs
spyod pa dang / de la sogs pa mang du bka' chems kyi shog ril bris 'dug ste/ ngan 'phel gyis dogs nas bzhag go/ /de thams cad kyang sprul pas srung ba sgo khang du klu'i
rten tshugs shig gnod sbyin gyi rten tshugs shig dpal lha mo'i rten bya ba la sogs pa mang du bka' bstsal nas/ rgyal po dang blon po bcu drug dang chas nas rgya nag 'phrul
gyi rgyal po'i chad btsan par bya ba'i phyir/ rgya'i so kha phyir 'bul ba dang / bod 'bangs bde la 'god pal dang / thugs dam gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i phyir/ mdo smad
shar phyogs su gshegs so/ /lha gcig khri btsun gyis bal po'i lha bzo spyan drangs lha khang gsum thog ma gcig bgyi bar 'dod pas nyis thog bzo byas/ 'og khang du rgyal
pos bka' bsgo ba ltar lha la sogs pa bka' bzhin bsgrubs so/ /ra mo cher lha khang rtsig dbang med/ sing dang la ma'i ra ba bgyid pal la ka ba'i bar so phag gis bcad pas sgo
khyud shar du phye bas/ lha'i zhal dang po nub tu gzigs pa de/ shar du rang bsgyur 'gyur bar grags so/ /jo

mo gcung mo mong bza' khri lcam gyis lha sa mkhar brag thugs dam du bzhengs so/ /zhang zhung gi rgyal po ling bkra'i sras mo lha gcig mig sman gyis lkog pa'i thugs dam bzhengs/
(de'i tshe sum pa ki kang rdos ngan sngags kyis shig ling / ) phya ra tsam btang nas shig phug ron tsam byung mchis/ de nas dgung lo bcu gnyis na rgyal po'i thugs dam
gtsug lag khang grangs thim khar yongs rdzogs rab dga'i lha khang bzhengs/ mdzad pa rgya chen po yang tshar nas dbus su gshegs/ jo mo rgyal btsun gyis brag lha mgon po
kun tu zhal brko ba la rdo rje phye bre re phed na tsha bre re bya dgar gnang bas tshar ro/ /gcung khri lcam dang zhang zhung bza'i thugs dam yang tshar/ gcen khri btsun
gyi ra sa bre kha spub pa 'dra ba zhig tshar ba'i slad rol du/ rgyal po blon po bcu drug dang bcas pa byon/ sna chain pos rje'i gdan khyer nas them skas la byon pa dang /
ra sa'i nang chus gang bar snang snyam ste nang du mchi ngar rngo ma thogs/ der rgyal po'i chibs lcag bor bas/ chu nang na lding ba ltar gda' ste/ slar chab kyi nang du
babs so/ /yang rgyal pos phyag sor gdu bu bskyur bas sil khrol te dkyil 'khor gyi rtsar song bas der yid ches te rgyal po'i khri dkyil 'khor gyi steng du brtsigs te bzhugs/
khyed blon po bcu drug po mi bzhis grong khyer nas mgron pos/ mi bzhis sha tshos/ mi bzhis chang longs/ mi bzhis 'dren pa gyis shig ces bka' bstsal to/ /blon po rnams
kyis bka' bzhin bgyis pa dang / jo mo khri btsun gser sel ma bre gang bsnams te rgyal po la phul snyun rmed/ lha gcig kong jos kyang gser sil ma bre gang bsnams te/ rgyal
po la phyag byas gser phul nas snyun rmed do/ /mong bza' khri lcam yang gser sel ma bre gang bsnams te rgyal po la phyag byas gser phul nas snyun rmed do/ /de nas rgyal
po'i zhal/ lha gcig khri btsun na re/ khong gi shing bzo legs 'dra ste nga'i 'phrul bzo legs 'dra ste 'phrul du snang zhes pas lha khang steng khang 'phrul snang bya bar
grags so/ /de nas rgyal pos bzhengs te/ nga'i lha thugs rje chain po la phyag bya'o gsungs nas thugs rje chen po'i gtsang khang du gshegs so/ /jo bo thugs rje chen po'i na
bzhengs/ g.yas na lha gcig khri btsun bzhengs/ g.yon na lha gcig kong jo bzhengs/ rgyab them pa'i nang la sogs pa na mong bza' khri lcam bzhengs/ sna chen po'i lag pa sgo
sked la 'jus/ rkang pa phyir bzhag mgo bo nang du bcug nas 'dug pa la/ rgyal pos zhal phyir log byas nas bod 'bangs rnams la lung bstan pa/ 'di la kha ba can gyi rgyal
khams 'di/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis rab tu bsngags pa yin/ /khyad par can gyis gnas su lung bstan te/ /byang chub sems dpa' mang po 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de nas gdung rabs bzhi
na rgyal po ni/ /so so skye bo'i byang chub sems dpa' 'byung / /de nas de srang byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /'phags pa'i gang zag rgyal po chen po 'byung / /chos bzhin gtsug
lag khang chen mang po bzhengs/ /mtha' 'khob rgyal khams thams cad dbang du bsdu/ /phyogs bzhi mtshams brgyad kun la dpya khral sdud/ /rgya gar gsang mdzod dam chos
mang po bsgyur/ /sprul pa lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa' ni/ /lo paN mang pos dam chos rgyas par byed/ /yangs

pa can gyi dam chos mang po yis/ /rab tu byung nas dge 'dun sde yang 'dzugs/ /brtson 'grus can gyi sngags pa mang po 'byung / /thun mong dngos grub thob nas mgo 'tshams mang
pa ston/ /de ltar chos skyong rgyal po chen po des/ /bod 'bangs bde skyid dga' ba'i chos la sbyor/ /rgyal po'i mdzad spyod phun sum tshogs pa yin/ /'bangs kyi bde skyid
phun sum tshogs pa 'byung / /des kyang sku gzugs 'di la zhabs thog byed/ /de sras byang chub sems dpa' gcig gis kyang / /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa'i bstod bsngags
brjongs/ /sangs rgyas bstan bsrung zhing rgyas par skyong / /sku gzugs 'di la zhabs thog byed par 'gyur/ /de'i sras su byung ba byang chub sems dpa' gnyis/ /gcig ni bdud
rigs rgyal po nag por 'gyur/ /de ltar bdud rigs nag po'i rgyal po des/ /bod 'bangs yongs kyi bsod nams zad pa dang / /sangs rgyas bstan pa nyams par gyur pas na/ /nag po
bdud kyi lha 'dre dar gyur nas/ gnam the dkar po'i sprul pa blon po 'byung / /de'i 'khor gyis 'gong po dgur sprul nas/ /bod la gnod pa byed pa 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de nas gnam
the dkar po'i sprul pa'i blon po des 'dre'i sprul pas sngags pa gsod par 'gyur/ /de yis dkar po'i phyogs kyi lha 'dre 'khrugs/ /nag po'i phyogs kyi lha 'dre thams cad
kyis/ /rgyal po bdud kyi phyogs kyi dpung byas nas/ /byang chub sems dpa'i rgyal po gnyis po yang / /gcig ni spyugs la gcig ni gsod par 'gyur/ /de nas nag po'i phyogs nas
dar gyur nas/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa shin tu nub par 'gyur/ /gtsug lag khang bshig phan tshun chad pa gcod/ /dge ba spyod la log pa'i bka' bkyon thebs/ /sdig pa spyod la
legs pa'i bya dga' ster/ /dgon pa thams cad ri dwags dgon par 'gyur/ /gtsug lag khang kun phyugs ra dag tu 'gyur/ /ston pa rnams ni las byed las khur byed/ /ban de rnams
ni lings byed rngon pa byed/ /kyi hud nag po'i phyogs rnams dar bar 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa nyams smad gyur pa na/ /nag po'i phyogs rgyas mun par 'gyur du nye/ /de
dag dus su sku gzugs 'di rnams kun/ /re zhig zab mo'i gter du gser ltar sbos/ /rgyal po de nyid tha ma gri ru 'gum/ /de sras ring nas bka' chad dbu yogs kyis/ /rje'u rnams
la 'bangs kyis kheng log byed/ /de dus ngan song 'gro ba mang po 'byung / /bcud rnams sas 'thung sman rnams nus pa chung / /ro rnams mi zhim lo tog sad ser mang / /'bru
rnams skyed khungs zhan zhing phyugs rnams bzhon she chung / /gangs dang stobs dang tsher dum rtsub pa 'dra/ /g.yang sa grog ral ma rungs pa rnams 'byung / /gcong rong sa
ral shin tu mi bde zhing / /rtsi shing skam zhing sa rdo ri bo nyil/ /gza' skar log gyur char chu mi snyom zhing / /nad mang tshe thung mu ge mang po 'byung / /'dre gnod
mang zhing 'dre chos mang du 'byung / /'gong po spun dgu mi yul bcas pa yis/ /phyugs kyi g.yang nyams 'bru bcud mi bzang ste/ 'thab rtsod mang zhing zhe 'gras mang du 'byung
/ /matson cha dar bas rgyan cha mtshon la re/ /dgra jag mang zhing rku 'phrog srog gcod byed/ /de ltar rgyal khrims nyams zhing chos khrims zhig pas na/ /bod 'bangs
rnams la mi bde sna tshogs 'byung / /de nas byang chub sems dpas bstan pa'i me ro slong / /sde pa dge 'dun mang

po 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' mang po yis/ /sku gzugs 'di la bsnyen bkur mchod pa byed/ /phyogs bcu kun tu gtsug lag khang skyong zhing / /dam pa'i spyod
pa tshul bzhin byed par 'gyur/ /de nas bdud rigs sprul pa'i ban de yis/ /sde rtsod byas nas dam chos nyams smad de/ /gnas la 'thab ras bskor nas dge 'dun dkor la spyod/
/gtsug lag khang la 'thab ra byed pa dang / /dgon pa'i gnas la 'phrog 'jom byed pa 'byung / /mtshon cha lha rten rnams la thob sha byed/ /dkon mchog gsum gyi rten la yang
zor byed/ /kye hud bstan pa thal ba bzhin du brlag par 'gyur/ /de yis bdud kyi phyogs rnams rgyas pa yis/ /gang zag rnams kyi shes pa bsgyur byas nas/ /mi 'tshams spyod
pa sna tshogs byed par 'gyuur/ /chos pa thams cad 'dre dang thun mong byed/ /sa gzhi 'di yang shin tu rtsub par 'gyur/ /chom rkun mi rgod mang po 'byung bar 'gyur/ /'dre
dang 'dra ba'i mi rgod mang po 'byung / /'di la chos byed rnam par 'tshe bar 'gyur/ /de dus nub kyi phyogs su sku 'khrungs pa'i/ /dge slong bya yi gdong pa can gcig 'byung
/ /bya chub sems dpa'i blo gros sgrub par ldan/ /rin chen bzang po zhes su grags pa des/ /'di la mchod pa bsnyen bkur rgya cher mdzad/ /skor ba phu dud rim gro byed par
'gyur/ /de dus rgyal po 'od kyi mtha' can ni/ /byang chub sems dpa' blo gros bstan pa 'byung / /de yis byang chub sems dpa' paNDi ta/ /bslab pa gsum ldan sdom gsum dag pa
yi/ /mkhas par sgrub pa mngon par brtson pa yis/ /rigs btsun yon tan ldan pa spyan drangs nas/ /sku gzugs 'di la mchod byed phyag kyang 'tshal/ /bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa byed par 'gyur/ /de yis bstan pa shin tu rgyas par mdzad/ /de'i slob ma tshul bzin bzhugs pa yi/ /dge bsnyen dam pa bstan pa'i mnga' dag ni/ /'di la bsnyen bkur byed
cing mchod par 'gyur/ /bstan pa'i mnga' bdag dge bsnyen bkur byed cing mchod par 'gyur/ /bstan pa'i mnga' bdag dge bsnyen dam pa zhig /byang chub sems dpa' 'dzam gling
rgyan grags pa/ /'khor gyi ni stong phrag phyed dang bcu gsum ldan/ /byon nas 'di la bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur/ /de bzhin byang chub sems ldan ston pa mang po skyong /
/de nas rigs pa smra zhing snang ba smra ba yi/ /ston pa rnams ni nam mkha'i skar ma 'dra/ /de nas dkar po'i phyogs rnams mthu chung zhing / /bdud kyi rigs rnams rab tu
rgyas pa yis/ /bdud kyis byin rlabs gang zag mang pa 'byung / /gzi brjid che zhing stobs kyang che ba dang / nus pa che zhing mthu yang che ba dang / /mngon shes phra mo
ldan zhing bden pa'i ngag tsam 'grub/ /de nas rtog chos mang po byed par 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa 'dre chos mang pos dkrug /'dra min chos lugs mang po ston par byed/
/blo gros phyin ci log tu 'gyur bar byed/ /med par lta ba dngos po'i phyogs bzung nas/ /kun rdzob bden pa khyad du bsad nas ni/ /lus ngag dka' thub 'gog par byed pa 'byung
/ /phyogs med rigs med byar med zer ba dang / /rgyud zad rkyen zad lhun grub zer ba dang / /lung ma bstan pa'i lha yang mang po 'byung / /rgyal bas ma gsungs mkhas pas
ma mdzad pa'i/ /lo paN ma bsgyur chos ltar bcos pa 'byung / /med par lta ba'i phung krol gzhi yang yin/ /de ltar

ston pa'i 'dre chos mang po 'byung / /de rnams 'gong pa spun dgu chas dgu gon/ /ra slog khyi slog re ba khre tshe mon gos gon/ /rtse zhu 'ben ldog khyi zhu gon pa 'byung /
/ber ka dbyug pa mang po thogs pa yi/ /bsod snyoms pa zhes grong sgo 'grim pa 'byung / /ka cig lto rgyag ched du dka' thub drag po yis/ /rang gi lus la gnod pa byed pa 'byung
/ /mngon mtshan grags pa sgrog par byed pa yis/ /gsang sngags glu ru len cing sgrog pa 'byung / /dge slong glu dang bro sogs byed pa 'byung / /bsam gtan dran pa nyams
par byed pa 'byung / /med par lta la lta ba rtog par byed/ /smyo thabs can la spyod pa byed pa 'byung / /smra kham can la gdams ngag can du byed/ /rmongs pa rnams la zig
po zer zhing 'du/ /spyod log can la rnal 'byor pa zhes sgrog /lung ma bstan pa'i chos kyi gtam zer zhing / /grags pa myos 'chol chos bshad mkhan du byed/ /'dre rgyud rnams
la rje btsun zer zhing 'khur/ /chos 'dul zer zhing bab col mang po smra/ /'dre lab can la ye shes 'bab ces zer/ /bdud kyi spro skyid byin brlabs zer ba 'byung / /gdams
ngag zer zhing log chos mang po smra/ /gdams ngag zer nas mu stegs gsang tshig ston/ /de ltar log pa'i rgyun la zhugs pa yis/ /bud med pho spyod tho co byed pa 'byung /
/rang lugs nyams shing 'jig pas chos lugs smad/ /de yis ngan song 'gro ba mang por 'gyur/ /sgrod lugs mi shes ngo tsha med par spyod/ /rgyu 'bras bden par mi dge sna tshogs
spyod/ /de ltar spyod log rnams la dad par 'gyur/ /byas pa'i chos kyis sangs rgyas mi rgya zhes zer/ /ma byas lhun grub rang byung dgos so zer/ /byed par ma nus tshe
na de la dad pa mang / dad pas bslus nas phungs pas snang zhes bsad nas bslus/ /dge bshes dang ltar snang ba'i yid 'grogs khrid/ /log pa'i lam zhugs ngan 'gror khrid/ /sngags
pa kha cig sngags la rtsings chos byed/ /dam chos yon la blangs nas gsang ba sgrog /gser chos zer zhing chos la rin thang gcod/ /la las ma thos rgyud la bshadang pa
byed/ /la la dbang ma thob par dbang bskur byed/ /bsnyen bkur chags shing 'dod la zhen pa yin/ /rlung bcud ma 'dus sems dbang ma 'dus pa/ /de dag mchod rten bshig dang khyad
par med/ /la la dge slong shes rab ye shes ni/ /bud med dag la len byed cing bskur/ /sdom brtson bshig nas dmyal bar 'phen par 'gyur/ /de ni log pa'i chos la spyod pa
yin/ /bsnyen bkur grags 'dod dam chos byed pa dang / /nyan thos bsam pa byed dang sgom pa dang / /chos bka' nyams pas ngan 'gror 'gro bar 'gyur/ /tshul khrims nyams dang
dam tshig nyams par 'gyur/ /chos bka' nyams dang spyod pa nyams pa yis/ /bshes gnyen bsten pa thams cad ngan 'gror 'gro/ /btsun pa'i chos gos gon zhing bslab pa bral/ /de
'dra'i tshul 'chos byed pa'i mi/ /dad rdzas longs spyod byed cing dkon mchog bslu/ /rang nyid ngan 'gror rang gis 'phen/ /bde ba'i longs spyod bsags pas ngan song 'gro/
/la la bde ba'i chos zer rang nyid las ngan byed/ /la la sngags btsun zer nas tshul khrims nyams/ /la la cha lugs tsam gon tshong dang khe spogs byed/ /cha lugs bzang pos
chos rkun rdzun spyod byed/ /kye ma sangs rgyas brdzus nas dmyal bar 'gro/ /de'i bcos ma bag tsam sna tshogs

'byung / /sangs rgyas bstan pa rim gyis 'jig par 'gyur/ /yun ring mi gnas rtag tu de rnams bstan/ /kye ma de dus mi lus thob pa kun/ /sems stobs ma zhan rtsol ba ma chung bar/
/yang dag dge ba'i bshes gnyen dam pa sten/ /des gsungs pa tshad mar nges par zungs/ /thugs kyis dgongs la spyod pa'i rjes su 'brang / /mi rtag 'chi bar ngais kyis dam
chos sgrub pa mdzod/ /nam 'aci rang dbang med pas dam chos myur du sgrubs/ /dngos po mi la'ang ma lta dam chos snying la zhog /rten 'brel 'phrul 'khor bden pas dam chos
sgrubs/ /sdug bsngal sdig pa 'byung bas las ngan spong bar mdzod/ /kun rdzob rgyu 'bras bden pas tshul khrims sdom pa srungs/ /'khor dgu nyon mongs spongs la byang chub
sems ma btang / /srog gi phyir yang byang chub spong mi bya/ /'khor ba'i gnas lugs spong zhing de la skyo bar gyis/ /'gro ba ma lus byams dang snying rjes zungs/ /de rnams
don du byang chub sems bskyed cing / /byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa ma nyams srungs/ /chos kun rang bzhin spros bral 'gag med sgoms/ /don dam kun rdzob bden gnyis zung
'jug gis/ /bla med byang chub lam la tshud par mdzod/ /khyim las rab tu byung ba'i chos mdzad kun/ /rang dang spyod pa ma nyams de nyid rnal ma yin/ /mngon sum mu stegs
spyod pa ma mdzad par/ /rang gis rang tshod bzung la rang sems drang por spyod/ /stong nyid tshig la ma zhen bden tshig rnam la mar spyod/ /chos rnams kha la ma 'khyer de
nyid rtogs par spyod/ /gzhan la sgro bskur ma 'debs rang sems dpang du tshugs/ /chos rnams bzang ngan ma 'byed de nyid gcig tu slobs/ /de ltar spyad na bkra shis bde legs
'byung / /gzugs sku 'di yang byang chub sems dpas ni/ /lo ni nyis brgyar bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur/ /de nas bstan pa'i sgron me ni/ /ston pa rnams kyis bsnyen bkur byed
par 'gyur/ /de nas bstan pa'i sgron me byang sems dge slong chen po ni/ /dam pa mang pos bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur/ /de rnams nang nas bsnyen bkur cher mdzad pa/ /dge
slong byang chub sems dpa' chen po ni/ /shar lho'i mtshams su sku 'khrungs pa'i/ /gsang sngags 'chang ba'i rnal 'byor chen po ni/ /smin grol mdzad pa'i skyes bu dam pa yin/
/zhal yang bsgyur zhing bsnyen bkur dam pa mdzad/ /de dag bsnyen cing bkur ba chen po mdzad/ /ci phyir 'phags pa'i gang zag yin zhe na/ /sangs rgyas dag la mdzad pa mang
po mdzad/ /'phags pa rnams la de ma mdzad/ /de'i phyir na 'di rnams 'phags pa'i gang zag go/ /de ltar 'phags pa'i gang zag rnams 'byung zhing / /'khor ni legs par gnas
pa'i gsung rab dang / /ston pa'i sku gzugs dngos su bzhugs pa dang / /ri bo yon tan can yang 'di na yod/ /tsa ri tsa gong bde mchog rang byung dang / /rdo chu rin po che
yang 'di na yod/ /ti se'i gangs la dgra bcom lnga brgya yod/ /bdud rtsi'i chu yang ri bo de la yod/ /bdud rtsi'i 'chi sos sman yang de la yod/ /gye re yar 'phrang brag la
yig drug rang byon yod/ /mkha' 'gro'i phyag rgya ri bo de la yod/ /ma pham mcho la klu rgyal byang chub sems/ /chu bo yon tan can yang de las 'bab/ /ri rgyal rtsi rgyal
grags pa'ang de la yod/ /la ngag mtsho la rgyal po ra ma Na dang srin po 'thab pa yod/ /khri shor mtsho la klu

rgyal byang chub sems/ /chu yin chen po kun la phan par mdzad/ /gnam mtsho phyug mo'i nang klu sman byang chub sems/ /thang la'i brag la dgra bcom mang pa yod/ snubs matso
gling dgu'i nang na klu rgyal byang chub sems/ /ha bo'i gangs la dgra bcom mang po yod/ /gnyi bdag gnod sbyin gang ba bzang po gnas/ /ri mtho sa gtsang gangs ri gnyan gyis
bskor/ /sgra dag skad snyan sam skri ta dang mtshungs/ /rgya skad chos skad sbyar ba'i sgra dang mtshungs/ /yangs shing tha gru che bde'i spyad dang yod/ /de ltar yon tan
ldan pa kha ba can gyi yul/ /de dbus skyes pa'i mi lus thob pa rnams/ /dam chos slob la rtsol ba ma zhan cig /sngon gyi smon lam dag pas de 'dra'i yul skyes nas/ /dad
gus mos pa yod par ldan pa ni/ /gzhan bya mi dgos sku gzugs 'di la gus pa thams cad ni/ /phyir mi ldog par rgyal bas lung bstan pas/ /'di la gus pas mchod cig bod 'bangs
rnams/ /bdag gis de skad skul ma 'debs byed pa/ /snyan phyir ma yin grags pa'i phyir ma yin/ /snying rje kun nas bslangs pa'i tsig yin pas/ /gus pas spyi bos btud de blang
bar mdzod/ /ces gsungs te/ rgyal po yab yum gsum po jo bo thugs rje chen po rang byung lnga ldan la thim par gyur te/ blon po sna chen po dang bod kyi blon po glo ba nye
ba rnams na re/ nged dang rgyal po zhal ma mjal zer na/ nga'i lha thugs rje chen po la gsol ba thob cig ci bsam don du 'grub par 'gyur zhes gyis shig lha gcig khri btsun
zhal phyir log mdzad nas sna chen po la/ bod kyi blon po glo ba nye ba rnams nged lha gcig khri btsun dang zhal ma mjal zer na/ nga'i lha thugs rje chen po la phyag gyis
shig ci bsam don du 'grub par 'gyur ro gsungs/ lha gcig kong jo zhal log byas nas sna chen po bod kyi blon po glo ba ne ba rnams na re/ nged lha gcig kong jo dang zhal
ma mjal zer na/ nga'i lha thugs rje chen po la phyag gyis shig ci bsam don du 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /gsungs nas yab yum gsum ga lha la thim par gyur to/ /de nas rgyal pos phyag
gnyis brkyangs nas lha gcig gnyis kyi spyi bor bzhag pas/ lha gcig khri btsun pad ma dkar po 'dab ma brgyad pa yi ge bam gyis mtshan par gyur to/ /lha gcig kong jo uta?pal
sngon po yi ge Ta~M gyis mtshan pa gcig tu gyur to/ /rgyal po zhal sgo ngos su log mdzad nas spyan zur zhig gzigs te/ jo bo thugs rje chen po'i rtsar gshegs pa dang
/ rgyal po'i dbu'i a mi de ba dang / jo bo thugs rje chen po dang rang byung lnga ldan gyi dbu'i a mi de ba gnyis po mnyam khad de gda'/ thugs rje chen po'i thugs ka nas
'od zer zla ba nya ba lta bu tsam pa zhig shar ba de las 'od 'phros nas song bas/ ra sa'i phyi nang thams cad khyab pas/ steng khang gi rta mgrin dkar po'i sku las 'od
zer dung lta bu byung ste ra sa'i phyi nang thams cad 'od kyi dra bas khyab par gyur to/ /yang steng khang dbu rtse'i sgo ngos la bcom ldan 'das mi bskyod rdo rje'i sku las
'od zer gser lta bu byung nas kyang de bzhin no/ /yang 'og khang gi sangs rgyas sman bla'i sku las kyang 'od zer baiDUrya lta bu 'phros nas kyang de bzhin no/ /'og khang
dbu rtse'i lho ngos nas 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sku las 'od zer gur kum gyi mdog lta bu 'phros nas kyang de

bzhin no/ /de nas khro rgyal sme ba brtsegs lapa'i thugs ka nas 'od zer 'phros pas/ 'od zer re re'i sna la khro chung re re bzhugs nas ra sa'i phyir nang thams cad khengs par
gyur nas kyang de bzhin no/ /gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje'i thugs ka nas 'od zer mthing ga 'phros pas kyang de bzhin no/ /byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo'i thugs ka nas 'od
zer 'phros pas kyang de bzhin no/ /yang dngul gyi byams pa mched gsum gyi thugs ka nas 'od zer 'phros pas kyang de bzhin no/ /ra sa'i gtsug lag khang thams cad khyab par
gyur to/ /de ltar gyur pa dang phyi nas blon po bcu drug po slebs te/ rgyal po'i ber khri thog na cam me 'dug rgyal po sku mi bzhugs par mthong bas/ der blon po bse ru gung
ston na re/ sna jachen po khyod rgyal po'i sku srung la bzhag pa yin pa la/ rgyal po gar gshegs zer ro/ /tshig de lan gsum du bzlas kyang sna chen po snyam na/ tshul de
lta bu su la bzlas kyang yid ches par mi 'gyur snyam nas/ mgo bstums te ngo gnong gnag par gyur to/ /de la blon po bal gyi gtan ring po ( sbas sgyid thag ring mo) na re/
sna chen po khyod bod kyi zhang blon rnams kyi bka' lan gsum du gcog gam ske gcad dam zer nas/ jo mo mong bza' snyam na/ sna chen po ske bcad na bod thams cad 'thabs nas/
yab rgyal po ni lha la thim/ sras ni chung / rgyal khrims zhig nas 'gro snyam nas/ khong rgyal po yab yum gsum ka lha jo bo thugs rje chen po'i thugs kar thim thal byas
nas/ der sna chen po'i bsam pa la/ jo mos shags 'byed pa 'dug snyam nas ji ltar gyur pa rnams dang / gsungs par gyur pa rnams smras so/ /de'i dpang po la rgyal po'i ber
kyang mngon gsum mo/ /jo mo gsum gyi phyag rten yang mngon gsum mo/ /jo mo mong bza' khri lcam yang mngon sum du yod byas pas blon po chen po rnams yid ches te/ yang blon
po dpal gyi brtan ( sbas sgyid thag ring mo ) nas/ rgyal po spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa yin pa'i gtan tshigs ci yod pa yin zer ro/ /blon po thon mi sam bho Da mi chung
na re/ rgyal po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa yin pa'i gtan tshigs gsum nga la yod de/ de pho brang byams pa mi 'gyur ba na sku bltams pa'i dus su rgyal po'i dbu
la a mi de ba'i dbu yod pa a mi de ba'i dbu la thod gsol te 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dngos yin bya ba dang / pho brang khra 'brug lha khang de nyid bzhengs pa'i dus su/
mchod rten dbu lha'i rtsa na dge slong gi gzugs gcig 'dug pa la phyag byas nas de ngo mtshar ram byas pas/ dge slong de kha byad shin tu ngan te rnam 'phrul 'di ngo mtshar
ram zer nas mchod rten dbu lha po lag sor la brten pas/ rgyal po na re/ khyod sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i bslab pa la zhugs pa ngo mtshar te/ nga rgyal srid skyong ba'i
rgyal srid skyong rgyal po'i spyi gtsug gi lha 'di ngo mtshar ram byas te dbu thod phud nas a mi de ba bstan pas/ dge slong na re/ lha gcig las mi 'dug pa zer nas/ der
thod pa dung khang kha phye ste dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i lha tshogs rnams bstan/ de'i tshe rgyal po a mi de ba bzhugs pas/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug kyang / li
yul du dge slong gnyis kyis 'phags pa 'jam dpal bsgrubs pas/ 'jam dpal gyi zhal nas nga la khyod ci byed zer/

'phags pa spyan ras gzigs zhal blta bar 'tshal zhus pas/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug da lta bod na rgyal po byed kyi yod/ der song la zhal la ltos gsungs nas lung bstan/ de
ma thag tu khong gnyis kyis phyag rten khyer nas yong bas/ yar lung u rar phyin tsa na rgyal khrims kyis chad pa phog pa rnams la nyes pa len pa'i mgo 'breg pa dang / mig
'byin pa dang / sgyid ma 'breg pa dang / lag pa 'breg pa la sogs pa'i chad pa gcod pa mang po mthong bas/ der 'di rnams ci yin byas pas bod kyi rgyal pos khrims kyi chad
pa gcod pa yin zer bas/ 'o na bod kyi rgyal po sdig pa can du 'dug 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa ma yin par 'dug zer nas phyir log de nas yang rgyal po lha sa
la bzhugs zer nas/ sbu ru'i dan 'bag gi thang la phyin pas/ yang rgyal pos chad pa bcad pa'i mig phyung ba dang / mgo 'breg pa dang / yan lag bcad pa phung por spungs pa
mthong / phyir log la 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis rang re spyan ras gzigs dang ma sprad par bdud dang sprad 'dug zer zhing rgyal po la rngan bgrang gin phyin pas rgyal po ra
sa na bzhugs palas mkhyen te/ nang blon zhig la chibs pa gur nag po bskyon nas khyod song la dan 'bag gi thang la mi cha byad mi 'dra ba gnyis 'gro yin yod de gnyis nan
gyis bos la shog gsungs nas/ de gnyis pos nas yong ba dang / rgyal pos de la li'i skad du smras te/ khyod gnyis ci byed du 'ongs/ gtad sa ci yod gsungs pas/ 'phags pa 'jam
dpal gyis lung bstan nas spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug da lta bod na rgyal po byed kyi yod der song zer 'ongs lags/ spyan ras gzigs bdud du gyur bya ba'i rngan chos mang
po smras pas/ rgyal po na re/ 'o na khyed nga'i dbu'i a mi de ba lta bar 'dod dam gsungs pas/ de lta bar 'dod 'tshal byas pas/ lha sa'i ne'u chung bye ma'i gling du khrid
nas dbu thod phud nas a mi de ba de gnyis la bstan pas yid ches te/ 'o na mig 'byin pa dang / mgo 'breg pa dang / sgyid pa gcod pa la sogs pa byed pa ji ltar lags zhes zhus
pas/ nga'i 'bangs 'khor nag po 'di rnams zhi bas mi 'thul bar sprul pa byas nas drag pos 'dul ba'i tshul byas pa yin/ da khyod rang mgo dang / mig dang / yan lag bcad
pa la sogs pa sprul pa yin pas bltar song dang / ngas ni rgyal srid bzung nas sems can la'ang gnod lapa byed ma myong gsungs pas/ khong gnyis kyis bltar phyin pas/ mgo dang
yan lag bcad pa'i phung po rnams rdo dang g.yam pa la sogs par song 'dug pas/ de sprul pa yin par shes nas khong gnyis skyengs so/ /rgyal pos gnyis la dngos grub ci 'dod
sbyin no gsungs pas/ kho bo cag gnyis la gzhan ci yang mi 'tshal te/ slar li yul du 'gro bar 'tshal zhes zhus pas/ 'o na khyed gnyis bye ma bre re thu bar thums la mgo
bo nga'i spus mo la sngas gyis shig gsungs/ de skad nyan nas byas pas de gnyis kyi gdong la phyag gis byil byil byas pas bye ma gser du bsgyur thu bar bzung gda'/ de nas
skad cig la li yul du phyin pa li'i lung bstan chen po nas lung de skad bstan gda' byas pas/ der blon po thams cad yid ches te thams cad gros byas nas phyi rabs pa rnams
kyi don du rgyal po lo brgyad cu rtsa bzhi la sku 'das/ li yul gyi za mo rar sku gshegs byas nas stag sgro

gser gyis bkang zhing rta la bkal nas mang sor bzhugs/ bod kyi blon po dang grong khyer ba na re/ 'od zer gyis ra sa'i phyi nang thams cad khyab pa ni ra sa'i gtsug lag khang
la thim nas bzhugs par kha 'chams/ dga' ston chen po yang byas so/ /de'i dus su rgyal blon rnams gleng blangs/ lha gcig kong jo'i rgya nag gi gtsug lag gi rtsis 'di ngo
mtshar che/ bud med kyi yon tan yin pas rtsis la rgya ma chod pa yod dam snyam nas rgyal blon rnams gros byas pa'i lo tsA ba pho nyar brdzangs te/ lha gcig kong jo'i yab
rgyal por blar rtsis la mkhas pa gcig bod du brdzangs par zhu bya ba'i zhu ba btang bas/ de rjes bod la rgyal po'i bla rtsis su rgya g.yu bzher btsan pa zhes bya ba brdzangs
nas btang ste bod du yong bas/ bod rgyal po'i blar rtsis pa byas so/ /rgya rtsis de ltar dar bar byas so/ /de nas rgya nag gi yul du bod kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam
po grongs byas pa dang / dbon sras byon pa dang / lha gcig kong jo grongs bya ba thos nas/ da gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne slar rgya yul du spyan 'dren/ mir skyes pa thams
cad cham la 'bebs pa zer nas dmag gi grangs grabs byas pas/ bod kyis rgya'i so so kha bsrungs par bas thos nas/ yul dbus su pho nya btang ste sa thag ring po'i zlo thos
phrin du springs pa/ bod du rgya'i dmag 'dren/ gser gyi shA kyang mu ne slar rgya yul du spyan 'dren/ bod cham la 'bebs zer bas/ nged kyi rgyal po kha nged kyis rgya'i so
kha thub thub mi 'dra'o/ /bod kyi bla blon rnams 'dun ma ma chung zhig zer ba byung ba dang / blon po rnams gros byas te ra sa'i jo mo mi bskyod rdo rje dang / ra mo che'i
jo bo shAkya mu ne lha brjes na grags drag zer bar 'chams te/ shAkya mu ne mi bzhis btegs te ra mo che nas phag gdong na mar chu la spyan drangs ra sa 'phrul snang du
bzhugs/ so phag gis legs brtsigs te mi mngon par bzhugs su bcug de'i sgo gdong la 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sku gcig bris nas bzhag go/ /bka' chems kyi yi ge nas rgyal po
srong btsan sgam pos ra sa 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang chen mo la sogs pa mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang / yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang / mtha' yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag
khang la sogs pa'i gtsug lag khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs pa dang / jo bo shAkya zhal gnyis dang / byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo dang / rang byung tsan dan gyi jo mo sgrol
ma rnams spyan ji ltar drangs pa dang / rgyal mes dbon rnams kyis dam pa'i chos kyi dbu brnyes srol btod pa'i chos 'byung rgyas pa'o/ /rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i sras
mang srong mang btsan/ rgyal po de dgong lo bcu dgu la sras gung srong gung btsan gzigs nas yab 'das/ mes kyis rgyal srid bzung / de'i sras 'dus srong mang po rje glong
nam 'phrul gyi rgyal po yab sras de rnams kyis kyang / yab mes kyi srol ka bzung nas gtsug lag khang re re yang bzhengs/ mnga' thang rgyal srid kyang je cher song / de'i
sras khri lde gtsug btsan ag tshom gyi ring la bsam yas ka chu'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs te/ pho brang btab/ lha khang bzhengs pa ni/ 'ching bu mchims phu rnam ral gling
gi khri rtse/ brag dmar 'gran bzang / ma sa gong gi lha khang dang / lha sa skar chung bzhengs/ sras 'jam 'jang

tsha lha dbon la rgya nag ho nang hu bya ba nas rgya nag po'i sras mo gyim shing kong jo btsun mor blangs nas bod du byon pa la/ rgya'i bkra shis khri sing khri sgo nas chas
nas byon dus/ dngul dkar gyi me long phyis nas gzigs pas/ sras rgyal bu 'jam 'jang tsha lha dbon te mi bu mi 'dra ba lha'i sras 'dra ba zhig 'dug par gzigs/ rgya bod sa
mtshams su byon dus dngul dkar gyi me long phyis nas gzigs pas/ lha sras 'jam 'jang tsha lha dbon de chibs rta rgyugs pas chibs las lhung nas grongs pas/ mes khri lde btsug
btsan ag chom bzhugs pa gzigs te/ kha ning gi lha sras 'jam 'jang tsha lha dbon de mi'i bu mi 'dra lha'i sras 'dra ba la/ da ni yab bgres po dbu skra thams cad dkar po/
zhal thams cad ni sma ra dkar pos khebs pa/ zhal gang na yod ngo mi shes pa de 'dra ba zhig gzigs pas/ der byad dang me long gi blta bya yin nam gsungs nas yar byon nas
slebs tsa na/ sras rgya bu grongs nas mi bzhugs pas/ der rgyal pos lha gcig gyim shing kong jo la 'dam ka gsum gsungs pa ni/ khyod kyi khyo rgyal bu ni rta rgyugs pas bsnad
nas grongs/ da khyod sa thag ring po nas yong bas/ yang na nged kyi blon po rigs bzang ba nor che ba/ pho rgod legs pa gcig la sdod dam/ yang na nga mi rgan la sdod
dam/ yang na rgya'i yul du 'gro/ rgya'i yul du ldog na ni ngas rdzongs chen po byas pa gtong gsungs pas/ lha gcig kong jos rgyal po mes ag tshom rang la sdod par bdams so//mnga'
thang yang je cher song / ag tshom gyi ring la bla mchod du rgya nag ha shang spyan drangs lha khang bzhengs pa ni/ lha sa mkhar brag brag dmar 'gran bzang / ka chu/
'chings mchims phu gnam ral/ gling gi khri rtse dang lnga bzhengs/ khri rtse mdo khams su bzhengs/ dbus gtsang du bzhi'o/ /der yab kyi blon po mchims khri thog rje 'bar
dang / cog ro skyes bzang rgyal dang / sna nam gyi zhang khrom pa skyes dang gsum gyis chos rnams bsnubs/ ka chu dang mkhar brag gi lha khang bshig de gsum la dkon mchog
gi bka' chad byung ste/ rgyal po chos la dad pa skyes/ der 'bangs blon po rnams kyang blo 'gyur/ sbas gsal snang mang yul gyi kha blon la btang ba ltar byas nas lo tsA
bslabs te/ slob dpon bho dhi sa twa shan ta rakShi ta spyan drangs/ de tshun chad slar chos byas te/ dkon mchog gsum gyi rten btsugs/ rgya dkar nag gi lo tsA mkhas pa mang
po spyan drangs/ glegs bam mang po bsgyur/ sad mi mi bdun la sogs pa brgya bzhi bcu rab tu byung ste btsun par bcug chos gra chen po btsugs/ chos gtsigs kyi rdo ring chen
po bsnan/ sgrom bcu gsum gtsigs kyi yi ge bsnan/ der mes ag tshom gyis rgya'i lha sras gyim shing kong jo bzhes pa la sras rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan gzigs so/ /'di
ni sa bcu'i dbang phyug 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa yin te/ 'di'i ring la dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ de'i lo rgyus ni 'phags pa 'jam
dpal gyis bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su dam pa'i chos dar zhing rgyas par bya ba'i phyir/ de yang rgyal po dbang che gcig tu sprul nas mnga' 'og tu bsdus te/ sems
can gyi don rgya chen po dang bod kha ba can la don byed nus par dgongs nas/ rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga nas

ye shes kyi spyan gyis gzigs pas/ bod yul gyi rgyal po khri lde gtsug btsan bya ba'i bka' 'og tu 'dug par gzigs so/ /der rgyal po khri srong lde gtsug btsan dang / gyim shing
kong jo gnyis pho brang brag dmar na rin po che'i khri steng na gzims nas bzhugs pa la 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi thugs kha nas 'od zer sna lnga'i sna la/ gser gyi khye'u
chung tshon gang ba zhig gyim shing kong jo'i mngal du spros nas zhugs pa las/ der yang yum gyi mnal lam na shar phyogs nas 'od nyi ma shar ba lta bu zhig byung nas mngal
du zhugs pa rmis/ tshul de lta bu yab rgyal po la smras pas/ bar snang gi lha phran zhig rang re'i bur 'ong ba yin te yong gsungs so/ /rmi lam de shin tu bzang gsungs nas
yab rgyal po shin tu dgyes so/ /de nas yum lus mi bde ba gang yang med par 'gul ba dang 'phar ba dang 'phrig pa la sogs pa byung ba dang / shes pa gsal ba/ lus yang ba/
bde ba/ nyon mongs mi skye bar gyur to/ /de nas zla ba dgu ngo dang bcu na yum la na tsha med par pho brang brag dmar du sras khri song lde btsan sku bltams so/ /de yang
tshems dung so 'khor ba yod pa/ dbu skra mthon mthing g.yas su 'khyil ba shin tu mdzes pa lha'i sras lta bu zhig 'khrungs so/ /rta'i lo dpyid zla ra ba'i tshe skar ma rgyal
