gyi nam langs nyi ma shar ba la sku 'khrungs/ mtshan ni khri srong lde'u btsan du gsol lo/ /de nas rgyal bu dgung lo lnga lon pa na sna nam zhang khrom pa skyes dang
/ sna nam pa rnams rgyal bu khri srong lde btsan nged kyi tsha bo yin zer nas rgya mo la dbang che byas/ rgyal bu 'phrog tu byung ba la/ der rgyal blon kun nyi ma gcig thams
cad tshogs nas dga' ston chen po byas nas/ sras rgyal bu la khyed kyi ma rgya mo yin nam/ sna nam pa'i sras yin ngos 'dzin tu bcug pa las/ sras rgyal po khri srong lde
btsan na re/ gral rim gyis phyag g.yas pa gdengs nas/ khri srong lde btsan rgya tsha la/ /sna nam zhang gis ci zhig bgyi/ /zhes gral rim gyis bsgrags so/ /de nas rig pa'i
gnas thams cad mkhyen cing dgung lo bcu gsum lon pa dang yab khri lde gtsug btsan dgung du gshegs so/ /der sras rgyal bu khri srong lde btsan rgyal por mnga' gsol lo/
/jo mo gsum khab tu bzhes pa tshe spong bza' me tog sgron dang / pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun dang / 'brom bza' byang chub sman dang gsum lags so/ /de nas lo bdun 'bangs
dang so tshigs phyi'i so kha srung ba dang / nang gi so tshigs mdzad cing rgyal srid bskyangs so/ /de nas lo nyi shu glang gi lo la dam pa'i chos bya ba'i thugs dgongs skyes
te/ sngon gyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam pos kyang bod mun pa'i smag rum 'dra ba la/ gtsug lag khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs/ dam pa'i chos bsgyur/ bal yul nas jo bo
mi bskyod rdo rje dang / byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo dang / rang byung tsan dan gyi jo mo sgrol ma dang / rgya nag nas gser gyi lha shAkya mu ne gdan drangs/ dam pa'i chos
kyi srol btod/ bod kha ba can gyi don mdzad cing bka' drin che ba lags par gda'/ da ni ngas kyang dam pa'i chos byas la dar zhing rgyas par bya snyam pa'i thugs dgongs
skyes nas/ dang thog mar dkon mchog gi rten zhig bzhengs dgos par dgongs kyang / blon po rnams gdug pa che zhing

chos la shin tu gnag pa las/ de la thabs ji lta bu'i sgo nas mdzad pa ni rgyal blon thams cad la dga' ston rgya chen po mdzad/ sngon rgyal mes dbon rnam gnyis kyi mdzad srol
las thabs ji ltar byas pa las glengs te/ las thabs ji ltar bya ba dang / rgyal khrims chos khrims ji ltar bya ba'i bya lugs glengs pa la/ rgyal pos blon po rnams la 'dam
ka btang ba ni/ shar ri rgyal po gdan la bzhugs pa 'dra ba'i rtse mor shel gyi mkhar zhang po rgyal yul mthong ba zhig brtsig dang gcig g.yas ru gtsang po zangs kyi sbubs
su 'jug dang gnyis/ shod kyi je ma bres 'jal dang gsum/ has po ri zangs kyis phur phub nas gzer thams cad kyi mgo nang du bstan pa byed dang bzhi/ 'bal mo grog po gser
gyis 'gengs dang lnga / yom 'bog gi thang la lha khang spa ru tsam zhig bzhengs dang drug 'dam ka btang ba las/ blon po rnams chos la gnag cing lha khang dkon mchog gi rten
bzhengs par mi spro mod kyi/ gzhan rnams mi 'grub pa'i stobs kyis lha khang rtsig par 'chams so/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la nga'i thugs dam gtsug lag khang 'gro
ba sems can gyi 'dren pa dam pa gcig bzhengs pa dpe ji lta bu zhig la blangs nas bzhengs snyam pa dang / der mkhan po bho dhi sa twa dang rgyal po gnyis glengs pas/ mkhan
po'i zhal nas ro langs gser gyi sgrub pa byed pa'i phyi pa mu stegs pa'i lta ba 'dzin pa gcig gis/ ro sgrub byas pas ro grub pa dang / ro de gser du 'gro ba la/ de'i
lce de shes rab kyi ral grir song nas/ de'i yu ba nas bzung bas nam mkha'/ bar snang / sa gzhi/ gling gzhan gar yang thogs pa med par 'gro bas/ de bsgrubs te gling bzhi thams
cad la bltas nas/ gang legs pa'i bkod pa blangs nas de ltar dpe byas te bzhengs pa 'thad gsungs pas/ de dge tshul gcig gis mu stegs ro sgrub byed pa de la grogs por
chags de bya dga' byin nas/ ro langs la dge tshul des 'dzings pas ro da'ei lce dge tshul de'i sos zin par byung bas/ de shes rab kyi ral grir song ba'i yu ba nas dge tshul
gyis bzung ste/ nam mkha' la thogs pa med par song ba'i yu ba nas dge tshul gyis bzung ste/ nam mkha' la thogs pa med par song ba las gling bzhi bye ba phrag brgya thams
cad bltas nas/ ri rab kyi steng na sum cu rtsa gsum gyi gtsug lag khang la dpe byas nas bzhengs pa la/ de'i sa gzhi mkhan po bho dhi sa twa shan ra rakShi tas byin gyis
brlabs te/ rgyal po la khyed kyis sa rkos shig gsungs nas rgyal pos sa brkos pa dang / sa'i zhag dang sa lu mang po byung bas rgyal po'i zhal du gsol/ dbu la yang byugs
so/ /de ltar btsan po dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gtsig stag gi lo la rmang bting nas bzhengs pa la/ rgyal gar yul nas mkhan po bho dhi sa twa byang chub sems dpa' de spyan 'dren
pa la/ rgyal po khri lde gtsug btsan ag tshom gyi ring la bod kyi lo tsA la mnga' ba snyags dznyAn ku ma ra dri med zla shar bya ba dang g.yog po gnyis la gser phye bre
gang zhu rten du phul nas byon pas sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs kyang / bod kyi lha 'dre gnod sbyin mthu bo che rnams gdug pa che bas rtsig tu ma btub pa las rgyal pos slob
dpon chen po lags/ bdag gi g.yar dam dkon mchog gsum gyi mchod pa'i rten gtsug lag khang ji ltar bzhengs pas

'grub pa lags/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas/ da byang chub sems kyi zhi bas 'gro ba sems can gyi don byed pas mi thul bas/ 'di na nged rang rgyal po dang skye ba snga ma la smon
lam lhan gcig tu btab pa'i o rgyan gyi rgyal po inda? bo dhi'i sras mdzad pa'i sprul pa'i sku pad ma 'byung gnas zhe bya ba/ rgya gar yul gyi tshur mtha'/ bal po'i yul gyi
phar mtha' na/ yang lo shod kyi brag phug na mchog gi sgrub pa mdzad kyin bzhugs pas de spyan drangs na lha 'dre gdug rtsub can thams cad 'thul zhing rgyal po'i bsam pa
'grub par mchi/ de yang ngas bzlas pa skad ma zer zhes rgyal po la smras so/ /de nas rgyal pos nang 'khor blon 'bangs rnams la/ mdang gsum ngi rmi lam na rgya gar dang bal
po'i so mtshams yang le shod kyi brag phug na o rgyan rgyal po'i sras mdzad pa'i slob dpon pad ma sam bha ba bya ba mthu rtsal che la dgongs pa zab pa sprul pa'i sku gcig
bzhugs pas de spyan drangs na/ nga'i bsam pa 'grub par rmis pas/ de spyan 'dren dgos pas khyed bang chen mi gsum gtong zhes bka' bstsal pas/ blon 'bangs rnams kyang de
'thad do zhes thag bcad do/ /bang chen pa khas len pa ma byung bas rgyal pos bka' bstsal te/ sngas mang rje gsal snang dang / se 'og lha lung gnyis g.yog po gsum dang bcas
la gser phye bre gang bskur/ bar gyi lam rgyags dang bcas lam du zhugs pa dang / slob dpon gyi spyan sngar srung ma rnams kyis bskul ba dang thugs kyis mkhyen pas/ bod
yul has po ri'i rtser bod kyi rgyal po lha sras btsan pos gtsug lag khang gcig bzhengs su gsol bas slob dpon chen po'i spyan sngar mang chen pa 'ong bas de rnams thang
chad nyon mongs pas slob dpon chen po mang yul gung thang tsam du gshegs pa zhu zhes srung ma rnams kyis bskul bas der slob dpon gyis rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' la byon nas
mang yul gung thang la zla ba gnyis bzhugs pa dang / bang chen pa rnams dang mjal nas slob dpon gyis mkhyen bzhin du khyed su yin/ gar 'gro gsungs pa dang / sbas mang
rje gsal snang gis nged bod kyi lha sras btsan pos slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas spyan 'dren du btang ba lags khyed rang lags sam zhus pas/ 'o na de nga yin/ zla ba gsum gyi
gong nas srung ma rnams kyis bskul te/ khyod lha sras btsan po'i bang chen pa rnams nyon mongs kyis dogs nas 'dir bsdad pa yin/ khyed la sku yod 'bul rgyu ci yod pa phul
cig gsungs pas/ phyag 'tshal skor ba byas te gus pas gser phul lo/ /da ci yod phul cig gsungs pas/ rgyal pos ni de las ma bskur lags/ nged mang chen pa gsum gyis lus ngag
yid gsum 'khor gsum yongs su dag tu 'bul zhes phyag 'tshal skor ba byas/ zhabs spyi bor blangs nas zhu ba phul ba/ slob dpon chen po sprul pa'i sku lags/ bdag cag bod
kyi lha sras btsan pos thugs dam 'gro ba sems can yongs kyi bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing gtsug lag khang gcig bzhengs pa la slob dpon bho dhi sa twas sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs
pas/ bod kyi lha srin gdug rtsub che bas bzhengs su ma btub par/ bod kyi rgyal po'i thugs dgongs sgrub pa dang / gdug pa can tshar gcod pa dang 'dul ba'i don du gshegs
par zhu 'tshal zhes zhu ba phul bas/ slob dpon thugs dgyes te nga khyed kyi dad pa dang gus pa dang g.yo zog

med pa la dga' bas khyed rnams sad pa yin/ nga la snang ba thams cad gser du yod gsungs nas/ phyag g.yas pa gung thang gi phyogs su brkyangs pas g.yas phyogs kyi ri thams cad
g.yom du bsgyur/ phyag g.yon pa nub phyogs su brkyangs pas sa rdo thams cad gzi mchong ron po che gser g.yur bsgyur nas bang chen pa kun la'ang byin no/ /nga'i rdzu 'phrul
'di ltar che ste/ khyed rnams yid dang ches te 'ong / yid chas par gyis shig rgyal po'i bsam pa 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /khyod kyi gser gyis nga la bya rgyu med/ 'on kyang
mnga' bdag gi dgongs pa rdzogs par bya ba'i don du re zhig blang gi gsungs nas/ mang yul dang bal yul gyi phyogs su gtor bas dus phyis bod kyi gser dngul thams cad bal
yul phyogs su 'dor bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/ /der bsgyur ba'i gser g.yu bang chen pa kun la byin pas kun rdzun yin nam snyam/ so sor kha phye nas bltas pas bden par snang
ste thams cad yid ches so/ /slob dpon pad ma'i thugs rjes bod yul du dpon slob rnams byon pa dang / mang yul don khar phyags phebs te/ de la stod mnga' ris kyi lha srin
mthu bo che rnams 'dus te/ jo bo gyer rgod la 'khor gnam sman bdun stong gis bskor ba/ gangs sman zhu le ma stong / g.ya' sman si le ma stong / spang sman yal le ma stong
/ brag sman khrol le ma stong / thang sman thor re ma stong / chu sman zu le ma stong / mtsho sman rgyal le ma stong / gzhan yang stod kyi rung dgu la/ tang rung gi
za ma tog ne'u'i su le rung / la kogs kyi ma ga rung / phyis ri'i te se g.yu rung / ra zad kyi she lo rung / pad ka'i 'ur re rung / khu phu'i shel yag rung / le mur gyi thog
rung / she mur gyi dpal rung / sad mig gi ting rung la sogs pa'i srid pa'i rung chen po rnams dang / the si'i lha btsan/ mon pha'i lha btsan/ bsu'i lha btsan/ yu mo gnyan
po/ srang ri'i g.yug khri/ zhang gi lha dgu/ rgyor dbang jo she/ jo mo tho mug blo rig rdo rje btsan/ la ngag gi do btsan/ sman gyi rgyal mo nags nyil/ le nag saman
gyi rgyal mo/ tshon phur bzhi'i lha mo/ dgra lha'i rgyal mo stag ri rong / srid pa'i rgyal mo mu tsa med la sogs pa/ ag se rgyal ba ra la zhon pa/ mu thur smug po khyung
la zhon pa la sogs pa/ stod mnga' ris kyi lha 'dre mthu bo che rnams 'dus te/ slob dpon g.yog rnams gangs bar btsir bar byas pa la/ slob dpon gyis phyag 'khar brag la btsugs
te lam btod nas ri'i kha na phar byon pas/ srid pa'i lha srin rnams skrag ste dngangs shing bred par gyur ro/ /der srid pa'i rgyal mo mu tsa med la sogs kyis srog gi
snying po mdongs gsol du phul te sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs so/ /mo'i gsang mtshan yang gangs kyi yum gcig rdo rje kun tu bzang bya bar btags so/ /de
nas mar byon pa dang / brin chu dbar gyi so mtshams kyi lha srin bkra shis tshe ring ma btul nas dam la btags te ming yang bdag nyid chen mo rdo rje kun grags mar btags
so/ /de nas mar byon pa dang stod btsan 'khor glen pa lkugs pa/ rmug po 'chong gong / rkyang rtags kyi rdo ring dmar po/ jo bo ri bo btsun ni/ stong chen po dgu la dbang
ste/ lcags stong nag po zangs kyi ska rags can na bdud kyi stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum/ zangs stong dmar po

g.yu'i ska rags can na btsan gyi stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum/ stag stong khra bo gzig gi ska rags can na rmu'i stong sde phyed dang gsum/ gzig stong thig le can na klu'i
stong sde phyed dang bcu bzhi/ bse stong gser po can na gza'i stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum/ g.yu'i stong sde gser mig can na ma mo'i stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum/ spyang
stong dkar po lhag pa'i ska rags can na rgyal po'i stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum/ ra gan thal ba stong na 'gong po'i stong sde phyed dang bcu gsum ste lha srin de rnams
kyang dam la btags so/ /de nas mar byon pa dang gnam sman dkar mos slob dpon la thog phab par byas pa dang / slob dpon gyi phyag g.yon pa'i mthil du chu me long gang tsam
bzhag pa dang / der swa zer song ba dang thog skam po sran ma tsam bdun du song 'dug der mo ya mtshan skyes te bred nas dpal mo dpal mtsho lha mtsho srin mtsho bya bar
bros so/ /slob dpon mtsho me dpung du bsgoms pas mtsha lhag gis khol ba dang mo'i sha dang rus pa bye ste bros pas/ slob dpon gyis rdo rje brgyab pas mig g.yas pa zhar te/
ston pa'i zhal skyin rdo rje thod 'phreng rtsal/ bar chad mi bgyid thugs kyis dgongs pa glod/ /bdag ni 'jigs shing skrag pas srog gi dbang po 'bul/ phyin chad slob dpon
bka' bzhin bstan pa'i srung bar bgyid/ ces ming yang gangs dkar sha med rdo rje spyan gcig mar btags so/ /de nas 'jad shul tu byon nas brag phug sgrub khang du zhag gsum
bzhugs/ sa'i kha gnon du mchod rten bzhengs/ sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs/ rdo la zhabs rjes bzhag go/ /de nas mar byon te shangs kyi lha phu'i zab phu lung du zhag bdun bzhugs/
'od yug tu byon/ sding ma'i steng phyogs kyi brag phug tu zhag bdun bzhugs/ lha klu gdug pa can btul nas byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas gnam du byon te gnam byang ngos
kyi brag phug tu zhag bdun bzhugs/ byang gi 'dre srin spun bdun btul/ sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas bod kyi bstan ma rnams kyis bar chad bya bar brtsams pas/ slob
dpon gyis ri gnya' thams cad zhabs kyis bcags/ phyag mkhar gyis bor de g.ya' ri dang gangs ri'i gnas thams cad bshigs te btul/ bstan ma bcu gnyis/ skyong ma bcu gnyis/ ya
ma bcu gnyis btul nas dam la btags te srog gi snying po phul lo/ /de nas pho lo sha lung du byon tsa na lha yar la sham po g.yag dkar po ri log tsam gcig tu sprul nas byung
bas/ slob dpon gyis lcags kyu'i phyag rgyas sna nas bzung / zhags pa'i phyag rgyas yan lag bcings/ lcags sgrog gi phyag rgyas bsdams/ dril bu'i phyag rgyas mnyed par
byas te/ g.yag de btul bas/ der lha yar la sham pos srog snying phul te dam la btags so/ /de nas thang lha'i sar byon pas thang lhas slob dpon nyams sad de/ gnod sbyin chen
po gcig tu lus sprul nas slob dpon 'khor bcas za ba'i tshul du byas pas slob dpon gyi phyag gis sdigs mdzub gtad pas byis pa gzhon nu g.yu'i zur phud can zhig tu gyur
te zhabs tog pa kun skrag nas slob dpon lha 'am pha gi ci lags/ bdag cag ni 'jigs par byung zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas 'di ni klu'i rgyal po mos thod dkar zhes kyang
bya/ gnyan chen thang lha zhes kyang bya ste/ 'di la ngas gro gcig blang gi gsungs nas 'khor kun la mi 'jigs

pa byin nas der bzhag ste/ slob dpon gyi thang lhar byon/ phyi dro 'khor tsa na chos gos kyi grar ci yang mi bro ba'i khur ba lab leb dang / zhal zas sna tshogs pa bsnams nas
byon te/ der thang lha mnga' 'og tu bsdus dam la btags so/ /de nas byang kha'i g.ya' ri gangs ri rnams kyi lha srin btul te/ shel tsha rgyal mo gangs kyi ming byang gi
'brog chen 'khor 'dul rdo rje bgegs kyi gtso mor ming btags so/ /de nas 'phan yul du byon tsa na byang gi kyin 'thing la ro sman dang / stag sman gyi gdong dang / byang
phug ma rnams kyis byang kha mthun gsum gyi lhag pa thams cad gcig tu bsdus te/ slob dpon 'khor bcas la brgyab pas 'khor rnams 'gyel la khad/ rengs la khad du gyur/ slob
dpon yang sku bser tsam mdzad nas der slob dpon gyis gangs ri rdza ri thams cad me dpung du byin gyis brlabs te bsgoms pas/ mar la lcags tsha mo phog pa ltar lhan gyis zhu
bar gyur pas der bod kyi gnod sbyin mo mthu mo che rnams btul te dam la btags so/ /srog gi snying po phul te ming yang byang gi kyin 'thing la ro sman du btags so/ /de
nas stod lungs bram bu'i tshal du byon te/ kha la brag rir dgung gcig tu bzhugs nas btsan thams cad dam la btags so/ /de nas ma zam phug tu bzhugs nas bdud thams cad dam
la btags so/ /de nas g.ya' ri gong du bzhugs nas rgyal 'gong dang the'u rang thams cad dal la btags so/ /de nas bsam yas has po rir byon pa dang / bod kyi mnga' bdag rgyal
po khri srong lde btsan dang rgyal blon kun gyis bsu ba la byon pa las/ der rgyal po rje 'bangs kyi thugs dgongs la nga sa bdag rgyal po yin/ rgyal khrims dang chos khrims
gnyis kyi bdag po nga yin pas slob dpon gyis nga la phyag byed snyam/ slob dpon gyi thugs dgongs la nga sprul pa'i sku yang yin/ grub pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa tshe'i
rig 'dzin brnyes pa yin/ rgyal pos nga la phyag byed snyam pas phyag la ma 'dum pas/ de la slob dpon gyis nga che nga btsan mgur bzhes pa/ khams gsum sems can gnas yin/
/khams gsum dbang sdud kyi gdams ngag yod/ /snang srid 'khor 'das kyi dpe cha la/ /drang don nges don gyi bshad pa byed/ /nga dge bshes pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /'khor 'das
shan 'byed kyi gdams ngag bdog /sems nyid rnal ma'i shog bu la/ /sgra tshig dang bral ba'i yi ge bris/ /nga yig mkhan pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /chos yi ge med pa'i gdams
ngag bdog /'di ltar gnang ba'i gyang logs la/ /don gnyis su med pa'i ri mo bris/ /nga lha bzo pad ma 'byung nas yin/ /snang stong gsal ba'i gdams ngag bdog /mi dug lnga'i
nad kyis gzir ba la/ /zag med sman gyis gso bar byed/ /nga sman pa pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /bdud rtsi 'chi sos kyi gdams ngag bdog /mi dad pa bskyed pa'i 'dun ma byas/
/mi tshe phyi ma'i bde skyid byas/ /nga gtso pa pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /'khor ba rtsad gcod kyi gdams ngag bdog /shes rab snying rje'i go mtshon thogs/ /rnam rtog logs
lta'i dgra bo btul/ /nga dpa' bo pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /'khor ba g.yal bzlog gi gdams ngag bdog /dug lnga gdon lnga dgrar langs kyang / /ye shes lnga'i dbyings su brgyab/
/nga mthu chen pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi gdams ngag bdog /khyed gdong dmar srin po

bod kyi rje/ /'jig rten dregs pa'i khengs sems can/ /nga rgyal 'khor bar skye ba'i rgyu/ /nyon mongs dug lnga'i rgyan gyis brgyan/ /bod kyi mnga' bdag lha sras la/ /khyed mnga'
thang che ba glo ba dga'/ /rgyal po nyid la phyag mi 'tshal/ /rgyal po'i na bza' bzhes phyag 'tshal/ /zhes gsungs nas phyag g.yas pa deng mdzad pas rgyal po'i na bza'
phyag gi 'od zer gyi zul rtser tshigs nas rgyal blon rnams bred de rgyal pos yab kyis phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas slob dpon pho brang du spyan drangs nas gser khri la bzhugs
su gsol/ zhal skyems dang bshos dang / 'jig rten gyi zhal zas sna tshogs drangs so/ /za 'og gi smug ber sku la gsol/ rgyal pos phyag rten dang bcas nas zhus pa/ e ma/
na mo ma hA gu ru rin po che/ /bdag ni gdong dmar srin po bod kyi rje/ /bod kyi mi ni gdul bar dka'/ /dam pa'i chos kyi rten gcig 'dzugs/ /slob dpon sprul pa'i sku bzhugs
pas/ /ma rung lha srin 'dul du gsol/ /sa gzhi byin gyis brlab tu gsol/ /zhes zhu ba phul bas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas/ bod kyi mnga' bdag rgyal po lags/ /bod 'di gnod sbyin
pho mo'i yul/ /gnod sbyin lha srin dam la btags/ /'di na bod kyi klu rgyal yod/ /gsungs nas/ klu gdug pa can de la klu gter 'jug dgos gsungs te/ de nas mal gro'i mdar
byon nas 'khor ba dong sprugs kyi cho ga mdzad/ /dpal ngan song sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas mnga' bdag rje 'bangs kyi sgrib pa sbyangs so/ /de nas mal gro gzi chen
la klu gter bcug pas blang ba'i cho ga mdzad do/ /de nas has po rir byon te chab gtor gzi'i phor pa gang la brten nas/ ting nge 'dzin gyis bskyed nas byin gyis brlabs
te/ slob dpon gyis lha 'dre thams cad zil gyis gnon lapa'i phyag rgya mdzad nas mgur bzhes pa/ hU~M nga ni pad ma 'byung gnas te/ /mngal gyi dri mas ma gos mtsho skyes rdo
rje yin/ /lus la gnod pas mi tshugs rgyu lus rnam par dag /yo ga tshe yi rig 'dzin grub pa brnyes/ /nga'i lus ngag yid gsum lha ru gsal/ /'jig rten lha 'dre thams cad
zil gyis gnon/ /'jig rten lha srin dregs pas sdigs su med/ /nam mkha' yangs pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ /'byung chen bzhi po shong yang shong / /shong yang shong de yangs kyang
yangs/ /sems nyid stong pa dmigs med la/ /lha yang med de 'dre yang med/ /nga la cho 'phrul ci bstan yang / /nga la gnod pa rdul tsam med/ /mchod sbyin gtor ma rgya che 'di/
/mang por ting nge 'dzin gyis bskyed/ /so sor thob pa sngags kyis byas/ /phyag rgyas 'thab rtsod rgyal pham med/ /tshigs bcad bden pas bkram ste bsngo / /'di zhes sa
gzhi gnang ba byin/ /khri srong lde btsan bsam pa sgrub/ /sngags 'chang nga'i bka' ma gcog /gum gum chum chum las la chums/ /lha khang rtsigs shig lha 'dre rnams/ /las la
'dus shig lha 'dre rnams/ /zhes gsungs nas mchod sbyin rgya chen po mang por bsngos te byin pas/ lha 'dre thams cad slob dpon gyi bka' 'og tu 'dus pas/ rma chen spom ra
yong du ma nyan nas/ bdag ni dbyar khams shin tu che ba gcig lags na ban chung khyed kyi bka' nan che bas mi yong du ma btub pas 'ongs kyis/ da bka' ci stsol zhes smras pas/
slob dpon gyis kho la chab gtor rgya chen po 'di 'khyer la mnga' bdag gi 'dod pa sgrubs shig ban chung nga'i

bka' ma gcog gsungs pas/ bka' bstsal pa gzhan rnams bgyid na/ bdag sna thong cig tu che bas skam chas gcig la dag bas/ zan 'phrul brul gyi mgo la chu blug pa 'di yi 'tshal/
ster sna rgya che zhing yangs pa'i mchod sbyin byed cig ces mchis nas rin po che gser dngul gyi snod du rin po che brdar nas/ nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i mchod sbyin
du byin gyis brlabs te byin/ kho'i rkang pa g.yas pa khams kyi g.yar mo thang la bzhag rkang pa g.yon pa bsam yas has po ri la bzhag ste/ lha 'khor sum brgya drug cu dang
bcas pa tshim lapar byas nas spom ra lha 'khor lcam dral zo dor dang bcas pa dam la btags te srog gi snying po phul lo/ /rgyal po'i bsam pa bsgrub par khas blangs dam
bcas so/ /lcam gyi ming yang rma ri rab 'byams drag mo rgyal du btags so/ /lha 'od de gung rgyal dang lha lcam dral thams cad dam la btags so/ /de nas kong gtsun de mo dam
la btags so/ /de nas btsan la sman gcig ma dam la btags so/ /de nas kha rag khyung btsun dam la btags so/ /de nas jo mo lha ri dam la btags so/ /gnod sbyin gang ba bzang
po la sogs pa gnod sbyin thams cad dang / bod kyi dge bsnyen nyi shu rtsa gcig dam la btags so/ /de nas g.ya' ri mo/ gangs ri mo nyi shu rtsa gcig dam la btags so/ /de
nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ brag dmar bsam yas su lha 'dre gdug pa can thams cad tshar bcad/ bod khams skyong ba'i bstan ma bcu gnyis/ skyong ma bcu gnyis/ ya
ma bcu gnyis dam la btags so/ /srog gi snying po phul nas bstan pa bsrung bar khas blangs dam bcas/ gza' chen brgyad dang rgyu skar nyi shu rtsa brgyad/ bar snang gi lha
bran thams cad mnga' 'og tu bsdus te/ sde brgyad thams cad las la bkol te/ ri rdo ri las phab/ klungs rdo klangs su bsdus te/ lha khang gi rmang brtsigs pas/ slob dpon bo
dhi sa twa dang / chos rgyal nyid kyis dbu rtse rigs gsum ri rab tshul du byas/ gling gzhi gling phran brgyad du byas te/ de la yang shar du rnam dag khrims khang gling
/ mkhyen rab 'jam dpal gling / tshang dmar skye ru'i gling / lho ru bdud 'dul sngags pa'i gling / arya pa lo'i gling / sgra bsgyur rgya gar gling / nub tu mi g.yo bsam gtan
gling / rdo sku byang chub gling / dga' ldan byams pa'i gling / byang du sna tshogs rin chen gling / ma chags pad ma can gyi gling / dpe har dkor mdzod kyi gling / nyi
ma lha khang / zla ba lha khang / gzhan yang shar lhor mchod rten dkar po sangs rgyas stong gis brgyan pa/ lho nub tu mchod rten dmar po pad ma stong gis brgyan pa/ nub
byang du mchod rten nag po mchod rten stong gis brgyan pa/ byang shar du mchod rten sngon po lha khang bcu drug gis brgyan pa bzhengs/ nub phyogs su ya mtshan rdzu 'phrul
ston pa klu'i gling bzhengs/ slob dpon pad ma'i gzim khang yakSha ltag 'og bzhengs/ star ka chen po bzhi la/ phyogs bzhir khron kha chen po bzhi/ me btsa' chen po bzhi la/
ri sna bzhi la mchod rten bzhi/ pho brang rim dgu dang / pho brang sing khang dang / rgya'i ha shang lha khang dang / phyi lcags ri mu khyud nag po dang / de'i phyogs
bzhir sgo bzhi la mgon khang bzhi dang bcas pal bzhengs so/ /btsun mo gsum gyis kyang / tshe spongs bza' me tog

sgron gyis khams gsum zangs khang gling bzhengs te 'og gzhi zangs la byas pa rgyal po'i thugs dam dbu rtse rigs gsum 'dra ba gcig bzhengs so/ /pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun
gyis bu tshal gser khang gling zhes pa/ bzo bo la zas sna mi 'dra ba bcu gsum drangs pa'i bzo sna khyad par can bcu gsum la/ phyi na gyang med pa bzo'i khyad/ nang na ka
ba med pa bzo'i khyad/ rgya phibs kha phyir bltas dang nang bltas gnyis su yod pa bzo'i khyad/ gza' chen brgyad kyis ka ba 'degs pa bzo'i khyad/ rgyu skar nyi shu rtsa brgyad
kyis gdung ma 'degs pa bzo'i khyad/ bya khyung mo'i sgo nga'i nang na lha mo brgyad khrus byed pa yod pa bzo'i khyad/ phyogs bzhi na gser gyi seng ge lug thong tsam
bzhi yod pa bzo'i khyad/ gser gyi gdung ma la g.yu'i rta rgyugs pa yod pa bzo'i khyad/ g.yu'i gdung ma la gser gyi rta rgyugs pa yod pa bzo'i khyad/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis 'bur
du dod pa bzo'i khyad/ g.yu'i sgo mo la gser gyi bye'u chung skad 'don pa yod pa bzo'i khyad/ gser gyi sgo mo la rus sbal gyi rgyab tu chu 'bab pa yod pa bzo'i khyad/
lha khang gi shing thams cad klu'i shing klag sha la byas bzo'i khyad lapar te de ltar bzo sna bcu gsum yod pa de bzhengs so/ /btsun mo 'bron bza' byang chub sman gyis lha
khang dge rgyas bye ma'i gling bzhengs te/ de yang khong gis sras rgyal bu ma gzigs pas/ nga la bu med pas phyis lha khang zhig gsos byed mkhan mi yong zer te/ lha khang
so phag gis brtsigs/ shing thams cad me yis tshigs nas mi yong zer nas klu shing klag sha la byas/ lha thams cad lugs mar byas so/ /mar me 'bul mkhan mi yong zer nas lha'i
spyan thams cad me shel las byas so/ /yon chab 'bul mkhan mi yong zer nas lha'i spyan gyi gzigs sar chu mig byas so/ /me tog 'bul mkhan mi yong zer nas lha'i spyan gyis
gzigs sar me tog ra bar byas so/ /de ltar lha khang dge rgyas bye ma gling bzhengs so/ /dbu rtse rigs gsum gyi phyogs bzhir rdo ring chen po re re'i steng zangs kyi khyi
bo che re yod pa bzhengs so/ /de ltar gting nas bzhengs pa la 'jig rten gyi lha srin thams cad kyis brtsigs pas der nyin mo mis brtsigs pa las nub mo lha 'dres brtsigs
pa mtho bar byung ngo / /de ltar rtsig pa tshar pa dang / shing dang rin po che dgos pa la/ der shing bzo mkhan pa rgya nag lang rtse he dang / bal po'i shing bzo ba sba
su la sogs pas/ rgyal po'i mdun du rte'u klad la skor zhing / rgyal po lha khang rtsig pa shing la rdugs so/ /shing gang na yod byas pa dang / rgyal pos 'di tsam gyi gtsug
lag khang gi shing dang rgyu rin po che gang nas btsal snyam pa'i thugs khral cher yod pa las/ de'i dus su slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis thugs dgongs pa la bzhugs
te/ lha srin sde brgyad kyis lha rtsig grogs byas pas gtsug lag khang brtsigs zin 'dug pa la/ bod kyi lha 'dre gdug pa can rnams kyi lus ngag yid gsum dam la legs par thogs
sam ma thogs snyam nas dgongs pa la bzhugs gzigs pas/ lha 'dre gzhan thams cad kyi lus ngag yid gsum dam la thogs nas/ lus dam la thogs nas bsam yas rtsig grogs byed kyi
'dug ngag dam la thogs nas rgyal po'i bsam pa bsgrub po zer zhing / slob dpon gyi bka' la nyan zer gyin 'dug

yid dam la thogs nas dkon mchog gsum la dad pa thob ste gsam pa gus pas lha khang rtsig gin 'dug pa la/ klu gnyan sa bdag rnams lus dam la thog nas bsam yas rtsig pa'i grogs
byed kyin 'dug ngag dam la thogs nas rgyal po'i bsam pa sgrub/ slob dpon gyi bka' la nyan zer gyi 'dug pa la/ yid dam la ma thogs par mthong ba'i dug dang / 'phro ba'i
dug dang / kha rlangs kyi dug sna tshogs gtong zhing sems can la gnod par gzigs pas/ der slob dpon gyis rgyal po la de rnams zhib par bshad nas/ klu gnyan sa bdag dam la
'dogs pa'i phyir du nga mchims phu phug pa chen mor sgrub pa la 'jug pas/ da ste zhag bdun bar du nga'i mtshams la bar cad ma byed cig mtshams ma rtog cig gsungs te/ slob
dpon gyis dgongs pa la bzhugs pa las/ rta mgrin na ga klu 'dul gyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye/ ran ma sngon nub mo nam phyed tsa na rgyal po gzim pa'i dbu sngas su/ lha sa rkyang
phu'i klu mi dkar rta dkar du byas nas spyi gtsug gi sbrul mgo dang sbrul mjug kyang mi mngon par byas nas/ spyi gtsug gi nor bu rin po che de dkrol nas rgyal po'i phyag
tu phul te/ rgyal po khyed kyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i shing dang nor bu rin po che thams cad ngas ka ru mar byed pas rang re grogs po bya'o zer/ der rgyal po mnal
sad lapa dang / ga re rang gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa la shing rin po che rdugs pa de rnams yong bar 'dug ron bu rin po che'i phyag rten yang byung bas dga' ste/ de
ltar rang re grogs po bya'o zhes smras pas/ nga'i dgos pa zhig rgyal pos sgrubs shig zer te chad pas/ khyod kyi dgos pa gang yin gsungs pas/ gzhan mi 'tshal te mchims phu
phug pa chen po'i ban de ya gi'i dgongs pa glod dgos zer bas/ de ltar bya bar khas blangs dam bcas pas de nyid du klu de mi snang bar gyur to/ /der rgyal pos mtshan mo
de jo mo la bskul/ jo mos nang 'khor g.yog mo la bskul/ des nang mi la bskul te/ blon po chen pa bdun sbron du btang bas/ blon po chen po rnams na re re la 'khor rta pa
lnga brgya res bskor ba rnams nam langs nyi ma shar ba la yom 'bog gi thang la 'tshogs pa las/ rgyal pos rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum nas chibs khar byon pas/ rje 'bangs yongs
kyis mchims phur byon te/ slob dpon gyi drung du song bas slob dpon mngon par shes pas mkhyen pas sgrub kang gi sgo la sgrim shing mdzad do/ /nyi ma dgong kar song yang
rgyal pos slob dpon gyi sgrub khang gi sgo ma rnyed do/ /thams cad ltogs skom thang chad par gyur to/ /nyon mongs par gzigs nas sgrib shing bkrol bas der rgyal blon rnams
kyis slob dpon gyi drung du phyin pa dang / de yang / mchims phu phug pa chen po'i nang na/ /sprul pa'i khyung chen 'jigs shing skyi bun pa/ /spu mdog btso ma'i gser
du snang ba la/ /gshog pa'i sgro ni ral gri lham pa 'dra/ /spu rtse rnams ni spu gri lham pa 'dra/ /mchu dang rus pa sder mo lcags sbar can/ /mgar ba'i so mal nang nas bton
pa 'dra/ /nyi zla'i spyan ni 'bur zhing 'phrul pa can/ /klu'i rgyal po mal gro gzi chen dang / /klu'i ded dpon nag po glong rdol gnyis/ /sbrul gyi sked pa phyag gis bzung
ste mjug ma zhabs kyis mnan/ /sbrul gyi kha ni gdangs btsum sked pa 'khyog cig 'gul/ /lag gnyis thal sbyar

sbrul mgo khyung gi zhal du gsol ba khad/ /khyung gi me chen spar bas brag phub tsheg sgra can/ /de ltar mthong nas rgyal po rje 'bangs kyis/ /khyung de slob dpon yin pa ma
shes nas/ /yang ni lan gsum mtha' ma mchims phu yongs rnams bskor/ /gar phyin gar btsal slob dpon ma rnyed nas/ /gzhug tu slob dpon khyung du sprul pa'i drung du phyin/
/phyag byas gzugs snems snyun dris pas/ /khyung chen cang mi smra zhing lta zur log log byed/ /dngos grub ya mtshan chen po yod ces zhus/ /dgongs pa glod par zhu ba nan du
phul/ /'on pa'i mi la smra ba bzhin du mdzad/ /slob dpon dgongs pa glod pas klu'i rgyal po ni/ /mal gro gzi chen nag po klong rdol gnyis/ /spyi gtsug nor bu bkrol nas rgyal
po'i phyag tu phul/ /lus kyis gus pa ston cing zhabs gnyis spyi bor blangs/ /de ltar byas nas klu'i rgyal po gnyis/ /mkha' la lho sprin 'atibs nas tshogs dang bcas/
/mkha' las thar pa 'bab cing si li li/ /'brug sgra drag po'i sgra ni di ri ri/ /rgyal po sku drin che zhes byang phyogs bzhud/ /de nas slob dpon gyi zhal nas rje lha sras
lags/ /gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i shing dang rin po che mi skog mi 'dug lags te/ bdag gis kyang lha ma srin sde brgyad kyi lus ngag yid gsum dam la thogs sam ma thogs
bltas pas dam la thogs 'dug klu gnyan de'i lus dam la thogs pas bsam yas rtsig pa'i grogs byed kyi 'dug ngag dam la thogs nas rgyal po'i bsam pa sgrub/ slob dpon gyi bka'
nyan zer zhing 'dug pa la/ yid dam la ma thogs par mthong ba'i dug dang / reg pa'i dug dang / kha rlangs kyi dug dang / 'phro ba'i dug gis mi dang sems can rnams la gnod
cing 'tshe ba byed kyi 'dug nas/ tshar gcod cing dam btags la phyi rabs su sems can rnams la gnod pa dang 'tshe ba mi nus lapar bya bsams pa lags te/ rgyal pos bdag gi klu
'dul ba'i dgongs pa glod pas/ da lnga brgya'i mtha' ma la sa gzhi dang 'og thams cad klu gnyan sa bdag gis dbang byed pa 'ongs/ mdze rigs dang gnyan nad bco brgyad dar
bar 'ongs/ gnyan rigs dar zhing 'phel dang shu ba dar/ mi phal yang 'og gdon gyis zin par 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de nas rgyal po rje 'bangs mar byon tsa na/ klus gtsang
po la shing bskyur nas bsam yas kyi mtha' thams cad shing gis nag mer re khengs par 'dug skad do/ /de nas rgyal po'i nyi shu rtsa gcig stag gi lo la rma bting nas brtsigs/
rta'i lo la 'byongs te/ dbu rtse yang thog rgya gar gyi lugs su bzhengs/ bar khang rgya nag gi lugs su bzhengs/ 'og khang bod kyi lugs su bzhengs te/ rten byon lugs
dang bzhengs lugs ni rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la/ nga'i lha khang du rten ji ltar bzhengs dgongs pa dang / rgyal po gzim pa'i mnal lam na bar snang nas lhas lung bstan te/
rgyal po khyod kyi yid dam gyi lha ba dmar po 'bud pa'i skad thag chad pa'i sa der bzhugs pas gdan drongs la/ gtsug lag khang du bzhugs su gsol cig bya ba byung ba dang
/ de'i skad byung ba thos pas skad thag has po ri'i rtse mor chad pa snyam byed pa byung bas/ de ma thag has palo ri'i rtse mor byon pas mngon sum par ci yang mi 'dug pa
la/ rgyal pos sa de 'di yin gsungs nas/ phyag gis brad pas/ byang chub chen po rdo sku rang byon de dbu'i gtsug

tor nyug gis byon/ de gdan drangs te 'og khang bod lugs kyi gtsug lag khang gi lha'i gtso bor bzhugs su gsol lo/ /dpal gyi bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa bzhengs/ mi 'gyur lhun
gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang / gzhi che dpangs mtho rgyu bzang bkod legs pa/ bkra shis byin che kun nas 'gran zla med/ dga' ldan sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha khang la dpe
blangs pas/ dpal nA len dra dang mtshungs pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhugs/ btsugs pa mi 'dra skyes pa 'dra ste mdo ste lhar stong gsum gcig gi lugs so/ /'dul ba ltar theg pa'i
skabs dang rim pa bzhin/ mngon pa mdzod kyi 'jig rten bstan pa dang yang bstun no/ /de yang sde snod gsum dang sbyar nas bzhugs su gsol ba ni/ steng khang rgya gar lugs
kyi lha ni/ dpal rnam par snang mdzad zhal bzhi/ 'khor nye ba'i sras brgyad/ phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ sgo srung brgyad de bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi
bzhugs so/ /ri mo'i logs la rdo rje dbyings kyi lha tshogs bzhugs/ lcog bzhi la ri mo 'jig rten gyi khams mdangs dga' bar sangs rgyas dga' ba'i dpal 'khor dang bcas pa bzhugs
so/ /chos skyong lag na rdo rje zhal dang / rgyal po rnam sras la gtad de bcol lo/ /dbu rtse bar khang rgya nag gi lugs la/ lha tshogs gtso bo dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas
'khor sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpal bcu'o/ /sgo ba kang king ngo / /khro bo rnam par rgyal ba dang khams gsum rnam par rgyal te lha tshogs bco lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo ni
snying po 'bum gyi gleng bzhi'o/ /skor khang ka phyir lta na mchod rten brgyad la/ nang gi lha sprin chen snying po'o/ /rnga khang na ri mi phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang
/ rdo rje sems dpa'a' dang gshin rje gshed kyi lha tshogs dang / chos skyong rnams kyi 'bag bris so/ /chos skyong rgyal po shing bya can dang lcam mo 'gro bzang ma la gtad
de bcol lo/ /'og khang bod kyi lugs kyi lha khang na/ lha'i gtso bo ngo mtshar can byang chub chen po rang byon dang / 'khor bskal bzang sems dpa' bcu'o/ /sgo srung mi
g.yo mgon po dang / rdo rje gtum po dang bcu gsum bzhugs so/ /snying po ri mo phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang / skor khang phyi nang na rin po che'i tog rnga khang na mdo
sde dkon mchog sprin gyi bkod pa'o/ /chos skyong mkha' 'gro ma/ khro bo rol pa la gtad do/ /'khor sa bar ma'i ri mo rgya che rol pa'i bkod pa bzhugs so/ /dkor mdzod dgu
la lha'i dkor mdzod gsum ni rin po che'i gter gyi mdzod/ chos skyong gshin rje nag po che gsum la gtad de bcol lo/ /nub phyogs kyi dkor mdzod gsum ni gsung rab rgyud kyi
mdzod do/ /chos skyong a tsarya mched gsum la gtad de bcol lo/ /byang phyogs kyi skor mdzod gsum ni rin po che nor gyi mdzod do/ /chos skyong ni nag po mched gsum la gtad
do/ /'khor sa chen mo'i nang gnyis na mdo sde sdong po rgyan bzhugs so/ /chos skyong klu'i rgyal po e na dang u ni la gtad do/ /dbu rtse la ka ba stong rtsa brgyad/ bsha'
rtse bzhi bcu zhe brgyad/ sgau mo sum cu so brgyad/ gru skas drug dkor mdzod dgu la lder so bzo bdun cu rtsa gnyis bzhugs so/ /yakSha ltag 'og gnyis la lha tshogs byang
chub chen po gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas stong bzhugs so/ /chos skyong

gnod sbyin gang ba bzang po dang / nor bu bzang po gnyis la gtad/ shar gyi gling gsum ni rnam dag khrus khang gling na/ lha tshogs byang chub chen po sku 'khor lnga bzhugs/
ri mo ni mdo ting nge 'dzin rgyal po'i bkod pa bzhugs/ chos skyong tshangs pa dung gi thor gtsug can la gtad do/ /so so thar pa'i tshul khrims len pa'i gnas so/ /mkhyen
rab 'jam dpal gling na lha tshogs 'jam dpal sku 'khor lnga / sgo srung gshin rje gshed gnyis te bdun bzhugs so/ /ri mo ni snang ba mtha' yas dang / tshe dpag med dang phal
po che'i rgyud ris bzhugs so/ /chos skyong ni gshin rje me'i 'khor lo can la gtad do/ /chos kyi 'chad nyan byed pa'i gling ngo / /tshang mang brda sbyor gling na/ lha gtso
bo shAkya mu ne gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /chos skyong rgyal po 'brug gi klag slog pa can la gtad do/ /'tsho ba zas kyi gling ngo / /lho'i gling gsum la/ bdud 'dul sngags
pa'i gling na/ lha tshogs lugs sku byang chub chen po gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo ni mdo nam mkha' snying po'i rgyud ris bzhugs so/ /chos skyong ma mo nyi shu
rtsa brgyad la gtad do/ /sgrub pa'i bar chad sel ba'i gling ngo / /thugs rje rgyun 'byung arya pa lo'i gling na/ lha tshogs ni kha sarpa Ni gtso 'khor lnga/ steng phyogs
na snang ba mtha' yas gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /glo 'bur na rigs gsum mgon po/ phra men gyi mchod rten rgyal po'i sku tshad/ dngul gyi thugs rje chen po/ rje btsun seng
ge sgra/ bse'i jo mo stong phrag brgya pa bzhugs so/ /ri mo za ma tog bkod pa/ lnga bcu pa'i rgyud ris yod/ chos skyong dbang chen gyi pho nya rnams la gtad do/ /mngon
par byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gling ngo / /sgra bsgyur rgya gar gyi gling na/ lha tshogs lugs sku byang chub chen po gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo rgyal ba
rigs lnga'i rgyud ris so/ /chos skyong gnod sbyin ra gdong can la gtad do/ /rgya la las bod skad du sgra bsgyur ba'i gling ngo / /nub kyi gling gsum la lung ston bai ro
tsa na'i gling na/ lha tshogs zangs kyi rnam par snang mdzad/ mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud ris bzhugs so/ /chos skyong ni seng mgo can la gtad do/ /gang zag lung ston
pa'i gling ngo / /dga' ldan byams pa'i gling na/ lha tshogs byams pa sku 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /sgo srung gnyis te bdun bzhugs so/ /steng gi lcog na a mi de ba sku 'khor
lnga bzhugs te lha bcu gnyis bzhugs so/ /ri mo byams pa'i skyes rabs dang / sangs rgyas sum cu rtsa gnyis bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan chen po bcu drug dang / bsam yas kyi dpe/
zhang rgya tsha lha snang gi skyes rabs rnams bris so/ /chos skyong mkha' 'gro ma gu ling gi mgo can la gtad do/ /sgrub rgyud kyi gdams ngag 'bebs pa'i gling ngo / /mi g.yo
bsam gtan gyi gling na lha tshogs rnam par snang mdzad gnyan po byin can gyis gtso byas pa'i rgyal ba rigs lnga/ bskal bzang byang chub sems dpa' bcu drug ste nyi shu
rtsa drug bzhugs so/ /ri mo tshe dpag med dang ngan song sbyong ba dang / gtsug tor 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gsum/ 'khor khyams na phal po che'i rgyud ris bzhugs so/ /chos skyong
rgyal po dngul mgo can la gtad do/ /bsam gtan sgrub pa byed pa'i gling ngo / /byang gi gling gsum la sna

tshogs rin chen gling na/ shAkya seng ge sku 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo ni 'phags pa gser 'od dam pa'i rgyud ris bzhugs so/ /chos skyong rgyal po bya'i sbar so can la gtad
do/ /'jug pa byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i gling ni/ gtan bde la gnas pa'i gling ngo / /sems bskyed byang chub gling na/ lha tshogs ni sangs rgyas ma chags pad ma'i spyan
la/ 'khor byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs rigs brgya bzhugs so/ /chos skyong ni gnod sbyin no/ /byang chub sems bskyed 'bebs pa'i gling ngo / /dpe har dkor mdzod gling na/
lha steng gi sangs rgyas dga' ba'i dpal gtso 'khor lnga bzhugs so/ /ri mo ni 'jig rten gyi khams mdangs dga' ba'i bkod pa'o/ /chos skyong ni rgyal po dpe har la gtad do/
/de ltar nyi ma'i lha khang ni/ lha'i bu nyi ma'i gzhal yas khang gi bkod pa'o/ /zla ba'i gzhal yas khang na lha'i bu zla ba'i gzhal yas khang gi bkod pa yod do/ /mchod
rten bzhi la shar lho'i mchod rten dkar po'i nang na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ring bsrel ma ga dha'i bre drug bzhugs te/ sangs rgyas stong gi brgyan pa bzhengs so/ /lho
nub kyi mchod rten dmar po'i nang na/ sngon bskal pa dang por jo jo rgod des khyung tshang nas bton pa'i khrab nya sha lto rgyab/ mdung kha dog mchog ldem ngal gri ngar
ma'i rdo gcod la sogs go mtshon bcug ste pad ma stong gis brgyan pa bzhengs so/ /nub byang mchod rten nag po'i nang na/ sngon bskal pa dang po la spre'u dang brag srin
las 'gro ba mi 'phel ba'i dus su/ arya'i drung nas khong tsho'i zas skal la byin pa'i yar lung zo thang du 'bru sna thams cad btab pa'i phud/ 'bru sna bskal pa bzang po'i
nas tshad za tshad bcug ste/ mchod rten stong gis brgyan pa zhig bzhengs so/ /byang shar mchod rten sngon po'i nang na sman mchog ma ru ra rnam rgyal dang / bdud rtsi 'chi
sos kyi sman dang / sman mchog thams cad bcug pa'i lha khang bcu drug gis brgyan pa gcig bzhugs so/ /mchod rten 'di shin tu ngo mtshar bas lha'i yul du 'phur nas gshegs
pa la phyogs bzhir gzer bzhis mnan pa bzhugs so/ /dbu rtse rigs gsum gyi gnya?dzir gser 'phru'i rtse mo na nor bu rin po che zla ba chu shel yod do/ /khyams chen po'i
logs ris la gling bzhi bye ba phrag brgya dang / mdo phal po che las gzhon nu nor bzang gis bla ma brgya rtsa brten pa'i ri mo/ gling bar gyi mun pa'i bkod pa dang / bsam
yas lhun gyis grub pa bzhengs tshar ba'i dus kyi rab gnas kyi bkod pa dang / gzhan yang rgya nag po thag rtsed kyi ri mo yang po yod/ chos skyong mgon po beng dmar dang
/ dpal lha mo dkar mo la gtad do/ /gtsug lag khang spyi dang dkor mdzod gling gi dkor srung ni rgyal po dpe har la gtad do/ /de yang / dkar zhal bkod legs dar dkar bting
ba la/ /dbu rtse rigs gsum shel dkar mchod rten 'dra/ /'khor sa rnam gsum rin chen khri 'phang can/ /gser gyi gnya?dzir 'khor lo 'od 'bar mdzes/ /lcog chen bzhi nas dar dkar
ba dan 'phyar/ /'phrul gyi rgya phibs char rlung nyi ma skyob/ /cong dril gsung snyan dus kyi rlung gis 'khrol/ /logs la rgya byi'u la sogs bya rnams lding / /nam mkha'i
me tog pad ma'i dud sprin gtibs/ /mchod pa'i lha mos dri bsung rnam par 'bul/ /rin chen gdugs mdzes bde gshegs

mchod pa yis/ /pad ma'i snying po bde bar gshegs pa'i brgyan/ /gsha' rtse nyi zlas brgyan pas nyin mtshan gsal/ /sra brtan mi 'gyur so phag baiDUrya/ /mthon mthing gser gyi
ka ba ka gzhu la/ /rin chen sna tshogs phra dang spar kab mdzes pa btab/ /phyam gdung sgo glegs sgo dang phims la sogs/ /spar bkab phra yis thams cad khyab par bltams/ /dga'
ldan lha yi khang pa mtshungs par bzhengs/ /gru skas ha res gshegs shul bde ba'i lam/ /seng ge stobs chen stod nas mchongs pa bzhin/ /tsan dan snying po'i khang bzang
gzhal yas khang / /rnam thar sgo gsum rin chen gser gyis brgyan/ /gser gyi dril bu 'khrol ba'i skad sgra 'byin/ /rnam par snang mdzad rigs lnga kun gyi gtso/ /longs spyod
rdzogs sku gling bzhi kun la brgyan/ /nye ba'i sras brgyad 'khor la 'dzum bag ston/ /skyil krung mnyam bzhag bzhugs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems dpa'
nyi shu bzhi/ /bdag lta ri bo nyi shu'i rtse mo nas/ /bsdu ba rnam bzhis 'gro don dgongs pa can/ /srid gsum sdug bsngal sel phyag 'tshal lo/ /sgo bzhi srung mdzad khro
bo chen po brgyad/ /mi khom rnam brgyad ma lus 'joms pa po/ /'jig rten chos brgyad snyems dang byams pa mgon po dang / /dus gsum sangs rgyas khams gsum kun gyi gnyen/ /sku
gsum snyem mdzad 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa/ /'jig rten gsum mchod khyed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sa bcu'i byang sems chos kyi sprin la gnas/ /dpal bcu ldan pa kun nas byams
pa'i thugs/ /pha rol phyin bcu spyod pa'i rnam dpyod can/ /byang chub sems dpa' bcu la phyag 'tshal lo/ /khro chen rnam rgyal nyon mongs bdud las rgyal/ /khams gsum rnam
rgyal las kyi zhags pa gcod/ /ma rungs 'dul phyir rno ba'i mtshon cha bsnams/ /khro 'dzum pad ma'i spyan la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rang byung sprul pa'i skur ston mar me mdzad/
/lung bstan rin chen gser gyi 'od dang ldan/ /stong gsum dag dang sprul sku bye bas rgyan/ /'gro ba'i mun sel khyed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mi mjed 'jig rten khams pa khyed
la bstod/ /bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' bcus/ /stobs bcu ldan pa skye ba gcig gis thogs/ /'jig rten don mdzad khyed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bstan pa'i 'khor lo
bcom ldan mi g.yo mgon/ /bdud bzhi 'joms mdzad brkyangs bskums tshul gyis bzhugs/ /bcom ldan rdo rje gtum po stobs pa che/ /nyon mongs 'joms mdzad khyed la phyag 'tshal
lo/ /bstan gnas bar du gtsug lag khang bzhugs shing / /me dang chu klung gnod pa mi 'byung zhing / /lha srin sde brgyad rtag tu gus mchod de/ /chos skyong srung mdzad rnams
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de ltar btsun mo gsum gyi las tshe spong bza' me tog sgron gyis khams gsum zangs khang gling dbu rtse rigs gsum dang 'dra ba gcig bzhengs/ pho yong
bza' rgyal mo btsun gyis bu 'tshal gser khang gling bzo sna khyad par can bcu gsum yod pa gcig bzhengs/ 'brom bza' byang chub sman gyis dge rgyas bye ma'i gling bzhengs/
lha khang thams cad kyi rgya phibs ka gdung / ka gzhu lcam sgo glegs ru bzhi thams cad la gser gyi spar kab la/ nor bu rin po che'i phra bcug pa/ bzo dang bkod pa khyad
par 'phags pa 'dzam bu gling na 'gran zla dang bral ba/ lha yul gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang 'dra ba bzhengs

so/ /bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ /sum stong lon nas bod yul dbus su 'ongs/ /rgyal po'i bka' bzhin snang srid dregs pa'i lha 'dre btul/ /thams cad sangs rgyas bstan pa'i
sgo ru mos par byas/ /dpal gyi bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa bzhengs/ /zhes so/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / mkhan po bo dhi sa twas bsam yas lhun gyis grub
pa'i gtsug lag khang gi rab gnas mdzad pas/ byin rlabs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas lnga byung ste dbu rtse'i lha rnams phyir shad kyis byon te/ yang lha khang nang gi so so'i
pad ma'i gdan la bzhugs pa dang / byang chub gling gi rnam par snang mdzad nam mkha' la 'phags pa dang / mchod rten sngon po sman gyi yul du 'phul ba dang / de la gzer bzhis
mnan pa dang / arya pa lo'i gling gi rta mgrin gyis rta skad khams gsum stong gsum ber ber lan gsum bsgrags pa dang / phyogs bzhi'i rdo ring bzhi'i steng nas zangs kyi
khyi pho bzhis skad bton nas mchongs pa dang / dbu rtse 'khor ba'i snyug ring khad kyis dus gcig la rdzogs par skyes par dang / gzhan yang bkra shis shing ya mtshan pa'i
ltas mang du byung zhing / byin rlabs cho 'phrul mang po byung / de nas rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / slob dpon bo dhi sa twa
gnyis gser gyi khri la bzhugs te/ 'jig rten gyi spyan gzigs sna tshogs drangs tegatang rag chen po phul lo/ /dga' ston chen po yang byas so/ /skye bo'i tshogs chen po la
yang sbyin gtong rgya chen po mdzad do/ /de'i dus su brag dmar mtsho mo mgur bya ba'i mtsho nang nas rgyu rin po che sna tshogs las grub pa'i me tog pad ma chen po gcig skyes
pa la rje 'bangs thams cad dga' ba dang spro ba chen po skyes te/ mtsho'i mtha' mar rin po che'i khri brtsigs rgyal po'i gdan bzhi dang / zhal lu'i skyogs bzhi dang
/ 'bangs kyi gral brgyad byas/ bal po'i ma ru chang / rgya gar gyi go la dang / rgya nag gi ja la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi spyan gzigs sna tshogs bshams nas/ rje'i mgur glu
bcu gsum bzhengs/ rgyal blon thams cad gos dang rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan nas lag pa 'brel te mi res glu re blangs/ rta res bang re rgyugs/ de la bkra shis kyi dong rtse/
bkra shis kyi bro mo che/ 'khor lo'i rtsibs ris/ rdo rje byang chub ris/ rin chen 'bar ris/ pad ma'i skor shon/ rgya khram gyi gsang lam ris/ dar ma'i bum chung / byang
chub kyi rgyun lam la sogs pa'i glu bro rtsed 'jo dang / bro gar mang po mdzad/ skyid kyi mi lo gcu gsum la rgyal khrims dang chos khrims gnyis ka bor te skyid byas so/
/rgyal po snga dar gyi dus lags so/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang mkhan po bo dhi sa twa gnyis rgya gar yul du bzhud par dgongs nas/ rgyal po la rgya gar yul
du 'gro gsungs pa las/ rje mnga' bdag rgyal pos bzhugs par zhu ba phul bar/ u rgyan yul nas byon pa'i pad ma 'byung gnas dang / /za hor yul nas byon pa'i bo dhi sa twa
dang / /bod yal dbus su skyes pa'i khri srong lde btsan gsum/ /sku skye ba yang snga'i dus tshod na/ /ma gu ta yi yul dag tu/ /mon phrug spun gsum dag skyes/ /de dus mchod
rten gartsigs shing smon lam btab/ /rgyal pos chos rgyal smon lam btab/ /mkhan pos de'i bla mchod dag tu btab/

/slob dpon pad ma 'byuung gnas kyis/ /dregs pa 'dul ba'i smon lam btab/ /skye ba so sor smin pa la/ bo dhi sa twa bram zer skyes/ /btsad po drang srong rigs su skyes/ /bdag
ni sra ma srin bur skyes/ /de gsum gcig tu 'tshogs nas ni/ /sngon gyi mchod darten de dag la/ /mchod pa chen po rab phul te/ /yang ni smon lam btab pa ni/ /drang srong bu'i
smon lam ni/ /bdag ni tshe 'di'i phyi ma la/ /'khyags pa 'khyags yul mtha' 'khob tu/ /chos skyong rgyal por skyes nas ni/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa 'dzin par shog /chos kyi
bstan pa skyong par shog /dge 'dun sde chen 'dzugs par shog /de skad smon lam btab pa yis/ /da lta rgyal por skyes pa yin / /bram ze'i bu'i smon lam ni/ /bdag ni mkhas
pa paNDi ta/ /rig pa'i gnas la mkhas pa yis/ /rgyal pa'i bstan pa 'dzin pa yis/ /slob dpon byed par smon lam btab/ /da lta bo dhi sa twa yin/ /sra ma srin po'i smon lam
ni/ /bdag ni sngags 'chang mthu stobs can/ /snang srid dregs pa 'dul bar shog /rgyal po'i bsam pa bsgrub par shog /de skad smon lam btab pa yis/ /smon lam btab mthu btsan
pas/ /za hor u rgyan bod kyi yul/ /so sor skyes kyang bod yul du/ /slob dpon yon bdag gyur pa yin/ /rgyal po'i thugs dam bsam yas 'di/ /stag la rmang bting rta la 'byongs/
/lo lngas lhag pa med par 'byongs/ /bgegs zhi dus su bsam yas grub/ /bo dhi sa twa pad ma 'byung gnas bdag /rgya gar yul du 'gro bar zhu/ /zhes gsungs pa las/ rgyal pos
slob dpon gnyis la gser bre re/ dngul skyogs bkang nas phul/ 'jig rten gyi zhal zas sna tshogs drangs/ phyag phul skor ba byas/ spyan chab bton nas zhu ba nan tan du phul
ba/ e ma ho/ za hor u rgyan yul nas byon pa yi/ /slob dpon rnam gnyis bdag la gson/ /skye ba sngon yang smon lam btab/ /rgya gar yul du skyes nas ni/ /yang ni smon lam
btab pa yin/ /slob dpon rnam gnyis rgya gar gyi/ /chos kyi yul du skyes pa yin/ /bdag ni kha ba can gyi ljongs/ /gdong dmar bod kyi yul du skyes/ /las kyi dbang gis rgyal
por skyes/ /bdag gi yid dam bsam yas 'di/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig stag la rmang bting nas/ /slob dpon bo dhi sa twas sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs/ /bod kyi lha srin gdug rtsub can/
/bgegs kyis rtsig tu ma btub nas/ /slob dpon bo dhi sa twas lung bstan nas/ /sprul sku pad ma spyan drangs grub par ni/ /dngos grub thugs dam bdang btsan byon/ /stag
nas rta'i bar lo lngas 'byongs/ /sngar yang sku drin che mod kyang / /khri srong lde btsan ma gum bar/ /bzhud par mi zhu bzhugs par zhu/ /thugs dam brtser dgongs gnang bar
zhu/ /zhes zhu ba phul bas/ slob dpon gnyis kyis bka' bgros pa/ slob dpon pad ma'i zhal nas rang cag gsum tshe skye ba snga ma yang snga 'di gsum 'brel ba las 'brel yod
pa yin pas rgyal po'i zhal ngo mi bskyungs gsungs so/ /slob dpon bo dhi sa twa'i zhal nas de shin tu legs pas de bzhin bgyi'o gsungs nas/ der slob dpon gnyis kyis rgyal
po la bkas gnang ba la/ skye ba gsum gyi smon lam gyis/ /las kyi 'phros kyis bod du 'tshogs/ /sngar yang btsan po dgyes par bgyid/ /da yang btsad po'i zhal mi bskyungs bar
bgyid/ /ces gsungs nas bzhugs par bkas gnang ngo / /de nas rgyal pos slob dpon gnyis la chos gsung par zhu

ba phul bas gser gyi khri la za 'og gi 'bol gsum brtsegs dang gab rtse'i gdan la slob dpon pad ma bzhugs/ dngul gyi khri za 'og gi 'bol gsum brtsegs dang gab rtse'i gdan dang
bcas pa la mkhan po bo dhi sa twa bzhugs/ gong gral la rgyal po nyid bzhugs/ g.yon gral la cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang ska ba dpal brtsegs gnyis gab rtse'i khri la
bzhugs/ de nas slob dpon gnyis la gser gyi maNDal khri gang pa re la g.yu'i me tog gi tshom bu gling bzhi ri rab gling phran nyi zlas brgyan pa phul/ lo tsA ba gnyis la yang
rin po che'i maNDal re re phul nas chos gsung par zhu ba ni/ e ma ho/ rgya gar chos kyi yul du sku 'khrungs pa'i/ /dam chos rin po che la mnga' brnyes pa/ /mkhas pa chen
po paNDi tar gyur pa/ /slob dpon chen po rnam gnyis kyis/ /gsang sngags dang ni mtshan nyid kyi/ /chos ni gsung bar zhu ba 'bul/ /lo tsA gnyis kyis bsgyur bar zhu/ /bod
yul mun par 'thibs pas na/ /chos kyi sgron me spor bar zhu/ /zhes zhus pas slob dpon gnyis kyis gnang ba/ e ma ho/ rgyal po chen po bod kyi mi rnams la ni dad pa med/
blon po chen po rnams ni chos la gnag pas/ rgyal po nyid kyi chos kyi bka' khrims dam po dar gyi mdud pa 'dra ba bca' dgos pas 'chos shig gsungs nas/ lug gi lo gzhug nas
spre'u'i lo gzhug yar bcad la/ slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis gsang sngags kyi chos rgyud sde bco brgyad bsgyur/ /gsang sngags kyi
chos sgrub pa la bar chad mi 'byung ba'i phyir gzi ldan 'bar ba mtshams kyi rgyud/ bdag tu 'dzin pa 'khor ba'i rgyu yin pas 'khor ba las sgrol zhing phung po lha'i dkyil
'khor du bya ba'i phyir zhi ba lha'i rgyud/ bdud dang mu stegs tshar gcad par bya ba'i phyir sku'i sgrub lugs bskal pa me ltar 'bar ba'i rgyud/ gsung gi sgrub rgyud lugs
dbang chen 'dus pa'i tantra/ thugs kyi sgrub lugs khro bo kun dha ri ka'i tantra/ yon tan gyi sgrub lugs lha mo ma gol pa'i tantra/ 'phrin las kyi sgrub lugs rig 'dzin 'dus
pa'i tantra/ rigs sngags kyi sgrub lugs he ru ka 'dus pa'i tantra/ 'jam dpal sku'i rgyud zla gsang nag po/ pad ma gsung gi rgyud rta mchog rol pa/ yang dag thugs kyi
rgyud he ru ka gal po/ 'jig rten 'das pa'i mdo/ bdud rtsi yon tan gyi rgyud bdud rtsi rol pa che chung / phur pa 'phrin las kyi rgyud bi to ta ma la 'bum sde/ ma mo sbod
gtong gi rgyud 'bum tig srid pa rgyud lung / phrin las kha skong ba dang rgyan rtags 'debs pa'i phyir shes pa stong khas brgyan pa'i rgyud/ las rgya mtsho ji ltar bstan pa'i
rgyud/ karma ma le 'phrin las kyi rgyud/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir tshogs rgyud che chung / mchod pa mi zad pa'i gter du byin gyis brlab
pa'i phyir nam mkha' mdzod byin gyis brlabs pa'i rgyud/ sgrol ba gnas su dag par bya ba'i phyir stobs chen yongs sgrol gyi rgyud/ sbyor ba gnas su dag par bya ba'i phyir
thig le klong gi rgyud/ brtul zhugs drag por bya ba'i phyir glang po che rab 'bog gi rgyud/ bkra shis pa la sbyin bsregs bya ba'i phyir za byed rol ba'i rgyud/ gtor
ma'i las thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro ba'i phyir gtor rgyud che chung / bka' 'khor skyong ba'i srung ma lhag

ma la dbang ba la las bcol ba'i phyir dpal 'bar khro mo'i rgyud/ bgegs gzir zhing mnan pa'i phyir zhing bcu sgrol ba'i rgyud/ de rnams ni ma ha yo ga'i rgyud yin no/ /lung
a nu yo ga'i sde la mdo bzhi sems dang lnga las kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo/ ye shes rngam pa srog gi 'khor lo/ dur khrod khu byug rol pa'i mdo/ sems lung chen po'i mdo/ sangs
rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa 'dus pa ni bka' thams cad kyi dems su bzhugs pa yin no/ /gsang ba sde drug la sku'i rgyud sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ gsung gi rgyud zla gsang
thig le/ thugs kyi rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa/ yon tan gyi rgyud rnam snang rgyud dra/ 'phrin las kyi rgyud karma ma le/ mjug sdud don bsdus pa rdo rje gdan bzhi'i rgyud do/
/sgyu 'phrul sde brgyad la/ sems dang ye shes rang lugs su ston pa gsang ba snying po/ 'phrin las kha tshang bar bstan pa sgyu 'phrul bzhi bcu pa/ dbang mngon du gyur pa
sgyu 'phrul bla ma/ dam tshig dang lta ba'i man ngag tu gyur pa sgyu 'phrul le lag don bsdus nas bstan pa sgyu 'phrul le'u brgyad pa/ rol pa mngon du gyur pa lha mo sgyu
'phrul/ de nas ma tshang ba kha skong ba sgyu 'phrul rgyas pa brgyad cu pa/ don dam pa ye shes su bshad pa 'jam dpal sgyu 'phrul lo/ /de rnams ni gsang sngags nang gi rgyud
sde'o/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ro/ /rgya dpe rgya gar shrI nA len dra'i gtsug lag khang nang bzhugs pa las/ slob dpon
pad ma 'byung gnas kyis rdzu 'phrul gyis blangs te/ rgya gar du ma lus par rgya dpe bsam yas dkor mdzod nang bzhugs so/ /slob dpon bo dhi sa twa dang lo tsA ba 'bro ska ba
dpal brtsegs kyis rig sngags phyi ma rnams bsgyur te/ de la yang kri ya'i chos bya ba spyi'i rgyud drug la/ rig sngags thams cad kyi khog dbub pa kri ya dpung bzangs kyi
rgyud/ rigs sngags thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba phyag na rdo rje dbang gi rgyud/ rigs sngags thams cad kyi gsang ba rig pa mchog gi rgyud/ rig sngags thams cad kyi 'dus
pa siddhi ka ra'i rgyud/ rig sngags thams cad kyi dgongs pa bsam gtan phyi ma'i rgyud dang drug go /bya ba bye brag gi rgyud ni/ spyan ras gzigs kyi skor khang /pad ma rtse
mo sngags kyi rgyud/ pad ma cod pan gyi rgyud/ cho ga sngags kyi rgyud/ yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyud/ a mo gha pa sha don yod zhags pa'i rgyud/ za ma tog che chung la sogs
pa'o/ /'jam dpal gyi skor la/ 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' dri ma med pa'i rgyud/ 'jam dpal rnon po sgrib pa med pa'i rgyud/ 'jam dpal mtshan yang dag par brjod pa bstod
pa glu blangs kyi rgyud la sogs pa'o/ /phyag na rdo rje'i skor la/ phyag na rdo rjer dbar bskur ba'i rgyud/ rdo rje sa 'og gi rgyud/ rdo rje be con gyi rgyud/ rdo rje bde
khros kyi rgyud/ rdo rje rnon po'i rgyud la sogs pa'o/ /gzungs gra lnga la sogs pa brgya drug cu'o/ /u pa ya'i rgyud bzhi la/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub
pa'i rgyud/ me dpung 'bar ba'i rgyud/ lag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba'i rgyud do/ /rnam par mi rtog pa'i rgyud do/ /yo ga'i rgyud chen po la bam po sum brgya yod pa ma 'gyur/
bsgyur/ rgyud sde chen po bzhi la/ mu la tantra rtsa ba'i rgyud/ ta tha sam tra ha dang pa sha ga ra rdo rje

rtse mo'i rgyud/ hri pad ma ra garya dpal mchog dang po'i rgyud nas/ sarba mu tsa ya rtog pa bsdus pa'i rgyud dang bzhi'o/ /de rnams gsang sngags phyi'i rgyud do/ /mkhan po
bo dhi sa twa dang lo tsA ba ska ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba'o/ /rgya dpe bsam yas na gter du sbas nas yod do/ /de rnams slob dpon gnyis dang lo tsA ba ska cog gnyis
kyis bsgyur ba'o/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i chos tshe gcig la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i chos rgya gar yul nas
grub thob rnams la da rung zhu bar gtang la/ bod kha ba can 'dir grub pa thob pa 'ga' ma byung na chos la yid mi ches/ phyi rabs kyang mi 'byung bas rgya gar du chos la
gajug tu gtang dgos snyam nas/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa la bod kyi mi drug rab tu byung nas btang ba ni snubs nam mkha' snying po/ rlangs dpal gyi seng ge/ gru gung u peg
sha/ ru yong sing ha ra dza/ 'bre rgyal pa'i blo gros/ ru gyong birya ra dza/ de rnams zhabs 'og nas rde'u bton nas dbu'i mchod gnas su bkur bar bka' bstsal te/ bka' la
gtags nas rgya gar yul du chos 'tshol du btang ste/ gser phye bre gsum bskur nas btang ba dang / der dge slong mi drug dka' ba dang bsdos nas rgya gar yul du phyin te/ da
lta rgya gar yul na gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa la grub pa thob par grags pa ji skad bya ba yod dris pas/ gser gyi brag bya skyibs can bya ba na slob dpon hUM ka ra bya
ba bzhugs zer bas/ slob dpon hUM ka ra'i thad du phyin nas nye gnas so kya de ba bya ba la gser rngan par byin nas slob dpon la nged chos zhu ba yin/ khyed kyis nged rnams
dang sprad dgos byas pas slob dpon skor khang rim dgu'i nang na dgongs pa mdzad cing bzhugs pas mjal du mi btub/ khyed rang rnams ngas nang du khrid kyi/ slob dpon gyi
spyan sngar btsan thabs su song la gser phul la chos zhus shig gnang 'ong gi zer nas/ der bod kyi ban de mi drug drung du phyin nas phyag 'tshal gser phul nas zhus pa/ slob
dpon chen po lags/ nged tsho bod kyi rgyal pos btang ba lags/ tshe 'di la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i chos shig zhu bar btang ba lags pas/ slob dpon
gyis gnang bar zhu/ zhu rten du gser phye bre gsum bskur ba 'di lags/ chos ma rnyed na nged rnams la rgyal pos chad pa la ske gcod du yong bas thugs rjes 'dzin 'tshal/
zhes zhus pas/ bod kyi rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i rigs/ /chos la thugs gzhol yod yin pas/ da sngon la dbang bskur dgos gsung nas/ gsang sngags kyi rtsa ba dbang yin
pas dbang ma bskur bar gsang sngags bshad du mi rung / sgrub tu yang mi rung gsungs nas zla gam drug cu rtsa brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor zhal bstan nas dbang bskur/ lha khrag
'thung lnga bcu rtsa brgyad kyis zhal bstan/ de nas zla gam lnga bcu rtsa brgyad dang / zla gam dgu pa dang / zla gam gcig pa dang / mar me bco brgyad pa dang / dpa' po
gcig pa dang / dug gsum yongs sgrol dang / thig le gcig pa dang / 'bru gsum dmug chung la sogs pa rim pas zhal phye nas bstan/ bdud rtsi sman gyi rgyud gsang ba ye shes 'khor
lo/ bdud rtsi mchog gi lung bam po brgyad pa/ man ngag sgron gsal la lag len yang khol/ nying khol bdud

rtsi thigs pa la sogs pa la brten nas bdud rtsi yon tan gyi sgrub pa/ dam pa rigs brgya'i dkyil 'khor du sman khrol bu'i sgrub pa/ ta kri ta brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor du sman
btags gtsags la brten nas sgrub pa/ de nyied rigs lnga'i dkyil 'khor du sman phye ma la brten nas sgrub pa/ gsang chen rigs gcig gi dkyil 'khor du sman gong bu la brten nas
sgrub pa/ mkha' dbyings dag pa'i dkyil 'khor bdun brtsegs kyi lha ngo sprad/ bkra shis dag pa'i rdzas tshe sgrub pa/ mkha' dbyings dag pa yum gyi mkha' la tshe sgrub pa/
gsang ba dag pa byang chub kyi sems dpa' la tshe sgrub pa dang gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du tshe bsgrubs nas 'chi med tshe'i dbang bskur/ yi nas dag pa'i chos nyid kyi dbyings
su byang chub sems sgrub pa/ mkha' dag pa sbyor ba chang byang sems dpa' sgrub pa/ snying rje dag pa sgrol ba byang chub sems sgrub pa/ gsang sngags spyod par dbang bskur
nas de rnams lag len du bshad/ dpal yang dgi skos byang rdzangs nas da lo gcig sgrubs la grub rtags re thon par gyis shig gsungs nas/ bod kyi ban de drug po gros byas
pas/ rlangs dpal gyi seng ge na re/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon gser ni thob/ chos la phrag dog byas nas bod du 'phel gyis dogs nyen yod pas/ 'o cag srog la babs nen che zer
nas mi lnga bod du 'gro bar chas pa la nam mkha'i snying po ni ma ngan yang bu la dug mi blud gsungs/ nga grub rtags shig thon nas 'ong gsungs nas zhugs/ slob dpon gyi gsung
nas sgrub pa mi byed par 'gro na bar chad yong nyen yod pas/ seng ldeng gi phur pa 'di byin gyis brlabs yod pas 'di khyer gsungs nas rlangs dpal gyi seng ge la bskur
ro/ /'di khyed rnams nyal khar sngas su thob cig bar chad 'ong nyen yod do gsungs so/ /khong rnams la dngos grub gnang nas 'ong ba dang / bal yul gyi mtsho 'gram zhig tu
nyal ba'i tshe rlangs dpal gyi seng ge nyal ba'i sngas su btab pa'i seng ldeng gi phur pa de khong gnyid du song ba'i dbu sngas nas grub gu u peg shas bton nas kho rang
gi sngas su btab po/ /sngar slob dpon gyi bka' la yid ma ches pas dam tshig nyams nas mtsho de'i nang nas klu nag po dam 'dzin zhes bya ba yod pas sbrul nag po zig byung
/ rlangs dpal gyi seng ge'i lus la 'khril nas rtse chung bcad de der gum mo/ /de nas dge slong bzhi pos rje'i spyan sngar phyin nas chos phul te mi gnyis po gcig rgya gar
du bsdad/ der rgyal po thugs ches pa la blon po gdug pa can rnams kyis chos la phrag dog dang bar chod byas te/ khyed mi drug btang ba la gnyis med par byas/ khyed rang
rnams kyang spyugs dgos zer nas 'bre rgyal ba'i blo gros byang tho yor nag por spyugs/ gru gu u peg sha zhang zhung yul du spyugs/ ru yong sing ha ra dza mdo khams smad du
spyugs/ ru gyong birya ta dza kong por spyugs/ de nas snubs nam mkha'i snying po la slob dpon hUM ka ras/ yang dag sgrub pa rtsa rgyud lta bu la 'brel chen sgron me lta
bu mdzad nas bshad/ yang dag lus kyi khog pa dang 'dra ba la de'i snying dang 'dra ba'i me gcig ma gnang nas/ lo gcig gser gyi brag bya skyibs can du bsgrubs pas dpal chen
po'i zhal mthong dngos grub thob nas rtags kyang bris sku bzhad pa dang / bdud rtsi mu tig dri ma med pa ltar

gyur pa dang / rakSha khol ba dang / gtor ma 'dod yon gyi lha mos dngos su 'bul ba dang / tshe 'phar ba dang / bsnyen phur 'tsheg pa dang / 'phar ba la sogs pa dang / rdzogs
rim ma byas par phyi nas mar byon pas khro bo'i gar dgu dang / dpal gyi chas brgyad dang ldan pa/ gtor ma yid bzhin gyi nor bu mchod sdong 'dod pa'i yon tan gyi lha mo
drug gis dngos su mchod pa 'bul ba lha la lha thim gyi tshul du byung ba dang / der bod kyi rgyal pos ngas zhabs 'og nas rde'u bton nas dbu'i mchod gnas su byas te/ chos
zhur btang ba tshur mo yong na/ kho'i rus pa snubs rgyud brlag par bya'o/ /gsungs pas der snubs nam mkha'i snying pos rgya gar nas bod du rdzu 'phrul gyis byon nas mnga'
bdag rgyal po dang mjal te/ rje la zhus pa/ khyed bzhed pa'i chos dpal yang dag sgrub pa zhes bya ba/ rgyu sems can la 'bras bu sangs rgyas phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos
grub thob pa 'di lta bu mchis so gsungs nas/ yang dag grub pa gcig bu nyid/ /sangs rgyas bde chen kun 'dus pa/ /rnal 'byor zab mo sku gsum rdzogs/ /mkha' 'gro sgyu ma
bde mchog bde/ /zhes gsungs nas kho rang gi khog pa dngul dkar gyi gri gus kha phye nas khog pa nas zhi ba'i lha tshogs sangs rgyas bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis bkra lam mer bstan
pa dang / rgyal po tshig dang don dang lha gsum kar yid ches nas nges shes skyes te phyag dbu thod bud bud du btsal lo/ /de nas rgyal pos mchod gnas su bzung nas dpal yang
dag gi chos bshad pa dang / blon po dang jo mo rnams kyis phrag dog byas te/ rgyal pos 'bangs rnams la slob dpon bya bar mi rigs pas 'di rgyal khrims la gnod pas gdug
pa gcig tu spyug go zer nas/ lho brag mkhar chur spyugs so/ /lcags phur can du sgrub pa mdzad pas grub rtags mar me rang 'bar ba dang / brag la sku rgyab gtad pas rjes dod
pa dang / phur pa brag la thebs pa dang / nyi ma'i zer la chibs nas gshegs pa dang / nyi zer la chos gos 'gel ba dang / dpal chen po longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skur zhal
mthong ste grub pa brnyes so/ /de nas dus lan gcig gi tshe rgyal po snyun gyis thebs te rim gro byas kyang phan pa ma byung bas/ mo dang rtsis byas kyang ma phan nas slob
dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la zhus pas/ 'di la gzhan cis kyang mi phan te/ snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang rgyal po dpon slob tu byas nas phyis spyugs pas dam tshig nyams pas
lan pas/ khong spyan drangs te dam tshig nyams pa bskangs na phan par 'ong gsungs pas/ lho brag mkhar chu nas spyan 'dren du btang bas khyed rang gnyis sngon la song zhig
nga nangs par zhag gsum dro bzi na yong bas khang pa dgu rim gyi steng du rgyal po'i gdan shoms shig gsungs te/ der zhag gsum dro bzhi na slob dpon nam mkha'i snying
pos nyi ma shar ba dang rgyal po'i spyan sngar byon no/ /'khor nang mis slob dpon la rgyal ba'i sku'i rim gro'i yas thags ci gsog 'tshal byas pas/ gzhan ci yang mi 'tshal
te rgyal po rang gis ci gsol ba'i zas rnams tshang bar khyer shog cig gsungs nas/ zhal skyems dang bcas pa nga la drongs shig gsungs te/ de ltar byas te drangs pas/ de zas
tshogs mdzad de gsol bas slob dpon gyis gsol ba zin pa tsam la/ 'bangs nang pa zhig gis rgyal po zhal mdangs

che ba snyam byed nas snyun dris pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas slob dpon gyis nga'i kha zas drangs pa gsol ba zin pa tsam la lha mo dkar mo gcig gis 'ongs te thal lcag na mo gcig
brgyab pas en gcig bde bar song gsungs so/ /de nas yang slob dpon la zhal zas sna tshang ba gnyis pa drangs pas gsol ba zin pa tsam la rgyal po zhal mdangs da ci bas kyang
cher song ba snyam byas nas/ yang 'bangs nang pa zhig gis rgyal po la snyun dris pas/ slob dpon gyis zhal zas gnyis drangs pa gsol zin pa tsam la nga la lha mo dmar mo
zhig 'ongs nas thal lcag na mo zhig brgyab bas/ da ci bas kyang cung zhig bde bar song gsungs so/ /yang slob dpon gyi zhal nas rgyal pos ci gsol ba ma tshang ba med pa
drongs shig gsungs nas drangs bas/ 'bangs nang 'khor ba zhig gis rgyal po la snyun dris pas/ rgyal po'i gsung gis slaub dpon gyis nga'i zas rnams gsol zin pa tsam la lha
mo mthing kha zhig 'ongs nas thal lcag da ci bas kyang na ba zhig brgyab song bas da ni nga'i lus la nad gang yang med par song gsungs pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas da rung
rgyal po snyung ba zhig kyang yod/ zas sna gcig tsam yang ma tshang ba med pa drongs shig gsungs pas/ gzhan ni ma tshang ba med de dro bar gyi dus na 'dren pa'i mdzo zho
la ka ra btab pa de ma tshang / rgyal po'i spyan gcig kyang snyung bas der de drangs pas gsol ba tsam la rgyal po yang gdangs so/ /der slob dpon la rgyal pos dam tshig nyams
pa yang bskangs so/ /de nas blon po kun na re/ rgyal po dang nam mkha'i snying po 'phrad 'dod pa yin no zer nas/ nyi ma phyed yol la khad tsam na ban des rje'i dbu skra
bsil zhig nyi ma phyed ma yol ba la dbu skra bsil ma zin na khyod rang la skyon 'bebs so zer bas/ der nam mkha'i snying pos de ltar bya'o gsungs nas nyi grib kyi mtshams
su seng ldeng gi phur pa zhig btab nas/ phyag sdigs mdzub nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gtad de/ nyi ma phyed ka gcig tsam ma btang ba la/ nyi ma stod la mnan par gyur pas
rgyal po'i dbu skra bsil ba zin nas/ slob dpon zhal nas da phyugs lug rnams tshud cig gsungs pa dang / nyi grib mtshams kyi phur pa btab pa bton pas/ nyi ma dus dang tshigs
la dbang bas yud kyis song bas/ ban de rdzu 'phrul can 'dis rang cag rnams la mthu byed du 'ongs pas gsod zer du byung nas/ rgyal po dang sku 'chag tu yong ba bsgugs pas/
der nam mkha'i snying pos thog phabs te/ hUM hUM hUM zhes hUM sgra drag po brjod nas thog sdigs mdzub kyi rtse la bskor bas/ blon po nag po rnams la la rengs/ la la brgyal/
la la bubs pa dang / slob dpon gyi zhal nas rje lha gcig sku ma nyes sam gsungs pas/ 'jigs pa che gnam lcags kyi thog sgra bas kyang ban de'i hUM sgra de rang 'jigs
so gsungs/ blon po nag po kun na re/ re 'jigs re 'jigs/ mkhar che re che zhes zer ro/ /de nas snubs nam mkha'i snying po mkhar chu'i brag la gshegs so/ /de nas rgyal po'i
mnal lam du dpal rdo rje sems dpa' nam mkha' la byon no/ /rgyu 'bras la bzla ba rtogs grol dus gcig la yong ba'i chos bka' rdzogs pa chen po bya ba yod pas/ bod kyi dge
slong mi gnyis tshol du thongs shig bya ba'i lung bstan byung nas/ der rgyal pos spa gor he 'dod kyi bu dang

rtsangs to legs kyi bu rtsangs legs grub gnyis bod du shes rab che bar grags nas/ de gnyis la bka' nan bstsal te mkhan po bo dhi sa twa la rab tu byung nas mkhan pos lo tsA
ba'i sgra bsgyur bslabs nas rgyal pos gser phye bre gang dang gser gyi pa tra gcig bskur nas bka' rdzogs pa chen po 'tshol tu btang bas/ gcan 'phrang pas gser 'phrog par
byas te spa gor bai ro tsa nas bye ma gser du bsgyur nas byin/ de nas rgya gar du phyin nas bka' rdzogs pa chen po la su mkhas dris pas/ slob dpon shrI ri sing ha mkhas
zer nas slob dpon gyi spyan sngar phyin/ gser phye bre gang po dang / gser gyi pa tra yang phyag tu phul nas tshe gcig la sangs rgya ba'i chos bka' rdzogs pa chen po bya
ba'i gdams ngag bod kyi btsan po lha sras la lung bstan byung nas bdag chos 'tshol du btang ba lags pas slob dpon gyis gnang bar zhu 'tshal zhes zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi bka'
gnang ba/ bod kyi rgyal po'i thugs dgongs dad pa dang ldan pa la/ khyed gnyis brtson 'grus dang ldan pa legs pas/ bka' rdzogs pa chen po 'di bod du dar bar 'gyur bas
ngas bshad kyi gsungs nas/ de yang rgyud nyi shu rtsa lnga bshad de/ dang po sems kyi don rtsa ba rgyas par bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che rgyas pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi
don rtogs par dka' bas de nyams su blang ba'i phyir nam mkha' che rgyas pa phyi rta'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don rnam par grol bar bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che grol ba'i
rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don mi 'gyur bar bstan pa'i phyir Tika rgyal po'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don thig le'i klong du 'dus par bstan pa'i phyir byang sems thig le'i rgyud
bshad/ sems kyi don rang byung ye shes bstan pa'i phyir ye shes thig le'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don rim pas rgyas par bstan pa'i phyir man ngag 'phreng ba'i rgyud bshad/
sems kyi don kun gyi thun mong du bstan pa'i phyir gsang ba rgyal po'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don rang gis rtogs shing khong dung chud par bya ba'i phyir shes rab ye shes
thig le'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don kun tu bzang po'i klong du thams cad gcig par bya ba'i phyir dbyings rnam par dag pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don thams cad mchog tu
bstan pa'i phyir man ngag snying po'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don mchog tu gyur pa de nyid yid ches pa bstan pa'i phyir snying po sidhi'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don rtsa ba
ma nor bar bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che rtsa ba can gyi rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don thig le nyag gcig tu bstan pa'i phyir nyag gcig dgongs pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don
ma nor ba rnal bar bzhag par bya ba'i phyir bsam gtan gcig pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don rim par brgyud nas bstan pa'i phyir bsam gtan brgyud pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi
don gzhung kun tu dgongs pa bstan pa'i phyir sgo mang gi rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don dbang rim pa bzhin bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che dbang gi rgyal po'i rgyud bshad/ sems
kyi don brjod pa'i tshig dang bral bar bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che yi ge med pa'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don dngos po thams cad ji lta bar 'byung ba bzhin du bstan pa'i
phyir rin chen 'bar ba'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don dngos po thams cad 'od gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir rin chen

sgron me'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don dgongs pa thams cad rang las byung ba bstan pa'i phyir rin chen 'phreng ba'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don khams gsum gyi ngang du gsal bar
bstan pa'i phyir nges pa snying po'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don mi 'gyur bar bstan pa'i phyir rdo rje gsang ba'i rgyud bshad/ sems kyi don sangs rgyas da lta nas yin pa'i
phyir ye nas sangs rgyas kyi rgyud bshad do/ /de nas lung chen po bco brgyad bshad de/ byang chub sems las 'byung ba'i phyir rig pa'i khu byug bshad/ rtsol sgrub thams cad
zil gyis gnon pa'i phyir rtsal chen bshad/ sems kyi don chos kyi dbyings su rdzogs pa khyung chen bshad/ sgom pa'i don dbyings su rdzogs pa byang sems sgom pa rdo la gser
zhun bshad/ sgom pa'i don mthar phyin pa mi nub rgyal mtshan nam mkha' che bshad/ sems stong pa nyid du la bzla ba'i phyir gnad du gyur pa bshad/ sems nyid kyi rang bzhin
chos kyi skur bstan pa'i phyir yang tig bshad/ sems skye shi med par srid gsum 'khor bar skor ba'i phyir srog gi 'khor lo bshad/ sems nyid la 'dod pa'i yon tan thams
cad 'byung bar bstan pa'i phyir yid bzhin nor bu bshad/ sems kyi ngang du rnam par rtog pa thams cad chos nyid mnyam pa'i ngang du bstan pa'i phyir kun 'dus bshad/ sems
la theg pa thams cad rdzogs shing 'byung ba kun nas rgyas par bstan pa'i phyir nam mkha' che rgyal po bshad/ sems nyid kun tu bzang po'i ngang la bzhag pa kun gyi mchog gi
gtso por bstan pa'i phyir rtse mo byung rgyal bshad/ sems kyi rang bzhin don dam pa'i ngang la spros pa bral zhing bde gsal la gnas pa'i phyir bde 'byams bshad/ sems nyon
mongs pa'i skyon gyis ma gos shing yon tan gyi 'bras bus spud pa'i phyir bde ba phra bkod bshad/ sems kyi klong du 'khor 'das kun 'byung ba bstan pa'i phyir rtogs chen
bshad/ sems kyi theg pa thams cad kyi spyi 'ching ba'i phyir chings bshad do/ /de nas slob dpon shrI ri sing ha'i zhal nas chos rdzogs par bshad pa yin pas/ rgya gar ba
chos la phrag dog che bas lam du srog gi bar chad yong nyen yod pas rkang mgyogs lo gcig sgrubs shig gsungs nas rkang mgyogs kyi gdams ngag gnang ngo / /slob dpon gyis spa
gor bai ro tsa nar ming btags so/ /rtsangs rkang mgyogs mi sgrub par rje la ngo so 'dod nas sngon la song bas gcan 'phrang pas bsad do/ /bai ros lo gcig bsgrubs te grub
pa dang / gcan 'phrang gi dpon ku ha dha ru bya ba dang grogs po byas rngan pa gser phye byin nas mna' tho byas/ chos thams cad rgya dpe ta la'i lo ma la bris nas khur te
rkang mgyogs rogs pos gcan 'phrang dang po las bsgral te log go/ /rgya gar gyi paNDi ta thams cad kyi rmi lam na/ rgya gar gyi nyi ma bod kyi ban de zhigata gis khur te
nub pa rmis so/ /de nas rkang mgyogs bkram pa dang gcan 'phrang gi dpon pos bod kyi ban de 'dra ba ma song / mtha'i mon bu spyi lham pa zhig song ste des ni cang ma khyer
bar song / de yin na deng sang bod du slebs yod byas pas der rkang mgyogs pa rnams log go/ /de nas spa gor bai ro tsa nas rje'i thad du slebs par 'ongs nas/ rje lha sras
bzhed pa'i chos tsho ni lon na'ang / rgya gar chos la phrag dog che la bod kyi blon po chos la gnag rgyal po'i

snyan khung srab pas snyan phra 'byung srid pas de la mi gsan par zhu'o zhes springs so/ /bai ros rkang mgyogs bsgrubs pas zhag bdun gyis bod du slebs pa dang / phyi na tshur
rgya gar gyis bang chen pa btang nas khyed bod kyi ban de des chos ma rnyed par mu stegs kyi ngan sngags mang po khyer song bas/ des bod khams phung bar byed pas sod cig
ces de skad bsgrags so/ /de nas bod kyi blon po kun gyis de gsod dgos/ nged bod rnams phung bar byed pas yin zer bas/ rgyal pos rgya gar chos la phrag dog byad pa yin
te de ltar ma yin gsungs kyang ma phan nas/ der mtha'i sprang po gcig bzung ste bai ro tsa na'i gos de la bskon nas zangs kha sbyar du bcug gzer gyis bsdams nas chu la bskyur
btang / bai ro tsa na pho brang mdzod du ka ba khong stong brus pa gcig tu bzhag nas/ nam phyed tsa na rgyal po chos gsan pa la/ sems sde bco brgyad kyi stod kyi chos
lnga tshar ba dang 'bangs nang pa gcig dang jo mo tshe spongs bza' me tog sgron gyis tshor nas phyir 'bugs pa dang / blon po phyi nang thams cad kyi tshor nas rje la thugs
nor ba chen po mnga' / yab mes kyi dkor mdzod kyi gser thams cad 'jim pa la byugs nas nga lha khang mdzad gsungs/ nga chos byed gsungs nas mtha'i mi bzung nas chu la
bskyur/ bod phung bar byed pa'i rgya gar gyi ngan sngags mkhan phugs su bcug nas des ci zer la nyan/ de la chad pa gcod pas sgor thon cig de la chad pa mi gcod na rgyal khrims
gshig zer bas de la rgyal po thugs ma mnyes nas 'o cag ji ltar bya bai ro tsa na la gsungs pas/ rje lags bdag sngon yang rgyal po tsha ba'i rong du rgyal mo legs bzher
dpal mo bya ba'i bur skyes/ da rung las kyi 'phro dang gdul bya skal ldan yod pas der spyugs shig rje nyid rang da dung rgya gar gyi paNDi ta rnams kyi nang nas mkhas
pa bi ma la ti tra bya ba bzhugs pas de spyan drongs la chos gra tshugs/ de'i dus su nga'i chos 'di bden pa ma nor ba gcig yin nam ma yin gtug tu gtong gis de btang ba dang
bod kyis yid ches nas rje nyid mjal te mche gsungs te/ rje la 'bangs med rgyal kha blon gyis bsgyur nas spa gor bai ro tsa na rgyal mo tsha ba rong du spyugs so/ /der
bod kyi rtogs chen pa byung zer nas shig gi dong du bskyur/ de la gnod pa cung zad kyang med do/ /bai ro tsa na bod kyi rgyal blon gyis rgya gar yul du chos 'tshol du btang
bas rgya gar gyis chos la phrag dog byas nas ngan sngags yod byas nas spyugs pa yin/ nga 'di'i skye ba sngon ma la rgyal mo legs bzher dpal mo'i bu dge slong parNa bya
ba de nga yin no/ /sngon gyi las 'phro yod pas 'dir yong dgos pa byung gsungs pas/ rgyal mo klu mo la sogs pas tshe snga phyi dran pas dge parNar 'dug zer nas bzhags pa
byas/ zhabs spyi bor blangs/ khong sbal dong dang shig dong bskyur pas sdig sgrig kyang sbyangs so/ /de nas rgyal mo klu mo dang rgyal bu g.yu sgra snying po la sogs pa
la bka' rdzogs pa chen po tshar bar bshad/ bai ro tsa nas bka' rdzogs pa chen po slob dpon shrI ri sing ha'i drung du zhus nas/ mthar rgyal mo tsha ba'i rong du spyugs pa
dang / de yang skal ldan rgyal po g.yu sgra snying po la bka' rdzogs pa chen po bshad pa'i skabs so/ /de nas

rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la/ nga yis bod kyi rgyal khams 'di chos la 'god par 'dod pas/ bod kyi shes rab can gang btang yang chos ngo mtshar can rnyed nas byung ba la/ blon
po chos la gnag pas phrag dog byas shing chos la spyod dbang ma byung / chos 'tshol du btang ba thams cad kyang blon pos rgyal khrims la snyad cing spyugs pas/ da ni rgya
gar nas paNDi ta mkhas pa spyan drangs/ bod kyi shes rab dang dad pa can thams cad bka' 'og tu bsdus te rgyal pos bka' bstsal pa/ nga chos skyong ba'i rgyal po yin pas dus
de ring nas chos khrims 'cha' ba yin no/ /rab tu sus byung nus/ lo tsA ba sus slob nus/ sgrub pa sus byed nus/ zhabs 'og nas rde'u bton nas de dbu'i mchod gnas byed do
zhes bka' khrims bcas so/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas 'das ma 'ongs da lta gsum gyi mngon par shes pa mnga' ba des/ gung gral nas rgyal blon rnams la/ bka' bsgo
gsungs pa/ rje gcig chos kyi rgyal po lags/ /chos khrims bcas pa shin tu legs/ /bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ /dug gsum sku gsum thugs su shes/ /dug lnga ye shes lnga
ru shes/ /rnam rtog chos kyi dbyings su go/ /nyon mongs rgyud la rtag tu 'chang / /de rtogs yon tan mngon shes kyis/ /phyi ma ci 'byung da lta shes/ /snga ma ci yin 'di
ltar shes/ /bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas dang / /mkhan po bo dhi sa twa dang / /chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan gsum/ /skye ba 'di yi snga ma la/ /ma gu ta yi yul du ni/
/mon phrug spun gsum dag tu skyes/ /ma ni dbul mo bya rdzi mo/ /ma'i dge rtsar mchod rten bzhengs/ /mchod rten bya rung kha shor kha/ /mchod rten brtsigs shing smon lam
btab/ /'khyags pa chags yul mata' 'khob tu/ /chos kyi bstan pa 'dzugs par shog /de skad smon lam btab pa la/ /skye ba 'di'i gong rol du/ /srin gyi bu dang drang srong bu/
/bram ze'i bu dang gsum du byung / /snga ma'i mchod rten de la ni/ /mchod pa chen po byas nas ni/ /smon lam so sor 'di skad btab/ /drang srong bu ni rtsad po yin/ /'khyags
pa chags yul mtha' 'khob kyi/ /chos skyong rgyal por skyes nas ni/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa skyong bar shog /yang de'i las dang smon lam gyis/ /chos skyong rgyal por skyes
pa yin/ /chos skyong rgyal po bya bar rigs/ /bram ze'i bu ni bo dhi sa twa yin/ /chos skyong rgyal por khyod skyes nas/ /rgyal po chos skyong bla mchod bgyi/ /yang de'i
las dang smon lam gyis/ /za hor skyes kyang 'di ru 'dzoms/ /mkhan slob rab byung bya bar rigs/ /bdag ni srin bu phra mo'i bu/ /da lta pad ma 'byung gnas yin/ /chos skyong
rgyal por khyod skyes nas/ /gdug pa 'dul zhing bstan pa skyong bar shog /yang de las dang smon lam gyis/ /o rgyan skyes kyang 'di ru 'dzoms/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa nga
rang srung / /bgegs dang log 'dren nga yis 'dul/ /rgya gar yul gyi ma ga dha'i/ /drang srong dpal ldan zhes bya ba/ /ma ni drang srong sha ta yin/ /a pa a ru tshe 'phos pa/
/bod kyi mnga' bdag rgyal por skyes/ /mi la dgos dgu gces pa dang / /sde snod gsum gyi chos rnams kyang / /rgyal po nyid kyi ring la byung / /rgya gar yul gyi sha ka'/
/smad tshong pra ma ni la ta'i/ /phru gur skyes pa tshe 'phos pa/ /dharma su tra tshe 'phos pa/ /khri bzang
