yab lhag blon po yin/ /dharma shi la tshe 'phos pa/ /mdo bzher sbrail chung blon po yin/ /dharma pradznyA tshe 'phos pa/ /khri 'bring lha 'od blon po yin/ /dharma ka ya tshe
'phos pa/ /shud pu dpal gyi seng ge yin/ /dharma pu tra tshe 'phos pa/ /rgyal po nang gi blon po yin/ /dharma mi tra tshe 'phos pa/ /ta ra klu gong blon po yin/ /blon po
drug pa de rnams kyis/ /'khyags pa chags yul mtha' 'khob kyi/ /bod kyi yul du byung ba yin/ /rgyal po nyid kyi blon por gyur/ /rgyal po nyid kyi ring las byung / /blon
po chos la gnag pa ni/ /blon po drug po 'di rnams kyis/ /skye ba yang snga'i gong rol du/ /dud 'gro'i lus su so sor blangs/ /skye ba yang sngar ci sbyangs pa/ /skye ba 'di
la mtshan rtags/ /sna rtser sme ba nag po yod/ /dbus 'gyur tshal de'i yul dag tu/ /glang rmon ta ra klu gong de/ /sngar yang glang rmon byas pa'i rtags/ /gnya' ba'i gong
na sme ba yod/ /yul phyogs de'i khyi mo ni/ /gnas gzhi bsrungs pala'i yan lag gi/ /sngar yang gnas gzhi bsrung pala'i rtags/ /dpral ba'i dbyings na sme ba yod/ /yul phyogs
de'i bya ka thub/ /mdo bzher sprel chung blon po yin/ /sngar yang bya ru skyes pa'i rtags/ /lte ba'i khung na bya spu yod/ /yul phyogs de'i lce spyang ni/ /rgya ta ngang
mi bya ba yin/ /sngar yang lce spyang byas pa'i rtags/ /ya thod lce spyang 'dra ba yod/ /dud 'gro'i tshe 'phos smad 'tshong ma'i/ /bu ru skyes nas bod yul du/ /'dus te
tshogs par smon lam btab/ /da lta rgyal po'i blon por skyes/ /blon po rnams kyang chos srid skyong / /phyi ma mtho ris chos dang phrad/ /chos la mi mos ngan 'gror 'gro/
/pur na pur mo bram ze'i bu/ /bo dhi sa twa bya bar skyes/ /dge slong mang po grangs med kyang / /mkhan po byas nas rab tu byung / /sgra bsgyur tshal gyi drang srong ni/
/dge slong sing ha tshe 'phos pa/ /dge slong dpal dbyangs bya bar skyes/ /na ra dza ra yul dbus kyi/ /smad 'tshong snying po brtul zhugs dang / /drang srong ku ma ra dza'i
bu/ /dge slong rgyal bu snying po de/ /tshul khrims bsrungs te tshe 'phos pa/ /rgyal ba mchog dbyangs zhes byar skyes/ /rgya gar yul gyi mu tra na/ /bram ze ghun si dhi
dang / /rgyal po legs bzher dpal mo'i bu/ /dge slong dze ta tshe 'phos pa/ /nam mkha'i snying po bya bar skyes/ /rdo rje gdan gyi smad 'tshong ma/ /ku ma ha snyoms ru ma
dang / /drang srong ku ma du rtsi'i bu/ /dge slong 'jam dpal tshe 'phos pa/ /klu'i rgyal mtshan bya ba skyes/ /ga'u cig ta zher la'i bu/ /smad 'tshong bu mo ni ra'i bu/
/rgya gar yul nas tshe 'phos pa/ /ka ba dpal brtsegs bya bar skyes/ /lcags kyi sdong po'i glang chen gyi/ /klu mo nyid 'gyur tshe 'phos pa/ /dran pa nam mkha'i bya bar skyes/
/drang srong bu mo ser skya lnga / /rgya gar yul nas tshe 'phos pa/ /dge slong mi lnga dag tu skyes/ /dge ldan bde skyid rgyal bu gnyis/ /rgya gar yul nas tshe 'phos
pa/ /ye shes dbyangs dang bran ka gnyis/ /legs drug dge slong dar skyes deng / /tsha ba rong gi rgyal mo'i bu/ /dge slong pur na tshe 'phos pa/ /bai ro tsa na bya bar skyes/
/bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ /snga ma ci yin de ltar shes/ /rgyal po nyid kyi sku ring la/ /chos

khrims shin tu dar ba 'ong / /zhes gsungs pas/ /bod ru bzhi rgyal po'i mnga' 'og tu bsdus pa rnams rjes yi rang ngo / /rgyal pos kyang chos khrims dar gyi mdun pa 'dra ba mdzad
do/ /chos khrims bsdams nas rab tu byung ba rnams gyi bting ste dbu'i mchod gnas su bzhag go/ /rab tu byung ba'i sde bcugs/ chos gang la mos pa ci dgar spyod pa bkas
gnang / mi skya pho mo la yang yig rtsis gang slob kyang slob palar gnang / bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' gsung sgrog pa dang / bka' yi ger 'dri ba po rnams la mchod gnas su
ming btags nas gnang ba byin no/ /shes rab su che ba dang kha lce bde ba rgya gar yul du chos dang / sgra bsgyur slob tu btang ngo / /'phral skad chos skad thams cad slob
dpon bo dhi sa twa la bslabs/ rab tu byung ba'i mkhan slob gnyis ka slob dpon bo dhi sa twas mdzad/ rgyal pos chos khrims bcas pa'i dus lags so/ /de nas yang mnga' bdag
rgyal po'i thugs la/ dam pa'i chos nyi ma shar ba lta bu byed pa la rgya gar yul nas paNDi ta mkhas pa slob dpon bi ma la spyang drang dgongs nas/ slob dpon de yang jo bo
thugs rje chen po'i sprul pa yin te/ rgyal po dharma a sho ka bya ba'i sras mo lha lcam dharma bodhi bya ba shin tu mdzes pa lha'i bu mo 'dra ba zhig yod pa la/ de gnyid
log pa'i rma lam na mi dkar palo shin tu mdzes pa 'od zer 'phro ba zhig byung nas/ bdud rtsi bum pa gang spyi bo tshangs pa'i bu ga na mar song nas lus bde bas gang ba zhig
rmis/ lus la ma bde ba med par bu tsha gcig btsas te/ khyo med pa'i bu ngo tsha nas bye ma'i gseb tu bor bas mig khra hrig ge 'dug ste yang blangs nas gsos pas/ zhag
dang zla ba gzhan bas skyed che ba zhig byung nas lo lnga lon nas rig pa'i gnas thams cad la sbyangs pas lhag par chos la mkhas par gyur to/ /ming yang bye ma la mig khrar
btags so/ /de nas rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs dang / cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / rma rin chen mchog dang gsum la/ gser phye bre
zhi gcig brdzangs nas rgya gar gyi 'bri ka ma la shi la'i gtsug lag khang nang bzhugs pa'i chos skyong ba'i rgyal po dharma tsakra la gser 'di phul la/ nga'i gser phul ba'i
skyes lan du phyi nang gi chos mtha' dag la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta gcig zhu gyis la/ lo tsA ba khyed gsum gyis spyan drongs shog gsungs nas btang ngo / /de nas lo tsA ba
gsum gyis 'bri ka ma la shi la'i gtsug lag khang du rgyal po la gser phul nas zhus pa ni/ nged bod kyi chos skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis btang ba lags/
gser phul ba'i skyes lan du phyi nang gi chos mtha' dag la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta gcig brdzang bar zhu yin gda' bas gnang bar zhu zhes lo tsA ba gsum gyis zhus pas/ rgyal po'i
zhal nas/ 'o na paNDi ta lnga brgya nangs par tsha ba la/ 'dir tshogs pa'i gral du zhu dgos gsungs nas/ rgyal pos kyang gser gyi maNDal re phul nas zhus pa/ bod kyi chos
skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis nga la skyes su gser bskur nas/ de'i lan du paNDi ta mkhas pa gcig zhu bya ba byung nas lo tsA ba 'di gsum spyan 'dren
du btang ba yin pas/ khyed rnams kyi nang nas phyi nang gi chos la mkhas pa gcig gshegs 'tshal zhes gsungs pas/

paNDi ta lnga brgya'i nang na mkhas pa chen por gyur pa/ slob dpon chen bi ma la mi tra gung gral la bzhugs pas/ g.yas kyi paNDi ta phyed dang sum brgya/ g.yon gyi paNDi ta
phyed dang sum brgya pos/ dbus kyi slob dpon bi ma la mi tra la spyan re re bltas pas/ don gyis song zhig par bskul nas/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tra bzhengs te/ bo dhi sa
twa dha thim zhes lan gsungs pas/ lo tsA ba la gsum po la go ba mi 'dra ba gsum skyes so/ /'bro ka ba dpal brtsegs kyi go ba la/ gzhu mo dag la brten pa'i mda'/ /skyes bus
mtheb mdzub rtsol phod na/ /mdas kyang 'ben ngor phyin par nus/ /zhes gsungs nas bzhud par go/ /rma rin chen mchog gi go ba la/ nyag thag dag la brten pa'i gru/ /skyes
bu'i skya bas rtsol phod na/ /grus kyang chu la sgrol bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs nas gshegs par go /lcog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi go ba la/ yon tan dag dang ldan pa'i mi/ /yang
yul min pa'i sa phyogs su/ /lus kyi bum pa gar 'dren pa/ /sems chu bo gzhan du 'bo/ /zhes gsungs nas gshegs par go /de nas rgyal po dang paNDi ta rnams kyis bka' phab
nas/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tra lo tsA ba gsum gyis spyan drangs nas ka ba li sor bzi pa gcig la rgya yig bdun bris pa zhig bsnams nas byon no/ /der bsam yas su phyag phebs
nas rgyal po rje 'bangs rnams kyis bsu ba byas/ bsam yas su 'khor sa chen mor spyan drangs pa dang rgyal po la yang phyag ma mdzad/ lha la yang phyag ma mdzad pas/ blon
po rnams kyis nged kyis lha khang 'dir sngar yang paNDi ta mang po spyan drangs/ da yang spyan 'dren pas khyed kyis rgyal po la yang phyag mi 'tshal/ lha la yang phyag
mi 'tshal pa ji tsug lags byas pas/ khyed rgyal blon rnams kyis phyag gi don mi shes sam gsungs pas/ rgyal pos phyag gi don mi shes gsungs pas/ ngas lha dang gnyis su med
pa'i phyag gcig btsal zin/ phyag lhas mi theg pas/ lha la yang phyag mi 'tshal/ rgyal po la yang phyag mi 'tshal lo zhes gsungs pas/ rgyal po'i thugs la 'o na nang pa sangs
rgyas pa rang yin nam/ phyi pa mu stegs shig rang yin nam snyam nas/ slob dpon gyis rgyal po la thugs yid ma ches sam gsungs/ bi ma las chos gos gsol nas rdzu 'phrul
gyis phyag mdzad pa/ rnam par snang mdzad gzugs sku la/ /bi ma la ye shes lha de'i phyag /kun rdzob ngo bos phyag 'bul lo/ /zhes phyag 'tshal ba'i tshul byas pas/ rnam par
snang mdzad dbu'i gtsug nas zhabs gdan khri'i bar gas so/ /rgyal po'i thugs la/ mu stegs pa rang yin par 'dug snyam nas/ zhal ngo nag ting nger song ba dang / yang slob
dpon gyis/ rgyal po yid ma ches sam ma dgyes sam gsungs pas/ ma dga' zhus so/ /yang slob dpon gyis/ rnam par snang mdzad ye shes lha'i lha/ /bi ma la mi tra ye shes lhas/
/ye shes lnga ldan rtags kyi dbang bskur ro/ /zhes gsungs nas/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi spyi bor phyag bzhag pas/ sngon la dbu rtse rigs gsum 'od kyis khyab/ de nas bsam
yas kyi lha khang 'od kyis khyab par gyur nas rab tu gnas pa yang mdzad do/ /de nas rgyal po la phyag bgyi 'o gsungs nas phyag gnang bas/ rgyal po la phyag bgyi 'o gsungs
nas phyag gnang bas/ rgyal po'i gsung nas phyir dge slong gi dge 'dun yin/ nang gsang sngags kyi grub pa

brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor par 'dug phyag mi mdzad par zhu zhus pas/ bi ma la'i zhal nas/ bod chos skyong ba'i rgyal por 'dug pas ces kyang phyag 'tshal gsungs nas/ phyag bstabs
pas/ rgyal po'i na bza' slob dpon gyi sku'i 'od zer gyis hrog hrog tshig pas/ rgyal pos bi ma la la phyag dbu thod bud bud 'tshal lo/ /de nas slob dpon bi ma la mi tra
gdan seng ge'i khri la bzhugs/ gab rtse dgu rtseg gi gdan bting nas za 'og gi smug ber sku la gsol/ 'jig rten gyi zhal zas rnam pa mang po drangs/ gser phye bre gsum dngul
gyi bum par blugs nas phul bas/ slob dpon gyis zhal gnag tshom mer bzhugs nas ci yang mi gsungs/ rgyal po'i thugs la lho bal 'dod pa can/ da dung ma tshim par 'dug snyam
pa dang / rgyal po'i thu bar/ slob dpon gyis bye ma bre gsum blugs nas dar cig bzung tsa na rgyal po'i thu bas thub par bye ma gser du song 'dug rgyal po chen po/ nga la
snang ba thams cad gser du yod/ rgyal po tshogs rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir du/ re zhig 'bul ba blang gis gsungs so/ /slob dpon bi ma la spyan drangs pa'i lo rgyus so/ /de
nas rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis seng nga'i yul nas/ slob dpon dha na shi la bya ba'i mkhas pa chen po spyan drangs/ rgya nag po'i yul nas slob dpon ka ma la shI
la spyan drangs/ za hor yul nas slob dpon bo dhi sa twa dang / kha che'i slob dpon bi ma la mi tra/ u rgyan gyi slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / slob dpon chen po rnam
pa lnga / lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan/ sna nam gyi ban de ye shes sde/ rma rin chen mchog dznyA ku ma ra/ lo tsA ba mchan bu 'dan ma rtse mang
/ snubs nam mkha'i snying po/ a tsarya ye shes dbyangs/ mgo 'brom pus 'byin/ lo ki chung / de ltar lo paN mang po spyan drangs/ rgyal pos chos gsung bar zhu ba phul re/
slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas ni/ sku mnga' spangs pas pad ma las sku 'khrungs pa'i phyir khams gsum dbang du sdud cing / dregs pa zil gyis gnon pa'i mthu mnga' ba yul gar
byon yang yul de'i lha srin gyis srog snying phul/ khyad par du yang dpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i sa gzhi btul bas gdan seng ge'i khri gsum brtsegs la bzhugs/
slob dpon bi ma la mi tra paNDi ta lnga brgya'i nang nas mkhas pa chen po yin pas bka' rgya mtsho sngags phyi nang / 'dul ba/ mdo sde/ mngon pa'i sde snod shes pas gdan
seng ge'i khri nyis brtsegs la bzhugs so/ /paNDi ta gzhan rnams ni gdan seng ge'i khri re re la bzhugs so/ /lo tsA ba rnams ni khri gab rtse la bzhugs so/ /rgyal pos
gser gyi maNDal re phul nas/ rgya nag gi nga / bal po'i go la/ bod 'bru chang / rgya gar gyi 'bras chang drangs/ phyag 'tshal skor ba byas nas zhus pa/ e ma ho/ bdag ni chos
skyong rgyal por zhal bzhes pas/ rgya gar yul na bzhugs pa yi/ chos bka' dang bstan bcos rgyud lung gcig kyang ma lus par 'dir ni gsung du gsol/ dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor
lo bskor du gsol/ dam pa'i chos kyi sgron me spar du gsol/ dam pa'i chos kyi char chen dbab tu gsol/ dam pa'i chos kyi rnga chen rdung du gsol/ dam pa'i chos kyi dung
chen 'bud du gsol/ dam pa'i chos rgyal mtshan sgreng du gsol/ zhes zhus so/ /de nas lo paN rnams arya pa lo'i

gling du spyan drangs/ sgra bsgyur gling du sgra bsgyur/ rnam par snang mdzad gling du chos bshad/ lo ni bcu gsum du chos grwa btsugs/ u rgyan skad dang / za hor skad/ kha
che'i skad dang / li'i skad/ rgya gar rgya nag skad du bsgyur nas bshad/ de nas rgya gar gyi slob dpon dha na shi la dang / dzi na mi tra dang / ka ba dpal brtsegs dang /
cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / sna nam gyi ban de ye shes sde dang / de rnams kyis sgra bsgyur dang lo tsA ba byas nas/ chos mdo sde dkon mchog brtsegs pa dang / phal
po che dang / lang kar gshegs pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa dang / bka' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i skor ma lus pa dang / rgya nag gi slob dpon ka ma la shI la dang
/ lo tsA ba rma rin chen mchog gis dpang skong phyag stong pa la sogs pa mdo sde rgya nag ma mang po bsgyur/ slob dpon bo dhi sa twa dang / lo tsA ba dang mchan bu ba
rnams kyis mdo sde dang / 'dul ba/ mngon pa gsum gyi gzhung thams cad bsgyur ro/ /gzhan yang sman bla dang / don zhags/ sgrol ma/ rnam rgyal/ rnam 'joms/ gdugs dkar la sogs
pa phyi kri yog u pa la sogs mang po bsgyur ro/ /slob dpon bi ma la mi tra/ lo tsA ba snyags dznyA na ku ma ra dri med zla shar gyis bka' rdzogs pa chen po'i skor dang
/ gsang sngags phyi nang mang po bsgyur ro/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / lo tsA ba snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis sgrub pa bka'
brgyad dang / bka' brgyad yongs rdzogs/ gsang sngags rdzongs 'phrang la sogs pa/ gzhan yang drag sngags thog ser bstan srung mang po bsgyur ro/ /de'i skabs su spa gor bai
ro tsa nas rgyal mo tsha ba'i rong nas rgyal bu g.yu sgra snying po btang ste ngas rgya gar nas dka' ba spyad nas slob dpon shrI sing has gsungs pa'i chos 'di yang dag
pa'i chos yin par 'dug gam mi 'dug ltos la shog cig da lta lo paN mang po tshogs nas bsam yas na sgra bsgyur dang zhus dag mang po byed kyi yod pas der song zhig zer te/
slob dpon bi ma la mi tras bka' rdzogs pa chen po gsungs pa las/ snga dro bi ma la la rgyal po rje 'bangs kyis chos gsan/ phyi dro g.yu sgra snying po la gsan pas/ mnyam
kri li li byung bas/ der bod kyi blon po rnams kyang spa gor bai ro tsa na spyugs pa la 'gyod nas slar rgyal mo tsha ba'i rong nas bai ro tsa na spyan drangs te/ dang po
rgya gar yul du chos 'tshol bar btang bas gcan 'phrang la sgyu ma'i gser gyis bslus/ rkang mgyogs grub pas rkang mgyogs kyis ma zin/ legs grub gcan 'phrang pas bsad/ nya
sul dgros/ (ri sul bgrod/) sgyu ma bltas kyang gser med pas/ de tshur bcad rkang mgyogs 'phrang srung ba med de drin che/ spa gor bai ro tsa nas sgra bsgyur nyi shu rtsa
gcig shes pas gzhan bas rgyal mo tsha ba rong du spyugs pa sdig pa'i dong / sbal ba'i dong / shig dong du bskyur bas ma shi ba/ sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yin pas/
gdan seng ge'i khri gcig brtsegs nas bzhugs so/ /bod kyi rgyal blon rnams kyis kyang spyugs pa la 'gyod pa skyes bshags pa phul/ zhabs spyi bor blangs so/ /de nas bai
ro tsa nas chos mang po bsgyur ro/ /lo paN mang pos bka' bstan bcos/ lung man ngag bka'

phyi nang / sngags phyi nang rgyud 'grel mang po bsgyur nas/ chos kyi 'khor so bskor ro/ /de nas rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyis slob dpon rnams la gsungs pa/ bdag bsod
nams kyang rab tu byung / bsam pa thams cad kyang yid bzhin du grub/ dam pa'i chos kyang ma lus pa nyi ma shar ba lta bu byung / rgya dkar nag gi chos kyang ma lus par bod
du bsgyur zhing / chod bshad pa bka' drin che/ bdag la tshe yang rab tu ring ba'i chos gcig zhu 'tshal zhes tshogs kyi 'khor lo yang yang bskor nas zhus pas/ slob dpon
pad mas gsungs pa/ rgyal po mnga' thang che ba dang / /bod khams dad pa skyes pa yis/ /cung zhig rgyal khams dar bar mchi/ /glang gi lo'i lo phud la/ /rgyal pos dgung lo
lnga bcu rtsa drug bzhes/ /de la rgyal po 'da' dus yin/ /sku'i rim gro bgyis pa yis/ /mi lo bcu gsum sku tshe bsrings/ /de la rgyal po dgung du gshegs/ /rgyal srid mnga'
thang chung du 'gro/ /de 'das phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa gcig /rgyal po ral pa can zhes bya/ /gdung rabs gsum nas 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de yis bstan pa rgyas par byed/ /rgyal
po de'i tshe smad la/ /bdud kyi rgyal po sdig spyod can/ /glang gi ming can 'byung nas ni/ /dam pa'i chos khrims snub par byed/ /dus ngan 'byung ba gdon mi za/ /rgyal
khrims zhig nas rgyal po gsod/ /bod 'bangs sil bu phyogs bcur chad/ /rgyal po'i sku'i rim gro gyis shig /gsungs nas paNDi ta dang lo tsA ba rnams bka' gros mdzad de/ phyi'i
bskongs rim gror thugs dam rgyal po'i mdo bcu bsgyur te/ shes rab snying po lta ba'i mdo/ 'da' ka ye shes sgom pa'i mdo/ byang chub ltung bshags bshags pa'i mdo/ rdo rje
rnam 'joms khrus kyi mdo/ bzang po spyod pa smon lam mdo/ tshe dpag med tshe bsrings pa'i mdo/ gos sngon can srung ba'i mdo/ nor rgyun ma nor sgrub pa'i mdo/ gtsug tor
dkar mo bzlog pa'i mdo/ yi ge gcig ma snying po'i mdo/ de rnams bsgyur nas rgyal po'i thugs dam du phog nas nar mar mdzad/ nang bskongs su sngags kyi spang skong cha lag
dang bcas pa bskyur nas yid dam mdzad/ de yang sngon sems can lus srul pos slob dpon bsad de mtshams med kyi las byas pas dmyal bar lhung ba la dpal kun du bzang pos thugs
rjes bzung nas bshad pa de bzhin du rgyal po'i dam tshig nyams chag bskongs te/ sdig sgrib byang bar gyur to/ /gsang ba'i bskongs su bshags pa bsnyen sgrub dang bcas pa
mdzad/ ye shes sku mchog brjod med kyi bshags pa/ mkha' 'gro sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor lha grangs kyi bshags pa/ lha ba'i klong bshags don dam lta ba'i bshags pa/ dam tshig
nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa/ sa ma ya 'bum sde bsdus te rkang grangs kyi bshags pa dang / gshags pa ru chen bzhi bsgyur nas bram ze thod pa can la/ dpal rdo rje sems dpas gsungs
pas sgrib pa dag pa bzhin du/ rgyal po'i dam tshig nyams chag bskangs te sgrib pa dag par gyur to/ /sku las 'byung ba bzhi las byung ba'i nad la/ rgya yi sman pa ha
cang te tsa dang / bla sman pa myang tsan pa shi la sogs pas sman dpyad mang po bsgyur ro/ /sman dang bcud len gyi sbyor ba'i thabs mang po yang mdzad do/ /slob dpon pad
mas mdos le'u stong phrag gcig dang / lha 'dre stong gi dra ba/ ma mo srid pa bem/ srid pa mtsho bzhi dang /

mtsho gcig la sogs pa pho mdos/ mo mdos mang po bsgyur/ gzhan yang gshen rje gshed 'char ka nag po/ rgyal po rtse mdos/ mdos phran mang po dang bcas pa bsgyur ro/ /klung sgrub/
klu gter/ klu rta bzhugs pa dang / pho brang gso ba dang / gdon 'grol ba dang / byad 'grol ba la sogs pa cho ga mang po mdzad do/ /rta mgrin na ga klu 'dul/ drag po
gsum sgril/ khro bo 'dul pa/ yang gsang khros pa/ sku lnga khros pa/ gnyen pokhyung gi sgrub thabs dang bcas pa bsgyur ro/ /srung ba'i cha lag brgya rtsa brgyad bsgyur cing
mdzad do/ /de ltar rim gro byas pas rgyal po'i sku tshe lnga bcu rtsa drug las med pa la lo bcu gsum sku tshe bsrings so/ /slob dpon pad ma'i zhal nas/ spyir bsod nams
kyang yang rab tu gyur pa la sku tshe yang rab tu gyur pa phyin tshad mi 'ong gsungs/ rgyal po'i sku'i rim gro'i lo rgyus chos 'byung ngo / /de nas rgyal pos rgya gar nas
gdan drangs pa'i paNDi ta rnams la gser phye sil ma bre gsum phul/ na bza' za 'og gi smug ber la sogs pa mang po phul te gtang rag btang ngo / /lo tsA ba rnams la chos
kyi rtsis dang bya dga' gnang ngo / /dbu'i chos gnas su bsten no/ /slob dpon bi ma la mi tra dang / rgya gar gyi paNDi ta rnams yul du gshegs pa gnang ste/ lo tsA ba dang
bod 'bangs rnams kyis rgya gar yul du bskyal ste/ rgya gar nas chos mi sdom par/ rgya gar gyi chos skyong ba'i rgyal pos bka' bkrol nas bod la shin tu bka' drin che ba lags
so/ /rgyal po khri srong lde btsan shin tu bka' drin che ba lags so/ /slob dpon pad ma/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa/rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gsum/ skye ba yang snga la
yang las 'brel gyis spun du gyur pa yin pas bzhud par ma gnang / slob dpon rnam gnyis kyis kyang bzhugs par zhal gyis bzhes te/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa byang chub gling
du dgongs pa la bzhugs so/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas mchims phu brag dge 'ur dgongs pa la bzhugs so/ /de nas mnga' bdag rgyal po'i thugs la/ da ni chos ma sgrub na mi
phan par 'dug pas/ gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i chos zhu dgos snyam nas mchims phu na slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas bzhugs pa la/ dar zab kyi khri brtsegs pa/ spyang dkar
gyi slog pa dang / za 'og gi smug ber sku la gsol/ 'bras chad dwangs ma dngul skyogs bkang nas phyag tu drangs/ 'jig rten gyi spyan gzigs sna tshogs drangs nas zhu ba
zhus pa'i tshul ni/ sku gsung thugs kyi sgo nas bstod de zhus pa/ oM thugs rje chen po 'gro ba'i 'dug tshul mgon/ /'bar ba'i sku ltar 'jig rten dregs pa 'dul/ /sa thob tshe
dbang dus gsum bgres rgud med/ /chos kyi sku dang mtshungs la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /a pad ma zla gam rdo rje'i ljags dkyil nas/ gsang sngags 'phro 'dui legs ldan dpal gyi
tshul/ zhi rgyas dbang drag gsang sngags rgyal po'i tshul/ /dpal chen gsung dang mtshungs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /hUM thugs khar nyi zla hUM la sngags kyi 'phreng bas bskor/
/rdo rje thugs kyi dkyil 'khor 'bar ba dang / /bde gshegs thugs kyi ngo bo mi bskyod pa/ /rdo rje sems dpa'i thugs dang mtshungs la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /sku gsung thugs
kyi bye brag sna tshogs dang / /bdag gi g.yar dam dpal gyi bsam yas 'di/ /slob dpon khyod kyis byin gyis bslabs

te bzhengs/ /sprul pa'i sku la bdag ni mos btus nas/ /zhu zhing snyan du gsol ba mi 'os kyang / /bdag la thugs ni brtse bar dgongs bzhugs la/ /tshe gcig sangs rgyas gsang sngags
sgrub pa'i chos/ /bdag la thugs kyis bzung nas gnang bar zhu/ /zhes zhus nas phyag dbu thod bud bud 'tshal lo/ /de nas slob dpon gyis rgyal po la gsungs pa/ e ma ho/
rgyal po chos skyong bstan pa'i mnga' bdag yin/ /bdag gis 'chi med tshe'i rig 'dzin thob/ /phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub brnyes/ /sngags dang sngags la rig pa'i
rtsal dbang thob/ /rgyal po'i thugs dgongs yongs su rdzogs par bgyi'o/ /gsungs nas/ sgra bsgyur nyi shu rtsa gcig shes pa'i bai ro tsa na dang / rgya bod yig rigs nyi shu
rtsa gcig shes pa'i legs byin nyi ma/ yi ge skyen pa phul du phyin pa'i 'dan ma rtse mang dang / snubs nam mkha'i snying po/ a tsarya ye shes dbyangs de rnams kyis yig
mkhan byas te/ u rgyan skad dang / rgya gar skad las bsgyur te/ rtsa ba'i rgyud la brten nas sgrub pa chen po sde drug mdzad/ gshen rje rol pa'i rgyud dang / gshen rja dmar
nag gi rgyud la brten nas/ 'jam dpal sku'i sgrub thabs mdzad do/ /rta mchog rol pa'i rgyud dang / pad ma dbang chen gyi rgyud la brten nas/ pad ma gsung gi sgrub thabs
mdzad do/ /yang dag rtsa ba khrag 'thung rol pa'i rgyud dang / he ru ka gal po dang / 'jig rten 'das mdo la brten nas/ yang dag thugs kyi sgrub thabs mdzad do/ /gsang ba
ye shes 'khor lo dang / bdud rtsi mchog gi lung bam po brgyad pa la brten nas/ bdud rtsi yon tan gyi sgrub thabs mdzad do/ /phur pa rol pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/ bi to ta ma
la dang / kI la ya bcu gnyis kyi tan tra la brten nas/ phur pa drag po 'phrin las kyi sgrub thabs mdzad/ ma mo rol pa rtsa ba'i rgyud dang / srid pa bem rgyud lung la brten
nas/ ma mo rbod gtong gi sgrub thabs mdzad/ de yar chad 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sgrub pa ste drug go/ /rig 'dzin rol pa'i rgyud dang / rig 'dzin 'dus pa'i rgyud la brten
nas/ rig 'dzin gyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsa gcig mdzad/ 'jig rten dregs pa 'dul pa'i rgyud la rten nas/ 'jig rten mchod bstod kyi sgrub thabs mdzad/ drag po sngags kyi rgyas
'debs la brten nas drag sngags dmod pa'i sgrub thabs mdzad do/ /de rnams la khyad par du gal che ba'i gdams pa gshin rje'i 'khor lo shes dka' bas 'phrul 'khor lde mig
tu bsdu ba mdzad do/ /phur pa sgrub dka' bas gzhi snying gcig tu dril ba mdzad do/ /ma mo grub kyang 'khor dka' 'khu ldog che bas/ ma mo srog gi 'khor lo shis pa bstan
pa mdzad/ pho rgyud las la myur kyang ldog cing gyong bas/ che ba ching dang log gnon gyi 'khor lo mdzad do/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis lhag par khyad par
du 'phags pa sgrub pa bka' brgyad du 'dus pa/ bde gshegs 'dus pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/ phyi ma'i rgyud/ ma tshang ba kha skong gi rgyud/ 'byed par byed pa lde mig gi rgyud/ phyi
ma'i phyi ma sngags kyi rgyud lnga la brten nas/ zhi ba rigs brgya dang / de nyid rigs lnga / de nyid rigs gcig khro bo 'jigs byed chen po'i dkyil 'khor dang / rdo rje
'jigs chung gi dkyil 'khor dang / sgrub thabs cha lag dang bcas pa mdzad/ de nas mchims phur bde gshegs 'dus

pa zhi khro'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas/ rgyal po dang / bai ro tsa na dang / snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / snubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin po che dang / ngan lam rgyal mchog
dbyangs dang / jo mo bkra shis mtsho rgyal dang / 'brog mi dpal gyi ye shes dang / rlangs dpal gyi seng ge phyi ma dang / dri med zla shar snyags dznyA na ku ma ra dang
/ shel dkar bza' rdo rje mtsho dang / 'brom bza' ti pa ma dang / ru yong bza' 'thing ma dang / mchims bza' rin chen sa le 'od/ mer gong bza' gsal le la sogs pa slob dpon
pad ma'i gzungs ma mtshan ldan drug dang / rgyal po rje 'bangs nyi shu rtsa lnga la dbang bskur ro/ /sgrub pa'i lung byin/ sgrub pa byas pas thams cad kyis grub pa thob
po/ /rgyal po nyid lnga bcu rtsa drug las tshe med pa la/ lo bcu gsum tshe bsrings pa dang / ting nge 'dzin zab pa'i grub pa thob/ bai ro tsa na phung po lhag med du sangs
rgyas/ snyags dznyA na ku ma ras bdud rtsi bsgrubs pas/ lung pa thams cad sman dris gang ste/ sems can thams cad kyi 'byung ba'i nad zhi ba'i grub pa thob/ snubs nam mkha'i
snying pos nyi ma'i zer la bzhon pa dang / nyi ma stod la non pa'i grub pa thob/ sangs rgyas ye shes rin po ches lo brgya dang buca gsum lon te/ gling gzhi ri rab skad
cig la 'khor ba'i grub pa thob nas/ rig 'dzin gyi gnas su gshegs so/ /ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs dpal rta mgrin grub nas spyi gtsug nas rta mgo bton te rta skad
thon/ 'brog mi dpal gyi ye shes mkha' 'gro ma'i zhal dngos su gzigs/ ma mo bran du 'khol/ dran pa nam mkhas thog chen mda' ltar 'phen/ g.yag rgod khugs so/ /'o bran dpal
gyi gzhon nu chu la nya ltar 'dzul chu la mi bying / rma rin chen mchog pha bong zas su za/ dpal gyi ye shes ri klungs thogs pa med/ mkhar chen bzas bsad pa'i mi ro slong
/ mi lo brgya thub pa'i dngos grub brnyes/ lang gro dkon mchog thog chen mda' ltar 'phen/ de la sogs pa'i grub thob mang po byung / rgyal blon thams cad kyis bsgrubs pas
grub pa thob pa'i lo rgyus chos 'byung lags so/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs dgongs la/ lnga brgya dus kyi snyigs ma la/ nga'i gtsug lag khang gi srung ma chos skyong gcig dgos
par 'dug bstan pa srung ba'i srog ser/ thog gtad khram la sogs pa yang dgos par dgongs nas/ slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po mdzad nas
zhus pa ni/ e ma ho/ slob dpon chen po bka' drin can/ /lnga brgya'i tha ma phyi phugs su/ /bdag 'dra rgyal po chos mi 'byung zhing / /blon po gdug cing 'bangs rnams sil
bur 'gro/ /dbus gtsang ru bzhi mtha' 'dulagyi/ /gtsug lag khang gi srung ma gang gis bgyi/ /bstan srung thog ser gtad la sogs/ /sngags kyi bstan pa srung ba gang la bgyi/
/slob dpon thugs rjes gzung nas gnang bar zhu/ /zhes zhus pas/ slob dpon gyis bka' bstsal pa/ e ma ho/ dus kyang je ngan je ngan 'gro/ /rje'i thugs dam bsam yas kyang /
/rgyal po'i snying du 'gong po 'jug /'bangs rnams nang 'thab dme khrug byed/ /gtsug lag khang la 'thab khang 'cha'/ /sgyogs dang me dong 'jigs pa 'ong / /dbus dang mtha'
'dul skor rnams ni/ /mi nag rnams kyis spyod par 'gyur/ /chos 'khor mda' bug dod par byed/ /chos 'khor gnyan

po 'jig par byed/ /sngags pa gri ru gsod par byed/ /rgyal po'i shul gyis lam mi thub/ /chos gos 'og tu gri thung 'jug /che btsan dug gis gsod par byed/ /skye bo nang 'thab
mtshon gyis gsod/ /sngags pa nang rgyas mthu 'dren byed/ /gong kha tsher thams bsdams byed pa dang / /so kha phyi sgo srung ba dang / /pha spun nang dme byed pa dang / /mtshon
gyi bskal pa dar bar 'ong / /chos byed btsun par mi byed cing / /zog po bslu brid mkhan la brtsi/ /gos ngan khyi'i thul pa gyon/ /zhwa ngan rtsid pa'i 'be zhu gyon/
/mtshon dang dbyug pa 'khyer ba dang / /chos ngan chad lta'i stong nyid ston/ /bstan pa 'jig pa'i ltas ngan yin/ /de tshe gtsug lag dkor srung ba/ /dkor srung rgyal po dpe
har dgos/ /bha ta hor gyi sgom gra nas/ /ka cha'i phyir ni 'brangs nas 'ong / /de tshe nga yis dkong srung bcol/ /gsungs so/ /de nas rgyal pos bha ta hor gyi sgom gra
bcom/ rgyal po shing bya can zhes kyang bya/ bdud ya bzher nag po zhes kyang bya/ g.yas kyi ru 'dren/ dpa' bo stag chas brgya/ g.yon gyi ru 'dren/ nyan thos dgra bcom brgya/
slad kyi rjes gnon ban de nag po brgya/ sngon gyi bshul 'breng ba/ bud med nag mo brgya/ phyi'i blon po lang ka ha ra brgya/ nang gi blon po mon bu spu tra brgya/ sku'i
skyo bsangs gar 'bag seng ge brgya/ sprul pa'i yang sprul spre'u byi la brgya/ dkor dang lha 'dre phyir ni 'brangs nas byung / de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/
dpe dkar dkor mdzod gling du rten btsugs nas dam la btags so/ /dpal bsam yas la sogs pa'i gtsug lag khang / mtha' 'dul yang 'dul thams cad kyi gtsug lag khang gi srung
mar bzhag go/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / spa gor bai ro tsa na dang / snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / sba ye shes dbyangs dang / dpon slob kun gyis lha
ma srin sde brgyad la dkar po ging / nag po bdud/ dmar po btsan/ srog gcod gnod sbyin/ shan pa srin po/ nad gtong ma mo/ drag po gza'/ gdug pa klu/ de rnams kyi sgrub thabs
bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bsgyur ro/ /khyad par du bstan pa spyi'i srung ma dpal mgon po nag po dang / dpal lha mo nag mo dang / sngags srung nag smug rnam gsum gyi
rgyud dang sgrub thabs bsam gyis mi khyab pa bsgyur ro/ /lha ma srin thams cad kyi sna 'dren gyis rdorje legs pa'i rgyud dang / sgrub thabs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gcig bsgyur
ro/ /steng nas nam mkha' la dbang byed pa'i gza' gdon la sogs pa dang / chu 'khyags ser ba/ gnam lcags thog dang / mgo nag la dbang byed pa'i klu bdud la sogs pas mdze
nad sna tshogs gtang ba'i gtad khram/ de la sogs pa'i drag sngags ngan sngags bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bsgyur ro/ /de nas rgyal po khri srong lde btsan la bstan srung
rnams gtad pa'o/ /bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas dang / bai ro tsa na nam mkha'i snying po dang / a tsarya ye shes dbyangs kyis/ skal ldan bod kyi rje khri srong lde btsan
la bdud rtsi thigs bsags gtad/ gtad do gnyer du gtad/ chongs shig thugs la chongs/ /yang na snod dang ldan na rab/ /yang na snying rje che na 'bring / /tha ma sgyu ma'i
nong la sbyin/ /'di gsum dag dang ma 'brel bar/ /gtad nas ngan sngags 'phel gyur na/ /sngags kyi bdag po bdag

mo yis/ /rgyal po'i tshe bskul ngan song lhung / /de bas rin chen srog ltar chongs/ /zhes gsungs te bstan srung rnams rgyal po la gtad do/ /de nas mnga' bdag rgyal po rab tu
dgyes nas/ rta chibs pa mtshal bu bya gdong gis sna drangs pa'i rgyal po'i 'og rta drug la gser srab g.yu mthur seng ldeng sga bra/ za 'og gi hor stan pho long ris su bris
pa/ gser ril ma bre zho gcig g.yu bre gang / rje'i mgul g.yu mtsho ro 'od 'bar mgal nas bkrol te/ de rnams slob dpon la phul nas phyag dbu thod bud bud 'tshal lo/ /slob
dpon gyi gsung gis sgyu ma'i nor la phangs pa med par phul pas ngo mtshar che/ phyag byad bzang lags gsungs pa dang / banga' bdag gi thugs dgongs la slob dpon kyang lho
bal nas byon pas nor phul ba la dgyes par 'dug nor dad rang che bar 'dug snyam pa dang / slob dpon mngon par shes pa mnga' bas rgyal po'i thugs dngogs la de ltar ba dang
/ slob dpon gyi zal rje mnga' bdag thu ba zed cig gsungs nas/ bye ma dang rde'u khrag khrog thu bar blugs nas en cig zungs shig gsungs pa dang / rde'u khrag khron g.yur
song nas dug pa dang / slob dpon gyi zhal nas/ rje'i sgrib pa sbyong ba dang / rgyu bsod nams kyi tshogs rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir blang bar zad kyi/ de min nga la snang
ba thams cad gser du yod/ nga la ni sgyu ma'i nor gyi dgos pa med pas/ rgyal po rang ci dgar spyod cig ces gsungs pa dang / rgyal po nyid thugs skyengs te ngo tsha bar gyur
nas 'gyod pas slob dpon chen po lags/ bdag ni mtha' 'khob rgyal por song / /sgrib pa che bas the tshom byung / /gnong ngo 'gyod do sprul pa'i sku/ /thugs rjes zungs shig
bka' dren can/ /dam tshig nyams pa skong thabs zhu/ /zhes lus gcer bur sa la brdams/ brkyangs phyag 'tshal/ spyan chab phyung nas phyag dbu thod bud bud 'tshal/ de nas
slob dpon gyis rgyal po la gsungs pa/ rgyal po nyid rga sems can lags pas sems rtog pa byung yang dam tshig nyams rgyu med/ nga ni rnal 'byor pa yin pas sems la khong khro
ba med/ rje rang bshags pa lta ba'i sgom la mdzod/ sems rtog dri ma lam la gzhug gtso bor dge bcu spyod pa mi dge bcu po spongs/ ci byas chos su spyod la chos khrims
dam par skyong sa/ sdig spyod blon po la ma nyan/ dgra'i the tshom chod/ ces gsungs nas/ dam tshig nyams pa skong ba'i skad du rgyun bshags gnang ngo / /ngan sngags kyi 'gyur
byang dang / rgyal po la dam tshig skong thabs gnang ba'i lo rgyus chos 'byung lasags so/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la/ rje mnga' bdag khri srong lde btsan
rje 'bangs nyi shu rtsa lngas/ bsam yas mchims phu phug pa chen por/ rdzogs pa chen po nam mkha' tshe'i dbang zhus pa'i dus su/ rgyal pos slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la
gzigs shing / brtags pas shin tu ngo mtshar skyes te/ slob dpon chen po khyod lta bu dang po bskal pa bzang po nas 'jig rten 'khor ba ma stongs kyi bar du sku tshe la bgres
rgud skye 'chi ma mnga'/ tshe'i rig 'dzin thob pa thabs ji lta bu'i sgo nas brnyes pa lags zhes zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas ngas rig pa rtse gcig tu bzung nas 'khor
'das kyi ru shan phye nas nyams su blangs te bsgrubs pas/ lus kyi 'byung ba dwangs nas rdo rja lta bur gyur

pa yin/ bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa la gsol ba btab ste bsgrubs pas/ dngos grub tshe la dbang ba lta bur thob nas tshe nyi zla dang mnyam par gyur pa yin/ de
nas skye 'chi med par gyur pa yin/ rtsa dang rlung gi bde drod la brten nas dwags snyigs phye nas/ gzungs ma mtshan dang ldan pa la nyams su blangs nas bsgrubs pas tshe
lo stong gi bar du gnas pa yang yod/ sman dang rtswa'i bcud la brten te bsgrubs pas/ tshe lo lnga brgya'i bar du bsrings pa yang yod do gsungs pas/ rje mnga' bdag rgyal po'i
zhal nas/ bdag kyang go ga tshe'i rig 'dzin thob nas phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa zhig zhu 'tshal/ zhes zhus pas/ slob dpon chen po'i zhal nas/ bdag
kyang rdo rje theg pa chen po phyi nang gsang ba gsum gyi dbang ma lus par longs spyod pas phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob/ mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa la gsol
ba btab cing bsgrubs pas tshe'i rig 'dzin thob nas skye 'chi med par gnas pa yi/ da rgyal po la yang de ltar bgyi'o gsungs nas/ dus de nyid rang du brag dmar g.ya' ma
lung gi dben rtsa ru bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa'i dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas/ tshe'i bum pa rin po che phra men gyi bum pa gcig gis thog drangs pa'i/ bcom
ldan 'das rigs lnga'i bum pa lnga / las bum gcig dang drug byin gyis brlabs nas/ rdzas bkod mdzad nas mtshams bcad do/ /mkha' 'gro bkra shis mtsho rgyal/ shel dkar bza' rdo
rja mtsho dang / 'bro bza' ti pang ma/ ru yong bza' ma 'ating ma/ mchims rin chen gsal le 'od/ mer gong bza' rin chen gtsug dang drug la segs te/ khyad par gyi bu mo gzungs
mar byas/ snubs nam mkha'i snying po/ lo tsA ba snyags dznyA na ku ma ra dang snan sba a tsarya dpal dbyangs la tsogs pa grub chen nyi shu rtsa lnga dang bcas pas tshe
bsgrubs te/ da ste zla ba gcig dang zhag bcu song tsa na tshe chu la rgyal blon rnams shog ces gsungs/ der tshe bsgrubs nas zla ba gcig dang / zhag bcu song tsa na/ brag
dmar g.ya' ma lung gi nam mkha' la bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa tshe'i lha mo nyanyi shu dang / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dpag tu med
pa mdun gyi nam mkha' la byon nas tshe'i bum pa la them pa dang / 'od zer dkar po 'phros pas/ 'jig rten rigs drug gi sems can la phog pas so so'i sdig sgrib sbyangs/ sdug
bsngal zhi bar gyur pa dang / 'od zer dmar po tshur 'dus pas tshe'i bdud rtsir gyur pa la sogs pa byung nas/ slob dpon gyis srung ma bskul nas/ rgyal po rje 'bangs tshe
chu la bos la shog gsungs pa dang / rgyal po'i mna' lam du yang brag dmar g.ya' ma lung nas tshe'i 'od zer rgyal po'i dbu la shar nas byung ba'i dus su srung ma rnams kyis
rgyal po tshe chu la shog byas pas/ der rgyal pos 'khor btsun mo dang / nang mi blon po la brgyud nas/ blon po chen po bdun sbron du btang bas/ blon po chen po bdun po
re re la 'khor lnga brgya lnga brgyas bskor nas/ yom 'bog gi thang la 'tshogs pa dang / rgyal po nam langs nyi ma ma shar gyi gong du/ sgo nas thon te chibs thog tu byon
pa la/ blon po chen po rnams kyis phyag byas zug bsnems nas zhe sa phul/ de'i dus su blon po chen po rnams kyi

nang nas/ ngan lam ta ra klu gong nag po bya ba des/ rje 'bangs mnga' bdag rgyal po'i chibs kha nas bzung nas rje lags/ tshe chu la bzhud pa ni blun rmongs pa'o/ /kha rtsang
zla ba sngon ma la mchims phur bla mchod paNDi tas rtsi dug nyos nas song skad do/ /rtsi dug bas kyang bzod pal/ ri gdong gi brag la yi ge bris nas/ bod na dug yos zon
gyis shig skad do/ /kha tsang dbang skur ba'i dus su yang / jo mo rgyal srid khor 'bangs dang bcas pa phul cig gsungs/ rje'i rgyal sa la mtha'i mon pa spyi bcings 'di snyob
pa ring nas gda' 'o/ /de bas da lan tshe chu 'di rang bshol na mi drag gam/ da res bshol la thong zhes zhus pas/ nang rtags phyi ru shar/ shing gi lo ma skyes pa 'dra/
thugs bsam gcig mdzod cig zhus pa dang / rje dar cig sems de sems pa la bzhugs pa dang / mi'i rnam par shes pa 'di dpag par dka' bas/ da lan gyi tshe chu de bshol la mthong
zhes te/ chibs kha nang du bsgyur bas/ blon po rnams sran phung la rdo brgyab pa bzhin so sor gyes so/ /de ltar rgyal po tshe chu la ma byon nas/ de ma thag skad cig
la srung ma rnams kyis tshul de ltar slob dpon gyi snyan du gsol bas/ slob dpon dbang bskur gyi sta gon dang dngos grub kyi bskul chog mdzad pa las/ zhal ras nag por song
ba las/ mtsho rgyal mi brjed pa'i gsungs thob cing / mngon par shes pa phra mo mnga' bas/ slob dpon la zhus pa/ rje mnga' bdag tshe chu la mi 'byon par gda' 'am zhus pas/
rgyal po rje 'bangs rang re la blo log pa bzung nas/ tshe chu mi 'thung bar yod gsungs pas/ yang zhus pa/ 'o na 'di 'atung pa'i skal ldan gang lags/ 'thung na yon tan ci
'byung zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas 'di skad gsungs so/ /mgon po tshe dpag med pas byin brlabs kyang / /tshe 'dod me tog u dum wa ra 'dra/ /skal ldan tshe la dbang
ba nyi zla tsam/ /'di 'thung tshe lo stong phrag bdun tsho gsum/ /sems can lus la skal ba bzang por 'gyur/ /rgyal po ma'i mngal kha stong srid dam/ /zung 'jug 'khor ba'i
las la spro srid dam/ /tshe tshu 'di la dbang ba'i skyes bu gang / /ma 'ongs skal ldan rnams la gter du bzhag /gsungs nas gter du sbas pa yin no/ /sku'i 'od zer gyis thal
le bor/ phog pa'i gnas brag dmar rdza phug gi gling bya ba bya khyung gi gshog pa 'dra bar/ slob dpon rang gi sgrub gnas brag mchod rten 'dra ba byin che ba yod pa la/ rin
chen phra men gyi bum pa dbus kyi nge dang / de dus kyi bkod pa'i rdzas dang / gtor ma rakta bdud rtsi tshe'i phur pa dang bcas pa sbas so/ /gzhan yang gu ru'i na bza'/
gser gzhong pa gang dang / gter yig kyang sbas so/ /gcig brag lha ri la sbas so/ /gcig nub kyi phyogs su brag rdo rje tshe brtan la sbas so/ /gcig byang phyogs brag lha
lung gi sgo'i nang du sbas so/ /gcig brag dmar gyi rdza la sbas so/ /las kyi bum pa zungs mkhar rdo'i mchod rten la sbas so/ /de rnams kyang slob dpon gyis zhabs kyis bcags
shing bsgrubs pa'i gnas yin pas gter yig kyang sbas so/ /slob dpon gyis tshe chu bsgrubs nas ma 'ongs skal ldan la gter du sbas pa'i lo rgyus lags so/ /de nas slob dpon
pad ma 'byung gnas kyis rje khri srong lde btsan la bka' bstsal pa/ bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas dang / /sba

gor bai ro tsa na dang / /snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / /a tsarya ye shes dalapal dbyangs kyis/ /rje'i rgyal khrims bsrung ba'i phyir/ /drag sngags ngan sngags bsgyur ba
ni/ /rgya gar skad dang u rgyan skad/ /sing nga'i skad dang sa la'i skad/ /li'i skad dang bal po'i skad/ /za hor skad dang bhe ta'i skad/ /ma ru tse'i skad dang rgya nag
skad/ /kha che'i skad dang gru gu'i skad/ /tho gar skad dang zangs gling skad/ /gser gling skad dang srin po'i skad/ /rta shang skad dang bod kyi skad/ /skad rigs mi 'dra
mkha' 'gro'i brda' skad bsgyur/ /gnod sbyin pho mo mang po'i skad du/ /'phrul 'khor bsdebs nas gsang sngags mang po bsgyur/ /bha ta hor gyi sgom gra bcom nas ni/ /mgo
nag dpe har bos nas bsam yas kyi/ /lha 'dre mang po gter gyi srung mar bskos/ /tshe gcig sangs rgyas sgrub pa'i dam chos mang po bsgyur/ /rgyal po g.yengs pas nyams su mi
len par/ /las kyi 'phro bzhag skye ba bcu bdun du/ /brgyud pa'i mtha' mar rgyal nyid dang 'phrad par shog /ces gter du sbas so/ /gsang sngags drag sngags mang po rnams/
/skal ldan 'ga' la gter du sba bar bya/ /de yang glang lug gi 'brug gshed bzhi'i lo/ /srog gi lag yin bton kyang srog mi 'chad/ /de bzhin ma yin gter gyi dbang skal med/
/gal te thon kyang myur du brlag par 'gyur/ /da lta rgyal khrims gnyan pas srog ser thog mi dgos/ /dus ngan 'byung dus dgos pas skal ldan rnams la bzhag /las can rnams la
rgya yis btab la bzhag /ces gsungs te/ yang rje mnga' bdag gis gsungs pa/ e ma ho/ slob dpon chen po lags/ slob dpon mngon shes mnga' bas phyi ma ci 'byung mkhyen/ /gter
du sbed na gang du sbed/ /bdag skye ba len na gang du len/ /chos dang 'phrad na gang ltar 'phrad/ /slob dpon bka' lung bstsal du gsol/ /zhes zhus pas/ slob dpon dang rgyal
pos chos dang ngan sngags rnams lho gter du sbas so/ /gter kha brgya dang rtsa brgyad du sbas so/ /de yang sbas lugs ni/ dbu rtse rigs gsum gyi gter mdzod re re ru/ /rgyal
po'i bla gter du sbas so/ /chos kyi gter mdzod yin/ khyad par gling gsum du/ bu tshal gser khang gling dang / khams gsum zangs khang gling dang / dge rgyas bye ma gling
du jo mo gsum gyi gter mdzod/ bla gter re re sbas/ yakSha ltag 'ong tu/ gter kha re re sbas/ dpe har gling dang mgon khang bzhir mthu gter phal cher sbas/ phyogs bzhi'i
mchod rarten bzhir/ dkar por chos gter sbas/ nag por mthu ster sbas/ sngon por bzo yig sbas/ dmar por sman yig sbas/ mchims phu yang dben du slob dpon thugs dam gyi gter
mdzod chen po sbas/ bre gu dge bu yang mdzod gsang sbas/ lho skyer chu'i lha khang du rgyud 'dod pa 'byung ba dang / sde snod kun 'dus dang / bum thang rtsi lungs su sems
phyogs thams cad sbas/ bum thang dge gnas su ma mo 'dus pa dang / mo rgyud thams cad sbas/ gtsang 'gram lha khang du gshin rje dmar nag dang / ngan sngags brgya rtsabacu
sbas/ byang spra dun rtse dang / skyaun dun rtse ru/ ngan sngags brgya rtsa brgyad sbas/ g.yas ru gtsang 'gram du/ chos sman rtsis rin chen rnam gsum sbas/ rtsis kyi
lha khang du rgyud lung man ngag sbas/ smyug gi lha khang du/ srog gi thig le sbas/ khams kyi klong thang sgron

ma ru/ lha mo'i rgyud gsum dang / spu gri rnam gsum sbas/ shar kong bu chu mthar legs kyi lha khang du/ mthu dang rdzu 'phrul sbas/ g.yo ru khra 'brug tu/ ngan sngags bcu gsum
sbas/ lho brag kho 'thing du/ bde gshegs 'dus pa sbas/ mdos dang ma mo sbas/ stag tshang seng phug tu/ drag sngags ngan sngags sum cu sbas/ mon kha na ring du spyi te
yo ga dang / reg gcod bzhi po sbas/ sgregs kyi yang rdzong du phur pa thams cad dang / gshin rje thams cad sbas/ pho ma rdzing phug tu bsi mo'i ngan sngags dang / gsang
ba'i phur gcig sbas/ yang phug ring mo ru/ klu bdud spu gri dang / smug mo'i snying thun sbas/ gtsang gi phung po ri bo cher/ gshin rje tshe bdag dang / cog brtungs nyi shu
rtsa gcig sbas/ ri dang brag dang gnyan sa thams cad du/ gter phran brgya rtsa brgyad sbas/ las can re dang 'phrad par 'gyur/ gter kha 'di rnams dbyungs pa'i dus ni/ zas
ngan lci ba za ste/ chos skor 'joms sing dben gnas 'jig bka' la nyo tshong byed cing mi bsad stong du 'jal/ gos ngan re ba gyon te las su dme 'khrug byed/ lus la lcags
cha gyon/ gnas brtan dmag dpon byed cing dge slong gri ru gsod/ gnas la 'thab ra 'cha'/ dben tsha grong dkyil mkhar la 'cha'/ sngags pa rdo rje dme 'thab byed/ zas ngan
dug gi sbyor ba byed/ dpa' bo rdo gtan byed/ shar ba mda' gtan byed/ gtso bo rgyab rten mna' za/ bod khrab rgya bye rgyun chad pa ltar sil bur song nas/ pha dang bu mi 'cham/
spun dang pha spun 'khrug pa byed/ dgra blar btsan dang gnod spyin 'dre 'bod/ ar pas lam 'phrang bsrungs shing 'joms / de'i dus su bod thams cad kyi snying du 'dre dang
'gong po zhugs/ byis pa'i snying la the brang 'jug bud med snying du bsen mo 'jug lha ma srin sde brgyad dang / snang srid lha 'dre thams cad 'khrugs pas/ nad dang mu
ge dang / 'khrug pa'i bskal pa 'byung / de'i dus su ma thub pa gsum 'byung ste/ sa yis rin chen gter ma thub ste/ chos gter nor gter 'byung / gser dngul rin po che'i kha
bye/ chos skyong gis gtad pa'i gnyer ma thub ste/ dge 'dun gyi nor la rku 'phrog byed/ chos pas bsgrubs pa'i chos ma thub ste/ rang mi sgrub par gdams pa zab mo zong du
'tshong / rang la nyams len med par mi gzhan la bshad 'dod/ dus ngan de lta bu gcig byung tsa na/ mnga' bdag rgyal po nyid skye ba bcu bdun brgyud pa'i tha ma la 'di nas
lho nub mtshams na yuul rta ro dmar po kha phye ba 'dra ba zhig gi nang na/ skyes bu 'brug lo pa shes rab dang snying rje che ba brtson 'grus che la sgrub pa la brtson pa/
dam tshig gtsang zhing rlom sems chung ba/ khong yangs shing kha nyung ba/ rgyud zhi la gzhan la sgro skur mi 'debs pa/ rig pa myur zhing yid gzhungs pa/ mdog dkar la ngang
rgyud ring ba/ skye bu de lta bu zhig tu skyes nas/ rgyal po nyid la ngas da lta gdams pa thams cad dang 'phrad nas skye ba de sa rgyun gcod par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po
nyid kyis spa gor bai ro tsa na dang / snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / chos kyi bdag po thengs re spyugs pa'i dam tshig gi sel dang las 'bras kyis/ chos la mi rnams yid
mi ches/ chos 'brel gang che ba thams cad snang ba thengs re ldog tu 'ongs bas/ de'i dus su nga'i bka' bzhin

byed na/ yul gyi snying por chos kyi dbyings bzung la pha yul spongs/ gnas kyi snying por nags khrod dgon pa rten la khang khyim spongs/ dgon pa'i snying por sems nyid stong
gsal brten/ khang po chos dbyings rgya chad med par sdod/ tshang bang snying por dran pa shes bzhin bzung la dge sbyor yo lang gyis/ mdzod kyi snying por kun gzhi byang
chub sems la sku gsum nor rdzas gsog so nam snying por lus ngag yid gsum tha mal ma sdod chos spyod gyis/ gros kyi snying por bde gshegs bka' dang bla ma'i zhal la dris/
pha'i snying por snying rje kun tu bzang po khur la snying rje zung / ma'i snying por byams pa kun tu bzang po khur la 'gro ba bu bzhin skyongs/ chung ma'i snying por ting
'dzin bde gsal sgoms la mi 'bral 'grogs/ bu'i snying por bla ma'i gdams ngag dpe char bris la lta rtog gyis/ zhing gi snying por dad pa'i zhing sa skyed la chos dang ci
mthun gyis/ 'khor gyi snying por ma sring dan can brten la mchod/ zas kyi snying por chos nyid bdud rtsi skye ba med pa zo/ skom gyi snying por bla ma'i gdams ngag zhal
gyi bdud rtsi ngoms par 'thungs/ gos kyi snying por dbang dang dam tshig nod la lus ngag yid gsum smin par gyis/ ltad mo'i snying por ting 'dzin 'phro 'du gyis la rig pa
rtsal sbyong gyis/ longs spyod snying por sgrub pal gyis la chos spyod lam rim slobs/ dgra lha'i snying por ye shes lha la mchod pa rgyun dun phul/ mchod gnas snying por
rdo rje slob dpon khur la kun tu spyi bor sgoms la gsol ba thob/ las kyi snying por dpe cha bris la gang la gang 'dod byin/ me long snying por dam pa'i chos la ltos la gsol
'debs gyis/ lha khang snying por rang gi sems la rtsigs la yi dam sgoms/ rgyan gyi snying por snying rje sems la 'khod la snying rje phyogs ris med par gyis/ chos nyid
snying por stong nyid spros bral ma bcos ngang la zhog dam tshig snying por rang sems sgyu med gyis la sems nyid gtsang sar thon/ man ngag snying por rgyud la zol med tshol
la snyan rgyud sgoms/ dkyil 'khor snying por dgongs pa 'gyur med chos nyid ngang la zhog lta ba chos sku 'gyur med ltos la rang ngo shes par gyis/ sgom gyi snying por
skye med chos dbyings sgoms la brtan par gyis/ spyod pa'i snying por blang dor med lapar spyod la chags med zhen med gyis/ 'bras bu'i snying por sku gsum thob par gyis
la rang las gzhan ma 'tshol/ de ltar byas na mnga' bdag nyid skye ba des mjug gcod/ nub phyogs bde ba can gyi zhing khams su pad ma la brdzus te skyes nas sangs rgyas par
'gyur ro/ /zhes mnga' bdag la lung bstan no/ /gter cos sbas lugs dang mnga' bdag lung bstan pa'o/ /bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ /sngon gyi las kyi 'phro mthud nas/
/sum stong lnga brgya lon nas bod yul dbus su 'ongs/ /lnga bcu rtsa gcig bod yul dbus su bsdad/ /rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyi bka' lung bsgrubs/ /bod kyi 'dre srin
lha srin thams cad btul/ /dpal gyi bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa de/ /rgyal pos stag gi lo la rmang bting nas/ rta'i lo la thugs dam bsam bzhin 'grub/ /chos kyi rgyal pos bstan
pa rgyas par byas/ /glang gi lo la rgyal lnga bcu rtsa drug bzhes/ /de las rgyal po'i sku tshe med pa la/

/sku'i rim gros bcu gsum sku tshe bsrings/ /drug cu rtsa dgu stag gi lo la dgung du gshegs/ /bdag ni 'di ru mi sdod do/ /sgrub pa'i gnas gcig 'tshol du 'gro/ /gsungs nas/ mchims
phur yang dben du zla gsum zhag gsum bzhugs/ brag dmar rdzam phug gling du zla gsum zhag gsum bzhugs/ brag dmar g.ya' ma lung du zla gcig zhag gcig bzhugs/ sgrub khang
zla gam dmar kapor lo gsum zla ba gsum zhag gsum bzhugs/ sgregs kyi yang rdzong du/ zla lnga zhag lnga bzhugs/ mon kha ne ring du zla gcig zhag gcig bzhugs/ mon kha brag
mtha' khra mor zla ba lnga zhag dgu bzhugs/ mon mgon brag phug tu zla ba gcig zhag bdun bzhugs/ mu tig shel gong du zla gcig zhag bcu bzhugs/ yar lungs shel phug tu zla
ba gcig zhag gsum bzhugs/ sgregs kyi yang rdzong shel phug tu zla ba gsum dang zhag bcu bzhugs/ zungs mkhar rdo rje'i mchod rten rdzong du zla ba gcig zhag gsum bzhugs/
lho brag mkhar chur zla gcig zhag bcu bzhugs/ brag phug de rnams kyang sgrub gnas khyad par can du byin gyis brlabs/ bod yul thams cad sku'i zhabs kyis bcags/ phyi rabs
skal ldan rnams la chos gter mang du bzhag nas sbas/ kha byang yang byang snying byang don byang lde mig rnams so sor bzhag go/ /las can re'i don 'grub 'gyur/ las can de
dang 'phrad par shog skal ldan gcig gis rnyed par shog de skad ces ni smon lam btab/ gter rgya/ sbas rgya/ gtad rgya/ zab rgya/ rtsis rgya phal cher btab ste bzhag go/ /sbas
so gter du sbas/ zab pa dam du chongs zhes gdams so/ /dus phyi ma gter dang 'phrad pa'i gang zag rnams la/ gdams ngag zhal gdams su bzhag pa/ dus kyi phyi ma la nga'i
chos dang 'phrad nas spyod pa'i gang zag rnams kyis/ man ngag 'tsho ma shes na 'phral rkyen 'ong bas gsang thub par gyis shig man ngag ngoms sngas na phrag dog skye/ zhal
gyis skur ba dang ngan yong bas sgrub pa rtags thon cig khengs grags dang 'byor ches na/ tshul ngan pa yong bas mthu dang chos su ldan par gyis shig dam tshig sa gzhi
ltar ma nyams par srungs/ dam tshig nyams na bkra mi shis shing dmyal bar 'gro/ sgom pa ni gser phur ltar tob cig goms pa ma brtan na byed lo'i chos kyis brtan pa mi thob/
spyod pa gdengs rang chas par spyod cig tshul 'chos lo 'dod kyis snang ba mi thul lo/ /man ngag gter ltar sbos shig spel drags 'acal nas rtsis mi 'ongs/ sgom sgrub gang
byas kyang rtsad bla ma la chod cig bla ma'i rgyud pa med na chos la byin rlabs mi 'ongs/ lta spyod rtsing na bar gcod lhung ba yong / lta ba kha 'byams su ma gtor zhig
spyod pa bab col du ma spyod/ chos kyi mtha' ni dam tshig dang rtogs pa dang snying rje la thug go/ /rang dam tshig gtsang du srung la gzhan snying rjes zungs shig chos rang
gi grub rtags ma thon kapar gzhan la ma shod/ ma byin gzhan yid mi ches/ chos la byin rlabs mi 'byung ngo / /gdams pa dang chos dus gcig la rdzogs par ma byin cig chos
khyer nas 'brel ba gcod pa mang bas snod brtag pa gces so/ /gter gyi chos 'di shin tu zab pas gzobs la spyod cig de ltar gzhung bzhin byas na/ byin rlabs ni shugs kyis
'ongs/ sangs rgyas ni rang la rnyed/ dgos rgu mi yis sgrub/ bkur sti gzhan gyis byed/ 'tsho ba lhas sbyor/ bsam

pa yid bzhin 'grub/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyud bzung / chos don dang ldan/ dge 'dun gyi rten 'grub/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyud bzung / chos don dang ldan/ dge 'dun gyi rten tshugs/ bstan
pa dar zhing rgyas par bya ba yin no/ /de ltar ma byas nas chos nyams su ma blangs par gzhan la spel/ mi ngo nor ngo zas ngor bgatang na/ sangs rgyas kyi bla brjo/ chos
kyi rkad 'dren/ dge 'dun gyi ngan dpe/ sdig pa'i ded dpon/ dmyal ba'i gros mkhan/ rang don med par byas nas/ mi lus rin po che chud gzon pa yin no/ /nga'i gter gyi chos
'di rnams shin tu gnyan pas 'tsho shes par gyis shig ces gsungs so/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ bod kyi sgrub gnas byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sa gzhi zhabs kyis
bcags pa dang / zhal gdams gnang ba'i lo rgyus chos 'byung lags so/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas srin yul lang ka pu ri nag po bya ba 'dzam bu gling sog ka'i yu
ba la/ srin yul yod pas/ de o rgyan dang thag nye bas srin pos mi gsod du 'ongs pas/ srin po 'dul zhing / srin po'i so kha bsrung bar thugs kyis dgongs nas/ bsam yas nas
bzhud par chas pa la/ lha sras mu tig btsan po rgyal blon dang / bod kyi rab byung / dge bshes/ sngags pa/ bon po/ lha rje/ rnal 'byor pho mo/ gtso bo/ skyes bu/ bud med
la sogs pas/ slob dpon la bzhugs par zhu ba phus yang / slob dpon bzugs par ma gnang ngo / /bod la thugs chad pa'i mgur bzhes pa/ bdag 'dra pad ma 'byung gnas kyis/ /sngon
gyi las 'phros bod du 'ongs/ /khri srong lde btsan bka' lung mnyan/ /bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa bzhengs/ /da ni bod du mi sdod de/ /bod kyi mi dang bdag mi mthun/ /rgyal
khrims chos khrims mi skyong bar/ /blon po chos med kyis kha lo bsgyur/ /bod kyi rgyal po dang nga mu mthun / /sdig spyod rgyal po la yi te mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul
la 'gro/ /tshig dang don du mi sbyor ba/ /bod kyi ston chen dang nga mi mthun/ /tha snyad mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /'dul khrims gtsang mar mu srung
ba'i/ /bod kyi btsun pa dang nga mi mthun/ /zhi gnas mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /mnyam bzhag rjes thob mi bsre ba/ /bod kyi sgom chen dang nga
mi mthun/ /zhi gnas mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /dam tshig gtsang mar mi srung ba/ /bod kyi sngags pa dang nga mi matun/ /dam nyams tsho la yi re
mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /lha rabs gtsang mar mi mchod pa/ /bod kyi bon po dang nga mi mthun/ /'dre chos mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /bzhi
brgya rtsa bzhi mi 'chos pa/ /bod kyi sman pa dang mi mthun/ /mi yi che skyong mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /sbyin pa phyogs med mi gtong ba/ /bod
kyi yon bdag rnams dang nga mu mthun/ /g.yo sgyu mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /mi chos lha chos mi bsre ba/ /bod kyi gtso bo rnams dang nga mi mthun/
/'dun ma mkhan la yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /dad pa dang saanying rje mi bsre ba/ /nya ma rnams dang nga mi mthun/ /kha ta mkhan la ye re mug /nga 'gro
rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /dkon macog dang bu khyo mi bkur ba/ /bod kyi bud med dang nga mu mthun/ /srin mo gson

ma rnams yi re mug /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /rang sems sangs rgyas don rtogs na/ /su dang mthun rung ma thun rung / /ces kyang de la gto ba med/ /phyi ma bde 'gro mtho
ris 'gro/ /nga 'gro rgya gar yul la 'gro/ /nga 'gro srin po 'dul du 'gro/ /grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ /mnyam bzhag rjes thob med par 'gro/ /slob dpon pad ma bod
kyi rgyal po dang / blon po/ dge bshes/ btsun pa/ sngags pa/ bon po/ sman pa/ gtso bo/ nya ma/ skyes bu/ bud med rnams la thugs chad pa'i lo rgyus so/ /de nas slob dpon
pad mas bod kyi rgyal po rnams la zhal ta bzhag pa/ bsod nams ldan pa bod kyi rgyal po rnams/ /rgyal po nyung na zhen nyen pas kha gzhi skyungs/ /rgyal po mang na 'bangs
dang zla mi bya/ /zungs thub gzobs la rab tu brtan par bzhugs/ /thugs ches nang blon bka' gros dris pa la/ /dgos don thugs tshod lhug par gsung bar gyis/ /srid la gnod pa'i
gros ni mnyan mi byas/ /khri zhing gtum par mi bya zhi dul bsgom par bya/ /rtsis dang bya dga' blon po mdzangs kyang ni/ /ha cang ma che ran tsam mdzad na legs/ /blon
po 'dod pa che zhing rig pa med/ /srid kyi mkhar ni 'jig pa'i nen mchis so/ /rgyal khrims gal la bab pa'i dus su ni/ /dkor la mi phangs sdig la mi 'dzem mdzod/ /rgyal khrims
nyams na rgyal po gya ba yin/ /bsgyur ba mi sla snan khung 'thug pa dang / /phyed tsam khong du bsad la khong pa bskyed/ /srid kyi chu mtha' ring bar bstod mchi yi/
/btsun mo rnams dang bud med gzhan dag la/ /'dod chags phyir ni thugs la btags drags na/ /nga khyod bsre zhing bzang ngan med par 'gro/ /yid ches med pa'i mi la thugs mi
gtod/ /legs par mi 'ongs rang srog 'phung nyen yod/ /phyi 'khor zhi bas skyongs la nang 'khor zas kyis skyongs/ /phyogs ris 'bangs la bka' nan mnyam snyoms mdzod/ /gtsug
lag khang dang lha khang mchod rten rnams/ /bsod nams che ste tha ma sdig pa'i rgyu/ /dam chos bsgyur la zhu tig dag par mdzod/ /lan gcig dus na bka' la tshad mar 'dzin/
/dkon mchog gsum la spyan ltar gces par mdzod/ /theg pa'i chos la gzhung lugs re re yod/ /kun gyi sgo nas 'bras bu thob med kyang / /gsang sngags rdo rje'i theg pa dang du
longs/ /bang so bzhugs gnas mang po phung ba'i nyen/ /thugs srab ma mdzad brtan zhing lhun chags bzhugs/ /jomo jo chung rnams kyang srid kyi gzhi ma yin/ /kho yangs che
la theg pal che bar mdzod/ /zas la yengs la lag byad bzang bar mdzod/ /lus tshugs thub cing bca' bsdar tho bar mdzod/ /g.yem la ma 'phyar spyod lam dul bar mdzod/ /smra
ba ma mang ngag 'jam zhe sa bsrings/ /pyi 'khor nang 'khor zas dang snyan pas skyongs/ /lha sras lcam dral rnams kyang chos la btsud na legs/ /'dir btsun phyi mar lha mi'i
go 'phang thob/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang slad kyis 'byon pa yi/ /mnga' bdag rgyal po'i thugs la de ltar zhog /ces gsungs pa ste/ rgyal
po rnams la zhal ta bzhag pa yin/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas gshegs pa'i dus su bod kyi blon po rnams la gsungs pa/ bod kyi rgyal po'i blon po byed pa rnams/ /rje'i
sku'i rim gror lus ngag yid gsum gus par gyis/ /nang gi khab so jo mo'i zhabs thog gyis/ /spyi'i chab srid

gros dang mdun mas skyongs/ /'bangs kyi so tshis sha tsha brtse bar gyis/ /blon po'i sku gnyer rje'i bka' blon gyis/ /rgyal khams bde la 'god cing rgyal khrims dam par 'abha'/
/dkon macog gsum gyi rten tshugs theg chen chos grwa tshugs/ /rgyal khams gzhung lugs so kha dam par srungs/ /byams sdang ngo shes legs nyes don la rtogs/ /sngar gros
mi zhan legs nyes sems pa dang / /phyis nas 'gyod pas mi phan thal zin 'chos mi btub/ /ci la'ang dang po bsams na phyis nas 'gyod pa chung / /chos la gnas shing dad pa che
la dkon mchog mchod na chos blon yin/ /gros mkhas rig pa che la legs nyes lde'u mkhas pa mdzangs blon yin/ /dpa' la zungs thub dgra bo thabs kyis 'dul na dpa' blon yin/
/khong 'dug zhe gnag 'brid pa'i thabs la mkhas na blon po 'jigs/ /rgyal po'i rgyal srid legs nes shes na blon po mdzangs/ /legs par rtog dpyod gyis la rgyal po'i chab srid
skyongs/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /blon po rnams kyi thugs la de ltar zhog /ces blon po rnams la zhal ta gsungs
pa'o/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas gshegs pa'i dus su rab byung btsun pa rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ thar pa'i lam la gshegs pa'i rab byung btsun pa kun/ /mi
chos nang nas lha chos nang du zhugs/ /pha ma gnyen bshes spangs nas chags med dam cos byos/ /skra bzhar chos gos gon nas bstan pa'i rab byung byos/ /makan po slob dpon
khrims mdzad dge 'dun byams sems can/ /'dul khrims bslab pa'i rim pa ma nyams bsrung bar mdzod/ /zhu gnang bcas dang lhung bzed bkru la sogs/ /mkhan slob dge 'dun bgres pa
rnams bya ba dang / /maNDal chag chag byi dor bya ba dang / /mchod pa la sogs mdzes pa'i bkod legs bya/ /srod dang tho rangs mi nyal dge sbyor gyis/ /sha chang lkog pa
mi bza' gtor ma chos spyod gyis/ /'dul khrims nyes pa bshags shing gso sbyong bya/ /bslab pa shing bzung la pham ltung spang bar bya/ /dge 'dun chos grwar 'dug la khyim pa'i
yul grong spongs/ /bud med ma dang sring mo ma yin brten mi bya/ /kun gyi mchod gnas yin pas kha na ma mtho spongs/ /de ltar byas na 'dir bde phyi mar lam sna zin/ /'khor
ba spongs pa'i rab byung btsun ma rnams/ /las ngan skye ba dman pas mkhas btsun blos mi gcog /skyes pa'i 'khri ba chod la 'dul khrims gtsang mar srungs/ /khyim pa'i
grong du ma 'gro phog pa'i sdom pa srungs/ /btsun ma log na 'di med phyi ma dmyal bar 'gro/ /sems bskyed gyis la sbyin pa brtson par thongs/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da
'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /btsun ma rnams kyi thugs la de ltar zhog /gsungs pa ste slob dpon gshegs khar rab byung btsun pa dang btsun ma rnams
la zhal ta gsungs pa'o/ /de nas yang slob dpon pad ma gshegs pa'i dus su/ dge bshes rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ mkhas shing che ba'i bod kyi dge bshes rnams/ /slob dpon
bla ma mkhas shing che ba la/ /'dri klog nyan dang bsam brjod kyis/ /sde snod gsum dang gsang sngags la/ /theg pa'i chos kun mkhas par slobs/ /mi shes bya phul du sbyang
ba'i phyir/ /rig pa'i gnas lnga makas par slobs/ /mi gzhan bkur ba'i gnas gyur nas/ /bsod nams 'du 'dzi byung

ba'i tshe/ /nga rgyal khengs sems phrag dog spongs/ /rang mthong che bcos spyod pa spongs/ /kha nas smras pa'i tshig rjes gsob/ /don dang mthun pa'i chos bzhin bya/ /nga mkhas
gzhan ni mi mkhas zhes/ /kha na ma mtho smra mi bya/ /slob par 'dod pa'i gang zag la/ /ci dga' ba dang ci mos shod/ /rang gi slob dpon drin can la/ /lus ngag yid gsum
bkur ste bya/ /nor rdzas la sogs ci yod 'bul/ /cung zad yon tan rnyed pa la/ /khengs shing rang mthong ma byed par/ /mkhas pa rnams la nyan dris gyis/ /che bcos stong ldir
ma che bar/ /yon tan chos kyis gang bar gyis/ /chos grogs rnams la 'gran sems bor/ /gtsor ni gzhan la snying rjes zungs/ /tshad med bzhi yi go cha bsgos/ /rang rgyud chos
kyis ma dul bar/ /gzhan dag 'dul bar ga la nus/ /mkhas na rang rgyud dul bar gyis/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /bod kyi ston chen da ltar bzhugs pa dang
/ /slad nas 'byon pa rnams kyi thugs la de ltar zhog /gsungs pa ste slob dpon pad ma gshegs pa'i dus su bod kyi dge bshes ston chen rnams la zhal bdams bzhag pa'o/ /slob
dpon pad ma gshegs pa'i dus su sngags pa rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ gsang sngags chos sgor zhugs pa'i sngags par khas len rnams/ /gsang sngags rtsa ba bla ma grub thob 'tshol/
/gsang sngags chos sgo rim pa dbang gis phye/ /gsang sngags srog tu dam tsig gdang mar srungs/ /rdo rje slob dpon yan lag mgo ltar khur/ /yid dam lha ni khong pa'i
snying ltar btsa'/ /mkha' 'gro dam can lus kyi grib ma bzhin du brten/ /gdams ngag zab mo mig gi 'bras ltar btsa'/ /snying po zab mo khong pa'i dbugs bzhin bgrongs/ /bskyed
rdzogs rim pa lus kyi srog bzhin sgoms/ /lta sgom spyod 'bras phyi rgya rlabs kyis chod/ /mi dge bcu spongs dge bcu dang du longs/ /chos kyi phyir ni rang gi srog dang
sdos/ /gtsor ni sngags dang phyag rgya rgyun ma gcod/ /nya stong brgyad dang nyi shu gnyis dag la/ /tshogs dang gtor ma gtong zhing bskang gso bya/ /gdol chos ra chod ras
gcod mi bya bla ma bzang la mnyan/ /'phrin las bon gyer mi bya gyer dang sgom du bstun/ /bsnyen sgrub 'phrin las rnam bzhi gzhung bzhin bya/ /gsang sngags dgra ni yid
gnyis the tshom spongs/ /gsang sngags nor du mami 'tshong spel mi bya/ /rang gis bsgrubs na dngos grub ci bsam 'grub/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ da ltar bzhugs
dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /sngags pa rnams kyi thugs la de ltar zhog /ces slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas gshegs pa'i dus su/ /sngags pa rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa'o/ /de
nas slob dpon pad ma bzhud pa'i dus su/ sgom chen pa rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ bod kyi sgom chen khas len kun gson cig /lta bas thag chod dgongs pa can la mnyan/ /sgom
pa'i nyams len sgom nyams can la zhu/ /spyod pa'i bya ba mnyam bzhag rjes thob bsre/ /'bras bu sku gsum rang gnas rang ngo rtogs/ /gsal 'debs bka' brgyud man ngag zab
mo lta/ /tshig la ma 'byams don la brtag dpyad bya/ /gdams ngag can gyi bla bzang por rten/ /sgom chen thos pa che na gol sa chung / /yid ches med par sgom pa'i tshul ma
bcos/ /the tsom gcod cing grub thob rnams la gtugs/ /tshul 'chos mi bya mi shes brdzun mi gdab/ /chos nyid mnyam

pa'i don la gnas pa'i tshe/ /bying rmugs rgod pa la sogs khar ma gtong / /snying po gsal stong ngang la nyid mtshan sgoms/ /chos nyid don mthong rgyud la skyes tsa na/ /bde
sdug la sogs thams cad grogs su 'gyur/ /chung ma byams kyang sgom pa'i g.yog mi gzhol/ /bud med slob ma mos gus che yang sgro skur rgyu/ /g.yog 'khor zhabs tog che yang
rgyang ring 'dug /'du long bsod nams bar chod rgyu yin pas/ /rang sems dbang du tshugs la yengs med bya/ /de 'dra'i sgom chen mi lus rgyal pa'i thugs/ /pad ma 'byung gnas
bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /sgom chen rnams kyi thugs la bzhag par zhu/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis sgom chen rnams la zhal ta
gsungs pa'o/ /de nas yang slob dpon gyis rnal 'byor pa rnams la gdams pa/ /bod kyi rnal 'byor pho mo kun gson cig /chos nyid don gyi rnal ma ma bcos la/ /rig pa ye shes
ngang du 'byor bas na/ /rnal 'byor zhes su mngi yang btags pa yin/ /lta ba zhe 'dod med do phyogs 'dzin khar ma gtong / /sgom pa dmigs gtad med do sems 'dzin khar ma gtong
/ /spyod pa blang dor med do ched 'dzin khar ma gtong / /'bras bu spangs thob med do 'dod pa'i khar ma gtong / /dam tshig srung mtshams med do zol zog khar ma gtong /
/chos la phyogs ris med do grub mthu'i khar ma gtong / /snang ba 'kharul pa yin tha mal khar ma gtong / /nor rdzas sgyu ma yin no 'dod pa'i khar ma gtong / /gos lhag lhag
srung yin no rgya chos khar ma gtong / /zas la gtsang rme med do zhib lta'i khar ma gtong / /mnyam ris med yin no 'khor gyi khar ma gtong / /rgyal khams 'phyo sa yin no
pha yul khar ma gtong / /phug stong grog stong sdod sa yin no dgon pa'i khar ma gtong / /chig ldum bzang po yin no sgom pa'i khar ma gtong / /chags med zhen med yin no rkyen
ngan khar ma gtong / /rang grol zig po yin no zol zog khar ma gtong / /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da lta bzhugs dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /rnal 'byor rnams
kyi thugs la de ltar zhog /gsungs pa ste/ slob dpon gyis rnal 'byor pa rnams la zhal ta bzhag pa'o/ /de nas yang slob dpon gyis skye bo rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ bod
kyi gtso bo skyes bu bgres gzhon rnams/ /rgyal po'i bka' khrims chos khrims srungs/ /rje'i bka' lung gnyan po snying ltar gyis/ /sgos ched yal bar bor nas gtso bo spyi
ched gyis/ /srog dang bsdos kyang mna' mi za zhing rdzun mi bya/ /chad pa'i tshig btsan dga' bshes grogs mi bslu/ /mang po'i mi kha mi bsdu spyi ched che bar gyis/ /bden
pa khyad gsod ma byed rang sems drang du gyis/ /gros kyis slebs par gyis la bsam mno sngon la tongs/ /mdzangs pa'i mdun gros yangs la che bar mdzod/ /dgra zad thub la ma
gtong rgyal tshod zin par gyis/ /zhal lce gcod na shes che'i kha stabs 'thab gtong / /dpa' bo rnams kyi gzhung lugs dgra bo tul/ /mtshon cha rdor la dmag dpung che bar gyis/
/'khor g.yog skyong la mig rgyang ring bar thongs/ /bran ni ci 'os byin la bkol/ /mi ni rgyang tag ring na yi chad med par skyongs/ /nor du mkhas dang gtam snyan gsog
par gyis/ /bu tsha 'tsho shes yon tan mkhas par slobs/ /ma sring chung ma mna' ma byams par skyongs/ /ma

bsams bya ba nyes pa mang / /gal te bcos pas 'chos na mkhas pa'i rtags/ /bcos su med pa sdug bsngal 'khor ba'i rgyu/ /dal por phyin pas gar 'gro'i sa ru slebs/ /dogs sar bgaskor
na 'jig pa'i sar mi phyin/ /'jam por smras na don grub mdzes pa 'byung / /yin du bsrings na dka' ba'i las kyang 'grub/ /dos drag yun thung tshi sha chad/ /'di phyi'i
don du dam pa'i lha chos gyis/ /phyi ma'i rgyags su sbyin pa mang du thongs/ /yun gyi don du 'byor pa spyod shes kyis/ /dkon mchog bzhugs par mchod pa brtson par gyis/
/dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i tshogs su bsnyain bkur zhabs thog skyed/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas bzhugs pa'i dus su bod kyi skye bo rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa'o/ /de nas yang
slob dpon gyis bud med rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ srid kyi mtsho mo bud med rnams/ /khyim gyi bdag mo yin pas khang pa'i gad dar gyis/ /srid kyi mtsho mo yin pas bu tsha
chos la tshud/ /lus kyi zla gogs yin pas khyo la bkur sti skyed/ /khyo bzang snying dang 'dra yi ci zer ngag la nyon/ /khyo ngan las 'phro yin pas brnyas dang saanying
ma ring / /gyos rgyug pha ma 'dra yi bkur ste phud du khur/ /yab skud pha ming 'dra yis zas dang khrel gyis skyongs/ /snying mo 'grogs yun thung gi bzang gyes gyis/ /'di
ngan phyi mar lci yis khyo min skyes pa spongs/ /bud med khyad par yin pas gtam zlos 'dzum mdangs phyor/ /pha ming rgyab rten yin pas lha ltar mchod/ /smra mang bud med
'chal bas sbra mchu nyung du gyis/ /rang phyogs gnen la khrel la bzang du gyis/ /bu khyo'i lam rgyags yin pas mgron la yangs skyongs/ /'khor dang gnyen bshes rnams la gdung
sems gyis/ /nor la sdom du skyed la zas la yangs su gyis/ /brtson 'grus che la lag byad gtsang bar gyis/ /snga gro snga langs dgong mo nyal phyir gyis/ /dus kyi so nam
brtson 'grus skyed la gyis/ /phyugs lug sgo khyi snying rje skyed la gso/ /sbyin pa'i phyogs su phangs pa med par thongs/ /bla ma dkon mchog dad dang gus pas mchod/ /'dir
ni dge legs phyi ma bde ba thob/ /rang gi phyir du ser sna khram ma gsog /de ltar byas pas 'jig rten cos lugs 'grub/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs
dang slad kyi 'byon pa yi/ /mo btsun bud med rnams la zhal ta bzhag pa'o/ /de nas yang slob dpon pad mas bod kyi mchod gnas rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ /chos la klog
'don byed pa'i yon mchod rnams/ /dang por gzhanon du 'bri klog legs par sbyongs/ /'bri mkhan yi ge'i gzugs ni legs par sbyongs/ /dkar nag cha mnyam ring thung med par bris/
/yon bdag khengs grags med par mchod gnas brten par gyis/ /dad pa'i sems kyis theg la gus pa'i sbyor ba rdzogs/ /mchod gnas 'dod pa ma bskyed ci phul mnyes par gyis/
/bsod nams yon mchod gnyis ka thun mong thob/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob pa'i rgyur 'gyur ro/ /yon bdag log rtog skyes pa'i bsod nams de/ /dang por sgra skad 'jigs kyang
skyo ba skyes/ /bar du the tshom byung bas bsod nams tshogs mi 'grub/ /tha mar gnyis ma mgu bas dam nyams rgyu ru 'gyur/ /de bas the tshom chod la dge la 'bad/ /gsal dag
snyan gsum bsgrags pas lha mi gus/ /sgra skad ma 'dzings gtsang ma 'don/ /bar du 'dren khugs sdengs dang sbyar/

/tha ma tshig 'bru'i lhag chad spongs/ /lhag chad med par gus dang dang bas sgrogs/ /chos la an g.yogs med dang tho yugs spongs/ /bdag nyid bstan pa'i bdag por soms/ /chos
kyi sgra chen bsgrags pa yis/ /'gro ba mi ma yin rnams mos pas nyan/ /chos thos ngan sdig grol bar bsam la 'don/ /thon nas tshig 'phro gcod tshe na/ /dge rtsa yon bdag mchod
gnas kyis/ /thun mong rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'grub/ /yon bdag dad dang ldan par yon gyis mnyes par phul/ /mchod gnas gang phul yon gyis mnyes par mdzod/ /de ltar ma yin
mchod gnas kyis/ /tshar gyis grangs brkus yon la rtseg 'thams byas/ /gsal dag snan gsum ma bton long gtam dag bsres/ /mkhas pa rnams kyang skyon par bshad nas bton/ /sgra
don ma nges g.yeng bas sems gzhan 'phros/ /mi mkhas pa yis shog bu bam bsgyur byas/ /yon bdag rnams kyi rgyags dang bkur sti med/ /yon gyis mchod gnas ma mnyes za mas
khong khro bsags/ /legs par ma bsgrags mchod gnas sdig la sbyar/ /yon bdag ma mnyes mchod gnas sdig la sbyar/ /de 'dra'i yon mchod gnyis ka dmyal bar lhung / /de ltar ma
byed gnyis kas chos dang ldan par mdzod/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang slad nas 'byon pa yi/ /mchod gnas rnams kyi thugs la de ltar zhog
/ces slob dpon gyis bod kyi bla mchod rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa'o/ /de nas slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas gshegs pa'i dus su bod kyi sman pa lha rje rnams la zhal ta gsungs
pa/ 'tsho byed gzhon bu'i sprul pa sman pa kun/ /dang po slob pa'i slob dpon mkhas par slobs/ /bar du rtsa ngo shases dang dpyad dang lag len sbyongs/ /rlung mkhris pad
kan ma nor so sor gces/ /sman sbyor dus na skor tson mnor sbyor/ /bar du slob dpon mnyes pa'i bkur sti skyed/ /tha mar nad 'chos gtsang rtog dregs pa skyungs/ /'byung bzhi
legs par rtogs la tsha grang phyed par gyis/ /glo bur nad la blo dang rig pas rtogs/ /gzhung dang ma 'gal sman dpyad ma nor gyis/ /sman pa mkhas kyang nad pa'i kha drod
ltos/ /mi shes rang bzo spongs la pho tshod che bar gyis/ /nad ngo ma zin sman dpyad ma legs na/ /rang 'gyod mi gces bsad pa'i ming gtam 'byung / /mtshon cha med pa'i mche
brkyangs mgo nag yin/ /'dod pa che na zas nor dka' sla dang / /nang du tshud dka' bar du bsten dka' tha me thon dka' na/ /de ni rang don 'tshong ba'i tshong dpon chen
po yin/ /de ltar ma byed dang po snying rjes gsos/ /bar du mgu yang thugs dgongs bzang du gyis/ /tha mar mgu sla zhe 'dod chung bar mdzod/ /gso dpyad gang byed sems bskyed
zin par gyis/ /zas kyi phyir ni bsod nams tshogs rdzogs mdzod/ /nor gyis phyir ni sangs rgyas thob par sngos/ /phyi ma lha'i go 'phang thob nas ni/ /skye ba stong du lus
la nad med bde dang ldan/ /yon tan dpag tu med pa thob par 'gyur/ /nad pa kun kyang dang po sman pa lhar ma lta/ /bar du sman pa mi 'dra log lta spongs/ /ta ma the tsom
chod la yid ches gyis/ /zas dang gtang rag g.yo sgyu med par phul/ /drag nas sman pa 'phrad par lam la 'dzur/ /bsam pa dkar pas gzhung srings dang tshig srungs/ /de ltar
ma byas nad pas sman par ma gus nas/ /dang po lhar mthong zug gzer chag nas mir mthong nas/ /tha mar drag nas

dgrar mthong lugs bzhin ma byas nas/ /de'i rnam smin tshe 'dir khrel med phyi ma dmyal bar 'gro/ /bskal bar lus la zug rngu nad kyis thebs par 'gyur/ /yang shi yang gsos thig
nag dmyal bar 'gyur/ /de ltar ma byed yid ches thob par bkur sti skyed/ /bsam pa dag pas 'bul nom bzang bar gyis/ /dei dge bas bskal pa mang por yang / /nad med bde skyid
thob par the tshom med/ /pad ma 'byung gnas bdag ni da 'gro bas/ /da ltar bzhugs dang smad nas 'byon pa yi/ /sman pa rnams kyis thugs la de zhog /ces gsungs pa ste/ slob
dpon gyis bod kyi sman pa rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa'o/ /slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas gshegs khar bod kyi slob ma rnams la zhal ta gsungs pa/ bod kyi slob dpon slob ma
chos 'brel byed pa rnams/ /dang po bla ma slob dpon phul du phyin pa rtogs/ /de nas dam chos mtha' rgya chod la mkhas par slobs/ /mtha' mar bsgrubs la grub rtags thon par

rdo rje mtsho dang / ru yongs bza' 'thing ma dang / mchims bza' rin chen gsal le 'od dang / 'brom bza' ti pang ma dang / mer gong bza' rin chen mchog gtsug dang / khyad
par gyi bu mo drug dang bcas pa rnams kyis/ rgyal po la bskor nas byon/ slob dpon pad ma lha srin sde brgyad kyis bskor nas byon pa la bod kyi bstan ma bcu gnyis/ skyong
ma bcu gnyis/ ya ma bcu gnyis/ dge bsnyen nyi shu rtsa gcig g.ya' ri mo/ gangs ri mo nyi shu rtsa gcig mkha' 'gro dang shugs 'gro mang pos bskor nas byon nas mang yul don
khar byon pa dang / thams cad kyis slob dpon la phyi pyag byas pa dang / der slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis mgur bzhes pa/ nga 'gro srin po'i yul du 'gro/ /nga 'gro
lta ba'i thang la 'gro/ /lta ba'i thang la 'gro tsa na/ /snang srid chos skur khyer nas 'gro/ /nga 'gro sgom pa'i thang la 'gro/ /sgom pa'i thang la 'gro tsa na/ /mnyam
bzhag rjes thob med par 'gro/ /nga 'gro spyod pa'i thang la 'gro/ /spyod pa'i thang 'gro tsa na/ /blang dor ro snyom med par 'gro/ /nga 'gro 'bras bu'i thang la 'gro/ /'bras
bu'i thang la 'gro tsa na/ /re dogs 'bras bu bsal nas 'gro/ /nga 'gro lta ba'i lam la 'gro/ /lta ba'i lam la 'gro tsa na/ /nyin mtshan sgom du med par 'gro/ /nga 'gro
sgom pa'i lam la 'gro/ /sgom pa'i lam la 'gro tsa na/ /bying rgod gnyis su grol nas 'gro/ /nga 'gro spyod pa'i

lam la 'gro/ /spyod pa'i lam la 'gro tsa na/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa bon 'debs/ /nga 'gro 'bras bu'i lam la 'gro/ /'bras bu'i lam la 'gro tsa na/ /rtogs pa mngon gyur gyi
sangs rgyas thob/ /nga 'gro lta ba'i thur la bab/ /lta ba'i thur la bab tsa na/ /chos kyi dbyings kyi sa la gnas/ /nga 'gro sgom pa'i thur la bab/ /sgom pa'i thur la bab
tsa na/ /sgom med ma yangs nga la gnas/ /nga 'gro spyod pa'i thur la bab/ /spyod pa'i thur la bab tsa na/ /bde gshegs bka' lung bzhin du byed/ /nga 'gro 'bras bu'i thur
la bab/ /'bras bu'i thur la bab tsa na/ /rang rgyud dag pa'i sangs rgyas lags/ /nga 'gro lta ba'i gnas su 'gro/ /lta ba'i gnas su 'gro tsa na/ /rnam rtog ye shes kyi rang
bzhin lags/ /sdug bsngal chos nyid rang bzin lags/ /nga 'gro spyod pa'i gnas su 'gro/ /spyod pa'i gnas su 'gro tsa na/ /'khor ba byang chub kyi rang bzhin lags/ /nga 'gro
'bras bu'i gnas su 'gro/ /'bras bu'i gnas su phyin tsa na/ /sems can sangs rgyas rang bzhin legs/ /nga 'gro srin po'i yul 'gro/ /srin pa'i yul du phyin tsa na/ /sems can
bde la 'god du 'gro/ /srin po chos la 'dzud du 'gro/ /bod kyi mnga' bdag blon 'khor rnams/ /yun du sku khams ce bder bzhugs/ /nga skye shi gnyis med kyi sku thob pas/ /mi
bde ba yi sdug bsngal med/ /snying rje rgyun chad med pa yi/ /khyed dad gus mos pas gsol ba thob/ /nga dang yang yang mjal nas mchi/ /zhes gsungs pas/ thams cad ma dga'
ste mchi ma byung ste/ slob dpon gyi phyi phyag gi lo rgyus lags so/ /de nas rgyal po dang bu slob thams cad kyis phyag btsal skor ba byas/ ngus mchi ma byung ba dang /
slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyi mgur bzhes pa/ nyon cig bod kyi rje 'bangs rnams/ /bya rgod po nam 'phang gcod pa la/ /'dod pa'i dbang gis zan la babs/ /rnyi la zin pa
ma tshor ro/ /nya mo chab la 'phyo ba la/ /'dod pa'i dbang gis gangs la rgyugs/ /dol gyis zin pa ma tshor ro/ /nga rang sems ye nas sangs rgyas la/ /'dod pa'i dbang gis gzhan
gnas btsal/ /'khor bar 'khyams pa ma tshor ro/ /khyod 'jig rten 'khor bar yengs yengs nas/ /'chi khar song ba ma tshor ro/ /zhes gsungs pas/ der thams cad kyis slob
dpon 'di 'dra ba dang mjal ba dka' na/ chos dang dbang thob pa lta ci smos/ 'di thams cad kyis zhus pas ni bzhugs par ma gnang / da bzung ba drag zer te/ rgyal blon kun gyis
slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas la 'jus nas mi gtong bar byas pas/ ma thub par nam mkha' stong pa la bzhugs nas bzung bas ma thub po/ /slo dpon pad ma'i gsung gis/ nga khyed
tshos bzung bas mi thub gsungs te mgur bzhes pa/ nga mi mang po'i 'du 'dzi byung tsa na/ /rang lus dgon pa'i gdams ngag mdog /grogs bu tsha'i 'du 'dzir ma chags na nga
phyir 'deng / /shes pa phyi ru shor tsa na/ /snang ba lam khyer gyi gdams ngag bdog /yul snang la ma chags na nga phyir 'deng / /dran pa sna tshogs byung tsa na/ /sprul
sku thugs phrad kyi gdams ngag bdog /tha mal shes pa 'chos na nga phyir 'deng / /sgom bying dang rmugs pa byung tsa na/ /bying rmugs chos sku'i gdams ngag bdog /sgom nus
pa yod na nga phyir 'deng / /mnyam bzhag rjes thob byung tsa na/ /mun snang mar me'i gdams ngag bdog /sgom

rgyun chad med par 'dod na nga phyir 'deng / /yul la zhen pa byung tsa na/ /pha yul bor ba'i gdams ngag bdog /pha yul la ma chags nga phyir 'deng / /mi skye bo'i ma dga' byung
tsa na/ /brag cha sgra'i gdams ngag bdog /mi kha la ma 'jigs na nga phyir 'deng / /mi sdang ba'i dgra dang phrad tsa na/ /lan chags bzod pa'i gdams ngag bdog /zhe sdang
dgra la ma zhen na nga phyir 'deng / /gnyen dang nye ba brtsi tsa na/ /'khor ba rtsad gcod kyi gdams ngag bdog /gnyen 'dun la ma chags na nga phyir 'deng / /bu slob yon
bdag la brtsi tsa na/ /chags med zhen med kyi gdams ngag bdog /bu slob yon bdag la ma chags na nga phyir 'deng / /'dod yon lnga la chags tsa na/ /skyar mo nya khyer gyi
gdams ngag bdog /nor zas la ma chags na nga phyir 'deng / /lus la na tsha byung tsa na/ /lus sgyu lus yin pa'i gdams ngag bdog /lus na tshas nyen na nga phyira'adeng / /'chi
ba'i nad kyis nyen tsa na/ /'da' ka 'chi brod kyi gdams ngag bdog /'chi bas 'jigs na nga phyir 'deng / /lus bem rig gnyis bral tsa na/ /rig pa rten med kyi gdams ngag
bdog /bar dos 'jigs na nga phyir 'deng / /lnga pa skye rgyun ma chod pa/ /'gro drug sgo 'geg gi gdams ngag bdog /'gro drug g.yeng bas 'jigs na nga phyir 'deng / /dgongs
sam rje 'bangs bu slob kun/ /dad pa gting nas ma skyes na/ /nges shes ye shes mi 'char ro/ /nges shes ye shes ma shar bas/ /bla ma'i gdams ngag mi 'phrod do/ /dad pa mos
pa gus pa yis/ /bla ma'i gdams ngag nyams su longs/ /nga skye 'chi gnyis kyi mtha' las grol/ /'gro dang mi 'gro nga la med kyi/ /ye shes thugs la rgyun chad med kyi/ /dad
mos la byin rlabs rgyun chad la med kyi/ /rang sems nor bu rin chen 'di la/ /bde sdug gi zug rngu lus la med kyi/ /spyi gtsug tu mos pas sgom nus na/ /nye ba dang ring
ba nga med kyi/ /rang lus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor 'di/ /gdos pa dang bcas pa nga la med kyi/ /mi dga' ci yod dga' bar soms/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / slob dpon pad ma 'byung
gnas kyi phyag phyi la rgyal po dang 'khor rnams kyis 'gro nus pa gcig kyang med do/ /slob dpon la rgyal po dang slob 'khor rnams kyis 'jus nas 'chi ma bton pas der slob
dpon lho nub mtshams su zhal log gis gzigs nas bar snang la gzha' tshon sna lha'i dkyil na bzhugs pa la bod kyi rgyal blon bu slob ngarnams kyis rjes su yi rang bas phyag
btsal skor ba byas gsol ba btab/ byin rlabs zhus nas de rnams kyang 'khor ba las phyir mi ldog par gyur to/ /de nas 'khor rnams kyis slob dpon srin po'i yul du bzhud pa
la yun ring gi bar la bltas pa dang / bar snang la pad ma 'od kyi gzhal yas na phar sku 'od zer dang bcas te ta la bzhud do/ /slob dpon lho nub srin po'i yul rnga yab gling
phran/ zangs mdog dpal ri la gshegs pa la bod kyi rgyal po/ blon po/ dge bshes/ sngags pa/ sman pa/ bon po/ btsun pa/ rnal 'byor pa/ sgom chen pa/ nya ma/ skye bo/ bud
