med bcas pas skyel thung dang phyi phyag btsal zhing dbang zhus pa dang / zhal gdams mkhan pos lung bstan/ slob dpon pad ma bod du mi lo lnga bcu rtsa gcig bzhugs nas/ lha
srin gdug pa can thams cad btul/ rgyal pa'i bsam pa bsgrubs/ dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa bzhengs/ sa gzhi

thams cad zhabs kyis bcags/ dben gnas thams cad sgrub gnas khyad par can du byin gyis brlabs/ dbang dang / lung dang / sgrub thabs rnams mdzad cing gnang nas bod thams cad
smin par byas/ rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyi ring la bla mchod mdzad/ sras mu khri btsan po'i ring la lho nub rnga yab gling phran du gshegs pa'i chos 'byung lags so/
/ma gcig jo mo bkra shis mtsho rgyal/ lha mo dbyangs can ma'i sprul pa/ mi brjed pa'i gzungs thob pa des/ phyi rabs kyi skal ldan rnams la/ slob dpon gyi thugs rgyud/ mnga'
bdag khri srong lde btsan gyi bka' chems/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rgyas par mdzad tshul/ dam chos 'byung khungs gtsug lag khang bzhengs lugs/ lha srin thams cad btul
lugs/ bod du paNDi ta dang lo tsA ba byung lugs/ sgrub gnas dang sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs lugs/ chos kyi gter ka sbas lugs/ rgyal po khri srong lde btsan dang / za hor gyi
bo dhi sa twa dang / u rgyan gyi slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas dang / lho phyogs bhe ta'i ka ma la shI la dang / kha che'i bi ma la mi tra dang / rgya nag ha shang ma hA
ya na dang lnga ste slob dpon chen po lnga / mu ne bar ma dang / phradznyA bar ma dang / shi len dra bo dhi dang / kha che dznyA na de ba dang / su ran dra bo bhi dang
/ dznyA na gha rba dang / mnya?dzu gha rba dang / dharma shi la phrabha wa dang / bha dza ya de ba dang / sha ya se thur dang / dznyA na sidhi dang / bhi shu de sing ha dang
/ kha che dzi na mi tra dang / bhirya a kar pra bha ba dang / kha che dharma ka ra dang / dha rma shri bha dra dang / shAkya se na dang / sha ya sing ha dang / bal po
shaNti gha rba dang / snyi de ba ko shan dang / lo tsA ba dang grub chen nyi shu rtsa lnga la/ lo tsA ba snyags dznyAn ku ma ra dang / dri med sha dha ra dang / sbas madznyushrI
dang / tran pa mu ri ti dang / sbas ye shes dbang po dang / gnyan dpal dbyangs dang / ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs dang / 'bro ka ba dpal brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i
rgyal mtshan dang / sna nam ye shes sde dang / dhar ta shi la dang / rma rin chen mchog snubs nam mkha'i snying po dang / chos kyi snang ba dang / dran pa nam mkha' dang
/ lce bkra shis dang / lce kyi 'brug dang / ban de dpal 'byor dang / mchog sbyin snying po dang / ye shes snying po dang / dha rma a lo ka dang / mchog gi snying po dang
/ rin chen sde dang / dznyA na rakShi ta dang / legs pa'i blo gros dang / lha'i zla ba dang / ban de dpal gyi snying po dang / ban de bzang skyong dang / lo tsA ba'i mchan
bu 'dan ma rtse mang dang / legs sbyin nyi ma dang / rtsangs dhe len ta dang / rnam par mi rtogs pa dang / kha che skyes bzang gi bla ma a nan ta/ go gom chos sgrub dang
/ lo kyi chung / 'khon klu'i dbang po srung ba dang / de pa tsan dra/ gru gu u pe sha dang / ru gyong bhiryar dza dang / de ba tsan dra dharma tsarya dang / de la sogs
pa'i lo paN mang po dang / khyad par gyi bu mo drug dang / de la sogs pa grub chen nyi shu rtsa lnga dang / lo tsA ba dang / lo tsA ba'i mchan bu rnams dang / rgyal po
khri srong lde btsan dang / mkhan po bo dhi sa twa/ slob dpon pad ma dang gsum smon lam lhan cig btab pa dang

/ gzhan grub pa thob pa dang / brtul zhugs kyis 'gro ba rnams chos la btsud pa'i rabs/ thugs rje chen po'i gsung yi ge drug pa'i yon tan yi ge rigs su bkod pa rnams gter du
sbas pa dang / gzhan bka'i yig rtsis che chung / bka'i thang yig che chung / bka'i gtsigs kyi yi ge mang du yod do/ gzhan yang rgyal rabs rkyang pa dang / khug pa/ zings
po can dang / yun po la sogs mang po yod do/ /zhu chen lo tsA bas bod dpe la bklags/ rgya dpe la paNDi tas zhu tig byed pa/ lo tsA bas tsheg bar bdun la tshig rkang gcig
tshig rkang bzhi la sho lo ka gcig sho lo ka sum brgya la bam po gcig bam po zhes pa'i tshad ni sho lo ka sum brgya dang sum cu rtsa gcig tshig rkang stong gcig gi sum cha
la bam po gcig tu bshad do/ /slob dpon zhi ba la sogs pas bam po zhes pa'i tshad ni sho lo ka stong gi sum cha la 'dod de/ che chung gi tshad ni tshig rkang ring thung
dang mi mang nyung la rnam par bzhag par bshad do/ /de rnams ni bstan bcos rin po che'i mtsho las bshad do/ /de'i dus su chos kyi mtshan thams cad rgya dpe la le'u mtshams
dang / zhabs na yod pa la dam pa yi chos khungs btsun pa dang rgyal po bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya yin pa dang / dam pa chos kyi skabs ngos bzung ba dang / skabs btsal sla
ba'i mtshan ched du smos pa dang / go sla ba'i dgos pa yod pa'i skad du bstan pa lags skad do/ /sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba de la gsol thang ni/ blon po chen po kun dang
mnyam mo/ blon po chen po'i za thang ni/ rgyal pos gsol ba'i gsum cha gcig yin no/ /rgyal po chen po'i gsol thang ni/ sku srung brgya brgya'i chas dang bcas pa na ma re
re la yod do/ /de nas rgya gar gyi slob dpon dha na shi la dang / dzi na mi tra dang / ka ba dpal brtsegs dang / cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / sna nam gyi ban de ye shes
sde dang / de gsum gyi lo tsA ba byas te/ chos mdo sde skyes rabs dang bcas pa dang / dkon mchog brtsegs pa/ sangs rgyas phal po che/ lang kar gshegs pa/ rgyas pa 'bum/
rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ gzungs 'bum/ bai ro tsa na la slob ma gsum gyis bsgyur ba'o/ /snyags dznyA na ku ma ra/ a tsarya rin chen mchog gnyis kyis bsgyur ba la klu 'bum
skya bo dang / rlangs khams pa go chas bsgyur ba bla 'bum smug po shas sgro can no/ /gzhan yang 'bum nag dang / 'bum dmar dang / shes rab khri pa dang / khri brgyad stong
pa dang / sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ 'phags pa bsdus pa rdo rje gcod pa/ shes rab snying po/ yi ge gcig ma'i bar pha rol tu phyin pa rgyas bsdus thams cad bsgyur ro/ /slob
dpon ka ma la shI la dang / rma rin chen mchog gis dpang skong phyag stong pa la sogs pa dang / mdo sde rgya nag ma la sogs pa mang du bsgyur ro/ slob dpon bo dhi sa
twa dang / lo tsA ba mchan bu mang pos chos mdo sde/ 'dul ba/ mngon pa'i gzhung thams cad bsgyur ro/ /slob dpon bi ma la mi tra dang / lo tsA ba snyags dznyA nas/ sgyu 'phrul
lam skor dang / de'i cha lag dang bcas pa/ phur pa sham sngon can du grags pa bsgyur ro/ /lha sras khri srong lde btsan gyis gyi ling rta'i khungs dang so yig khams
dang rigs thams cad kyi rta dpyad la mnga' brnyes pas/ der yul chen po lnga nas rta mkhan chen po drug

bos so/ /gru gu'i yul nas gru gu se thod dang / gru gu go cha bos/ 'bro yul nas 'bro kho sbyor dang / 'bro bzang la yug bos/ cog ro'i yul nas cog ro mang po bos/ 'do rgod kyi
yul nas 'do khu mdo bos/ 'bro snya'i yul sde gsum las/ g.yu bzher legs khri bos/ de rnams rta dpyad 'gran pas/ gru gu se thod kyis stangs bcad de rta la rigs rnam pa lnga
mchis te/ 'byung ba lnga dang bstun pa/ se tho sa'i khams dang gcig gyi ling chu'i khams dang gnyis/ gyam shing me'i khams dang gsum/ mdo ba rlung gi khams dang bzhi/
gung ron nam mkha'i khams dang lnga'o/ /de ltar ngos bzung stangs su phul bas rgyal blon thams cad mnyes so/ /bya dga' yang che thang du gnang ngo / /de'i dus su pho brang
rim dgu'i sgo khang du mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i dbu la gor bus phra brgyab pa ltar mdzad nas/ zhal chems ye shes dbang po la bzhag nas sku gshegs so/ /de'i spur bsam yas
has po ri'i rgyab tu bzhugs nas mchod rten gcig bzhengs so/ /der btsan pos ye shes dbang po chos dpon du ring lugs su bskos/ mdun du yang bla'i 'og tu bton/ rab tu byung
ba mang bas chos grwa'i dpon dang / nya ma'i dpon yang so sor bskos/ na bza' rnams dang / rgyal blon mang pos 'phan gyis sbyor/ slob dpon ring lugs pa la zla ba re re'i
phogs la nas khal bdun cu/ chos grwa'i dpon la nas khal sum cu rtsa lnga/ chos slob pa la nas khal bcu gnyis re thang du bcad/ slad kyi ye shes dbang po mngon shes dang
ldan pas/ dkon mchog gsum gyi rten yun ring du gnas pa'i ched du/ rten la 'bangs mi khyim brgya/ ban de re la 'bangs mi khyim gsum gsum bcad/ 'bangs lha ris pa la/ bla nas
dbang che mi bya bar chad/ gang zag shes rab can dang / brtson 'grus ldan pa rnams/ thos bsam sgom gsum la bcug mgo 'dren rnams la mtshan mkhan po dang / bshes gnyen du
btags/ chos grwa chen po bcu gnyis su chos slob/ stangs 'bul gyi sa drug tu stangs 'bul/ sgom grwa chen po lngar sgrub pa nyams su len/ 'bri dang / klog pa dang / bsgyur
ba dang / 'chad pa dang / nyan pa dang / sems pa dang / bgro gleng dang / dpang sgong gi phyag mchod/ sman lha'i mdo chog ltung bshags kyi phyag 'tshal/ sher snying gi
mdo sgrub/ lho bal bas kyang lhag pa mdzad do/ /chos lugs bzang po mi nub pa'i rgyal mtshan btsugs/ de rnams kyi 'tsho ba bla nas sbyor pa'i cha rkyen la/ zhing dang / dar
zab/ gser dngul/ zangs lcags/ rkang 'gros tshong skyed rnams bshams/ dbang kha dge 'dun la bskur/ nyan ting nge 'dzin bzang po la sogs pa ye shes dbang po la mi nyan pa
mi mchi dgu mchi bas/ ye shes dbang po bros nas lho brag mkhar chu btsan gyi brag phug la bsgom du song / phrag la ga sha bkal/ spa la zam pa btsugs/ lus sa la byas/ sa
rdo la bas pa ltar 'dug khrims grogs la bya yang gnyen du mi 'jug de'i 'og tu dpal dbyangs chos dpon la bskos pa dang / rgya nag gi mkhan po ma hA ya na'i slob bu sgom phrug
pa rnams dar te 'khor bar skye ba'i rgyu/ rang ngo rang gis ma shes pas lan/ rang ngo rang gis shes na rtogs nas sangs rgyas/ de'i phyir sems ngo 'phrod dgos/ de ngo
shes na dkar po chig thub yin/ 'di'i gzhung 'dzugs pa la/ sems len bsu bya ba'i bstan bcos gsum mdzad do/ /sems

ngo 'phrod na nyal bas chog pas/ bsam gtan nyal 'dug gi 'khor lo dang / de'i gnad ston pa'i bsam gtan gyi 'khor lo dang / de'i gegs sel ba la bsam gtan gyi yang len no/ /de'i
gdams pa rigs pas sgru pa la/ man ngag lta ba'i rgyab sha dang / de lung gis sgrub pa la mdo sde brgyad bu khungs zhes bya ba mdzad/ de nyams su len pa la yas babs dang
/ mas 'dzegs gnyis/ cig car ba dang / rim gyis pa'i lugs gnyis yod pa la/ chos 'di ni dbang po yang rab kyi don/ khyung nam mkha' las babs pa dang 'dra/ cig car ba yin
no/ /sems ngo ma 'phrod na/ lus ngag gi chos spyod dang dge ba byas pas mtho ris thob pa las/ sangs rgyas mi thob/ bya ba btang / ci yang yid la mi byed par byar med/ 'dod
'dun spangs te bdag 'dzin grol nas/ sangs rgyas zer nas sgom bslabs pas/ bod ril pa khong gi chos la dad de bslab po/ rdzogs byed mdo bculas/ spros pa med pa'i chos nyid
la bsams la/ gzung 'dzin bral ba'i rim pa ma sbyangs pas/ ton min rtsen min dag gi chos nyid bzhin/ rang gi rnam rtog de nyid ye shes 'dod/ bsam gtan sgom pa'i sgo sar
nga yis bshad/ ces so/ /de yis bsam yas dang / lha sa la sogs pa'i mchod pa byed pa nyung du song / lus ngag gi dge sbyor mtshan bcas byed pa 'phro chad pas sba rna dang
/ bai ro tsa na dang / sba dpal dbyangs la sogs nyung shas shig slob dpon bo dhi sa twa'i grub mtha' 'dzin/ de ltar lta spyod ma mthun par gyur to/ /btsan pos rgya'i ston
pa'i chos min byas pas ston min pa bya bar grags/ drang srong bzod pas lus la me spar nas mchod pa phul bas/ sems can la brtse ba'i sgo nas tshogs bsags pa gal che byas
pas/ btsan po na re/ lus la me spar ba'i brtse ba de yang / chos min nam byas pas brtse min pa bya bar grags so/ /btsan pos lta ba dang spyod pa mthun par brtse ba min pa
ltar yin byas pas/ ston min pa rnams khros nas nyang sha mis rang gi sha nye spangs/ rngog rin po che dang / snyags bi ma yis/ rang gi pho mtshan brdungs/ rgya'i ston pas
mgo bstud de bro bor/ gzhan rnams chu gri re btsugs nas/ brtse min pa ril gsod zer/ de btsan po'i snyan du bzlas pas/ ji ltar bya ma shes te/ ban sde rnams la btsan pos
sku yon btang ste ye shes dbang po 'bod mi btang bas ma khugs/ nang blon chen po khams pa go cha btang ste khyod kyis ye shes dbang po spyan drongs na/ bya dga' byin gyis/
ma khugs na khyod rang gsod do/ /zhes bsgos nas/ btsan po'i bka' shog gi sgrom bu bskur nas btang ngo / /khams pas lho brag tu phyin/ bka' sgrom phyag tu phul nas/ khyed
byon na bdag la bya dga' yang gnang bar bdog ma byon na bdag 'gum pas bdag ni brag phug 'di nas mchongs te 'gum mo/ zhes zhus pas/ 'di nga la bar chad kyi bdud gcig byung
/ da khyod kyi srog 'don no gsungs nas/ nga 'ong gis rta ded la shog ces 'phrin bskur bas/ khams pa dga' ches nas btsan po'i snyan du gsol bas/ bya dga' yang gnang nas/
gor bu bcu drug ded nas ye shes dbang po spyan drangs/ pho brang du btsan po la phyag bzhes/ btsan pos btsun pa 'khrugs pa'i lo rgyus zhib tu smras nas rgya dkar nag gnyis
chos lugs la ma 'chams pas/ de gang bden khyod kyis smros shig gsungs so/ /ye shes dbang po na re/ de la

bdag dgug mi 'tshal te/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i zhal chems bdog go/ /bdag sgom pa'i bar chad ma byas na tshe ring / btsan po'i sku tshe yang ring / dam pa'i chos kyang 'phags
pa byams pa byon pa'i bar du gnas pa yin la/ bod la skal ba ma mchis/ mkhan po 'da' kar 'di skad gsungs te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos gang du dar ba der/ mu stegs kyi sgom
pa'i grwa re 'gran du yong ba yin te/ bod yul du lnga brgya'i tha mar gyur pa dang / slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas kyis bstan ma bcu gnyis la gnyer gtad pas/ chos dar yang
mu stegs ni mi 'ongs na/ nang pa sangs rgyas pa'i nang na lta ba ma mthun pas rtsod par 'gyur gyis/ de tsa na nga'i slob ma ka ma la shI la bal yul sdod kyi/ de khug la
chos kyi bgro glengs kyi shags 'debs su chug cig rtsod pa chos phyogs su 'dum par 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs so/ zhes gsol pas/ btsan pos bal yul du paNDi ta ka ma la shI' la
spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya ba brdzangs pa dang / ha shang gi slob ma ston min pa rnams/ yum rgyas pa spyan drangs te/ bsam gtan gling sgo bsdams nas/ zla bzhi'i bar shags
bslabs so/ /mdo dgongs pa nges par 'grel ba rtog pas sgrib cing 'di chos min zhes 'bar ro/ /de'i bar du ye shes dbang pos/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa dang / ha shang gnyis kyi
lta ba dang / dgongs pa ji ltar yin pa btsan po'i snyan du gsol bas/ dgongs pa grol nas dgyes te/ ye shes dbang po'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal zhing / khyed nga'i a tsarya'o/
/dus der ka ma la shI la 'byon gyin yod ces pho nya ma byung bas/ rje blon yos chab kar bsu bar byon pa dang / ha shang 'khor dang bcas pa yang chab kar bsu ba la byon/
de nas btsan po gong la bzhugs nas/ ston min pa dang / rtse min pa chos kyi bka' bgro zhing shags gdab par byas/ ha shang g.yas gral du byas/ 'khor jo mo byang chub dge
dang / gzims mal bco mang dang / sru yang dag sde la sogs pa gral ring po byung / a tsarya ka ma la shI la g.yon gral du bzhugs te/ 'khor bai ro tsa na dang / sba rata?n
dang / dpal dbyangs la sogs pa nyung shas gcig las ma byung / btsan pos ston rtsen re re'i phyag tu gser dkar re dang / me tog dkar po'i 'phreng ba re phul te bka' bstsal
pa/ nga'i mnga' ris bod kyi rgyal khams 'dir/ thams cad nag po la dga' ba'i dus su/ za hor gyi rgyal po'i bu bo dhi sa twa spyan drangs nas bod nyung shas gcig chos la
bkod/ dad pa can kha cig rab tu byung / dkon mchog gsum gyi rten btsugs pa'i skabs su/ rgya'i mkhan po ha shang ma hA ya na 'dir byon/ bod kyi btsun pa phal cher khong la
slob par gyur/ bo dhi sa twa'i slob ma nyung shas tsam las slob tu ma btub nas/ ston rtsen gnyis su chad/ de gnyis lta spyod ma mthun par rtsod par gyur pa las/ ngas zhal
lce gcod par ma rangs nas/ nyang sha mi dang / rngog dang / snyags la sogs pa kun gyis lus la na tsha bskyed/ ha shang me gos bro dor/ der btsan g.yon bskur/ da ni bo
dhi sa twa'i 'khor ka ma la shI la yin pas/ khyed ha shang dang gnyis shags gyis la/ su gtan tshigs bzang ba de la su ngan pa des nga rgyal mi byed par me tog phul cig bstan
pa rgyal du 'jog pa yin no gsungs nas/ rgyal po dang mkhan po rnams kyis dpang byas lung rigs ngan pa dang

su mi rigs pa la khrims kyis chad pa gcod do zhes bka' bstsal to/ /de la ha shang na re/ nga gzhi la snga bas nga yis dri 'am lan gdab zer ro/ /ka ma la shI la na re/ khyod
kyi dgongs pa ltar shags thob cig ces zer ba dang / ha sang gi gsung gis nga yis las rgyu 'bras mi shes pa min/ gdul bya rnams nges don gyis khrid na lam nye bas/ thams
cad sems kyi rtog pas bskyed pas/ sems dge mi dge dag gis las dge mi dge spyad pas/ ngan song gi 'bras bu nyams su myong zhing 'khor ba na 'khor zhing / gang zhig ci la mi
rtog ci la yang mi sems pa de 'khor ba las yongs su thar bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar na rgyu 'bras stong nyid du zab pas/ lta ba rtogs pa dang / snying rje chen po rang shugs
su skye ba yin/ stong nyid snying rje chen po can du gnas/ mi dge 'chol rtag tu spyod pa min/ de lta bas na ci yang mi bsam mo/ /skyabs 'gro sems bskyed nas sbyin pa la
sogs pa chos spyod bcu rang rgyud du spyod pa ni/ spre'u ltar mas 'dzeg yin no/ /skye bo dge ba'i las 'phro med pa zhang blon dbang po brtul po rnams la lam kha 'dren du
bstan pa yin no/ /blon po blo sbyangs pa dbang po rnon po dag la sprin dkar nag gis kyang nyi ma sgrib pa ltar/ dge sdig gnyis kas sgrib kyi ci la yang mi sems mi rtog mi
spyod pa ni mi dmigs pa'o/ /khyung lding pa ltar yas babs kyi chos yin no/ /cig car 'jug pa ni sa bcu pa dang 'dra'o/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / atsarya ka ma la shI las smras
pa/ ngas gnas lugs yang dag pa'i don mi shes pa min/ gdul bya la lam rim gyis drang dgos pa ston pa'i gsung rab kyi dgongs pa yin/ khyod ji ltar ci la yang mi bsam zer
ba de ni/ so sor rtog pa'i shes rab spangs pa yin no/ /yang dag pa'i ye shes rtsa ba ni/ so sor rtog pa'i shes rab yin pas/ de spangs pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab
kyang spangs pa yin no/ /so sor rtog pa'i shes rab med pas rnal 'byor pa gang gis kyang rnam par mi rtog pa la gnas/ gal te chos thams cad dran pa med cing yid la byas
pa med yin no snyam na nyams su myong ba thams cad mi dran zhing yid la bya ba mi nus so/ /gal te babadag gis chos dran par mi bya'o/ /de shin tu dran pas yid la byas par
'gyur ro/ /dran pa dang yid la bya ba med pas btsan po la bya ba yin pa skad du byas nas/ de gnyis dpyad dgos te/ med pa ni rung mi rung / dran pa tsam med pa tsam gyis
rnam par mi rtog par 'gyur na/ brgyal ba'am 'gog pa'i dus na dran pa med de/ de mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin du 'gyur ram yang dag pa'i so sor rtog pa med par/ rnam par mi
rtog pa 'jug pa ni thabs med do/ /dran pa tsam po bkag kyang so sor yang dag pa'i rtog pa med na/ chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa la ji ltar 'jug nus/ stong pa nyid ma
spangs par sgrib pa spangs par mi 'gyur ba de kho na'o/ /btang snyoms kyi stong pa nyid ni gnyid log pa dang 'dra 'o/ /de bas na yang dag pa'i so sor rtog pa'i shes rab
kyis phyin ci log gi snang ba rgyang bsrings pa yin no/ /des na dran bzhin du mi dran pa byar mi rung ngo / /dran pa yid la bya ba med par/ sngon gnas rjes su dran pa dang
/ thams cad mkhyen par mi ltar 'gyur/ nyon mongs pa yang ji ltar spongs/ de bas na yang dag pa'i shes rab

kyi don nges par rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas/ dus gsum phyi nang thams cad stong par rtogs pa yis/ rtog pa nye bar zhi nas lta ba ngan pa thams cad spangs te/ de bstan nas thabs
dang shes rab la mkhas pa/ sgrib pa thams cad bsal nas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad thob par 'gyur ba yin/ zhes gsungs so/ /yang a tsarya ka ma la shI las/ khyed kyi
dpe don gnyis ka mi 'thad pas/ thog mar dpe mi 'thad de/ khyung nam mkha' la glo bur du 'dab gshog rdzogs par skyes nas shing rtser babs sam/ brag la sogs par skyes nas
rim gyis 'dab gshog rdzogs par byas nas babs/ dang po ni mi srid la gnyis pa ni rim gyis pa'i dper rung gis/ de la mkhan pos dpe'i lan ma thebs pa dang / der atsaryas khyed
kyi dpe de nor bar ma zad don yang 'khrul te/ rnam par mi rtog mi sgom pa de ci/ rnam rtog phyogs gcig bkag pa tsam yin nam/ rnam rtog mtha' dag bkag dgos/ phyogs gcig
bkag pa yin zhe na/ gnyid dang brgyal ba'ang rnam par mi rtog par thal/ rtog pa phyogs gcig tsam yod pa'i phyir ro/ /rnam rtog mtha' dag bkag pa yin no zhe na/ de ltar
na/ khyed rnam par mi rtog pa sgom pa'i tshe/ sgom snyam pa'i rtog pa sngon du gtong dgos sam mi dgos/ mi dgos na khams gsum gyi sems can la'ang sgom skye bar thal/ sgom
snyam pa'i rtog pa sngon du ma btang yang sgom skye ba'i phyir ro/ /mi rtog pa sgom snyam pa'i rtog pa sngon du dgos na/ mi rtog pa sgom pa'i dam bca' nyams te/ dper na
smra bcad byas pas/ smra bcad shor ba dang / ku co ma byed yang yang brjod pas ku cor song ba bzhin no/ zhes bya ba la sogs pa/ rigs dang lung gis lan btab pas/ rgya'i mkhan
pos lan ci yang mi gsung bar gyur to/ /yang rgyal pos lan yod na gsungs shig ces pa dang / rgya'i mkhan po'i zhal nas/ snga ma brjod pa las lhag pa'i lan ci yang med
do/ /gsungs so/ /btsan po'i zhal nas khyed ston rtsen shags gang bzang ba'i 'khor kun gyis kyang lan mchid shags thob cig ces bka' bstsal pa dang / dpal dbyangs kyis mchid
nas/ rgya'i lta bar cig car 'jug cing rim gyis sbyong du ma mchis na pha rol tu phyin pa drug 'dzin pas ma chags pa'i slad du/ sbyin par ming btags kyi/ chags pa btang
yongs su 'dzin pa med pas sbyin pa btang ba yin no/ /sgo gsum chags sdang spangs na tshul khrims yin/ khro ba med na bzod pa'i sa mchog lags/ le lo dor ba la brtson 'grus
su ming btags/ sems la g.yengs pa ma mchis na bsam gtan/ chos spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid shes pa shes rab yin/ ston pa 'das nas rang bzhin du lta ba mi mthun pa ma mchis/
slad nas dbu sde rnam pa gsum ma mthun te/ ston min cig car du 'jug mchis te/ ma 'tshal ma rtogs pas de ltar gyur/ 'jug sgo tha dad kyang sangs rgyas bar gcig 'bras
bu'ang gcig ces kyang / don gyis mi mthun skad du smras/ ye shes dbang pos smras pa/ cig car 'jug bya ba dang rim gyis 'jug bya ba gnyis dpyad dgos te/ rim gyis 'jug na rgyu
ma mchis na nged dang mi 'dra/ cig car 'jug na da rung ci byed dang po nas sangs rgyas na ci nyes/ des na ri la 'dzeg pa la yang gom pa re res 'dzeg dgos te/ gom pa gcig
gis bgrod mi nus pa ltar/ sa dang po thob pa yang dka' na/ thams cad mkhyen pa la lta ci smos/ khyed la lung

bstan pa'i khungs dgos/ ston rtsen mi 'dra ste/ nged rtse min pa gsung rab kun gyi don kun bslabs/ shes rab rnam pa gsum la brten nas don ma nor bar shes/ chos spyod bcu la
bslabs/ sgom pas sa dang po la bzod pa thob/ yang dag par skyon med par yang 'jug ste/ de nas sa dgu yang dag par rim par sbyangs/ pha rol tu phyin pa bcu la bslabs/ brgyud
sbyangs tshogs gnyis rdzogs nas sangs rgyas brnyes pa lags na/ khyed ltar na tshogs ma bsags/ blo ma sbyangs par 'jig rten gyi bya ba yang mi shes na thams cad mkhyen
pa'i rigs dang shes bya thams cad la 'jug par ji ltar 'gyur/ ji ltar tshogs yang ma bsags ci yang ma byas na gum nas zan yang ma myong par ltogs te mchis na/ sangs rgyas
rang bzhin gyis don phun sum tshogs pa/ de'i rgyu ci las grub/ stong pa gcig pus rang la rang mi phan/ gzhan gyi don lta ga la 'grub/ khungs med cing thabs shes ya bral
ba'i chos kyis sangs rgyas skur te bslus pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i ni sems can gyi don du sems bskyed nas 'gro ba'i don lhur byas nas tshogs bsags te/ thabs mkhas par
bslabs nas shes rab rnam gsum la blo sbyangs/ ye shes tshogs bsags sgrib gnyis sbyangs glo bur gyi dri ma thams cad spangs nas sangs rgyas te/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas
kyi sa la dgod par mdzad pa'i 'phrin las 'khor ba ma stongs bar du lhun gyis grub pa yin pa lung du ma nas gsungs/ ci la yang mi sems pa ni bya'i sgo nga dang 'dra'o/
ma brtags par gom bor yang grag snyam ste/ chos ga la rtogs/ des na mdo sde'i don khong chud par bslabs shing / zhi gnas dang lhag mthong dben par yid la byed/ rang la
myong ba dang rtogs pa shar/ de ltar ma rtogs pa'i don du tshogs bsags shing / sems ci lta bur sgyu ma lta bu ste don dam par de ma skyes te med par ma rtogs/ chos thams
cad chu shing gi snying po lta bur ma bcos par rtogs na dus gsum du mi dmigs par 'gyur te/ chos dang gang zag la bdag ma mchis te/ bying rgod ma mchis par zung sbrel du 'jug
pa lags te/ sgom pa la de ltar lags zhes mchis pa dang / ston min pas rim gyis theg pa la shags lan smra bar ma nus te/ spobs pa lan med gyur nas me tog gtor nas pham
blangs so/ /rtsod pa chos phyogs su 'dum par byas so/ /de nas btsan po'i zhal nas don la mi mthun pa tsam mi 'dug ste/ lam sbyong lugs la ha shang gi chos cig car du 'jug
mchis pa de/ dbang po yang rab sbyangs pa can gyi lam yin la/ dbang po 'bring man chad chos spyod bcu la skyon bkal/ sems ni bying / tshogs ni ma bsags/ gzhan gyi blo sbyong
'phro bcad pas chos kyang nub par gyur pas/ 'phro chod la khyed rang yang sgoms shig da phyin chad lta ba ni na ga dzu na'i lta ba bzung / spyod pa pha rol du phyin
pa drug la gyis/ chos spyod bcu nyams su longs/ sgom pa shes rab gsum gyi blo sbyongs/ thabs dang shes rab zung du 'brel bar gyis la sgoms/ da phyin nga'i bod 'bangs rje
blon gang gis kyang chos byed par 'dod pa rnams kyis bod mtha' 'khob tu gyur pa dang / rig pa blun zhing rang kha mang ste/ chos rtog par dka' zhing zab par gyur pas/ rgya
gar gyi mkhas par rab tu grags pa rgyal pos spyan drangs te/ lo tsA mkhas pas gtan la phab pa de la 'jug par

bya'o/ /zhes gsungs nas bka' nan du bstsal to/ /bod khams kun la dril bsgrags so/ /cig car 'jug pa'i dpe cha rnams bsdus te/ bsam yas su gter du sbas so/ /de nas rgya nag gi
mkhan po ha shang ma hA ya nas mi g.yo bsam gtan gling du lha khang gcig bzhengs nas/ gtsan pos kyang 'bul ba mang po mdzad/ ha shang yang mnyes so/ /da rgya gar gyi yul
du 'gro gsungs nas rdo rje gdan du gshegs so/ /de la/ la la na re/ mkhan po yi mug pas rang gi gnas su song ngo / /lham ya gcig lus pas/ ma 'ongs pa na nga'i bstan pa lham
tsam yong zhes 'khor la lung bstan pa dang / kha cig na re/ mkhan po mgo la mar me spar te nub bde ba can du kha bltas nas 'das pa dang / nye gnas pas dbang po brdungs
te lcibs so zer ba dang / rdzun gtan mang po bsgrags pa byung ste de ltar ma yin no/ /der matsan po'i thugs dgongs kyang grub ste/ tshong 'dus su bad rngam pa'i lha khang
bzhengs te dga' ston mdzad pa'i dus su bod 'bangs thams cad 'tshogs pa dang / kun chos la gzud cing chos mi bya mi rung ba'i phyir/ dbus mtha' thams cad du slob dpon bskos/
zhang blon gyi bu tsha dang / btsun mo srid ma zin pa kun ka ba li re thogs nas chos slob tu bcug sems lan gsum gyi bar du slob dpon ka ma la shI la la chos thams cad
thos bsam gyis bdag med par gtan la 'bebs pa'i tshe de ji ltar lags pa gcig yi ger bkod par zhu zhes zhus pa la/ sgom rim dang po brtsams nas gnang ba/ btsan pos gzigs
pas de'i don gdan gcig gi thog tu sgom na ji ltar sgom zhus pas/ sgom rim bar ma brtsams nas gnang / de ltar bsgoms pas 'bras bu ji ltar mchis zhus pas/ sgom rim phyi ma
brtsams nas 'bras bu bstan pa'i zor la/ ha shang gi lta grub de zhor la dbu ma'i don de sgoms gsungs/ de la shin tu dgyes nas de'i don 'grel du ka ma la shI las bo dhi sa
twa'i dgongs pa la/ rgol ba byung gis dogs nas lung dang rigs par 'brel bar dbu ma snang ba brtsams nas gnang ngo / /de nas rgyal pos a tsarya nyer gcig ha shang gi mi
lnga byams pa gling du dar zab kyi khri sgor mor bshams te bzhugs so/ /mchos pa dang bsnyen bkur mang du phul/ rang rang gi yul du gshegs pa rnams la yang / yin po che gser
dngul mang po'i rdzongs mdzad do/ /de nas chos dpon re la lo re la nas khal bdun cu rtsa lnga / na bza' dgu phyug re re/ spod mar srang stong gcig brgya/ chibs 'og theg
rta re/ shog bu deb bcu bzhi/ snag tsha yug gsum/ lan tshwa zad med/ mchims pha'i sgom chen nyi shu rtsa lnga la/ nas khal lnga bcu rtsa lnga / spod mar srang brgyad brgya
re/ na bza' drug phrug re/ mtshams kyi ban de rang kha ma rnams la/ nas khal brgyad brgyad/ shog deb gnyis re/ snag tsha yug re/ slob dpon gyi gnyer pa nyi shu rtsa lnga
la nas khal nyi shu rtsa lnga lnga / gos sum phrug re re/ thos bsam dang dge ba nyams dang dpags nas byed pa rnams la zan dang chod ma'i tshul rgyun du gnang / yon bdag
pho mo nya ma chos nyan rnams la yang dus dus su dga' ston/ bza' mgron gyi bya dga' yang rgyun du gnang nas/ lha chos dar bar byas pas rje bka' drin che ba lags/ /de nas
btsan pos snga 'gyur dag par byed pa'i 'phror lus pa la tugs ma tshim nas paNDi ta mkhas pa btsal bar bya

dgongs pa dang / nub mo sgra sgyur gyi khang par ka ma la shI la mu stegs kyis gshed ma btang bas gzim lam du mkhal ma mnyes nas bkrongs kyang zer te/ de ni g.yog po gser gnyer
ba rgya gar dha na shrI bya bas bsad pa yin no/ /de'i skabs la ye shes dbang pos 'bras chan gsol nas/ de phyin chad khams kyi zas spangs nas ting nge 'dzin gyi zas dang
brje bar bya'o gsungs nas grongs pa'i dus su nam mkha' las sgra dang 'od byung / gdung khang has po ri'i rtser brtsigs na legs bya ba'i sgra byung ngo / /thams cad gdung
ba'i skad bton/ ye shes dbang po'i bu mo byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa zhig gis pha'i mchod rten brtsig pa'i sa klus bstan/ mchod rten de la lha mo
gsum gyis skor ba gyis zer ba dang / btsan po'i zhal nas bo dhi sa twa'i gsung dang sbyar na/ kho bo tshe yun ring po mi thub gsungs nas rje thugs las chung ba las gzhol
bar bzhed nas sgom mdzad par dgongs nas sras mu ne btsan po/ mu tig btsan po/ gcung khri lde btsan dang gsum mnga' ba las/ sras mu ne btsan po la chab srid 'bogs par bzhed
de/ blon po zhang bu ri btsan la bsko bar dgongs pas rgyal po yab sras dang / blon po zhang rgya tsha lha snang / bu 'u ring btsan pa dang / rgyal blon gsum dbu rtse'i
bar khang gi rnga khang na 'tshogs pa yum me tog sgrol gyis mthong nas/ thugs gtum pas dogs 'tshal nas chab srid sna nam pa la ster nges snyam/ mu tig btsan po la smrar
bcug lha sras kyis 'u ring sgo bar du btsir nas chu gris bkum/ yab na re/ 'u ring gar song gsungs pas/ 'u ring rgyang ring por song zer nas gri khrag can bor nas bar khang
du bros/ der rje'i thugs dam yang 'gyangs nas g.yar mchu byung dogs te/ blon po mdzangs pa kun gros byas nas blon po 'gos dpal 'gar gung btsan bya ba blon po 'gos kyis
zhal lce dga' gsum du bcad/ chad srid mu ne btsan po la mnga' bar gyis/ thun tshags su dkar dmar mdzad nas gtad/ sna nam pa dga' bar stong bcal/ lha sras la mi sha mi blang
bar byas nas/ yab zung mkhar du sgom du gshegs/ btsan pos bka' gtsigs kyi yi ge gsum mdzad nas gcig lha sa na yod/ gcig khams su khyer/ gcig rje'i phyag sbal na mchis
te/ bse'i sgrom bur bcug kha la sgo lcags brgyabs nas gnod sbyin rgya dam nag po la gtad/ che long gcig zhang blon rnams la yang dar bar byas so/ /dbang phyug phun sum tshogs
pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po khri srong lde btsan gyis/ grong khyer thams cad du gtsug lag khang dang gnas gzhi btsugs/ dben sa ru sgrub khang byas/ lcags ri brgya
rtsa brgyad kyi mchod rten gyis bskor/ mi thams cad tshogs gsog pa dang / bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa la bkod/ spyod lam thams cad chos spyod/ lugs thams cad chos lugs/ so
nam thams cad chos dang mthun par byed du bcug bod 'bangs thams cad bde skyid la sbyar/ sems can thams cad bde ba la bkod nas/ rtags dang yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa
byung ste/ drug cu rtsa drug la dgung la gshegs nas/ mchad pa yar lung sgyer pa sar bang so'i khrod du brtsigs nas lha mi la sbyin gtong rgya chen byas so/ /de nas mu ne
btsan po dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga lon tsa na/ jo mo ru yongs bza' rgyal mo khab tu bzhes te rgyal srid gtad

nas/ chab srid rgya che bas yab kyi zhal chems dkar dmar dang mthun par 'bangs kyi tshis bgyid par dgongs nas/ bla'i mchod gnas rab tu byung ba'i mnga' thang dang / chos 'khor
stod smad kyi zhabs thog yab kyi srol bzhin dung mdzad/ rgyal po de'i sku ring la/ yi ge mkhan po tshe spongs byang chub ces bya ba byung ste/ rje la yi ge'i stangs phul
pas/ sbur nag bal gyis btums pa 'dra ba gcig byung / rje'i dbu rten gyi 'og tu sbas te bsnams nas mdo khams smad du spyugs te/ khams yig tu grags so/ /brag dmar bsams
yas lhun gyis grub pa'i lha khang du/ sangs rgyas kyi dus mchod chen po bzhi btsugs te/ bod kyi rje blon yongs kyi 'phral gyi rkyen bzlog pa dang / yun gyi tshogs gsog pa'i
sa mdzad/ mchod rten chen po bzhi'i gzugs dang / dbu rtse'i bya 'dab lcags thag gis sbrel nas nam mkha' la dar po che dang 'phan gyis bres/ sa gzhi man ji gling gi mdangs
dang / gser dngul gyi phor pas bkang / dbu rtse'i thang mchod rdzas kyis khengs par bgyis nas/ bla'i mchod gnas rab tu byung ba rnams kyis mdo chog mang po mdzad/ sngags
btsun rnams kyis rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas/ mchod pa phun sum tshogs pa phul/ lcags ri'i byang ngos kyi phyogs bzhi nas 'bangs rgyan dang bcas pa
mchod rdzas dang bcas te rtse bro sna tshogs byed/ gar dang / seng ge dang / 'bag dang / rgya rta dang / glu dang / gzhas dang / shon dang / bro byed/ la la rta rgyug 'phongs
dang / tshabs dang / kha tshon smra'o/ /btsan pos dbu rtse'i sgo khang nas/ seng ge'i khri steng nas mchod pa phul bas thugs dad pa skyes nas dbu thod dang dar zab
kyi na bza' phud nas lha la 'bul/ de nas btsan po'i zhal nas/ nga'i yab kyi thugs dam gyi lha khang la/ khyed bod 'bangs thams cad kyis go ru dang mtshon cha ma gtogs pa
dad gus ka?s mchod pa'i rdzas phul cig gsungs nas bka' bstsal/ 'bangs thams cad kyis rje'i bka' bzhin du bzhin du mchod rdzas mang po phul bas/ kha cig gis g.yu dang / ber/
gser dngul zangs lcags/ dar zab sna tshogs kyi gos/ kha cig med pos kyang ras slog dang gos zas gang yod 'bul ba phul bas/ mchod rdzas kyi phung po chen po rnams dkon
gnyer ba bskos pa kun gyis bsdus nas mchod pa byed do/ /rgyu bzang ngan byung bas btsan po'i zhal nas khyed 'bangs rnams dad pa che chung khyad par re che ba la las gser
dngul 'bul nus/ la las ras slog dang gos hrul las 'bul mi nus pa gsungs pas/ mi ltogs phongs pa kun na re/ rje gcig lags/ ngos cag dad pa chung ba ma lags te/ yod pa gser
dngul/ med po dbul rgyu de las ma 'byor/ dbul rgyu che ba kun longs spyod che ba lags so/ /zhes snyan du gsol bas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ kye ma nga'i mnga' ris su/ la las
zas skom tsam yang ma 'byor/ la las lhag pa dang bcas 'di mi rigs pas gsungs nas/ ru bzhi phyogs phyogs su las pa dang / pho nya khrims sdom pa btang nas/ bkres phyug med
par phyug ltogs yo byad thams cad mnyam por bgos nas snyoms por byas so/ /de nas mngon par byang chub pa'i zla ba'i sa ga nam mthong che chung sa ri (sa ga sa ri nam mthong
che chung la) 'dul ba'i mchod pa bgyid de/ zhing pa kun thong po bor nas rmon pa dang rol du thong gshol

ldem me bzhag nas mchod pa la yong ngo / /lha sa dang bsam yas kyis chog zer/ de dus su sngar bzhin mchod rdzas phul ba la dngos po bzang ngan byung bas/ yang bkres po dang
phyug po nor lan gcig bsnyams so/ /de tshul 'dzugs kyi zla ba la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas/ mdo sde'i mchod pa bgyis te zhing pa kun yur ma'i gral bshig nas/ sngo snod
rdos mnan nas mchod pa byed du 'ongs pas yur ma chag zer ro/ /yang sngar bzhin mchod rdzas la bzang ngan byung bas yang bkres phyug lan gcig bsnyams so/ /de nas ston zla
tha chung cho 'phrul rta'i zla ba la/ chos 'phrul chung ba zer te/ mngon pa'i mchod pa bgyis te/ yang mchod rdzas la bzang ngan byung bas/ sems can rang rang so so'i bsags
rgyab tu mkhyen te dgongs nas/ bod khams su ltogs phyug lan gsum bsnyams/ sa 'tsho ba dang mgron du rgyu ba dang kun la rgyags phye lam du skyel mi dgos/ bla nas sbyar
ro/ /sems can gyi srog gcod pa dang / rku ba la sogs pas 'tsho ba sgrub mi dgos par bod bde ba la bkod pas/ sras mu ne btsan po'i sku drin che ba lags so/ /de nas pho yongs
bza' rgyal mo btsun yab rgyal po'i thugs la 'dogs pas yab 'da' khar pho yongs bza' lha sras kyis khab tu bzhais shig ces bka' bstsal pas/ lha sras gsum la tshe spongs
bza' me tog sgrol ma rangs te/ yab sku gshegs pa'-i 'og tu/ tshe spongs bzas/ pho yongs bza' 'grong bar bya bsam pas/ pho yongs bza' skra gsar bgyis nas rgyan ma thogs par
gda' ba de la snyad byas nas/ ral gri rdeg snyam pa dang / sras mu ne btsan pos g.yon bskor nas/ yum tshe spongs bza' glo ba la gcags pas blon po te gu ste chung bya ba
phyag tshang du bskos nas pho brang yum bu mkhar du sras la kha zas ngan pa drangs te/ lha sras mu ne btsan pos rgyal srid zla ba bcu gnyis mdzad nas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa
bdun pa la sku 'das so/ /bang so skye'u ldem bur brtsigs/ tshe spongs bzas pho yongs bza' la mu ne btsan po'i ral gri btsal nas nyin re la shags sgo re btab cing sen
mos sha srang re bcad cing dkrongs so/ /de nas mu tig btsan po mon na spyugs te yod pa khong la dbang bskur bar chad byas te spyan drangs pa dang / sna nam pas 'di byed na
zer te/ mu tig btsan po'i brang kha phye nas dkrongs so/ bang so rgya bo zang zang du brtsigs so/ /de nas 'bangs yongs bgros bgyis te/ gcung po khri lde btsan dbang bskur
bar byas te/ kha cig na re/ rgyal bu nar ma son 'bangs kyi tshis mu yong / de bas lan gcig la blon po mdzangs pa gcig bskos te/ khrims bu chung bca' 'o zer/ kha cig na
re/ de mi yong / sngon yang mes ag tshom 'ongs pa'i dus su/ rgyal bu nar ma son nas/ zhang blon gsum la khrims gtad nas khrims bu chung byas nas lha chos bsnubs pas bod
phung bar byas/ gyod kha chen po la gtugs pas da rgyal por rab dbang bskur te blon po mdzangs pa bskos nas 'bangs cos dang mthun par bskyangs pa legs zer bas/ rgyal bu yong
ngam mi yong sad par kha 'chams nas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi la rgyal sar dbang bskur nas srid gtad pas sad pa bzhin legs par byung nas/ rgyal po sad na legs bya ba
'jing pa yo la sku dbang che bas bla dwags sad na legs 'jing yon zhes grags/ rgyal po de'i sku ring la yi ge'i

mkhan po 'bri yon tan zhes bya ba byung ste/ rje la yi ge stangs su phul bas/ nya rting dkar chu nas bton pa 'dra ba zhig byung ste/ gung blon rnams kyi g.yar dam du bzang
bzang rjes rtsis dang bsnyen bkur ba ni/ dbu ston/ gzhung ston/ tha ston/ za srung / zla ston/ skra 'khrud chu ston/ za 'degs/ bya dga'i ston mo dpag tu med do/ /rgyal bu
de na tshod du son nas/ btsun mo pho yongs bza' lha btsun bya ba dang / 'bro bza' mang po lha rgyal khab tu bzhes te/ 'bro khri bzung blon por bskos te/ rgyal po de'i zhal
nas/ 'dzam bu gling na rgyal po che/ bod kyi rgyal po la nga che bas/ nga lag ris lha khang nyi ma rgya ji tsam yod dris pas/ nyi ma la dpag tshad lnga bcu tsam yod pas/
bod kyi sa gzhi la mi shong gsungs pas/ 'o na zla ba tsam zhig byed do gsungs/ skar dga'i ltas la ni/ nabs so la sogs pa'i skar ma che ba rnams dpag tshad gnyis so/ /skar
phran rnams la rgyang grags te/ grangs ni dung phyur gnyis/ bye ba phrag brgyad/ sa ya phrag lnga'o zhes so/ /byang 'brog yangs par rtsig go gsungs so/ /blon po kun gyis
mchid nas/ bla blon kun gyis longs spyod dbus su byed pas/ byang du brtsigs na lha khang stong par lus so zhes gsol bas/ 'o na nyang ror rtsig go gsungs pas/ de yang
thugs gcig byed par brtsigs phul/ rgyal sder skar chung tsam zhig rtsig par chad byas nas/ skar chung rdo rje dbyings kyi lha khang bzhengs su gsol lo/ /rgyang grags gcig
yod pa de rmang brus pa dang / bzo bo rnams kyis khengs dregs byas te/ rtsig pa mkhan po na re/ nga'i rtsig pa med na gang yang byar mi gtub pas nga gtso che zer/ lder bzo
mkhan po na re/ nga'i lha bzo med na de dag gang byas kyang lha khang mi 'byung bas nga gtso che zer nas/ dang po ko ba btsos nas lder bzo 'phrul 'khor du bzhengs su gsol/
de nas ka ba btsugs bskor bas rgya phigs bkal/ de nas phyi tha la rtsig pa bgyis pas gtsug lag khang khyad par 'phags pa grub pa lags/ rgyal po des yab mes kyis srol
kha ma shor bar mdzad do/ yab mes kyi thugs dam kun zhig ral gso ba dang / rgyan btags pa dang / mchod pa 'bul ba dang / lha sa'i khyams phra mo bzhengs pa la sogs pa phyag
rjes mang po mdzad do/ /rab tu byung ba'i mnga' thang bstod/ me pho khyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ lo sum cu rtsa gcig rgyal po mdzad/ 'bangs chab srid chos bzhin bskyangs/
lnga bcu rtsa bzhi me bya la dgung du gshegs pa'i rgyal po de bod la bka' drin che ba lags so/ /rgyal po de la lha sras lnga byung ste/ khri gtsug lde ral pa can/ lha sras
gtsang ma/ khri dar ma 'u dam btsan/ lha rje lhun grub/ khri chen 'de'u dang lnga 'khrungs so/ /de la gcen gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rja'i sprul pa khri gtsug lde
btsan mnga' bdag ral pa can/ chu mo 'brug la 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gnyis lon pa dang / me bya'i lo la rgyal sar btod/ dbang bskur nas chab srid gtad do/ /cog lo bza' dpal
gyi ngang tshul ma dang / mchims bza' khyung dkar ma dang / sna nam bza' a rje pho legs/ tshe spong bza' lhun gyi bu mo/ lha lung bza' me tog ma dang lnga khab tu bzhes
so/ /sbas mang rje lha 'od kyis blon po byas/ ban chen po dpal gyi yon tan gyis

chos kyi blon po bgyis te/ mes kyi bad rngam pa'i lha khang la dpe bgyis te/ thugs dam gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i dus su/ rgyal po de'i sku ring la/ gra shod gnyis bya
ba yi ge'i mkhan po gnyis byung ste/ rje la yi ge'i stangs phul bas/ seng ge gnam mchongs 'dra ba dang / mu tig bstar la rgyus pa 'dra ba gcig byung ste/ rje sa bdag rgyal
po'i thugs dam 'bri bar bzang bas/ zha'i gtsigs kyi rdo ring gi 'gram du yi ge'i dpe gcig btab nas bzhag gser yig ni dge rgyas bye ma gling gi bzang po spyod pa dang
/ yer pa'i phung po gsum pa'i mdo/ mdo sna bzhugs pa'i gser 'bum de rnams 'bri ba'i dus su rjes rtsis gnang ba ni/ bsu ba zhu rten/ gdan g.yas gral/ gtang rag gi 'bul ba
bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang / rtsi sar zhing dor gcig skyo rogs su rtsed 'jo sna tshogs pa gnang ngo / /bod yul du gsung rab mang du bris shig ces bka' bstsal to/ /de nas
rje'i zhal nas yab mes kun gyi ring la btsan po la bya ba gsum yod de/ thugs dam gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa dang / bod 'bangs bde ba la bkod pa dang / sku'i dgra la
dmag drangs pa'o/ /gong ma rnams kyis la las re re tsam mdzad/ la las gnyis gnyis tsam mdzad/ yang rim pas mdzad de/ ngas gsum dus gcig tu byed do/ /zhes bka' bstsal nas/
thugs dam gyi gtsug lag khang gi rmang 'ding bar byed tsa na/ rje'i zhal nas/ lha sa mkhar dang 'dra/ bsam yas grod dang 'dra/ skar chung mchad pa dang 'dra/ nga lha khang
gsha' ma zhig byed gsungs nas bka' bstsal pa dang / rgya dkar po/ nag po/ li yul/ kha che/ bal po/ bod yul gyi bzo bo mkhas pa thams cad bkug ste/ rgya nag gi ju zhag
mkhas pa zhig gis sa btsal/ 'on kyang rdo'i bzo bo mkhas pa zhig li'i yul du lcang ra smug po na li rje la yod pa thos nas/ gla ba gcig bzung nas lcags kyi dra bar bcug nas/
bod kyi btsan po'i spos kyi glang po yin pas 'di bzhes la li yul spyod pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba bzo bo mkhas pa gcig yod zer bas/ de bod kyi btsan po'i thugs dam lha
khang gi bzo bo byed pa la gnang bar zhu bya ba dang / de ma gnang na rgyal po thugs khros nas dmag 'dren no bya ba'i bka' shog gi sgrom bu bskur nas pho nya ba btang /
pho nya bas li rje la bka' shog gi sgrog bu phul bas/ li rjes bka' shog gi sgrom bu gzigs pas spos kyi glang po'i ril ma tshur bcad/ spos kyi dri snom pa byung bas zhu rten
la yang mnyes/ btsan po'i bka' la ma nyan na/ dmag yong ba la yang 'jigs nas/ bka' shog sgrom bu na ji ltar yod pa bzhin brdzang bar chad nas/ li yul spyod pa'i rgyal
po la bod yul du mchi 'tshal bar bsgo bas/ ngos rgas pas nga'i bu gsum btsan po'i phyag tu 'bul lo zhes pas/ li rje na re/ khyod dang btsan po g.yar ma mjal na/ li yul du
btsan po'i dmag yong bas/ sngon yang rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i rta dmag drangs nas li yul phung / cham la phab zer bas khyod li yul spyod pa'i rgyal po lam du gum yang
mgo bo btsan po'i phyag tu phul zhing / bu l-i gser gzungs/ gser 'od/ gser thog gsum ni lha bzo ba'i mkhas pa'i mchog yin pas bod du bzo byed du rdzongs/ pho nya ba la
skyes bskur nas 'ongs/ zhes smras/ der li yul spyod pa'i rgyal po yang ma gum par btsan po dang zhal mjal te/

rgyal po mnyes so/ /de nas 'dzam bu'i gling na rdo bzo la mkhas pa'i bal po rdo mkhan la sogs pas bzo bgyis te/ 'og khang gsum sgo re bzhi man chad rdo la byas pa'i rdo khyad
par 'phags pa byung ste/ de'i phud la ra sa'i gtsug lag khang du/ mes kyis chos kyi srol btod pas bka' drin che bas rdo ring phul lo/ /ri mo'i phud du dar la bris pa'i
ma dpe 'bum brgya rtsa brgyad phul/ lder tsho'i phud la lha tshangs pa dang / brgya byin gnyis bzhengs nas phul lo/ /lugs ma'i phud la cong chen po dril bu'i tshul du btags
nas phul/ bar khang lha khang gsum po so phag las byas/ steng lha khang gsum shing dang ko ba dang zangs ma la byas/ rgya phibs kyi 'og tu rlung gi 'khor lo bskor te/
rab tu byung ba mang po skor ba rgyun du byed do/ /bya 'dab la phyogs bzhir lcags thag bzhi mchod rten chen po bzhi la brtod/ rlung chen po nub nas byung ba'i tshe/ shar
gyi lcags thag lhod tsam song ba dang / rgya phibs shar du yo tsam 'gro/ rlung shar nas g.yo tsa na/ nub kyi lcags thag lhod tsam song bas/ rgya phibs cung zad nub tu yo
tsam 'gro/ ri nag gi rtse la na bun byung ba dang / lha khang gi khyung mgo la yang na bun thul le yong ba'i mthon po zhig ngan song sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor du bzhengs su
gsol lo/ /bya 'dab dgu brtsegs la sogs pa yab mes kun gyi lha khang las lhag pa/ bzo sna bcu gnyis kyis khyad par 'phags pa/ ngo mtshar du gyur pas sna drangs pa'i 'gur
mo dang / gang ngar dang / btsan thang dang / nyang ro/ rtsibs kyi lha khang khrab sgo can gyis kha bskangs nas bzhengs so/ /de dag gi dge bsgos su 'os pa rnams la gnyer
bsgos nas/ bsnyen bkur dang gnang sbyin che thang du mdzad/ btsun mo rnams la srid byung ba chu sman gyis khyer nas/ sras rgyal bu mi mnga' yang / 'bangs bde ba la bkod
pa/ zas dang gos tsam gyi bde ba ni 'phral gyi bde bar gsal/ dus yun gyi bde ba ni lha chos la bkod pa'i phyir/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' gsung rab thams cad gzigs pas/ chos
pa la la ni rgya dkar po'i skad/ la la ni rgya nag po'i skad/ la la ni bal po'i skad/ la la ni o rgyan gyi skad chos smra ba/ mes kyi lha dang chos skad sna tshogs su
'byung ba 'di slob dka' bas ma legs pas/ sangs rgyas rgya gar du byon nas chos rgya gar du gsungs pa yin pas/ da yang rgya gar gyi skad du/ gzhan gyi skad rigs kun bsgyur
nas rgya gar gyi skad yug gcig tu 'gyur ba byed ces bka' bstsal nas/ bod phrug blo rno ba sum cu tham pa la gser mang po brdzangs nas/ rgya gar du lo tsA slob tu btang bas
la la sgra ma shes/ la la tshad pas gum ste don ma 'grub po/ de nas btsan po/ khri srong lde btsan sku tshe'i smad la byon pa 'bro ka ba dpag brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i rgyal
mtshan/ sna nam gyi ye shes sde gsum la bka' bstsal nas 'gyur skyon thams cad bsal te/ ma 'gyur ba dang / ma grags pa gnyis/ 'gyur chad pa dang lhag pa gnyis/ 'gyur log
pa dang 'gyur 'khrugs pa gnyis/ 'gyur dman dang 'gyur gcong gnyis te/ 'gyur skyod brgyad kyi cha cung zad kyang med par byas nas 'gyur thams cad dag par byas/ rgya gar
nyi 'og gi mkhan po atsarya/ kha che'i paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / su ren dra bo dhi dang / bIrya ka ra pra

bha de dang / dhAn shI la dang bzhi spyan drangs te/ gtan la phab nas/ sngar gyi bsgyur ba rnams ni mi nyams par bya ba dang / phyis 'gyur slob pa rnams la phan pa'i yan lag
tu/ thig par rta che chung dang / bka' bcad dang / dkar chag gi yi ge gsum yang mdzad do/ /lo paN bgres po de rnams la sgra bsgyur rgya gar gyi gling du cha rkyen bla nas
sbyar te/ mes kyi lha khang na bzhugs pa dang / bod yul na bzhugs pa'i gsung rab ma lus pa rnams spyan drangs te/ sngar 'gyur ba rnams la yang / ston pa dang 'khor gyi
tshogs la zhe sa gzhug par 'os pa dang / mi 'os pa'i khyad par bcug ste/ theg pa che chung gi sngar mdo sde so sor yod pa rnams ni mdo mang stabs gcig tu byas/ dkon mchog
brtsegs pa dang / sangs rgyas phal po che dang / mya ngan las 'das pa dang / lang kar gshegs pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ de bzhin gshegs pas klu'i yul du
blo mun pa'i don du gsungs pa'i rgyas pa 'bum/ mi yul du mi dad pa che ba'i don du gsungs pa'i bar pa nyi khri dang / lha'i yul du lha dbang po yang rab kyi don du gsungs
pa'i 'phags pa brgyad stong pa/ sras yum bcu bdun/ shais rab khri pa/ khri brgyad stong pa/ 'phags pa sdud pa/ rdo rje gcod pa/ sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ shes rab snying
po/ yi ge gcig pa la sogs pa gzungs bran bu dang bcas pa thams cad sde tshan du byas sgra bsgyur te/ sgra thams cad rgya gar ba'i 'gyur du bcos so/ /gzhan yang bstan bcos/
'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dbu ma rigs pa'i tshogs rnams dang / de rnams kyi cha lag dang / bstod pa skor la sogs pa dang / de rnams kyi 'grel pa dang / bstan
bcos phra mo mang po dang / mngon pa gong ma dang de'i 'grel pa dang / mngon pa 'og ma/ mdzod rtsa 'grel dang / bstan bcos sde bdun dang / de'i cha lag mang po bsgyur
ro/ /byams pa'i chos lngas gtso byas pa'i byams pa rang dang 'brel ba'i chos nyi shu/ dbyig gnyen gyi rab tu 'byed pa'i sde brgyad/ de rnams kyi rtsa ba 'grel pa/ spyod tshogs
skor gsum/ 'dul ba dang / mdo rtsa'i 'grel pa/ rgya cher 'grel pa/ rang grol las chog la sogs pa cha lag du ma dang / sum brgya pa rtsa ba dang / 'grel pa/ 'od ldan
dang / phra mo rnams dang / bstan bcos che chung mang po bsgyur ro/ /gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud rnams kyang sngar gyi 'gyur legs pa kun sor bzhag skad ma dag pa
rnams legs par bcos/ lo tsA ba rma rin chen mchog gis paNDi ta bi ma la mi tra spyan drangs nas/ sgyu 'phrul gyi skor la/ 'jam dpal sgyu 'phrul dra ba bsgyur/ de nas rnam
snang sgyu 'phrul dra ba bsgyur/ rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba la rtsa rgyud gsang ba snying po/ le lag ye shes bla ma/ sgyu 'phrul bla ma/ lha mo sgyu 'phrul/
brgyad pa/ bzhi bcu pa/ brgyad cu pa/ khyad par gsang snying rtsa rgyud 'phyong par khab lugs bshad dang bcas pa/ dra ba che chung / rgyan dam pa/ 'phrin las sha ra brgyad
man ngag dang shar chung bcu gnyis dang bcas pa bsgyur nas dag par byas so/ /skad gsar bcad kyis gtan la phab nas/ sde snod gsum khri gcig gi steng nas gsung bar byas te/
chos lugs bzang po mdzad/ dkar chag btab nas phyogs phyogs su bsrings so/ /bka' rgya che chung yang yi ger

btab mdzad do/ /tha na bre dang / srang dang / zho la sogs pa rgya dkar po ma ga dha dang bstun nas 'on chang rdo dang / skyid shod sho ma ra gtan la phab/ btsan po dad pa
che bas mdun sa chung ba rab tu byung ba la phul bas/ lo tsA ba kun gyi zhal nas bod 'bangs 'dul dka' bas chad pa la brten dgos/ rab tu byung ba ston pa'i bka' bzhin byed
'tshal bas/ chad pa bgyid mi rung / mdun sa gnang ba mi len zhes gsol bas gsung bzhin mi bgyid pa la ngas zhang blon kun bgyid du bstsal/ chab srid bzhes par zhu zhes gsungs
so/ /thugs dad pas rje'i dbu thod phud/ rab tu byung ba'i gdan du bting / rab tu byung ma thag la zhabs spyi bor len/ gos ngur smrig skye bos gyon pa gzigs na yang phyag
deng mdzad/ dan gyi lcang tshal du bla sgo dang po dge 'dun la phul/ rgya nag po dang / bod yul dang / gzhan yang rje ral pa can gyi mnga' 'og na yod pa rnams la bka'
bstsal nas/ lha khang stong rtsa dang / mchod rten bye ba bzhengs so/ zhang blon gyis snyung phyag gi rten phul nas snyung phyag nyi shu rtsa gcig phul yang lan mi gnang
/ bod yongs la rje'i dpya bsdus nas/ dge 'dun la bla nas 'tsho ba 'bul/ rab tu byung ba re re la yang 'bangs mi khyim bdun bdun lha ris su phul nas na bza' sbyor/ rab byung
gi gos lhan pa can gzigs nas/ de'i lha ris la bris nas bka' drag tu bstsal/ skye bo khyim pa chos la mos pa kun rab tu byung ba'i mdun sa bzhin chos dang bstun pas shin
tu bde zhing skyid par mdzad/ dam pa'i chos dag cing gtsang bar mdzad pa rje bka' drin che ba lags/ de nas sku la bsdo ba dmag drangs nas cham la phab pa ni rgya nag
po dang dbon zhang gnyis bsdum bya bar chad pa ma 'chams nas/ bod ru bzhi nas dmag sde bco brgyad/ blon po chen po zhang khri gzhung rab shags dang / blon mang rje lha lod
la sogs pa dar tshan zhig gis khrid nas rgya'i yul du dmag drangs te/ rgya'i gyen po thams cad bkum nas/ rgya thams cad cham la phab nas/ lces gces mkhar nyi shu rtsa bzhi
yar bcad mnga' 'og tu bsdus/ seng tog mkhar/ gog chu'u/ mi nyag gha lga la sogs mkhar sum cu so bdun tsam brdungs/ snangs mang po bcad/ rnga mong dang / rta dre'u phal
cher phyag tu phul/ mi nyag 'gang sgang dgar skya mor byed dus/ rgyal po rnam thos sras dngos su byung nas/ btsan po la zhu ba zhus pas/ khyed kyis 'dul ba'i dus 'dir nga
la khab gcig zhu gsungs pas mi nyag gha lga byin no/ /de 'dra'i 'dra 'bag rgyal po ral pa can la/ rgyal po rnam sras pus mo btsugs pa'i gzugs kyang yod do/ /de nas rma
chu 'og ma la lcags kyi glang ru phar bcad tshur bcad byas te lcags zam kyang btsugs/ rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar byon dus/ dbus ri'i steng du 'od dang 'od sprin gyi gseb
tu bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal seng ge la bzhugs nas/ rgyal sras khri phrag gis bskor bar gzigs shing / gzhan yang gnam mkha'i ngos kun gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten mang
pos gang bar gzigs so/ /de'i gzugs kyang btsan po rang gis bzhengs pa'i lha khang gi phyi'i ngos la bris nas yod do/ /de dus rgya'i ha shang dang / gyang chung dang / lcang
la bo mang po dang / bod kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams 'dus nas/ khong rnams

kyis bar dang dpang po mdzad nas/ dbon zhang bsdums mdzad do/ /rgya'i gong gu ma rur rme rur rgya'i gtsug lag khang gcig dang / bod kyi gtsug lag khang gcig dang / gnyis bzhengs
su gsol lo/ /gzhan yang lha khang mang po zhig bzhengs te/ de bar du sa la btsan po dbon zhang / gnam la nyi zla las med do bar glegs glengs nas pha bod la nyi zla'i
gzugs byas pa 'di tsong kha mtsho sngon gyi lha shar na yod do/ /gong gu ma rung rme ru yar bcad du rgya'i dmag mi yong ba/ de man chad du bod kyi dmag mi 'dren pa'i mna'
byas so/ /de rgya bod gnyis kyi mtshams yin no/ /dpang por lha gnyan klu gnyan mang po bzhag dbon zhang ji ltar chad byas pa'i rtsis gtsigs kyi yi ge gsum la mchis te
ker shir khri sgo dang / nga sa'i lha khang dang / gong gu ma ru rme ru gsum por rdo ring la bris nas yod do/ /gzhan yang rgya gar/ bal po/ li yul then/ sbal bru sha/ dmang
zhang zhung / hor yul/ sog yul/ yu gur/ ka mi log la sogs pa 'dzam bu'i gling gi rgya mo khyi khyo can/ sog po spre lag can yan chad gling gi gsum gnyis mnga' 'og tu 'dus/
ma rungs pa thams cad kyi mgo bregs nas de thams cad bod kyi rgyal po mnga' bdag ral pa can gyi mnga' 'og tu bsdus so bya ba'i dril chen po phyogs bcu thams cad du bsgrags
so/ /de nas btsan bag pos mdun sa chung ba rab tu byung ba la phul nas chab srid chos dang mthun/ dbang dge 'dun la bskur te phul bas/ blon po nag po la dga' ba kun
dpya mi 'tsham par bsdu ba dang / byi dang rku ba la sogs pa bag med spyod pa shin tu dog par byung bas/ rje'i snyan du zhang blon tshos bskos pa kun sgrub pa la/ dpya
lo thang du bsdus nas dmangs dge 'dun la 'bul ba 'jug lags/ nged rnams kyis snyung phyag nyi su rtsa gcig rten dang bcas pa bgyis kyang bka' lan mi gnang bar dmangs rab tu
byung ba la dgyes bzhin du phyag mdzad pa ci lags zhes pa la sogs pa zhus pa'i lan du/ btsan pos bod 'bangs skya btsun yo bsdus nas rab tu byung ba'i mtha' bstod/ chos
byed par 'dod pa rnams la yang bka' drin chen po gnang / zhang blon rnams la phyag dang / snyung rmed btab ma dgu rtseg can dang / zings po sna tshogs can la sogs rigs mi
'dra ba sna tshogs gnang / mi chos dang lha chos gnyis ka gtan la phab/ ra sa dang / bsam yas dang / skar chung la sogs pa'i yab mes kyis thugs dam bzhengs pa'i 'phro thams
cad kyang ma lus par bzhengs par mdzad do/ /zhig yal thams cad kyang gso ba'i dus der lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi rgyal srid bzung / de la 'bangs nag po la dga' ba rnams kyis
nged 'di tsam du spyod pa dog pa de cis lan zhes gleng bsher byas pas/ blon po rnams kyi snying du bdud zhugs nas/ 'di btsan po chab srid dam drags pa'i dbang gis lan zer
bar 'chams te/ blon po nag po rnams kyi snying du gnam the dkar po/ bar the khra bo/ sa the nag po gsum zhugs nas/ dmangs dang btsun pa la dbang gtad pas nongs zer/ spyod
pa rtsing du btang bas de la bka' bkyon nan cher bstsal bas/ de pha gis lan zer nas/ rab byung la mdzub mo btsugs pas/ nga'i rab tu byung ba la mdzub mo btsugs nas zer
te/ ker byed na mdzub mo chod cig ces bka' bstsal to/ /mtshang can ston

pa'i brda byas pas/ de khrims la skyon gcig gsungs nas mdzub mo bregs/ dus phyin chad nga'i rab tu byung ba la mdzub mo btsugs na zer te ker byed na mdzub mo chod cig ces bka'
bstsal to/ /yang de rnams spyod pa dog pa pha gi kun gyis lan zer te mchu yo byed pas nga'i rab tu byung ba la mchu yo byed pa kun mchu bregs shig gsungs nas mchu bregs/
de bzhin mig log gis brda byas pas mig phyung / chos pa'i ka ca brkus pa la dkon mchog gi brgyad cu 'jal la sogs kyis len pa'i khrims mdzad pas der zhang blon nag po
kun lkog tu gros byas te/ chos khrims bshig pa'i chad byas pas de la btsan po ma bkrongs na chos khrims mi zhig zer nas/ kha cig na re/ rje ral pa can la sras med kyang gcung
lha sras gtsang ma chos la dga' bas/ srid 'dzin te chos khrims mi zhig zer/ yang ban chen po bran ka dpal gyi yon tan chos byed pa la dbang che bas chos khrims mi zhig
zer/ de la rje la snyan phra bcug pas chog zer nas bran ka dpal gyi yon tan dang / btsun mo dpal gyi ngang tshul ma gnyis nyal bshams so/ /zhes blon po dbas rgyal to res
snyan du gsol bas/ chad pa che thang du zhus pas mi bden gsungs nas ma gnang / yang yang zhus pas mi srid gsungs/ khong gnyis kyi zhabs ma gnyis brkus nas gzigs pa phul/
zhang blon gyis dpe med ces zhus pas/ 'o na khrims chod gsungs pa la ban chen po bran ka dpal gyi yon tan gyis lcags kyi srog tsa bsgrubs pas ma grub pa la phra ma btsan
par byas te/ 'phan yul g.yung thang du bkrongs so/ bran ka dpal gyi yon tan bsad pas bod kyi phywa g.yang nyams bya ba yin no/ /yum dpal gyi ngang tshul can dmod mo bor
te brag las mchongs te gum mo/ /de ma thag lha sras gtsang ma rab tu byung nas rdzong nga tshon po dang bcas te spa gro mon yul du spyugs so/ /bod kyi bsod nams nyams pa
dang / lha srin kun kha langs nas rgod pas blon 'bangs nag po la dga' lha gdong gis kun gyi gros kyi kha lo bsgyur te/ dbas rgyal to re dang cog ro legs sgra ldong phung
'dre mi gnyis kyis zha'i bor khyer 'or cher rgyal po dbu sgra bzil ba'i dus su/ btsan po rgya'i 'bras can gsol ba la dug sna tshogs pa drangs pas ma sto bar/ der lan dkar
du stangs ldong btsan dang skud po cog ro lha lod kyis rje mnga' bdag ral pa can dgung lo sum cu rtsa drug pa lcags pho bya'i lo la ltag gcus nas zhal ltag par bstan/
cog ro bya'u bgyis nas sku bkum/ rgyal po khri srong lde btsan chu pho rta la rgyal sa mdzad/ rje ral pal can lcags mo bya la dgung du gshegs pa'i bar du lo brgya tham pa
song / de'i bar bod kyi rgyal khrims dang / chos khrims gnyis ka dar bas 'di skyid pa'i gdung rabs yin no/ /de nas btsan po dar ma 'u dum btsan po dgung lo bcu dgu pa la
chab srid btang / rgyal por dbang bskur/ bod 'bangs chos la gnag pa kun gyis/ dbas rgyal to re the rang sprel mgo chos la mi dga' ba de nang blon du bskos/ sna nam rgyal
tsha khri 'bum rje khra mgo ba phyi blon du bskos/ blon po kun gyis chos khrims dang 'gal ba mang du byas/ chos ji ltar bsnubs na/ rgya nag pos bod kyi rig pa thams cad
thub pa la/ chos kyi rig pa dang rgyal po'i bsod nams ma thub nas/ lo gcig tu gab rtse thams cad bkram/

ju zhag brtsis pas thabs rnyed de/ bod kyi rgyal po dang / btsun mo/ blon po gsum la lta log dang spyad log gyim shang byas te/ 'dab nor dang / dpya skyes kyi tum bu gsum byas
te bskur ro/ /khong gsum gyi phyag tu re re bzhag skad do/ /der gnam the dkar po/ bar the khra bo/ sa the nag po gsum zhugs nas/ der thugs su gdon gsol te/ rgyal khrims
dang chos khrims rnal ma ma byung ste/ lo tsA ba la sogs mchod gnas rnams kyis/ rje mnga' bdag ral pa can gyis chos dang mthun par mdzad pa 'bangs kyi so tshis la sogs
pa 'di ltar lags zhes zhib tu snyan du gsol bas kyang / btsan pos chos khrims sngar bzhin ma byung / rab tu byung ba kun gyis rje ral pa can la sras mi mnga'/ btsan po dar
ma 'u dum la thugs rgyus mi mnga'/ chos khrims dar gyi mdud pa zhig tu nye zhes brtags pa'i tshig rtag tu smras pas/ btsan po'i sku shig gi phung por song / der lo gcig
chos dang mthun pa tsam byung / de nas lo paN rnams kyi cos kyi sgra bsgyur ba'i 'phro lus/ mdo sde chos kyi rgyal po/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdo dang / spang gong phyag
stong pa dang / yongs su rgyas pa rtogs pa chen po dang / sangs rgyas phal po che'i smad khog chad/ mdo sde za ma tog bkod pa dang lnga lus/ chos sgyur grwa zhig 'on jang
rdo'i lha khang rje'i thugs dam dgu brtsegs dang / jo mo'i thugs dam tsan dan lha khang la zhal gro rab gnas ma 'grub par lus/ slad kyi btsan po sku dbang skyes pa dang
'gyur te/ blon po nag po la dga' kun dang gros byas te/ chos khrims la snyad gsol bar dgongs snyad ma rnyed/ paNDi ta dha ma shI sa/ rme rur mtshams bcad nas dzam bha la
bsgrubs pas grub nas/ tsan dan gyi sku la rdo rje brgyab pas gser phye lte ba'i khung du nas slebs pa byung / de la rgyu byas te thugs rje chen po'i sku kha saraphaNi bzhengs/
se ru na bzhugs/ gsung gi rten gser gyi phyed dang sum stong pa 'ga' zhig bzhengs/ 'bras mo na bzhugs/ thugs kyi rten dngul gyi byams pa 'khun bu can la sogs pa rten
mang du bzhengs so/ /nye gnas kha che ud pa las/ dngul gyi byams pa bzhengs nas lha sar bzhugs so/ /dgung 'dus kyi mchod pa bya bar grags pa btsugs/ dus der lha sa ru
sad dang / ser ba dang / btsa' dang / mu ge dang / mi nad dang / phyugs nad byung bas/ de la btsan pos 'bangs kun la 'di lta bu byung ba cis can zhes dris pas/ nges cag
gis mi shes zer bas/ ngas shes te sngon rgya mo kong co bya ba'i gnod sbyin mo zhig gis/ gnod sbyin gyi shAkya mu ne zer ba'i bkra mi shis pa gcig spyan drangs/ ri rab kyi
rtse mor 'ongs nas lha yul thams cad pham par byas nas phung bar byas/ de nas o rgyan du 'ongs nas o rgyan thams cad phung bar byas/ de nas ma ga dhar 'ongs nas rgya dkar
po thams cad phung bar byas/ de nas rgya nag por 'ongs nas rgya nag po thams cad phung bar byas/ de nas bod yul du 'ongs nas bod yul phung bar byas pa'i gtan tshigs mo
pa dpyad la mkhas pa yin zer nas/ lcags po ri seng ge gnam du mchongs pal 'dra ba la/ sgal tshigs nyi shu rtsa gcig la/ mchod rten nyi shu rtsa gcig gis me btsa' bzhag spyi
por mchod rten nag po khri dpangs dgu pas mnan/ mkhal khung du lha khang byas nas gtad la mnan/ de

ma mnan na rgya gar mnga' 'og tu 'du ba yin/ yang dmar po ri stag mo khung du 'dzul ba 'dra ba de sna la shing gnar ma'i phur pa gdab/ de ma btab na rgya nag dbang du 'du ba
yin/ yang yar lungs yar sna'i gdong la/ ri 'bras kyi ljang pa 'dra ba yod/ de sked pa gcod/ ma bcad na bod la mu ge yong ba yin/ yang nyang ro na ri stag dang seng ge 'thab
pa 'dra ba yod/ stag seng gnyis kyi mjug ma bsnol ba 'dra ba de gcod/ bar du rin po che'i mchod rten gyis mnan/ de ma mnan na/ btsan po 'phrul mnga' ba dang / blon po
rig pa can rgyun mi 'chad par 'ong ba dang / bod la mi dpa' bo rgyun mi 'chad par 'ong ba yin/ drang srong srin po ri dang / rgya nag stong khun gnyis kyi bar na ri pi
wang gi rgyud 'dra ba yod pa de las/ yul gang dang rdzas dang yon tan thams cad ma chad par 'ong ba yin/ de mos gnod par bya bar ma nus pas/ da lta yang rgyun mi 'chad pa
yin no/ /bod 'bangs thams cad rab tu byung bas/ bud med bkag nas chos byed de zer nas/ shes rig thams cad rabs bcad nas bod kyi chab srid rgya'i pha ming la gtad 'dod pa
yin/ bod kyi sa gnyan ri gnyan la bcos kha mang po byas pas/ mo rang mdzes khyer nas/ ro lhas sar bzhag nas bang so med pa de tsug yin zhes bya ba la sogs log pa'i lung
mang po khrid nas/ da rgya gar gyi skad pa ra pi ra 'di la go rgyu gang yang med/ chos kyi nor btub pa mi yong / 'o cag rang thams cad chos pa'i rtags dang phral la khyim
par 'jug zla ba drug tu yab mes kyi chos khrims bcas pa thams cad bshig go zhes gleng nas/ bka' shog bgyis khrims log byas nas/ blon po nag po'i phyogs la dga' ba rnams
so sor bskos te/ btsun pa brtags bor du ma btub pa rnams mda' gzhu dang / rnga cha lang dang dung la sogs pa bskur nas/ khyi ra ba la byas/ der mi nyan pa kun srog dang phral/
rab tu byung ba tso snga dro shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gsungs/ phyi dro mngon pa gsung ba'i dus su mkhan slob kyis dbu mdzad pa'i dge sbyong tshul khrims mi
gtong ba thams cad bsad/ de nas sngags pa rnams phab/ de'i dus su mthu che ba snubs nam mkha'i snying po yin pas/ der khong la skyon 'bebs zer bas/ khong na re/ yi dam gyi
lha sgom du gsol zer bas/ sdigs mdzub gcig mdzad pas thog phab nas brag la brgyab pas/ rgyal po nyid la yang bya'o gsungs pas/ khyed la skyon mi dbab po/ /da phyin chad
sngags pa la mi do 'o zhes zer ro/ nam mkha'i snying po shar phyogs su chos gos kyis gshog pa byas nas 'phur te/ rol mo'i sgra sna tshogs dang bcas pas bsus nas nam mkha'
la gshegs so/ /slob dpon pad mas rab gnas mdzad pa'i lha khang mchod rten rmas bshig tu ma btub nas/ bsam yas dang / 'phrul snang la sogs pa rnams sgo la 'dag zhal brgyab/
glegs bam gyi po ti phal che ba lha sa'i brag lte ba can dang mchims phu'i rdza la sbas/ lha shAkya mu nes gtso byas/ lha yas mar 'ongs pa yar skyol/ mas yar 'ongs pa
mar skyel bar byas pas/ blon po dad pa can kun na re/ btsan po'i thugs su gdon gsol bar nges/ mes srong btsan sgam po dang / bal mo bza' khri btsun dang / rgya mo bza' kong
jo gsum ni sprul par 'dug de'i rjes nas dang / rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' rgyal po khri srong lde btsan

'phrul mnga' ba dang / blon po sbas gsal snang dang / 'gos rgan dpal/ ma grung snyan/ khri bzang yab lhag la sogs pa'i rig pa can mang po byon/ rje ral pa dang / ban chen po
bran kha dpal gyi yon tan la sogs pa blon po rig pa can mang du byung yang / blon po nag po'i phyogs la dga' ba rnams kyis mi rigs pa byas/ da ni btsan pos chos khrims
bshig 'dod pa'i snyad 'dogs pa yin/ lha shAkya mu ne la bod 'bangs thams cad kyi bde skyid re ba yin te zer lta zhing mya ngan byed cing mamig nas mchi ma gtong / de nas
bod 'bangs dad pa can kun gyis lha yar mar spyan mi 'dren pa'i thabs byas so/ /rin po che jo bo'i sku sgul bar ma nus zhes snyan du gsol bas rje'i zhal nas gzu ba tshugs
la bor zhig zer nas/ lha bzhugs khang du bye ma bting nas/ gzu bdang thag pa btags te 'then pas thag pa mang po chad/ de nas rje la zhus te/ sngon yang zhang ma zhang gis
lha bye thems su sbas/ da de bzhin du bye thems su zhugs sam zhus pas/ de tsug gyis gsungs nas bye ma'i thems su bcug go/ /btsan po'i zhal nas/ jo bo shAkya mu ne sbas/
glo 'bur gyi byams pa la jo bo yin byas te/ chu la skyel bar byas te chad nas ra sa'i steng du cho nges btab pas lho nub dkyil 'khor gyi steng na/ btsan po mi dge ba'i khrims
'cha' bas thos nas/ ci zer tsi nyes zer ro/ /lha shAkya mu ne'i 'og na rgyal pos klu mthong ba'i dug can mnan 'dug byas pas/ sku phyir nam la ton zer 'don la khad/ da
sku'i steng du bye ma blugs la bzhag byas pas/ de legs/ de ltar gyis zer/ shAkya mu ne'i bzhugs khang bye mas bkang / sgo la 'dag pa byugs/ rgyal po dga' la re nas btsun
pa chang 'thung ba'i gzugs la sogs logs la byas bzhag byams pa'i sku smad ras kyis g.yogs/ mi dpung pa gzhibs pa'i bar nas btsan pos gzigs tsa na/ gser lhag lhag pa mthong
bar byas te/ mi mang pos thag pa btags te drud pa zhag byas/ nyi ma nub pa dang / sku drud du ma btub 'o thang gi mtshor bskyur byas pas/ rung zer bas/ byams pa yar gdan
drangs/ glo 'bur de nyid du sngon ma bzhin du bzhugs/ mtshor rdo bor nas swa btab pas/ btsan po na re/ de ci yin zer/ lha chur bskyur pa yin byas/ de shin tu legs zer/
nangs par blon po 'ga' chab kha na lta zhing sked pa kyog kyog byas pas/ btsan pos gzigs pas/ khyed tsho der ci byed zer/ sku 'tshol ba yin te mi 'dug nya sram gyi zos
sam byas pas/ 'o de tsug yin shin tu legs zer ro/ /de'i dus su paNDi ta gu ya dang / snubs sangs rgyas ye shes gnyis skye ba sngon ma'i spun yin kapas/ nu bo bod la chos
khrims bshig nas 'dug pa phu bo paNDi tas mngon shes kyis mthong nas/ bstan srung gshin rje dmar nag btang / ma mo dpon g.yog skyel du byon nas/ lam lho lam la 'grims te
g.yog po ku ma ra dang gnyis byon pa dang / 'brog mi dpal gyi ye shes dang yar 'brog sha bo sgang du mjal/ paNDi ta gsang ba'i dbang phyug la zhabs thog byas nas dad cing
gus pas zhus te/ srid pa'i ma mo rgyud dgu cha lag dang bcas pa bsgyur te/ mo bsgyur 'brog skor zhes su grags so/ /snubs sgregs pa sangs rgyas dang paNDi ta bha su dha ra
rnam gnyis kyis chos rgyud gdams pa man ngag lag len dang bcas pa bsgyur/ chos kyi bka' babs lugs bdun byung

ste/ snyags dznyA na la g.yu sgra snying po dang / bi ma la'i sems sde dang / bdud rtsi'i bka' babs dang rje gu ru pad ma'i gshin rje gshed skor gsum gyi bka' babs/ rma rin
che mchog la bi la ma sgyu 'phrul gyi bka' babs/ 'brog mi la ghu ya ma mo'i bka' babs/ rlangs chung dpal gyi seng ge la sangs rgyas gsang ba'i bka' babs/ nam mkha'i snying
po la hUM ka ra'i yang dag dang / rje gu ru pad ma'i gshin rje gshed 'od byang gi bka' babs/ ka cog rnam gsum la dzi mi tra la sogs kyi mtshan nyid rnams kyi bka' babs/
de rnams las gyes pa'i chad tshul byung ste/ snyags dznyA na las dpal dgu ru gyes/ mkhar chen bza' dang / cog ro bza' las gyes pa dang / snyags dznyA na dang / sog po dpal
gyi ye shes las gyes pa dang / sgregs pa sangs rgyas las gyes pa dang / rma rin chen mchog las mang gsum dang / khyung po dbyig 'od dang / khu byang chub 'od dang / zhang
dznyA na sde gsum dam tshig nyams pas/ gsang ba snying po mchong med kyi skor zhes grags/ khyung po'i slob ma dar rje dpal gyi grags pa/ des sgrigs pa sangs rgyas te
yongs su grags pa dbus lugs zhes zer/ khyung po las byung ba/ de rjes khams su bros nas bshad pa ni khams lugs zhes su grags/ khu byang chog 'od las gyes pa ni/ sgyu 'phrul
bka' lugs zhes grags so/ /rgyal po glang dar mas bstan pa bsnubs dus su/ gcug lha sras gtsang ma spyugs pas/ yab mes kyi bka' dpe dang / zab chos kyi gdams pa rnams dang
/ drag sngags rnams dang / rje gu ru pad ma'i gdams pa rnams bsnams nas gshegs nas/ 'od khra snar lo gcig bzhugs nas/ de'i dus su blon po nag po rnams kyis/ gsod pas
sdigs nas bzhugs su ma ster ba'i dus su/ nyang ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ snubs nam mkha'i snying po/ snyags dznyA na ku ma ra la sogs pa lo tsA ba chen po rnams 'tshogs te/
bka' bgros te/ de nas chos thams cad gter du sbas par byas te/ rgyud du 'khrugs pa sdeb pa/ lung gcus pa bsrong ba/ man ngag gab pa gsal ba'i gnad kyi yi ge la sogs pa
rnams snyags dznyA na la btad de/ snyan khung thugs rgyud du byas te/ yi ge mi 'khyams par gtsigs bzung rgyas btab/ ral gcig ma dang dpal mgon lcam sring srung mar bzhag
thugs gter du sbas/ po ti rnams la srang srong srin po ri/ la la dpal chu bo ri/ bzad kyi du ra gdong la sogs par brgya rtsa brgyad sbas/ kha yag la brgya rtsa brgyad sbas/
chos 'khor stod smad kyi gtsug lag khang so phag gis brtsigs/ lha sku rnam pa du ma sbas/ shangs kyi lha phur ma mo sbas/ ru bzi'i mtha' 'dul gyi sgrub gnas rnams su gter
phran nyi shu rtsa brgyad sbas/ bum thang rin po che'i bzhugs gnas su pad ma'i chos gsum/ yig mdo nyi shu rtsa gsum dang bcas pa sbas/ nyang ting nge 'dzin gyis bi ma
la'i rdzogs chen rnams dbu ru zha'i skyer tshang du gter rgya dang bcas nas sbas/ snyags ku ma ra la paNDi ta thams cad kyi bka' babs pa yin te/ des slob ma dpal chen dgu
la gdams/ de rnams kyi bcud dang / nam mkha'i snying po la sogs kyi gnad don thams cad snubs sangs rgyas ye shes la bsdus te/ sgregs kyi yang rdzong na bzhugs so/ /de nas
lha sras gtsang ma lho brag 'kho 'thing du byon/ zhig ral thams cad gsos/ gter tshan gcig sbas/ de nas spa

gror byon/ skyer chu'i lha khang rnying pa gsos/ gsar pa brtsigs/ yab mes kyi bla dpe dang / khrims kyi yig tshang dang tshan che ba gcig sbas/ stag tshang dang seng ge phug
tu gter kha mang du sbas/ spyal kar brgya rtsa brgyad sbas/ gter phran mang du sbas/ de nas lha sras gtsang ma la spyan 'dren med pas thugs mug ste/ bsam yas skyer tshang
gi bla dpe zab mo rnams spyan drangs te spyal ka'i brag la sbas/ lha sras sku 'khor rnams gshegs pa'i shul du/ nam mkha'i snying po mkhar chur gshegs/ nyang ting nge 'dzin
zha ru bzhud do/ /lo tsA ba gzhan rnams so sor bros/ paNDi ta la la spyugs/ la la rang yul du bskrad/ de'i rjes la dar ma rje blon gyis mi tong po mang po bkyes te/
nyang ting ge 'dzin bzang po dbu ru zha ru bkrongs/ rma rin chen mchog bud med du brdzus nas 'u yug tu zla ba dgu yib/ slob dpon la phyag rgya bsten pa la snyad btags te/
srod du chu kha gcig tu bkrongs/ ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs la bkrongs par brtsams pas/ spyi gtsug tu rta skad bton nas/ mi tong po'i co to nas bzung ste skad la bskor
bas ma nus te slar bred do/ /dar rje dpal gyi grags pa dang / snubs sangs rgyas rin po che dang / mgo 'gom sgom tshul khrims dang / mkhar chen dpal gyi dbang phyug dang
/ mchims shA kya pra ba dang / 'brog mi dpal gyi ye shes dang / shud pu dpal gyi seng ge dang / sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms dang / sog po dpal gyi ye shes dang / rlangs
chung seng ge dpal/ 'o bran dpal gyi gzhon nu la sogs pa lo tsA ba bgres po rnams la rgya gar gyi paNDi ta grub pa thob pa'i snyan khung brgyud pa'i gdams pa mnga' ba dang
/ slob dpon chen po bo dhi sa twa dang / slob dpon pad ma sam bha'i byin rlabs zhugs pas sku tshe ring ba dang / lha dang srung ma dbang du 'dus pa dang / sku snang mdangs
mi snang ba la sogs kyis grub pa thob kyang / rgyal po'i log spyod ma bzlog ste/ so sor ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs so/ /gzhan sgrub pa po mang po btsan sa ru bskungs nas
yib po/ /de ma yin pa chos mdzad rab byung tshul khrims mi gtong ba kun bsad do/ /de nas re zhig na/ yer pa'i lha ri snying po na/ la la rtags ma bskyur bar ri dwags rngon
pa dang shan pa la bcug chos kyi 'chad nyan dang sgom sgrub/ 'bri klog phyag mchod thams cad rgyun bcad/ bstan pa bsnubs te ming yang med par byas so/ /de nas re zhig
na/ yer pa'i lha ri snying po na spe'u se ru ma ru na/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje sngags btsun shed rtsal dang ldan pa gcig sgom byed pa'i dus su/ nam phyed tsam na/ dpal
lha mo bud med kyi gzugs su dngos su byung nas/ deng sang bod na grub thob mang yang / dus la ma babs pas khyod la grub thob thams cad kyi byin rlabs zhugs pas/ rgyal po
sdig can gsod ran zer ba zhig byung / de nye gnas la rmi lam du byung ba skad byas bshad pas/ nye gnas kyis slob dpon la chos bsnubs pa'i lo rgyus rnams zhib tu snyan du
gsol bas/ rgyal pos lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje bzhugs pa yang tshor/ gros byas bkrong bar rtsom pa'i gshed du ma btub pa dang / lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje btsan po la snying
rje chen po skyes te/ rgyal po log spyod tshan chen po da rung spyad nas ngan song gsum du skyes te/

bskal pa grangs med par 'khor bar 'khyams pa a tsa ma snyam ste/ de la thabs dang rten 'brel brtsis nas khong rang gi 'khor la nga rang log log gi bar du rnga dang dril bu
dang rol mo'i sgra thun drug tu ma chag par gyis shig ces bsgos nas/ slob dpon snubs nam mkha'i snying po la zhus pas/ nga khams kyi zas spangs pas/ de khyed kyis sgrol cig
lam thams cad myur du bgrod do gsungs nas byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas khong gis rta dkar po gcig la sol phye nag po byugs so/ /ber nag nang dkar po la phyi nag po gcig
gyon/ lcags mda' dang / lcags gzhu zhig thogs/ mdung dkar po la sol ba nag po byugs pa gcig khyer/ lha sar phyin pa'i dus su/ btsan po na re/ nga khams gcig kyang ma bde/
mdang rmi lam gcig kyang ngan/ snying gcig kyang mi dga' zer zhing / ra sa'i rdo ring gi yi ge klog gin 'dug pa la/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje mi gcig dang 'phrad pas/
de na re/ jo bo mi nag gar 'gro zer bas/ nga btsan po la phyag byed pa yin te/ rje gang nas bzhugs byas pas/ rje rdo ring gi yi ge klog gin 'dug zer/ btsan pos lha lung dpal
gyi rdo rje byung ba mthong nas/ mgon po nag po byung zer nas/ gtsug lag khang dang dga' ldan gyi bar gyi mchod rten la sku mnyes nas bzhugs 'dug pa'i mdun du/ lha lung
dpal gyi rdo rjes rta babs nas/ pus mo la brten nas gzhu brdungs pas/ btsan pos de phyag byed par go nas bzhengs 'tshal zer/ phyag dang po byas/ rten phyag gnyis pa byed
tsa na mda' ltong kha sbyar/ phyag tha ma zin te ral pa rgyab tu bskyur/ mtheb bkrol te/ btsan po'i brang la brgyab nas/ rgyal po sdig can de ltar bsad do/ /nga bdud yab
zhur nag po bya ba yin zer kha pha smras so/ /btsan po na re/ nga lo gsum gyis bsad pa sngas/ yang na lo gsum gyis bsad pa phyis pas zer grongs/ lo bcu dgu nas nyi shu
rtsa gcig bar du/ lo ngo gsum zla ba bco brgyad rgyal po byas zer ro/ /de nas mi kha cig na re/ sras yong ba dang / gcung po ma spyugs pa la dgongs pa yin zer/ kha cig na
re/ snga na chos mi bsnubs/ phyis na phyis byed dpyis phyin pa bya ba yin zer/ lo gsum sdig rgyal byas nas/ bod khams kyi sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyams smad par byas so/
/der lha sras btsan po bkrongs par thams cad ra mda' rgyugs shig ces sbran nas/ la la lha ris sgang rgyud na mar byung / la la pha brang dmar po ri na mar byung ngo /
/bdud yab zhur bgyi ba skyid chu'i mtsho khol ma la bsdad nas bde nyal byas te/ rta'i sol phye bkrus pas dag ber pyir slog lcags gzhu 'phyar zhing / nga lha gsanam the dkar
po bya ba yin zer nas song ngo / /ded pas ka cig na re/ ngan pa de do zin pa la drang sring srin po ri'i snar sa sros nas bor zer/ kha cig na re grib bse sgrom gyi phu
ru sa sros te ma matong bar shor zer/ kha cig na re than mo rdo ring nas sa sros nas shor zer ro/ /de zin pa la ma matong zer ro/ /gsum 'ongs pa 'di dpal gyi rdo rje'i sprul
pa yin par nges/ 'di gsod de zer nas stangs dgu des gsod du phyin pas mi kun na re/ khong sngar bas mtshams dam par byas/ rol mo'i sgra yang thengs drug tu 'khrol zhing
'dug zer/ dpal gyi rdo rje'i sgom khang gi mdun du phyin nas bltas pas/ tha mtha' rgya bris

sgo la 'dom sdom ba ra bi ra'i dra ba dang grog zhing kad de 'dug pas/ nang dar dkar gyi yol ba'i phag na spyang rlag slog dang bya rgod kyi thul pa bzhag dkar khung chung
chung ma gcig gi ba gam bya spu tul le byas nas 'dug de nas mi kun na re/ rgyal po chos la mi dges pas lha 'dres bkrongs pa yin zer/ dpal gyi rdo rjes mngon pa/ 'dul ba/
mdo sde/ 'od ldan karma sha dam gsum khur nas khams na mar bros phyin no/ rgyal pos chos snub dus su/ g.yo ru sdod gan byang chung gi dmar shAkya mu ne/ lho 'brog gi g.yo
dge ba'i 'byung gnas/ 'jad khyel gyi gtsang rab gsal dang dge slong gsum dpal chu bo ri la sgom pa'i dus ad dan cig pa dang / lha lung 'tshag po dang zha lnga 'khyams po
bya ba btsun gsum gyis khrid nas rnga brdungs/ rol mo dkrol/ mgo la bya sgro btsugs/ sham thabs snga log phyir log byas nas ri dwags la mda' 'phen pa g.yo dge 'byung gis
mthong bas de la ma rangs nas ban rgan 'khrul lam/ btsun pa smyo gsungs pas/ ci zer dris pas matong ba bzhin du smras pas/ rngon pa na re/ slob dpon ma 'khrul btsun pa dbang
med smyo ru bcug pa yin zer nas/ rgyal pos chos bsnubs pa'i lo rgyus zhib tu bshad pas/ 'o na de 'dir bos dang zer nas/ de pa la gtam dris pas/ khyed la bka' chad ma
phog pa mkhar rje che zer/ nged kyis khyed ltar 'ongs pa yin/ da khyed rang yang 'bros dgos zer/ btsun pa gsum pos gos re bas dril nas sprang chas su zhugs nas bros te/
chos 'dul ba dre'u'i khal gcig bkal nas mnga' ris stod nas lam byung / rgyal khrims mi gcig pa'i sa cha nas bstan pa dar bar bya bsams nas/ gang du yang ma nus nas/ nyin
mo gab cing nub mo byon/ dge bsnyen shes rab go cha bya ba gcig la ming shAkya shes rab tu btags/ de g.yog la khrid nas mdo smad lho ngos be re'i sa cha/ de'u tsha tsho tshwa
mtsho nas lam byas/ rma lung rdo rje brag ra a chung gnam gyi yang rdzong gtsug lag khang rgya phibs yod pa dang / dan tig shel gyi yang dgon du byon nas/ phyis dan
tig yang dgon las mched pa'i lha khang rgya phibs khyung mgo can brgya lnga bcu rtsa gcig byung ba mchis/ sngar gyi btsun chas su zhugs pas/ de na yod pa'i mi kun na re/
a pa pha/ rgyal po sdig can gyi khrims kyis ma phog pa'i mi yang gda' zer bas/ bred nas skrag ste/ nags su bros phyin pas 'tsho ba med par snyung ste bzhugs pa la/ dge bsnyen
ma gcig gis bgata re btegs/ la la na re/ a me mes chen po'i sprul pa yin pas/ bla ma dang mkhan slob med zer/ sdom pa'i bka' bon gyi yin/ de'i rtags kyang bzhi yod zer/
la la na re/ bkag mi mchog grags pa mkhan po yin zer ba smra mod kyi/ de ltar ma yin skad do/ /de'i dus su grong yul de'i zhang lnga mun dzam pa mnya?dzu dpal 'bar gyi
bu mnya?dzu ka ra phan dang zer/ lu mnya?dzu ka ra phan dang zer/ mnya?dzu dge 'bar bya ba dkon mchog gsum mi phyed pa'i dad pa yod pa shes rab che ba/ brtson 'grus dang
/ ngo tsha dang / srung sems che ba'i byis pa gcig ra 'tsho bas mthong nas/ khyed de na ci mdzad ces dris pas nged gang byung du sdod pa yin gsungs pas/ 'o na khyed za
ma'i 'tsho ba ci gsol zer nas/ snga dro gro ma 'dra za zer/ 'o na ngas nga bdag la zan blangs

la 'ong ngam byas pas nged 'di na 'dug pa mi la ma smra gsungs/ de nas zan lhag byin pas/ za 'phro gris bcas nas bor de ji ltar lags byas pas/ 'dul ba'i chos nas mi rung bar
bshad pas/ kho dad pa skyes nas/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje byung ba dran te/ khyed 'dra ba'i mi gcig shel gyi yang dgon du yang byung zer/ de da lta gang na 'dug dris pas
ra rdzi na re/ kha (na )ning yang khyed 'dra ba'i mi gsum byung nas/ gar song cha med byas pas/ de kun la 'di gtod zer nas po ti gcig bzhag nas yod/ kho rang gar song
cha med zer/ der dge slong gsum pos po ti spyan drongs la shog byas pas/ khos len du phyin nas phyag tu gzigs pas/ mdo 'od ldan karma sha dam gsum 'dug 'od ldan gyi gleng
bslangs bag re byas pas/ ra rdzi na re/ da nga yang btsun pa byed par zhu zer/ chos 'di nas byung ba bzhin byed nus na bya'o/ /'di ltos shig byas pas kho dad pa skyes nas
klog gin spyi bor blangs te song bas/ bdag sangs rgyas thams cad kyis rab tu bnga du gsol zer/ sang nangs par 'di nas byung pa ltar byed na re dga' zer bas/ der g.yo dge
'byuung gis mkhan po byas/ gtsang rab gsal gyis slob dpon byas nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa phog pas/ ming yang mkhan slob las dras te dge ba gsal du btags nas/ chos 'dul
ba lo lnga gsan no/ /kho shes rab che bas phyis mngon par shes pa mnga' bas/ bstan pa'i rtsa bar gyur pas/ ming bla chen dgongs pa gsal du grags so/ /de nas khong karma sha
dam ltar byung bas/ 'di dge tshul gyis ltar mi rung / 'di lta na bsnyen rdzogs byed dgos byas pas/ nga dge slong byed par zhu zer/ de la yuul dbus su dge slong bcu/ mtha'
'khob tu lnga dgos te/ 'di na gsum las med gsungs pas/ nga kha ning gi chos khyer nas byuung ba de 'tshol du 'gro zer nas de btsal pas/ rgya dar rtse'i tshong 'dus na
