lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje las kyi kha skong zhus pas/ ngas mi btub ste bstan pa'i don du rgyal po sdig can de bsad pas sdom pa med/ 'on kyang nga yis grogs bya'o zer nas
song bas/ rgya nag nas ha shang dge slong ke dbang bya ba dang / gyim phag bya ba'i dge slong gcig dang gnyis khrid nas byung ba dang / dad pa'i dge 'dun gyi kha skong mdzad
nas/ bod kyi dge slong gsum dang / der lnga pos sdom pa phog nas dge slong byas so/ /dmar ban shAkya mu nes gsang ste'i dge 'dun mdzad/ dge slong rab byung drug yod
pa la/ de nas lo gnyis gsum nas grum 'bar ba byang chub kyis rab tu byung ba zhus pas/ mkhan po bya rgyu ni/ nged rgas skyong ba mi nus/ sngon sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
kyi zhal nas glang po che smyon pa'i sna la ral gri btags nas sems can gsod du bcug pa ni sla yi/ rab tu byung nas de ma bskyangs pa ni de lta ma yin no zhes bka' bstsal
gsungs pa/ mnyadzu dge 'byung gis/ sdom pa yang khyod kyis phog gsungs/ dam pa'i cos 'dul ba dang sbyar na/ nga yis lo lnga las ma lon/ mi rung zhes pas/ mkhan po byed rapa
gnang ba la dge salnga byas nas lo bcu lon dgos par bka' bstsal byas pas/ lo lnga lon nas mkhan po byas pa la nye sapa gcig las med/ ston pa'i bstan pa spel ba'i ched
du nged mkhan slob la dri mas phog ste/ de khyad du sod la mkhan po gyis shig pha rol po la sdom pa skye yi

gsungs nas/ nged kyis gnang nas nyes pa med kyi gsungs/ lung legs par byin nas mkhan po byas/ ming rin po che ye shes rgyal mtshan du btags/ des khams pa mi drug rab tu byung
ba yin no/ /ming ni spa gong ye ses g.yung drung 'bar/ rin chen gsal gnyis btsun pa re byung / phyis mkhan po yang byas/ ja ye shes seng ge dang / lce shes rab byang chub
gnis ni mkhas btsun ldan pa yin/ de gnyis kyis zi na rin chen dang / gtsang dge ba'i shes rab gnyis rab tu byung ngo / /de gnyis kyis mkhas pa drug shes rab grags tab
tu byung ngo / /des mtha' bzhi rgyal 'phags rab tu byung ngo / /de nas 'al pa rdo rje dbang phyug dang / snubs phag shing rta chen po gnyis rab tu byung / slob gnyer tshul
bzhin mdzad/ snubs phag sing rta'i rgyud pa la mkhas rgyud zer/ grum shing rlag lag can gyi rgaya?d pa la btsun rgyud zer te yongs grags so/ /sde pa ni mang du 'phel lo/
mched po gnyis 'tshogs nas lhan cig tu chos kyi bka' bgro ba mdzad dus lan gcig tsa na/ 'brel 'bel gtam byas pas grum shing rlag lag can gyi zhal nas/ da gzims par bgyi/
nga mal gang du bgyi gsungs/ snubs phag shing rta na re/ dpal gyi dbang phyug kyang zer/ 'dir stabs gcig tu bgyis gsungs pas/ khyod lkog na 'bu kha gsol bar grags/ nga
sla khab bla gab bsrung 'atsal byas pas/ snubs phag shing rta khros nas/ e shing rlag lag can gyong po 'di zer bas/ grum shing rlag lag can bya bar grags/ de gnyis kyis
bslab pa blangs nas lo bco lnga tsam re bzhes nas yod pa'i dus / lo 'ga' re nas 'du 'dzi bag re mdzad pa la/ mkhas gral/ gtsun gral/ rme gral gsum du phye nas bsnyen bkur
rim pas phye nas byed pa la/ mkhas btsun gyi gral ring por song ste snyan bkur rim pas phye nas byed pa la/ mkhas btsun gyi gral ring por song ste snyan pas khyab nas dbus
gtsang du grags so/ /bla chen po'i slob ma ni macog drug yin te/ btsun pa spa gong ye ses g.yung drung yin/ des grum ye shes rgyal mtshan la 'dul ba bshad do/ /bla chen
po'i mkhan bu la/ 'bar rin che gsal/ mkhas pa 'al pa rdo rje dbang phyug snubs dpal gyi dbang phyug dang / mkhas la btsun pa ja ye shes seng ge dang / co shes rab byang
chub po/ gzhan yang shog chung pa shes rab grags dang / bka' 'bar ba byang chub la sogs mang po bka' drin la bkod pa lags so/ /bod kyi rgyal srid phyogs su chad pa ni/ btsan
po glang dar ma la btsun mo che chung gnyis yod pa la/ sras ma gzigs pa la btsan po bkrongs nas yi mug tu lus pa la/ rang rang so so'i blon po rnams kyis bsrungs so/
/chos khrims dar gyi mdud pa 'dra ba grol/ rgyal khrims gser gyi gnya' shing chag bod dmangs mi sog ma'i phon thag chad/ ban chen kapo bran ka dpal gyi yon tan bsad pas
bod kyi phywa g.yang nyams/ pha zer la bu ni nyan/ rje zer la 'bangs mi nyan/ dpon zer la g.yog mi nyan/ bod sil bu rang khar dgar song / rje'i btsun mo 'bal phan bza' ma'i
sras khri brtan po yum brtan yin te/ da lta dpal gyi bsam yas na yod pa rnams yin no/ /lcang rgya na yang yod do/ /de gnyis gcen po gang gis byed par ma 'chams nas blon
po kun 'khrungs te/ dbu ru dang g.yo ru gnyis su chad do/ /tshe spong bza'i

sras khri gnam lde 'od srungs yin no/ /chu mo phag la 'khrungs so/ /de dang cog ro bza' lha btsun rje legs su bshos pa'i sras rje dpal mgon btsan yino / /de cu mo glang la
sku 'khrungs/ lo bcu gsum la rgyal sar bton/ de'i ring la gna' dasu bzang po rnams zhig mi rnams kyi bsam pa rnams 'gyur te/ rje la khengs log 'khrug pa byung ste/ dang po
khams su byung / de nas bod 'od 'bar mchims su byung ste/ dar rje dpal gyi grags pa khams su bros/ de nas dbu ru/ g.yo ru/ g.yas ru/ ru lag dang gsum du byung / de nas
dbu ru'i khengs log byung / de'i dus su snubs sangs rgyas ye shes kyis sprang por brdzus nas bal yul du bla ma rnams la mjal du 'gro dgongs nas/ gtsang na yar byon pa dang
/ lhan gyi lung mdar/ lcang gong phud dkar dang / g.yan ban ma bon dang mjal/ jo bo skyes mchog gang nas byon zus pas/ snubs yul rong nas 'ongs gsungs pas/ snubs sangs
rgyas ye shes yin par shes nas/ bdag gis zla ba gcig gnyis kyi mthun rkyen dang / zhabs tog bgyid bzhugs par zhu byas pas/ rung gar skyid pha yul yin gsungs nas/ des mtshon
pa byas nas so ye shes dbang phyug dang / khu lung yon tan rgya mtsho dang / dpa' 'gor blon chen 'phags pa dang / sru legs pa'i sgron ma dang / thugs kyi sras bzi rin
po che gsum gyis dbang bskur stabags su zhus te/ de rnams la gdams pa so sor rdzogs par gnang ngo / /de'i dus su 'o bran dpal gyi gzhon nu snye mor bros pa las/ tsha bo blo
gros dbang phyug la sogs pas rgyud pa mdzad/ snubs yon tan rgya mtsho la rgya gar dha na ta las gshin rje gshed kha yun dang / man ngag zam mo mang po de'i dus su gnang
/ de nas rgya gar du gshegs so/ /'o bran blo gros dbang phyug la rgya gar tsan dra gir tis gsin rje gshed 'theb rgya can la sogs pa gnang ste bsgyur ro/ /de gnyis gsang
sngags snga 'gyur gyi gzhug mar song ste/ de nas gcig kyang 'gyur byang rnams bsgyur ba med do/ /dus phyis gzhan gyis btsal yang dpe cha dam dum 'dra en tsam ma yin pa/
paNDi ta dang chos gcig kyang ma rnyed de ma byung / dus de tsa na dbus gtsang na sdom pa dang bshad pa'i gdams ngag bka' chad nas med/ gtsug lag khang thams cad kyi lde
mig btsun gzugs dbu gtsug phud can sham thabs gong ba can gyon pa 'ga' re'i ming gnas brtan dgra bcom par btags pas 'dzin/ mchims smad na chen po rgyal ba dang zhang lcam
'bre chung ba gnyis kyi klog shes pas mi shi ba'i dge bar glegs bam klog pa la/ byis pa dang bu chung shi ba la sum brgya pa klog mi che ba shi ba la bde chen 'don/ de gnyis
sin tu shes rab che zer nas mkhan po ser po gdugs pa 'di bsdus par 'dug zer/ rtsa 'grel sdeb ma shes pas mkhan po'i dpe cha bshig gnas bltas pas/ mkhan po'i khar tsang
gi chos de'i go ba legs pa zhig 'di na 'dug zer/ mkhan po na re/ sngon gyi bgres po kun gyi bsnyel yig rnying pa yin te mchi zer/ der yig sna la rtsal bshad 'ga' re 'phel/
dus der mdo smad na mkhan slob kyi bka' brgyud ma chad par 'dug bya ba'i grags pa cher thos so/ /de nas bstan pa'i me ro bslangs pa ni/ spu rang gi btsad po lha bla
ma ye shes 'od dang / dbu ru'i khri lde mgon btsan dang / bsam yas kyi tsha la na ye shes rgyal mtshan dang gsum

gyi sku drin gyis bskyabs nas chos kyi khungs btsal lo/ /de la bstan pa'i me ro smad nas bslangs pa ni/ dar mas bstan pa bsnubs nas mi rabs 'ga' nas langs te/ de yang yum brtan
khri brtan po'i sras khri lde mgon po/ de'i sras rig pa mgon dang nyi 'od dpal mgon zhes bya ba gnyis byung / rig pa mgon gyi sras po khri lde/ de'i sras 'od po/ de
la sras gsum ste/ a tsa ra/ mgon po btsa'/ mgon brtsegs so/ /nyid 'od dpal mgon gyis sras/ mgon spyod yin/ de'i sras tsha la na ye shes rgyal mtshan no/ de la 'od po'i sras
mgon btsan dang tsha la na ye shes rgyal mtshan gnyis ka'i ring la tshul ji ltar bstan pa bslangs na/ bod dbus gtsang na bka' gdams pa bya ba rtsa ba bzhi sna yul la yod
pa srung ba dang / dgag dbye bya zer nas dbyar zla gsum gsum srung la/ de min mi srung ba gcig dang gnyis kyi rtags tsam 'dzin pa las med pa la de'i dus su/ btsan po de
nyid kyis dbus gtsang gi mi rnams la thar pa'i don 'byung bar bzhed pas/ sdom pa mtshan nyid pa blangs sa ga na yod rtsad bcad pas/ dang po rje dar mas bstan pa bsnubs
nas dmar gtsang g.yo gsum mar bros pa las mched pa mdo khams smad na 'dug ces gsan no/ /khong gnyis kyis dbus gtsang nas dad pa can bskul lo/ /der bod dad pa can 'ga' zhig
phyin/ dge bsnyen re tsam byas nas phyin pas ni sde pa 'phel ma nus so/ /de nas dbus gtsang gi mi khams nas sdom pa blangs pa la lo rgyus chos 'byung 'ga' yod do/ /mi bcu
gnyis lam nas log pa gcig dang bcu gsum 'ongs/ bla chen dgongs pa gsal gyis mkhan po mdzad/ grum ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis slob dpon mdzad/ sgro mnya?dzu shrIs gsang ste
mdzad nas/ dbus sha tshar gyi klu mes shes rab tshul khrims/ sum pa ye shes blo gros/ 'bring ye shes yon tan/ rag shi tshul khrims blo gros/ lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug
tshong btsun shes rab seng ge/ 'a brgyad spun gnyis/ u pa ta ka ra dang lnga ni gtsang pa'o/ /lam rgod sna dang 'phrad pas/ klu mes rag shis sdom pa phog nas/ 'a btsun
'phags pa blo gros su ming btags/ mdo smad du ma byon pas sdom pa rnal ma med zer ba'ang byung / klu mes kyis grum la 'dul ba lo gcig gsan/ yar byon khar mkhan po la mos
pa'i rten du na bza' gcig mchod gnas zhus pas/ khong rang gi dbu la gsol 'phrobon po'i zhwa 'ob dang gru bzhi ser po btab pa gcig gnang / de klu mes kyis gsol bas mo byis
gcig na re/ skra lo 'dug zer bas/ klu mes kyi btsun zhes grags so/ /sde pa'i gtsug lag khang kun na yod do/ /mi lnga yar byon pa'i dus su mkhan po'i zhal bskos su springs
pa/ klu mes mkhas btsun pas mkhan po gyis/ 'bring skyong mkhas pas gnas brtan gyis/ lo ston mthu che bas bstan pa srungs/ tshong seng ge blo rno bas ston pa gyis la chos
shod/ sum pa la khyed rang sgrub pa gyis gsungs nas yar byon lugs so/ /mi lngar byed na/ klu mes/ sum pa/ dbus pa gsum mo/ /lo tsA ba gnyis te gtsang pa gnyis yin no/ /de
yang dang po g.yog bcu yis rab tu byung zhing / mtha' 'khob kyi bsnyen par rdzogs par byas so/ /de yang yar byon pa'i lam du sba dang 'a gnyis dang mjal te/ klu mes las
rab tu byung ngo / /de ltar mi lha'am bcu yar byon/ de nas khong rnams kyis sras su tad sna su la gtad

gros byas pas/ chos 'khor bsam yas su phyags phab/ der btsan po khris khrong rnams kyis sna blangs nas/ khyed tsho'i dpon su yin dris pas/ klu mes yin byas pas/ dbu rtse'i
lde mig rtsa btsas khyer chag pa gang phyag tu gtad/ 'khor sa'i sgo phye bas nang 'dre tsher dang skya 'gal gyis gang / de'i yal ga'i chus ri mo thams cad byid/ rnga khang
na dbus mtha'i ka ba ling bcu gnyis 'dug pa'i bzhi 'phreng thag chad/ gzhan kun skam bu zing gda'/ 'khor sa bar pa na/ wa tshang bcas dkor nor gyis gang 'dug pa gzigs/
dbu rtse'i lder bzo'i phyag dang dbu rgyan thams cad la bya tshang bcas/ dbu rgyan thams cad bya lud kyi rul 'dug klu mes kyis dkar mdzod gzigs/ sgom thams cad sbrul bdud
la sogs pa'i 'phrul thag byas rgya btab pas/ phyir rdzab zhal byas nas lde mig thams cad btsan po la gtad/ nga mkhan por bskos pas/ mkhan po rnams dkor la 'bags pas/ nga
'di mi 'dzin gsungs/ khams gsum zangs khang gling phul bas kyang ma bzhes so/ /bu tshal gser khang gling lo tsA ba gnyis la phul bas kyang ma bzhes/ gdul bya re so so na
yod gsungs nas lo tsA ba gnyis gtsang na yar bzhud do/ /rag shi la dge rgyas phul/ gzhug bu tsal yang gtad/ de nas klu mes la ka chu phul bas/ dbu ru g.yon ru'i lam btegs
bya gsungs nas/ klu mes kyis dbu rtse gso ba'i chas rkyen rta khal mang po bsnams nas/ dbu rtse nyams pa rnams gsos/ lde mig rnams sba dang rag shi gnyis la gtad do/ /rag
shis bu tshal bzung / sbas dge rgyas bzung / 'bring gis khams gsum bzung / de nas chad nas sde pa 'phel te rim pas bskyangs pa ni/ mchims phu stod smad dang / dmyal gyi
brag 'gu ra dang / byang gi sha mtha' dang / lo ror 'chad khrod dang / ljon sna spang dur la sogs pa lung ba gsum du rgyas par 'phel lo/ /klu mes dang sum pas ka chu bzung
/ dbu rtse thams cad kyang bla'i mchod gnas kyis gang bar byas so/ klu mes kyis 'dul ba lo gcig thams cad la gsungs/ de nas rag shis lan pa spyil bu bzung / sbas sha'i
zha'i lha khang bzung / klu mes kyis yer bab rang mdzad nas bzhugs/ mkhan po yun ring du mdzad nas sde bskyangs/ mkhan bu mang du byung yang yongs su grags pa'i bu yin
te/ rngog byang chub 'byung gnas kyi slob ma po to ba/ de'i slob ma sha ra ba/ de'i slob ma chu mig pa/ de'i slob ma snar thang pa gro mo che/ gzhu'i kun dga' ra ba dang
/ yer pa rlan ye shes shes rab gnyis kyis mdzad/ sum pas rgya gsar khang mdzad/ gung gsum gyis dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyis brag rgyab mdzad/ sna nam rdo rje dbang phyug
gis rgyal gyi lug lhas mdzad/ gru mer ye shes 'byung gnas kyis sol nag mang chen mdzad/ de rnams las gyes pa'i gtsug lag khang gi bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / klu mes kyis
mkhan lapo mdzad pa'i ring la mkhan po gzhan sus kyang ma mdzad/ sde la rigs gnyis dang tha dad kyang med/ dge 'dun gyis sde chos bzhin skyong ba las/ zhing dang phyugs
la yang mi 'dzin/ 'bru rjen pa mi 'chang ba las/ sde 'phel ba'i stobs kyis khong bzhed pa bzhin ma btub nas/ da dge 'dun chos nas bshad bzhin du sde mi srung bar snang
/ gang zag so so rang rang gi bslab pa la nan tan bya gsungs nas rgya gar mtha' 'khob tu bzhud

pa la lam du sku 'das so/ /de nas rngog gis mkhan po mdzad de/ sde tha dad du byung / rngog 'das nas rgya gsar sgang gi gnas brtan 'tshal chung ba mkhan por bskos/ de 'das
nas rgyal gyi kun tshul khrims byang chub mkhan por bskos/ 'dul pa yang lan kha yar mdzad do/ /'dul ba zhig nas mkhan po yang mang rab tu song / phyis gsum pas gnas gzhi
yang brtsigs/ mkhan po yang mdzad/ 'bring gis yun ring por dgon ser du sgrub pa mdzad/ phyis mkhan po yang mdzad/ de ltar dbus gtsang mi lngas bstan pa 'phel zhing rgyas
par mdzad do/ /de ni mkhan po'i brgyud pa'o/ /brgyud pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa 'od srungs chen po la bka' bsgos te nyer bar 'khor la 'dul ba
gtad/ des dgra bcom pa lnga brgyar gcig gis mi tshang ba'i thugs rgyud las bsdus/ khyad par du kun dga' bo la gtad/ des sha na'i gos can la gtad/ des nyi ma gung pa la/
sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa yin te nyer sbas la/ de'i dus su dgra bcom pa bdun brgya'i thugs rgyud las bsdus nas/ des nag pa la/ des dan ti ka la/ des legs 'doms la/ des
phyir mi 'ong blo mi phebs la/ dgra bcom pa de dag gis bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad/ des kha che dge 'dun bzang po la/ des slob dpon dbyig gnyen la/ des slob dpon yon tan 'od
la/ des shAkya 'od la/ des paNDi ta seng ge'i gdong can la/ des za hor rgyal po'i bu dge slong shan ta rakShi ta/ des mkhan po mdzad nas/ rgya gar dha na shi la dang /
kha che dzi na mi tra dang gnyis kyis slob dpon mdzad nas/ bod kyi dge slong la snga ba sba ye shes dbang po rab tu byung ba dang / de la ming rin chen nam mkha'i mdzod
skyong / des dmar shAkya mu ne/ des g.yo dge ba'i 'byung gnas/ gtsang rab gsal la/ de dag gis bla dgongs pa gsal la/ des sgron mnya?dzu shri'i la/ des grum ye shes rgyal
mtshan la/ des dbus gtsang gi mi lnga'am bcu la brgyud nas/ klu mes/ des gru mer la/ des kyo gang ba sdings la/ des gzus ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan la/ des dazus ston rnyog
gi bu bzi ste/ dbu ru'i rlan glan tshul khrims byang chub/ g.yo ru'i lce tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ gtsang rong 'khar phug tu sne bo grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'dzims pa shes
rab 'od la sogs pa so so la bshad do/ /'dzims pa'i slob ma mnga' ris pa rgyal ba'i shes rab dang / ko khyim pa ye shes bla ma/ nyang mtshams rin chen bla ma dang / sog
ston tshul khrims bla ma la bshad/ des rgya 'dul ba 'dzin pa ye shes seng ge la/ des mtha' bzhi 'dul ba 'dzin pa la sogs su gyes/ des rma tsho byang rdor la/ des rgya'i slob
ma sha mi chen po dang / kyi pho tshul 'phags dang gsum/ des bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa brtson 'grus 'bar la/ des rtsis pa gzhon seng la/ des ba char rtse mo la/ des dbang
phyug grags pa la/ des mnga' ris dgra bcom pa rgyal mtshan la/ de dag gi slob ma dang / mkhan po dang / nying slob tu ma gyur ba'i rab tu byung ba ni bod na ye med japa yin
no/ /'dul ba smad lugs su grags so/ /bstan pa yas dar ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i rtsa ba'am gzhi mar gyur pa ni/ tshul khrims kyi bslab pa yin te/ de'i rkyen che
shos mkhan slob yin/ de'i brgyud pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ slob dpon

bram ze chen po sa ra ha/ de gnyis kyis klu sgrub snying po/ des bha bya legs ldan/ paNDi ta ye shes snying po/ des shan ta rakShi ta/ bo la sa twa dzi na mi tra/ dha na shi
la/ dharma pa la/ sa tu pa la/ gha na pa la/ ba pa la/ pra dznya pa la/ de dag gis bal lapo'i paNDi ta shAkya se na la/ mkhan po zhang zhung pa dang / drang srong phyi
phud pa/ des rlung lo tsA ba la/ des drang phyo chu'i rgyun la/ des kyi 'dul ba 'dzin pa la/ des gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan la/ 'dzims pa la/ de'i dus su jo bo rje byon nas
'brom gyis lo tsA ba mdzad nas/ mdo rtsa dang / sum brgya pa dang / karma sha dam dang / 'od ldan la sogs gsan/ gzhan yang bshad pa mang po mdzad/ dbu ru ka tsal du bzhugs
zhes sde snod thams cadal ma rmongs pa zhang pa tshab pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gsung ngo / /de ltar stod dang smad nas dge slong bla chen po'i mkhan brgyud bcas pa 'phel
lo/ /bstan pa'i me ro smad mdo khams smad nas 'phel bas/ khams pa la a mi zer ba de tsug yin no/ /de ltar smad nas me ro langs pa dang / stod nas langs pa gnyis las/ mnga'
ris stod nas langs pa ni/ chos snga 'gyur gyi gzhug chad nas glang der gyis lcags pho bya'i lo la chos bsnubs nas/ mi rabs drug yan chad la lo brgya dang brgyad tsam
song ste/ mnga' ris nyi 'og rgyal khams na sdom pa gsum gyi bka' ni chad/ bshad pa dang gdams ngag gi gnad ni med/ sgrub brgyud ni chad/ tshul dang mthun pa'i tos bsam sgom
gsum ni ye med do/ /de ltar tshul ji ltar bslangs na/ dar ma'i sras khri gnam lde 'od srungs/ de'i sras dpal 'khor btsan/ de la bsam yas mchims phu'i sgrub po po lha
lung dpal gyi yon tan bya bas/ mdo sde thar pa chen phyag mchod/ spang skong gi phyag mchod/ de bzhin gshegs pa sman lha'i mdo chog rnams gtan nas/ khyed sngon yab mes kun
gyi bkra shis bde legs thams cad 'di las byung bas sgrubs shig gsungs nas gnang ngo / /grub thob nam mkha'i snying po dang snubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin po che'i zhal nas/
yab mes kyis dka' ba spyad cing byin rlabs thams cad 'di ltar nyams su blangs pas dngos grub thob pa yin gsungs nas gsang sngags yang phur dang / 'jam dpal zhi khro ma
gshin gyi bka' rnams gtad do/ /dus 'khrugs te lo bco brgyad rgyal po mdzad do/ /rim gyis gtsang du byon/ grom pa lha rtse'i brag la pho brang mdzad nas bzhugs so/ /lo sum
cu so gcig chu mo lug la sku 'das so/ /de la sras gnyis te bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal dang / khri skyid lde nyi ma mgon gnyis las/ gcen po khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal
la sras gsum byung ste/ che ba dpal lde'i rgyud pa ni/ gung thang pa/ klu rgyal ba/ spyi pa/ lha rtse ba/ glang lung pa/ rtsad skor pa rnams yin no/ /bar ma 'od lde'i rgyud
pa ni/ grom pa ba/ srad pa/ nyang stod kyi lha chen dpal la sogs yin no/ /chung ba skyid lde'i rgyud pa ni/ mus pa 'jad pa/ nyang stod na'ang 'ga' zhig yod do/ /khri
skyid lde nyi ma mgon chibs kha gyen la bskyod nas mnga' ris stod du gshegs pa la yab kyi zhal nas/ lho mon dong kha phye ba 'dra ba dang / bru sha dang / sbal ti dang /
sa sgang gi 'brog grog mo la sogs pa mi dang mi ma yin pa'i gnod pa mang po yod pas/ yi dam dang srung

mar mdo sngags kyi cho ga 'di rnams gyis shig gsungs nas gnang bas/ mnga' ris kyi btsad po rnams chab srid dang / mnga' ris mtho bar byin rlabs che ba yin/ blon po gnyis kyis
gtsang bye ma g.yung drung bar du bskyal nas/ zhang pa tshab nyi ma rdo rje yis dre'u gcig phul/ cog ro phag sha lha legs kyis spyang khu'i thul pa gcig phul/ rje khri
skyid lde nyi ma mgon gyi zhal nas/ ngas stod phyogs 'dir rgyal sa zin na khyed gnyis la bslang rgyu re yod do gsungs nas so sor byon te/ mtsho ma pham gyi byang du bzhugs
nas/ blon po shes rig che ba gsum stod bskor gsum blta ru btang bas blon po spu rang du blta ru btang ba 'khor nas byung bas/ rje la phyag byas mnyes dris pa dang / ji
ltar 'dug gsungs pa la/ lung pa rta bshas kyi khog pa gangs kyis bskor ba 'dra ba na mi srin po 'dra ba zhig mchis zer/ gu ger phyin pa na re/ lung pa nya ltar dkar gyi
khog pa 'dra ba g.ya' yis bskor ba zhig la mi lug 'dra ba gda' zer/ mang yul du phyin pa na re/ yul ko mog chab kyis gang ba gangs kyis bskor ba 'dra ba zhig gda'/ mi sbal
pa 'dra ba gcig gda'/ go ang gsungs/ rang re rje blon rnams bla ma dkon mchog la mchod pa 'bul/ gsol ba gdab po gsungs nas dang po spu rang du byon nas tshong mang po mdzad/
mi rnams zas kyis brid/ thams cad dad par byas nas khrims bcas dbang du 'dus pa dang / dmag bshams gu ge la brgyab/ mnga' 'og tu bcug de nas mar yul du byon/ rgyal
khrims bcas nyes pa shor ba rnams la nyes pa blangs/ mgo bregs nas de ltar stod mnga' ris bskor gsum rgyal khrims gser gyi gnya' shing 'dra bas mnan/ de nas spu rang du sku
mkhar nyi zung brtsigs/ stod kyi mnga' bdag rgyal po mdzad/ de nas zhang blon gnyis kyis bu mo gnyis btsun mor phul lo/ /pa tshab ma la tsha bo ma byung / cog ro zangs
kha ma la sras gsum byung / che ba dpal gyi mgon gyi rgyud ni/ yar lung dang spu rang lugs kyi yul gyi btsad po rnams yin no/ /bar pa bkra shis mgon gyi rgyud pa rnams ni/
zhang zhung phyi nang dang / spu rang dang / ya rtse'i rgyal po'i rgyud rnams yin zer ro/ /mon yul na ci rigs pa yod do/ /chung ba lde gtsug mgon gyi rgyud ni/ khum bu
ba/ ding ri ba/ mon yul na ci rigs pa yod do zer ba rnams lags/ bkra shis mgon gyi sras kho re dang srong nge byon/ kho re'i sku tshe'i stod la btsun mo bzhes rgyal srid
bskyangs/ de la sras de ba ra dza dang / na ga ra dza gnyis 'khrungs/ sku tshe smad la mon yul na bslu rkun yod zer/ des rkyen byas nas thugs zhen pa log ste/ 'jig rten
la skyo ba skyes/ dam pa'i chos la dad pa skyes nas sngon mes dbon rnam bzhis dam pa'i chos dar bar byas pa/ glang dar mas bsnubs pa gso ba dang yab mes kyi rjes snyegs pa
bod la phan gdags pa'i phyir rgyal srid gcug po srong nge la gtad nas/ khong rang gis khong rang rab tu byung nas/ bslab pa ni gsung rab dang dkon mchog la blangs/ mtshan
yang bla ma ye shes 'od du gsol/ de'i dus su rgyal khrims ni sil bur song / snga 'gyur gyi bka' ni chad/ yongs grags mgo reg zer ra chod ras gcod byed/ snyan rgyud mda'
ltar mngag yongs su rdzogs pa ri khrod 'grims zer/ de'i dus su bla ma nyid mtshan nyid theg pa spang byar ston

pa rnams/ sangs rgyas kyi bka' yin par mkhyen yar gsang sngags 'bras bu'i theg pa rnams rgyu mtshan nyid dang / lam gyi spyod tshul mi mthun par 'dug pas/ bka' yin pa la the
tshom zhugs nas/ de'i dus su bal po pad ma ma ru rtse bya ba chos bag tsam mkhyen pa gcig la sems bskyed thob cing / byams sems snying rje 'byongs pa'i gang zag bzang po
zhig byung nas/ de la mnga' bdag lha bla mas chos zhu gsungs pas ngas mkhas par mi shes/ rgya gar na mkhas pa yod/ nga yis spyan drang ngam zer nas/ de la zhu rten gyi
gzer bskur btang bas paNDi ta mkhas pa smri ti dznyA ghir ti dang / a tsarya phra la ring ba bya ba'i mkhas pa gnyis spyan drangs nas yong bas/ lo tsA ba ma ru rtse pho log
glang thabs kyis bal yul du shi nas/ paNDi ta gnyis bod skad mi mkhyen tshur byon pa'i lam du dpal mo dpal thang du jag pas khrid nas bran du byas/ bros kyi dogs nas btsongs
nas rin bza' 'o zer te/ rta nag tu khyong rje shag btsan bya ba la btsongs nas lug rdzi lo 'ga' byas/ glan tshul khrims snying po la rin po che spungs pa gsungs te/
de nas grub pa tob par shes nas bzugs par zhus pas ma gnang / de nas khams su byon/ yol ri la bzhugs/ lo 'ga' shas nas bod skad byang nas sgra rang 'gyur du chos gzhung
dang / sgrub thabs dang / gdams ngag rin po che spungs pa la sogs mang po gsungs so/ /lo gong ye shes rin po che la mngon pa mdzod rtsa 'grel dang / sgra smra sgo mtshon
cha dang rang 'gyur du gsungs so/ /de nas cog ro zhang btsun dang / g.ya' ston shes rab grags dang / pa tshab ri khrod pa dang / zangs kha mdzod khur la sogs pa kha mched
de dbus su dar ro/ /gzhan yang 'jam dpal gyi 'grel pa rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang / de'i sgrub thabs cha lag dang / rnal 'byor gyi rgyud dkyil 'khor la sogs pa mang po
rang 'gyur du mdzad do/ /a tsarya phra la ring ba ni sku bgres/ rtsa ring du sku tshe 'phos so/ /lha bla ma'i ring la smri ti byon yang lo tsA ba med pas ngo ma shes te/
byon pa ma tshor ro/ /chos mang po bsgyur yang khams su lus pas lha bla ma'i thugs dgongs ma rdzogs so/ /lha bla ma ni sbyor lam rtse drod kyi ye shes la gnas par 'jam dpal
rtsa rgyud las lung bstan pa ni/ byang phyogs gang ri'i rgyud can du/ /rigs ni rgyal sras zhes bya ste/ /ye shes 'od ces bya ba 'byung / /zhes dang / mdo snying rje pad
ma dkar po las/ kun dga' bo mya ngan ma byed smre sngags ma 'don/ nga mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og tu byang phyogs su dge slong ye shes 'od ces bya ba 'byung ste/ de yis
bstan pa rgyas par byed do/ /zhes lung bstan to/ /lha bla mas thugs brtse bas dgongs te/ sras gnyis kyang rab tu byung ste/ khong gi mchod gnas ser po zhes bya ba dang /
sa sgang gi 'brog mi bgras te/ des ser po can bsad pa la/ lha bla mas nga'i mchod gnas bkrongs pas stong 'dod gsungs te/ mnal lam du gser rta stan tsam gcig dbul lags kyis
zer nas/ dong rtse wang gi gser sa bya ba phul bas/ bug pa re nas gser bre khal gyis bcu ru byung nas spu rang du kho char dang / sil chog tu rta po dang / mar yul du
nyar ma dang / dbu rig tu sha ling dang / gu ger tho ling gi gtsug lag khang chen po bzhengs so/ /gtsug lag khang

de'i lcags ri gcig gi khongs na gnya?dzir btsugs pa'i lha khang drug cu rtsa bzhi yod do/ /de nas bstan pa 'phel zhing / the tshom gcod pa'i phyir stod mnga' ris bskor gsum
na blo rno ba shes rig dang ldan pa'i byis pa rnams bsags nas/ de'i nang nas khyi'u nyi shu rtsa gcig mi lo bcu pa las mi rtan mi gzhon pa dbyug gu dang chu tshod kyis blo
gros brtags te/ dang po gzhung 'dzin pa dang / de nas don spyod pa dang / mthar mnyam par 'jog pa la brtags te/ rab 'bring tha gsum du phye/ rab bdun/ g.yog bdun/ blo
gros mgo 'don pa bdun re ste/ nyer gcig pha ma la nor gyis blus/ rgyal khrims btsan pas mi gtang dum btub nas/ de dag la gser phye phul gyis bshang te bskur nas/ rgyal po
la phyag rten dang / chos kyi zhu rten gyis la/ rgya gar nas nyi zla ltar grags pa'i 'dus pa rnam gnyis dang / shar phyogs nas paNDi ta dharma pa la dang / kha che nas rin
chen sde la sogs kapa la gser la ma rtseg par mang du phul la spyan drongs las shog ces bka' bsgos te brdzangs pas/ bcu dgu tshad pas shi/ zhang zhung gi lha bzo rin chen
bzang po dang / spu rang gi lo chung legs pa'i shes rab gnyis las/ bod la gzhan tshos phan thogs pa ma byung / lo chen lo chung gnyis mkhas par gyur te/ de gnyis kyis
dang po kho char du byon/ sgra legs par sbyangs/ tsan dha ha ri la la gsang ba 'dus pa lugs gnyis zhus/ 'jig rten gsum snang gi dkyil 'khor du lan bdun zhugs pas mos pas
me tog 'jam dpal la phog lo tsA ba gnyis rgya gar du lan gsum byon no/ /rnal 'byor gyi rgyud de gnyis nyid 'dus pa dang / dpal mchog dang po dang / rdo rje rtse mo dang
/ rdo rje 'byung ba dang 'grel pa ko sa la'i rgyan zhus/ dpe cha rnams bsnams nas byon/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la sngags pa gsar mar gyur nas/ chos kyi 'phongs pa la/ de gnyis
nyid 'dus pa la byas/ ko sa las gtan la 'bebs byed byas/ chos ma yar bu yar bsdebs nas bshad do/ /de'i dus su mnga' ris stod du/ lung bshad shin tu dar bar byung ba la/
rdo rje 'byung ba tsan ches nas ma rdzogs/ gtsug dgu yod pa thos nas lha khang rnying pa kun tu dpe cha 'tshol du btang bas ma rnyed/ lo chung la bsdus pa gsungs pas/
rdo rje chos kyi sgrub thabs che ba lha bcu gcig pa dang / chung ba lha bcu gsum pa dang / phyis 'grel pa stod 'gyur nas gtsug dgu byung nas/ gnyis po de rnams mes bsregs
so/ /lan gsum pa la dpal mchog hong kong can bsgyur ro/ /gsum pa la rngog rin chen rgyal mtshan yul dbus pa/ lte ba gung thang du bcad pa lo tsA ldab ldib shes pa gcig gis
bal yul bhi ha ri'i gtsug lag khang nas rnyed zer nas/ stod 'grel rdo rje 'byung ba/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ gtsug dgu'i cho ga'i dkyil 'khor cho ga rnams kyi rgya dpe
rnams phul nas/ gsang ba 'dus pa ye shes zhabs lugs kyi dbang bskur dang chos rnams zhu zer bas dgyes te/ de ma thag gnang nas/ ghang gha dar ra dang / bi dza ya shrI bha
dra dang / su pa shI ta dang / dharma shrI mi tra dang / ka ma la gu ta dang / g.ya' a nan ta dang / ku ma ra shrI dang / dznyA na shrI dang / a ma ra dza Na Da dang / sha
ya shrI dang / dha na shI la dang / de rnams kyis dpe cha bsnams nas byon no/ /maya yul sum

mdo'i chos 'khor nya mar/ paNDi ta budha si shan tam ba dang / dhudha pa la dang / ka ma la gub ta gsum dang mjal nas zhu ba phul/ chos mang po bsgyur/ de'i dus su gtsug dgu
dang / rdo rje 'byung ba la sogs pa dkyil 'khor cho ga rgyas pa thams cad bsgyur/ lo chen lo chung gnyis ka phyi nang gnyis la mkhas shing / khyad par du skye ba snga ma'i
bag chags sad pas/ gsang sngags la mchog tu mkhas so/ /so so thar pa'i tshul khrims/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa/ gsang sngags kyi dam tshig dang / lung nod pa yang
mdzad nas/ kha che paNDi ta dharma pa la dang / pra ta ka ra warma dang / padma ka ra warma dang / mkhas pa mang po spyan drangs/ rang gi slob ma lo tsAb rma dge ba'i blo
gros dang / mar lo rig pa'i gzhon nu/ cog ro ting 'dzin bzang po/ tshul khrims yon tan/ chos kyi blo gros/ shAkya blo gros la sogs pas kri yog gi 'grel pa dang / de gnyis
'dus pa'i don gyi 'grel pa/ a pa dha ras bkrol ba'i sangs rgyas gsang ba'i lugs dang / ko sa la'i rgyan zhes bya ba stong phrag bzhi pa/ shAkya bshes gnyen gyi bshad lungs
dang / kun dga' snying po'i de kho na nyid snang ba'i bshad lugs stong phrag brgya pa dang / dpal mchog dang po'i stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa dang / rgyud rgyas pa'i
bshad pa rdo rje rtse mo/ khams gsum rnam rgyal mgon po kun snang / ngan song sbyong ba thams cad gsan/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa/ gzhan rgyud sde chen
po bzhi'i bka' yang mang po bsgyur/ /dus phyis sngags mtshan nyid kyi 'gyur 'go thams cad lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos btsugs pa yin te/ mkhas pa chen po de ni zhang zhung
gi yul du sku 'khrungs pa yin/ gdung ni lhur bzo bya ba yin/ rigs rje rigs/ chung chung nas dad pa dang shes rab che ba/ 'jam dpal gyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ thugs rus
dang spyad pa gzhan bas che ba ste/ sku tshe stod la kha che dang rgya gar du rab tu sbyangs pa chen po mdzad nas bka' bstan bcos tshad med pa bsgyur nas bshad rgyud kyi
bstan pa dar bar mdzad/ sku tshe smad la dben gnas gsum gyi sgo la zangs dang dngul dang gser gsum gyis yi ge bris nas/ bdag mi dge ba'i bsam pa skyer 'jug na/ bdag lung
du ma bstan gyi/ bsam pa skyer 'jug na/ bdag dge ba'i bsam pa kho na mi skye bstan gyi/ bsam pa skyer 'jug na/ bdag dge ba'i bsam pa kho na mi skye na/ rdo rje 'chang gis
bdag gi mgo bo 'gems par gyur cig ces bya ba'i gi ge btab nas/ thugs dam thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor gyi dam bca' brtan po mdzad nas sgrub rgyud kyi bstan par dar zhing rgyas
par mdzad do/ /paNDi ta dza na dha la zhus nas/ gso ba rig pa'i yan lag brgyad pa rtsa 'grel dang / nag po rgyud gsum la sogs pa mang po bsgyur ro/ /rin chen bzang po la
slob ma log 'tsho ma 'dres pa bzhi ni/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab spu rang pa/ bkra pa gzhon she/ kyi nor nya na/ snya nam gnya' nang pa mang nang du bzhugs pa gung shog
brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ de bzhi la gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab kyis thug go/ /des sgur nyi ma lo'o/ /des kun tu dar ro/ /lha bla ma dang / lo chen gyi sku tshe'i gzhug
la srong nge'i sras lhang nge gzigs bkra shis ldes/ kho char du dngul sku chen po bzhengs so/ /paNDi ta

sum pa shrI spyan drangs so/ /lha lde la sras gsum/ lha byang chub 'od/ zhi ba 'od/ lha zhal/ lha zhal gyis rgyal srid chos la phul nas rab tu byung ngo / /de gsum gyis lha
khang bzhengs pa spu rang du tsha ba sgang / gu ger mang nang dang sde gsar yil chog ru la sogs pa'o/ /khong gis lo tsA yang mkhyen/ zhi ba 'od kyis kha che'i paNDi ta dha
na ta la spyan drangs nas dus 'khor bsgyur/ skad gsar bcad byas/ rdo rje 'phreng ba bsgyur/ des rwa dge slong blo gros snying po dang / rab zhi bshes gnyen/ khyung po
chos kyi brtson 'grus/ mtshur la dkar si ti/ gro ser dkar shAkya 'od/ mang nang grags 'byor shes rab/ mtshur dbyig rgyal mtshan/ sum pa dar ma yon tan/ spu rigs pa tshul
khrims gzhon nu la'o/ /lha lde la sras gsum/ byang chub 'od/ zhi ba 'od/ 'od lde dang gsum yin/ byang chub 'od kyi thugs dgongs la/ chos thog tu chosartsa 'grel sdeb/ rang
gi shes rab kyis gzhal nas/ slob dpon mi dgos zer zhing gzhung la rtsal bshad byed/ nyams len ni shin tu zhan pa'i dus/ bod kyi rgyal khams la phan gdags par dgongs nas
phan gang che bsams pas chos lung med la byin rlabs mi 'byung bas/ paNDi ta mkhas pa bzang ba zhig spyan drangs na phan che bar 'dug bsams pas/ gung thang pa tshul khrims
rgyal ba la sogs pa mi lnga la gser srang gsum cu rtsa gnyis dang / gser ling pa gcig bskur nas pho nyar btang ste/ nyang stod stag tshal ba/ khum bu yul pa lo tsA ba/
rgya brtson 'grus seng ge la dpon bgyis nas/ rgya gar shar phyogs za hor gyi yul na rgyal po dge ba dpal gyi sras rgya gar yul dbus ma ga dha rdo rje gdan na/ 'bri ka ma
la shi la dang / dpal na len dra'i gtsug lag khang du rig pa'i gnas lnga la legs par sbyangs pa/ mkhas pa chen por gyur pa/ theg pa gsum gyi brtul zhugs la legs par gnas
pa/ sgrub pa phun sum tshogs la nan tan mdzad pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gnyis pa lta bu rje di baMka ra shrI dznyA na zhes bya ba/ 'bri ka ma la shi la na/ paNDi ta sum
cu rtsa gnyis bzhugs pa'i nang nas mkhas shing grub pas brgyan pa de la/ bod kyi btsad po byang chub sems dpa'i slob dpon du zhu rten phul nas zhus pas/ ngas brtag pa gcig
bya gsungs nas/ do kyer gyi lha khang gi mkha' 'gro mas kyang bod la phan thogs par lung bstan/ jo mo sgrol ma'i zhal nas kyang u pa si ka dge bsnyen gcig la brten te
bod kyi sems can la phan togs pa gcig yong bar 'dug ces lung bstan/ bod du byon par zhal gyis bzhes nas/ bal yal thang bhe ha rir bzhugs/ gnas brtan la spyod bsdus gsungs/
de nas mang yul du 'phags pa'i drung du cung zhig bzhugs/ de nas gung thang du byon/ de nas spu rang du byon/ bsu ba byas/ tho ling du byon nas/ jo bos lha khang gi lha
rnams la bstod pa mdzad do/ /der chags phab/ lha byang chub 'od kyis zhu rten du gser srang drug brgya phul nas thog mar zhu ba gsum byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la
rim gyis 'jug pa lags sam/ cig car du 'jug pa lags sam/ phyi nang gi khyad par gang lags/ dge slong gi rdo rje sngags kyi dngos dbang gong ma rnam gnyis blang du rung mi
rung zhus pas/ rim gyis yin gsungs nas/ lam rim lam sgron mdzad/ skyabs 'gro dang / lta ba bka' btags kyi phyag

rgya bzhi yod med yin/ gsang ba shes rab ye shes ni tshangs par spyod pas blang bar mi bya zhes gsungs so/ /skye bo mang po bsnyen gnas la bkod/ mang por sgrub pa'i gdams ngag
gnang nas yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs pa mang du byung / lo chen rin chen bzang pos ma hA paNDi ta shrI dznyA na spyan drangs nas khong gi gzims khang na/ sngags kyi dkyil
'khor gyi bris sku mang po yod pa dang / sgo mdun na bcom ldan 'das mi g.yo ba'i bris sku bzhugs pas de la thugs rje dbyings kyi bstod pa mdzad de phyag mdzad/ de nas dkyil
'khor gzhan la yang bstod pa sho lo ka re mdzad nas phyag mdzad do/ /de sngon rin cen bzang pos jo bo rje phyag ma mdzad chos ma zhus/ nga sngon rgya gar na slob gnyer
byed tsa na/ jo bo ban chung chung ngu gcig 'dug da lta mkhas pa chen po byung 'dug dgongs nas/ 'bul ba dang bsnyen bkur chen po mdzad/ de'i rjes nas phyag rtse sprod
mdzad/ chos zhus lo tsA yang lo chen rin chen bzang pos mdzad do/ /brgyad stong pa rtsa 'grel la sogs pa mang po bsgyur ro/ /dbu ma rtsa 'grel/ gsang 'dus lugs gnyis sgrub
thabs mang po dang / btags pa dug mtsho che chung / sprul pa khye'u chung gi zhu lan mthong ba spyan gyi me long / gso dpyad/ chos skyong mgon po lcam sring dang / nor
lha'i sgrub thabs mang po bsgyur/ gzhan yang gsang sngags kyi brda dang / sbas pa dang / mdo sde drang nges dgongs pa ma shes par sgra'i rjes su 'brangs nas/ sbyin pa dang
tshul khrims la sogs pa thabs kyi tshul la bslab mi dgos/ sems nyid gcig pu rkyang 'ded kyis sangs rgya zer ba dang / blo mi sbyong bar theg pa chen po yin zer ba dang
/ so so thar pa'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa med par dbang skur dam tshig thob zer ba dang / chags sdang dang sdig pa sna tshogs spyod cing / sgrib pa mi
'gos zer ba'i log chos smra ba thams cad lung dang rigs pas tshar bcad/ lha btsun pa byang chub 'od dang / lha bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang 'gyur
mang po bcos/ mang po bsgyur/ bstan pa la phan btags so/ /lha bla ma'i sku tshe smad la spu rang pa zhang chung btsun gsal shes rab la bka' bsgos nas/ yul dbus kyi paNDi
ta shrI badzra bo dhi dang / lo tsA ba gyi cho zla ba 'od zer gyis dus 'khor dang / ma rgyud 'ga' bsgyur ro/ /mnga' ris stod du lo gsum bzhugs/ de nas bod kyi ston pa
mang po byon/ 'brom gyis gtso byas gabus gtsang gi mi che ba rnams kyis dbus su byon par zhu ba phul/ spu rang gi rgya zhing dgon po lo chen gyi gnas su/ gser sil ma zangs
gzhong gang phul te/ mar spyan drangs nas byon/ jo bo dbus na bzhugs pa'i dus su/ lha bzo ba kha che gzhon nu shes rab skyabs bya ba mkhas pa dpon g.yog gnyis byon no/
/lam du 'gro ba mang po la byin rlabs mdzad/ bsam yas su phyags phebs/ chos mang po gsungs/ de nas lha sa dang yer pa par byon/ snye thang 'or du bzhugs nas skal ldan 'brom/
stong tshab nam mkha'/ de'i slob ma dang / yol rdo rje dbang phyug rngog legs she/ khu sher brtson/ 'gar ston dge ba/ chag khri mchog dpal dgon pa gong ma ba/ lung a
mes byang chub/ rnal 'byor pa rdo rje shes rab/ 'dzeng sgom dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ g.yo rdzong rnal 'byor/

zhang sna chung ston pa la sogs pa skal ldan mang po smin par mdzad do/ /jo bo'i sras kyi thu bo 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ de'i slob ma rin po che sku mched gsum
la sogs so/ /dge bshes blo chung phul byung pas slob bu ma bsten par sgrub pa kho na mdzad do/ /po to ba dang / spyan snga rin chen gnyis las/ slob bu so sor byuung ba
la/ bka' gdams gzhung pa ba dang / man ngag pa gnyis su grags so/ /de gnyis las mched pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen ngo mtshar can mang po byung ngo / /khams pa lung pa dang /
glang ri thang pa dang / rgya lcags ri gong kha ba dang / sha ra ba dang / sha po sgang pa dang / brag brgyab pa dang / nam 'bar ba dang / ja yul ba dang / sne zur ba dang
/ ka ma pa dang / mtha' bzhi brtson 'bar ba dang / stod lung pa rin chen snying po dang / rin chen sgang pa sogs dbus su mang po byon/ gtsang du yang / yul la ba dang /
ram sdings ma ba dang / chu mig pa dang / snar thang pa dang / rje lung pa dang / don mo ri ba dang / de rnams la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / /jo bo dbus su
bzhugs pa'i dus su mnga' ris pa'i lo tsA ba ting 'dzin bzang po/ rgya gar kha cher 'khrungs pa/ rab tu sbyangs pa/ yul ma ga dhar mkhas par grags pa paNDi ta tsan dha ra
hu la chen po spyan drangs nas/ rtog ge rig pa tshang ma'i bstan bcos phyogs glang gi mdzad pa kun las bsdus pa dang / de'i don gyi 'grel pa/ chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i
sde bdun bsgyur ro/ /dge bshes mtha' dge mthong la sogs pa rnams kyis shes rab rgyas par mdzad do/ /de'i dus su rgya gar kha che dzi na mi tra yang / lo tsa ba zu dga'i
rdo rjes spyan drangs nas/ khyung po grags se dang / 'brom ston rdo rje rin chen dang / dwags po dbang rgyal la sogs pa chos nyan pa'i dus/ rngog legs pa'i ses rab kyi
tsha bo rngog blo ldan shes rab kyis mnga' bdag rtse lde'i drung du phyin nas paNDi ta surya shrI spyan drangs/ bdag kha cher 'gro bar zhu zhus pas/ mnga' bdag gi zhal nas
paNDi ta mkhas pa 'di rnams la chos nyon gsungs pas/ cis kyang kha cher 'gro ba zhu zer te ma nyan/ gser brdzangs te btang / kha cher brtol tsa na/ rgyal po dang yul mi
kun na re/ paNDi ta mkhas pa kun bod yul du bzhud/ khyed ci byed zer nas/ paNDi ta gzhan med dam dris pas/ 'bring po 'dra yod zer bas/ skal ldan rgyal po la tshad ma rgyan
bslabs/ des kyang ma chog ste/ paNDi ta go mi 'chi la byams pa'i chos lnga cha lag dang bcas pa dang / byams pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ dul ba'i sde/ mchog gi sde/ rnam
par snang mdzad las/ seng ge bzang po'i 'grel chung dang / spyod phyogs la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang phra mo mang po la sbyangs/ 'bum phrag gsum pa las rnam nges la sogs
pa'i tshad ma rnams bslabs/ 'bum phrag gsum pa bod du spyan drangs nas byon/ rtse lde'i sras dbang ldes 'gyur gyi yon bdag byas te chos rnams bsgyur ro/ /mar byon gtsang
du/ ar byang chub ye shes la sogs pa mang du 'phel lo/ /paNDi ta dang gangs pa she'u blo gnas 'gran pa yang mdzad do/ /paNDi ta yang mnyes nas bod bzang zer/ 'bro shes
rab 'bar/ 'dul dkar gzhon nu tshul khrims/ se dmar ba dang / 'bre mgur ba la sogs pa byung / de'i dus su rngog

gi 'gyur bzhugs tsa na dbu ma'i bstan bcos ni/ ka cog rnam gnyis dus kyi bka' ni chad/ sngar tshad ma lha'i zhor la byung ba'i rang rgyud shar gsum la sogs pa yod kyang / don
gyi de kho na nyid ma shes pas/ lo tsA ba pa tshab pa nyi ma grags kyis kha cher lo nyi shu rtsa gsum sbyangs te/ paNDi ta mchog tu mkhas pa shi na ka warma zhes bya ba
spyan drangs te/ dbu ma rig pa'i tshogs dang / de'i 'grel pa rnams dang / rgyal po la gdams pa gnyis dang / zla ba grags pa'i bzhed pa rab tu rgyas pa tshig gsal dang /
stod skor gdams dang / bstan bcos phra mo mang po bsgyur ro/ /pa tshab kyi slob ma dar ma yon tan grags/ de'i slob ma pha bong kha pa/ de'i slob ma rma bya byang brtson
no/ /des kun tu dar bar byas so/ /de nas de rnams kyi bar skabs su zhang zhung pa rgyal ba shes rab kyis paNDi ta pra dznyA pa la sdom pa blangs nas/ de nas bal por byon
nas/ bram ze 'dul 'dzin pre ta ka la 'dul ba lag len zhus/ phyis bod du kha che'i mkhan po dznyA na shrI la lung dang / so so thar pa dang / 'grel pa 'dul ba bsdus pa gsan/
kha che'i paNDi ta chen po bhu dha shan ti ba la/ dge 'u lo tsA bas bsgyur nas sum brgya pa rtsa 'grel gsan/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu mchog gis spyan drangs pa'i paNDi ta ya
thang he ha ra la bslab pa'i gzhi mdo rtsa gsan/ de ltar yas mas su khyung po skyong la sogs pa rab tu byung nas/ de'i slob ma smon 'gro 'dul 'dzin/ de'i slob ma hu ber
rgyal ba'i shes rab/ tshul khrims blo gros dpal 'byor zhing mo bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' zla ba rgyal mtshan la sogs su 'phel/ 'dul ba stod lugs zhes grags/ chos mngon
pa mdzod ni/ sngon ka cog zhang gsum nas brgyud pa bar skabs su stongs pa la/ dus phyis smri tis 'gyur gsar mdzad de nas thog ma'i bshad pa rnams mchims rgyud kyis dar bar
mdzad/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten/ mchims brtson 'grus bla ma/ de'i sras rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras sgom pa/ de'i sras don grub rgyal/ de'i sras rig 'dzin/ de la sras bzhi
ni brtson 'grus seng ge/ chos kyi seng ge/ cho ga zhang btsun no/ /de'i sras blo gros seng ge'o/ /mngon pa kun las btus ni glang dar gyi dus su bskungs nas bzhugs so/ /byams
pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ blo brtan/ gang ba spel/ dzi na mi tra/ shi len dra bo dhi/ cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan/ ka ba dpal brtsegs/ sna nam gyi ban de ye shes sde/
ka cog gi slob ma sbas rgyal ba'i ye shes/ gru mchog gi ye shes/ se btsun gzhon nu/ dhar mi yon tan g.yung drung / khu ston shes rab brtson 'grus lha sdings pa yin no/
/ra khri bzang 'bar dang / rgya rgyal bu tshul la/ de gnyis kyis rong ngur smrig pa brang ti dar ma snying po dang / ye 'byung gnyis/ des bhan rog la bshad de/ lugs gnyis
su grags so/ /mngon pa'i me ro bslangs lugs so/ /de nas de'i skabs gcig tu/ chos 'khor gyang gi mkhan po shAkya gzhon nu dang / slob dpon se jo sras ye shes brtson 'grus
kyi slob ma 'brog mi shAkya ye shes dang / stag lo gzhon nu brtson 'grus dang / ling shAkya brtson 'grus dang gsum bcad dpyad pa che bas/ mkhan slob kyis gser mang po brdzangs
nas/ bstan pa'i rtsa ba 'dul ba yin/ bstan pa'i snying po phar phyin yin/ bstan pa'i nying khu gsang

sngags yin pas slobs la shog gsungs nas bal yul du phyin/ 'brog mis bal po hang du dkar po shan ta bha dra bya ba dang / pham thing ba la 'jug so zhus/ rgya gar du song / nga'i
bla ma mkhas pa nyan ti pa can rgyugs gsungs/ stag 'brog gnyis po bsdongs la zur du song / rdo rje gdan du phyin pas stag lo dad pa skyes skor ba 'ba' zhig byed/ de'i
dus su ma ha dha'i mkhas pa sgo drug bya ba yod/ shar gyi sgo srung rata?n a ka shan ti pa/ de la tshad ma la gtsor 'dri ba mang / lho sgo na ngag gi dbang phyug grags
pa bya ba/ sgrol ma la chos gsan pa de la khyad par du sgra tshad sngags dang lung la sogs pa 'dri ba mang / nub sgo na shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros sbas pa la/ khyad par
du mu stegs kyi grub mtha' la gtso bor 'dri/ byang sgo na jo bo na ro pa la theg pa chen po la lung nod pa dang 'dri ba mang / dbus ka chen gnyis ni rna chen rdo rje dang
/ dznyA na shrI mi tra gnyis yin te/ ka chen gnyis zer yang / gzhan bas yon tan ni che rgyu med zer/ 'brog mi thams cad mkhyen pa shan ti pa'i drung du sbyangs pa cher
byas/ sgra thang log thad klog la shin tu mkhas par gyur to/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi dge slong dpa' bo sde la sogs grub thob 'ga' bsten/ bod du byon nas mkhan slob dang
mjal/ lo rgyus brjod pas mkhan slob na re/ 'brog mi la mkhas pa chen po byung 'dug pas/ stag lo tsA ba khyed sher snying rgya gar klog las mi shes pa ci yin gsungs/ 'brog
mi kho ka ba li khyer kyin de shed du phag tu 'gro yin 'dug stag lo na re/ ngas ma hA bho dhi mthong bas dad pas skor ba byas gsol ba btab nas tha snyad ma bslabs zer/
sku btsun pa dang bsam pa bzang bas/ phyis mkhan slob kyi gdan sa byas/ dge 'dun gyi sde chen po 'phel stag tsho zhes gcung du e'i lha khang chen po bzhengs te/ paNDi ta
gha ya dha ra byon nas/ gser srang bcu bdun phul te/ kyai rdo rje rgyud gsum zhus nas/ ma rgyud bcu bzhi dang / ra li'i rgyud nyi shu rtsa bzhi dang / rgyud sgrub thabs
'ga' dang / lo paN gnyis kyis bsgyur grub pa dang / gdams ngag gi ngo yang 'ga' re gsungs nas zhu ba 'dam kha bya gsungs/ lo re la gser srang brgya brgya 'dod/ de stair na
bya gsungs pa khas blangs/ lo gsum bzhugasra gdams pa lam skor rdzogs par gnang / gser phul bas mnyes te/ rgya gar du gshegs so/ /de nas a tsa ra dmar po byon/ gsang sngags
pho nya myur ba'i lam zhus nas bsgyur te gser mang tshad phul lo/ /de'i rjes la 'gos khug pa lha btsas kyis/ 'brog mi'i drung du slob gnyer la phyin pas/ snod rtog byas
pas ma mgu/ nga rang gi phyag rten thongs zer nas rgya gar du song / paNDi ta grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa bdun cu dang mjal/ sbyangs pa cher mdzad/ mthar bla ma
'gos dang / shangs pa ra bo che gnyis kyis/ sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po dang / nag po zhabs dang / rgya gar mngon shes can dang / za hor btsun mo can rnams la rgyud dang sgrub
thabs man ngag rnams zhus/ de nas bod du byon/ gser mang po btsal nas rgya gar du byon/ paNDi ta sprin gyi shugs can dang mjal/ spyan drangs nas byon nas gsang sngags
rnams zhus/ de nas bod du byon/ gser mang po btsal nas rgya gar du bla ma med pa'i rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa

la klu sgrub yab sras kyi bzhed par bkral ba'i lugs rnams zhus/ gzhan yang dpal rdo rje gdan bzhi cha lag dang bcas pa dang / dgyes pa rdo rje rgyud gsum dang / 'khor lo bde
mchog rgyud sgrub thabs dang / sgyu ma chen po rgyud 'grel sgrub thabs dang bcas pa dang / thig le rgyud drug dang / sgrub skor sde bdun dang / gshin rje nag po 'char ka
dang / chos skyong mgon po gdams ngag tu gab pa mang du bsgyur/ gsang sngags pa rgyud kyi bshad nyan shin tu rgyas par mdzad/ mkhas pa'i phul du phyin/ grags pa chen po
thob/ der rjes nas mar pa lho brag pas 'brog mi la bal po'i skad dang yig tshang bslabs/ chos zhu byas pas nor mang po 'dod zer nas/ 'dir bya rlags glags mi 'dug zer nas
bal yul du song / bal po spyi ther pa la 'jug sgo zhus/ rdo rje gdan bzhi mnyan/ chos skyong lha mo dur gsol zhus/ lo gsum nas rgya gar du byon/ paNDi ta ye shes snying
po la gsang ba 'dus pa gsan/ sgyu lus 'od gsal gyi gdams pa zhus/ de nas pu la ha rir byon/ bla ma na ro paN chen dang mjal/ sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur/ dgyes
pa rdo rje'i rgyud gdams pa dang bcas pa ma lus par gsan/ dpal me tog mdangs 'phrog gi dgon par/ rje mnga' bdag mai tri pa dang mjal/ dpal dgyes pa rdo rje la bstod pa glu
blangs dang / sems dngos po'i 'dug tshul gtan la 'bebs pa'i gnad phyag rgya chen po la sogs pa zab kyis gsan no/ /de nas ha la par ba tar dug mtsho khol mar dpal zhi ba
bzang dang mjal/ ma hA ma ya zhus/ sgyu ma sum rgyud kyi gdams pa ma lus par gsan/ lar snga pyi la rgya gar du lo bcu gsum bzhugs/ bod yul gsar ma'i lo tsA ba la gdams pa
che bar grags/ de'i slob ma ni mes ston tshon po/ 'tshur ston dbang nge rngog chos sku rdo rje/ klog skya dge bzang / mar pa mgo legs/ a bo mthu chen la sogs pas 'gro ba
yang dag pa'i lam la bkod pa lags so/ /de'i dus su kha rag gi gnyos 'byung pos rgya gar du byon/ mkhas pa rnams kyi zhal 'grims/ sgra bsgyur shin tu mkhas/ khyad par bla
ma grub thob bha ling a tsarya dang mjal/ gshin rje gshed dgra nag rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud sgrub thabs gdams pa/ dgyes pa rdo rje dang 'jal dpal gyis mtshan yang dag
par brjod pa dang / gsang ba 'dus pa dang / chos sde chen po zhus/ gsar ma'i jo sras thob pa'i mi bzhi'i dang po ni/ gnyos lo tsA ba yin skad/ de'i sras gnyos rdo rje/
gnyos gzi brjid/ gnyos rin chen rgyal po'o/ /gnyos kyi rgyud bya bar grags so/ /rgya gar du sasnga phyi la lo nyi shu bzhugs so/ /paNDi ta gnyis spyan drangs/ gsang ba 'dus
pa ye shes zhabs kyi lugs/ lung dang mthun pa'i chos bcu bzhi dang / gnyos yon tan grags kyis gshin rje nag po skor gsum dang / chos skyong gur mgon po la sogs pa mang
po bsgyur ro/ /gnyan chung lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyis rgya gar du phyin/ paNDi ta jo bo ma ti la 'jam dpal zhus/ bsnyen zhing bsgrubs pas sgra dang / snyan ngag dang
sdeb la tshegs pa med par mkhas par gyur nas/ paNDi ta mang po bsten/ sbyangs pa cher mdzad/ paNDi ta su na ya shrI spyan drangs te/ gsang ba 'dus pa ye shes zhabs kyi lugs
su bkral ba/ rgyan dang tho che chung la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang gzungs phran mang po dang / rje

btsun sgrol ma dang / chos skyong gi sgrub thabs dang / phyag na rdo rje bye spu dang drag po mngon spyod kyi las dang / rdzas sbyor nag po'i las mang po bsgyur ro/ /stod nas
bla ma zangs dkar lo tsA bas kha che dang rgya gar du byon/ kha che rin chen rdo rje la sogs pa bsten/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel cha lag dang bcas pa shin du rgyas
pa rnams dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rgyas pa mang po dang / phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa'i chos bcu/ rgyal po'i chos gnyis
te/ rnam sras la sogs pa mang po bsgyur ro/ /zangs dkar gyi dbon po lo tsA ba gzhon tshul khrims kyis kha che legs smon ka ra la zhus nas/ slob dpon bha ba lhas mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus/ dkyil 'khor cho ga sbyor kha chen po cha lag dang bcas pa dang / me lce 'phreng rgyud/ rdo rje be con gyi rgyud/ rdo rje gsang ba'i rgyud la
sogs pa bsgyur/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen grwa pa mngon shes can la gdams nas dar bar mdzad do/ /de'i dus bod du lo paN byon tshad bla ma gra pas 'degs shing 'bab pa lags skad/
de'i dus lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung grags kyis rgya gar dang kha cher phyin/ chos mang po btsal/ bal po dza hUM dang gnyis kyi 'gyur mang du mdzad/ gzhan yang lo tsA
ba nyi ma dngos grub kyis mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i lugs rnams dang / sgeg pa rdo rjes mdzad pa'i lugs dang / 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad
pa'i lugs rnams bsgyur ro/ /gzhan yang shi'u lo tsA ba rdo rje lha dang / lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang pos paNDi ta su ma ti kir ti/ bal po thugs rje chen po spyan
drangs nas/ mtshan brjod kyi 'brel pa gsar ma dang / phyag na rdo rje drag po gsum 'dul gyi rgyud snga phyi dang / de'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dza wa ris mdzad pa dang / gzhan
yang lo tsA ba'i chos drug tu grags pa bsgyur ro/ /paNDi ta a bha ya ka ra ghu pa ti'i slob ma/ lo tsA ba yong zhes zhe gsal ba gnyis kyis 'bro shes rab grags dang /
dge bsnyen shes rab brtson 'grus kyis dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdo rje 'phreng ba bsgyur ro/ /mi nyag lo tsA ba rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas dpal dus 'khor 'grel chen cha
lag dang bcas pa dang / khams pa shes rab 'od zer dang / mi nyag kun dga' grags dang / steng pa dkar 'od tshul khrims 'byung gnas kyis 'khor lo bde mchog rgyas bsdus dang
chos skyong mgon po phyag bzhi pa/ las mkhan bya rog gdong can dang bcas pa'i rgyud sgrub thabs dang bcas pa/ zab pa'i gdams pa mang po dang bcas pa bsgyur ro/ /de'i slob
ma khams pa dga' blos kyang grub pa thob bo/ /gtsang pa lo tsA bas kyang 'gyur gyi zhus dag rnams byas so/ /khams pa ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags pas paNDi ta a mo gha
badzra spyan drangs nas/ bya spyod kyi rtogs pa mang po dang / phyag len dang sgrub thabs brgya rtsa brgyad/ bla med kyi dkyil 'khor cho ga bka' zab pa mdzad cing bsgyur
ro/ /rlan glan chung lo tsA ba dang ong po phu ru lo tsA ba dang gnyis kyis don yon zhags pa bsgyur ro/ /yar 'brog do ri mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi dbang phyug gis kyang
dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi sgyur sgrub thabs rgyas pa cha lag mang po bsgyur ro/ /des ze ba blo ldan

seng ge la bshad de dar zhing rgyas par byas so/ /gnyal pa skor ni/ ru pa lo tsA ba shes rab dpal dang ye shes grags kyis rgya gar du lan gsum phyin/ paNDi ta grub thob ka
ro ba dang mjal nas gshin rje gshed dgra nag dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud/ sgrub thabs dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ 'grel pa/ de rnams kyi cha lag dang / gzhan yang phyag
rgya chen po'i rgyud lnga grub rting / snang ba sde bdun/ nges pa sde bdun/ mtshan brjod shes rab snying po/ de rnams kyi gdams pa/ mgon po dpon g.yog gsum pa de rnams
bsgyur ro/ /leng lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyis kyang dgra nag dang rdo rje phag mo la sogs pa bsgyur ro/ /'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyis kha che zla mgon spyan
drangs nas dus 'khor 'grel pa che chung sngags dang bcas pa bsgyur ro/ /de nas 'jam dpal zab don la sogs pa mang du bsgyur ro/ skyo lo tsA ba 'od 'byung gis kyang dpal rdo
rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud snga phyi/ dkyil 'khor gyi cha ga sgrub thabs rnams/ gsang sngags gnad kyi gdams pa rnams bsgyur ro/ /lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar dang / lo tsA
ba shes ston byang chub 'bar dang / lo tsA ba ma chings yon tan 'bar dang / lo tsA ba bar ston thos pa dga' bzhis bal yul nas paNDi ta rgya gar phyag na'i zhabs la gtugs
nas/ a ma si la/ 'khor lo sdom pa bcu gsum gsum pa'i dkyil 'khor du zhugs te/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs mdzad/ snying po skor la do ha skor gsum dang / grub skor
sde bdun/ mai tri pa'i chaso chung bcu gsum dang / rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa la sogs pa bsgyur/ de nas rgya gar phyogs nas/ 'brog mi'i sras po lo tsA ba
tsad tsa ye shes rdo rje spyan drangs nas/ bod du byon pa la/ spu rang pa grags mchog ses rab dang / zhal mnga' ring mo dang / khyung po lo tsA ba dang / bod kyi ston pa
mang pos gdams pa zhus/ mthar gtsang shod pa la/ phyag rgya chen po rdo rtsa bcu gsum/ kha thor rgyab rten dang bcas pa gsungs so/ /jo sras ye shes rdo rjes kyang 'gyur 'ga'
byas so/ /lo tsA ba klog skya shes rab brtsegs dang ye shes brtsegs kyis kyang 'jam dpal gyi man ngag dang / 'khor lo sdom pa'i rgyud kyi 'gyur bsgyur ro/ /lo tsA ba
kyi bye ma lung pa dang / lo tsA ba 'phags mchog gis 'jam dpal gyi 'grel pa dang / rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi sgrub thabs 'ga' bsgyur ro/ /mal gyi blo gros grags pa dang
/ yu cher lo tsA ba dang gis sgrol ma'i chos skor bsgyur ro/ /rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis rwa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed dang / phag mo mngon 'byung dang / de'i cha lag mgon
po mngon 'byung la sogs pa bsgyur/ sgo lo tsA ba bsod nams tshul khrims grags kyis kha che gzhon nu 'bum spyan drangs nas sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud/ a bhi dha na la sogs
pa'i rgyud/ sgrub thabs man ngag mang po bsgyur ro/ /sman lung khu khang gi ser tsha dang spyal lo tsA ba bsod nams rgyal gyis kyang dgra nag gi 'grel pa la sogs pa bsgyur
ro/ /lo tsA ba g.yung drung 'od kyi paDa Di ta a sho shrI bya ba lo lnga brgya zhes pa gcig spyan drangs nas/ 'bring mtshams kyi lo tsA ba zhang shes rab bla ma dang
/ zhang mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyis gshin rje nag po skor gsum bsgyur ro/ /yar lungs kyi khu lo tsA ba dge

bsnyen ne tso dang / khu bsod nams 'bar dang / spu rang lo chung dang / yar lungs pa sma ra ser po can dang gsum gyis/ hang du dkar po spyan drangs nas/ rdo rje phag mo'i gzhung
man bsgyur/ de rjes la spyal lo tsA ba kun dga' rdo rje bal yuul du lan gsum byon nas dgyes phag thams cad rdzogs par bsgyur ro/ /'dzims pa lo tsA bas phag mo'i sgrub
thabs bsgyur ro/ /chag lo tsA ba dgra bcom dang / zha ma lo tsA ba seng ge rgyal pos gzhung man ngag mang po bsgyur ro/ /gzhan yang bod la thugs rjes gzigs nas lnga brgya'i
thams cad mkhyen pa rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas pa/ paNDi grub pa thob pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dam rgya gar dang / paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang /
a tsa ra dmar po can dang / rgya gar gsang spyod pa dang / kha che ye shes gsang ba dang / bla ma zangs gling ba la sogs pa gdan ma drangs par 'gro ba'i don la byon nas/
gdul bya skal ldan rnams smin pa dang / grol ba'i lam la bkod do/ /gong gi lo tsA ba de rnams kyis dka' ba ji ltar spyad pa dang bla ma gang yin pa dang / chos yon du gser
ji ltar phul ba dang / bsgyur ba'i yon bdag su yis byas pa dang / rjes 'jug gi slob ma ji ltar byung ba la sogs pa yod de/ yi ge mang bar 'gyur bas ma bris so/ /de ltar
bsgyur ba'i chos sde la/ lha bla ma'i sku drin la brten nas/ bdag nyid chen po rin chen bzang po nas bzung ste/ de rjes bsgyur ba thams cad dang / 'gyur snga ma ka cog yan
chad kyis bsgyur ba rnams dang / cung mi 'dra ba 'dug pa rnams la bltos nas bod kyi mi rnams kyis gsar ma zhes grags te ming du chags so/ /de ltar sngar 'gyur rnams la
rnying ma zhes grags te/ snga 'gyur gyi bsnyen sgrub dang bshad pa'i srol rnams ji ltar rgyas na/ glang dar gyis chos bsnubs tsa na/ chos dang gang zag bskungs nas bzhugs
pa'i zhang dznyA na'i slob ma dpal chen dgu la/ mkhar chen dpal gyi dbang phyug sog po dpal gyi ye shes/ shud pu dpal gyi seng ge/ gnyan chen a tsa ra dpal dbyangs/ 'o
bran dpal gyi gzhon nu/ rlangs chen dpal gyi seng ge/ bran ka dpal gyi yon tan/ dar rje dpal gyi grags pa/ cog ro dpal gyi dbang phyug rnams dang / srin po ri'i lang lab
byang chub rdo rje dang / snubs nas mched de/ snubs sangs rgyas rin po che la/ zhang dznyA na'i sems sde bco brgyad/ bdud rtsi bam brgyad cha lag dang bcas pa la/ rgyud gsang
ba ye shes 'khor lo/ 'grel pa brtag 'grel/ lung bam po brgyad pa/ man ngag sgron gsal/ lag len yang khol nying khol bu don ma la sogs te bdud rtsi'i skor/ nam mkha'i
snying po'i yang dag dar rje'i sgyu 'phrul/ nam mkha'i snying po dang dznyA na'i mdo byang / bka' brgyad/ rdzongs 'phreng / ba su dha ra'i gdams pa/ che btsan skyes nas
brgyud pa'i dgongs pa 'dus pa la sogs lung gi mdo lnga / kun byed ma bu dgu skor/ sems phyogs rnams mnga' ba mkhas pa bcu gcig gi bka' babs 'dus pa de gtsang du byon/ ye
shes dbang phyug dang 'jal nas/ so la lta ba sgang dril nas bshad pa ni/ sems sde bco brgyad lnga snga 'gyur sngar lngar bsdus nas gsungs/ nam mkha'i snying pos yang dag
rgyas bsdus/ phyis shel dkar bzas zhus pa dang / nam snying gis mkhar chen dpal gyi ye shes brtsegs la brgyud/

des rlangs dpal brtsegs la/ des cog ro dpal gyi dbang phyug la/ des mkhan po dpal gyi mchod gnas ma la/ des so ye shes dbang phyug la/ des sras skal po/ des sras dbang gi gtsug
gtor/ des sras rgyal po/ des sras chos ye des ra dza 'bar/ de ltar rgyud pa rnams dngos grub ma chad pa ste/ yang sems so lugs zhes grags/ snubs sangs rgyas ye shes
kyis gshin rje dmar nag la sogs drag sngags rnams dang / bskyed rdzogs sgrub thabs dang / sems phyogs/ chos skyong / nor lha/ bzo/ rtsis/ gso ba/ 'phrul 'khor rnams khu lung
yon tan rgya mtsho la gnang / des sras ye shes rgya mtsho/ sras pad ma dbang rgyal/ des chen po dajam dpal/ des ye shes gzungs/ snubs hUM la thug bar nus pa dang ldan
te/ de'i rgyud pa dang / de rnams las gyes pa'i slob bu rnams mthu rtsal dang ldan pa 'ba' zhig go/ /bdud rtsi ni/ bi ma las dznA na la/ des sog po dpal gyi ye shes la/
des sangs rgyas ye shes des sru legs pa'i sgron ma/ des sras gzhon nu snying po la/ des skor thung shes rab ye shes/ des slugs shes rab 'phan/ des rgya 'bar skyid la gnang
ste bdud rtsi rgya lugs zhes grags so/ /de ltar so/ snubs/ sru/ sba gor dang bzhi yod de/ snubs sangs rgyas ye shes kyi thugs kyi sras bzhi bya'o/ /gzhan yang snubs dpal
sdong rin po che/ khyung po dbyig gi rin po che/ stong tshab byang chub rin po che ste/ rin po che gsum la sogs te bdun dang gze sgom dang / rong thung ma la sogs pas/
sangs rgyas ye shes rin po che'i chos rgyud dar bar byas so/ /'jam dpal sku'i sgrub pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'/ longs sku gshin rje gshed po/
sprul sku 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ 'jam dpal bstan pa/ ro langs bde ba'i rdo rje/ rgyal po bha he ta/ drang srong da bi sha ta/ sras bha ha te/ dge slong ma dhe ma/ a tsarya
de ba ha sa/ bha ra ha sa/ las kyi rdo rje/ bde ba'i myu gu/ des pad ma sam bha ba/ des khri srong lde btsan/ rdo rje gnod sbyin/ nam mkha'i snying po/ dznyA na ku ma
ra/ snubs sangs rgyas ye shes dang lnga la gnang / des yon tan rgya mtsho/ des ye shes rgya mtsho/ pad ma dbang rgyal/ chos kyi snying po la sogs pa la brgyud do/ /gsang
sngags rdo rje phur pa ni/ rje pad mas mchims shAkya pra ba la brgyud pas/ phur pa mchims lugs su grags so/ /sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms la brgyud pas sna nam lugs grags/
mkhar chen bza' la brgyud pa la jo mo lugs su grags/ jo ma la lang lab byang chub rdo rjes zhus pas phur pa lang lab mar grags/ lcam mchod gnas ma'i lugs la phur pa lcam
lugs su grags/ mkhar chen dpal gyi dbang phyug dang / shud pu dpal gyi seng ge la phur pa rtsa thung du grags/ lang lab kyi nag gyen 'gyel la brgyud pa phur pa kyi lugs su
grags/ rje pad ma/ bal po shI la mnya?dzu/ bi ma la gsum gyi dgongs pa bsdebs nas/ rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan la gnang bas/ phur pa rnam gsum rgyal po skor du grags/
bi ma las dznyA na la gtad pa/ des 'o bran dpal gyi gzhon nu la gnang / 'o bran gyis phur pa sham sngon can/ mdo lugs lu gu brgyud du grags/ gzan yang pad ma dbang chen
rta mgrin gyi skor/ rta mchog rol pa cha lag dang bcas pal/ sangs rgyas dbang gi rgyal po/ pad ma las kyi sems

dpa'/ slob dpon na ga mnya?dzu na/ a de ba/ shing gi lha mo 'od mtshungs ma/ mkhan po inda?r bho dhi/ ma ha ra dza/ lha'i rgyal po de ba ra dza/ g.yu sgra snying po la gdams
pa dang / zhu ba po dge slong ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs la gdams pa gnyis la dbus lugs khams lugs gnyis su grags/ de gnyis kyi slob ma 'di na gsal ba'i rdo rje dang
/ rtse rom rgyal ba'i yon tan/ beg yon tan legs pa/ g.yas chen legs pa'i blo gros/ smra ston dpal gyi rgyal po/ sog ston ye shes blo gros/ sog po dpal gyi dbang phyug
'tshal chung shes rab rin chen yan chad rab tu byung ba yin/ de nas sngags pa yin te/ so ston 'byung gnas byang chub/ so ston smyon pa/ so ston pad ma sangs rgyas/ so pad
ma seng ge/ so ye shes 'bar/ so pad ma 'bar/ so chos kyi rin chen rab tu byung ba grub pa brnyes pa byung ngo / /'tshal chung gi slob ma gnyan ston byang chub shes rab la
sogs pa rim par brgyud do/ /gsang ba sgyu 'phrul gyi bka' dang / mdo lung sems phyogs rnams sangs rgyas ye shes kyis thugs sras bzhi la dar bar mdzad de/ thabs kyi rgyud
gsang sngags sgyu 'phrul gyi brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang pa/ rgyal ba rigs lnga/ thub chen longs spyod/ rdzogs pa'i skur bzhengs nas/ rgyal sras rigs gsum la gsungs/
de'i nang nas don sdud pa po phyag na rdo rjes/ skal ldan rgyal po dza/ dge salnga ku ku ra dza/ dge slong ma kun dga' mo'i sprul pa inadra bho dhi dang gsum la bshad/
des sras mo gho ma de byi/ dge slong ma kun dga' mos sangs rgyas gsang ba/ sangs rgyas zhi ba la ste lugs gcig yin/ gho ma de byis/ klu sgrub/ des rdo rje bzhad pa/ des
rdo rje bzhad pa/ des rdo rje hUM mdzad/ bi ma la/ shan ti garpa/ ka ma la shI la/ pad ma 'byung gnas dang lnga la bshad de/ rgya gar gyi brgyud pa'o/ /bod du lo tsA ba
snyags ye shes gzhon nu dang / rin chen mchog gis bsgyur nas/ des gtsug ru rin chen gzhon nu/ des zhang rgyal ba'i yon tan dang / dar rje dpal gyi grags pa la/ zhang gis
ye snya yod tan bzang po/ des zhang byung chub 'byung gnas/ des za rig ye shes 'phags la/ des snubs bla chen byang snying / yol lcags glang sngon can/ phug rog byang bsod/
spyal ser tsha ma ru dang bzhi la bshad do/ /de bzhis re khud kyi snyan dbang grags/ des zur po che shag 'byung ngo / /yang lugs gcig la/ rma los dar rje dpal grags/
des snubs/ des so ye dbang / ngab thung chung chub rgyal mtshan/ skor thung shes rab ye shes/ ra thung ye shes tshul khrims/ nyang shes rab mchog ye shes 'byung ba/ zur po
che'o/ dgongs pa 'dus pa dang / lung gi mdo lha'i brgyud khungs ni/ sangs rgyas sku gsum gyis/ srin po blo gros thabs ldan/ lha tshangs pa blo gros dad sel/ klu 'jog po
blo gros rgya mtsho/ mi li tsa byi blo gros rab zhi/ gnod sbyin skar mda' mdong blo gros/ sangs rgyas rigs gsum gyi nang nas gsang bdag gis/ dge bsnyen li tsa byi dang /
rgyal po dza/ rgyal po u pa ra dza gsum la gdams/ rgyal po dza yis/ shA kya spu ri dang / sras mo gho ma de byi gnyis la/ des ti ra ma ti/ bzhad pa'i rdo rje/ des hUM ka
ra/ des ka ma la shI la dang / di na mi tra dang / sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang gsum pos/ chos blon bde ba dang /

mkhan po chos rgyal skyong dang / chos kyi byang chub dang / dharma rakShi ta dang bzhi la bshad de rgya gar gyi brgyud pa'o/ /bod du lo tsA ba che btsan skyes kyis mdo khams
mkhas pa bzhi la gtugs nas bsgyur ro/ /de rjes nas dharma rakShi ta dang dharma bo dhi gnyis la lo tsA ba snubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin lapo ches zhus te gtan la phab/
des thugs sras bzhi la/ bzhis spa gor blon chen 'phags pa la gnang / des dan yon tan mchog des begs gsal ba'i byang chub/ des rgya blo gros gzhon nu/ des zhu bsod nams shAkya/
des rgya shAkya mchog des bla chen zur po che la'o/ /sems phyogs a ti'i brgyud tshul ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang pos rang dang tha dad mi mnga' ba rigs lha'i ngo bo
dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la/ des don sdud pa po tha dad med pa rdo rje snying po la'o/ /des yang sprul dga' rab rdo rje/ des 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ des gdung rabs nyi shu rtsa
lnga la sogs pa mkhas pa lnga brgya la brgyud/ des paNDi ta shrI sing ha/ des lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na/ des rim par g.yu sgra/ dznyA na/ sog po dpal gyi ye shes/ snubs
yon tan rgya mtsho/ ye shes rgya mtsho dang / pad ma dbang rgyal/ nyang chen nyang chung / zur po che la'o/ /bod kyi brgyud pa'i bka' babs lha rje chen po 'ug pa lung pa/
zur po che shAkya 'byung gnas la/ slob ma rtse mo bzhi ni/ lta dgongs sgom sgrub kyi rtse mo zur cung shes rab grags pa/ bshad pa'i rtse mo bres kyi mi nyag 'byung grags/
mkhyen rgya'i rtse mor gyur pa ra za gling pa'i zhang 'ges chung / phyag bzhes kyi rtse mo shangs mtsho nya'i bzang sgom shes rab rgyal po/ rtse lkog brgyad ni/ dge bshes
lo rog bram ze rtsags bla ma/ sum pa blo rgya/ lo chung shAkya rgyal po/ rta ro/ sum pa dbang tshul/ bla chung 'od skyid/ chags ston nam mkha' 'o/ /gzhan yang sgom chen
pa brgya rtsa brgyad byung ngo / /lha rje rgya bo pa zur cung shes rab grags pa la/ thugs sras bka' babs bzhi ni/ bdo'i bka' babs shab lung nag skyed lung yang khyeng
bla ma/ sems phyogs nyams len gyi bka' babs/ ra sa gong bu'i skyo ston shag yes/ sgyu 'phrul gyi bka' babs g.yas ru cu bar ba glan shAkya bzang po/ phyag bshes man ngag la
mkhas pa'i bka' babs nag mo ri gseb pa dha ti jo shag go/ /gdung 'dzin brgyad ni/ bskyed rdzogs gsum gnyis la mkhas pa nyang ro chu sgo'i ma thog byang 'bar/ shangs nya
tshal ba/ glan shAkya byang chub/ sna nam pa/ snubs ston bag ma/ shangs bram pa/ rtsags shag rin/ ne ser gyi skyo ston chos seng / dbus pa sangs rgyas rdo rje/ la stod byang
pa/ shud ston zla grags/ stag sde ba/ rtse rom byang chub dpal lo/ /bde gshegs rgya bo ba'i slob ma la mnga' ba/ 'gos bya tsha/ meg chung dbang seng / spyal ston yon
tan rgyal po/ 'gar ston rgu ru/ lo ston shes rab rgyal po/ de rnams cha phran yin/ de rnams la sgro phug pa shAkya seng ges zhus/ de la slob ma nag po bzhi/ me bzhi ston
bzhi ring dang lnga / co rog pa brgyad la sogs rgya dpon pher ba stong phrag thon nas/ bka' sde zur tsho zhes grags te/ skor re la gdugs thogs kyi dge bshes stong nyis brgya/
rnga thogs kyi ban de stong lnga brgya re thon te gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi me ro bslangs nas/ mdo sgyu

'phrul sems phyogs kyi bstan pa dar bar mdzad/ gsang sngags ma mo'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas mngon rdzogs rgyal po che mchog he ru kas/ don sdud pa po gnod 'dul lha
la/ des me ri 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang du phra men rgya mtsho ma la brgyud/ des ri bo ma la yar/ blo ldan rgyal po da la/ des tho gar yul du/ li tsa dri ma med pa la/
des o rgyan gyi ri nag po theg bsdus su/ za gad skya rings blo ldan la/ des dbu rgyan gser mig tu/ khye'u mad dri chung ba la/ des dur khrod bsil ba tshal du/ pad ma 'byung
gnas la bshad/ gye gye ru tsan dan gyi gling du yang shinti garbas/ srid pa bems/ 'bum tig bdud mo bkol byang / mkha' la skar tshogs/ srid pa stong gi dra ba rnams bshad
do/ /rdzogs pa chen po/ bka' ye shes gsang rdzogs rgyud lnga dang / zab ma gter gzhung nyer gcig dbang bskur ngo sprod dang bcas pa lo tsA ba chen po bai ro tsa nas g.ya
sgra la/ des sba sgom rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rim par/ rab snang lha'i dbang phyug gru mchog gi ye shes/ nyang shes rab 'byung gnas/ nyang rdo rje snying po/ nyang ri khrod
pa chen po zag med kyi sku brnyes pa 'dar ston dge 'dun/ gnyan lcags byil pa/ spa se ras pa/ rtse phrom par lhas pa/ glan rdzing 'bring ba/ glan shAkya mgon po/ dbas
grub pa sogs pa la gnang nas so sor dar zhing rgyas par mdzad do/ /snyags dznyA na'i slob ma/ mdo smad pa 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa thams cad mkhyen pa a ro ye shes
'byung gnas kyis gdams pa phyi skor/ nang skor gsang skor/ gzer ka che 'bring la sogs pa gsungs te/ zangs ka mdzod khur/ kha rag gru sha rgyal bu/ ya zi bon ston/ gru gu
glog chung / kong rab mtsho/ ltam dar ma/ 'tshe me byang chub rdo rje/ sba sgom bsod snying / kha rag sgom chung / ba rang sgom chen/ ma gcig nyang mo/ des dam pa shAka
rgyal la brgyud do/ /kun byed rgyal po ma bu dgu skor ni/ bai ro tsa na/ g.yu sgra/ gsang ston ye shes bla ma/ a ro ye shes/ sba sangs rgyas mgon po/ sba rakShi ta/ ya zi
dar ma shes rab/ nyang ston pra ba/ mar pa khrom rgyal/ de la slob ma bzhi/ lho brag gi mar pa shes rab 'od/ gtsang pa'i gsum pa dbang tshul/ dbus kyi nag rog ston pa/
jo mo sgeg 'phreng ma dang bzhi/ de bzhi la 'bri mtshams lung pa can pa/ shangs pa nag pos zhus zer te brtag lang tsha dar ma shes rab bsod nams/ de la dha tsha hor po/ dam
pa shAka rgyal po/ sems phyogs khams lugs zhes grags so/ /skor ston shes rab grags pa la skor lugs su grags/ gtsang gi mkhas pa chos kyi bzang po la rong lugs su grags/
bram ze'i lugs ni/ paNDi ta bi ma la dang / nyang ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur/ des gter du sbas/ 'dan ma lhun gyi rgyal mtshan gyis bton/ des shangs pa lce chung ye
shes rgyal mtshan la gdams/ des phyogs kun tu dar ro/ /rdzogs chen bla med ni/ bi ma las ka cog rnam gsum la gdams/ nyang ting 'dzin bzang pos gter du sbas/ des bsam yas
kyi zhang chen po dang / rje btsun seng ge dbang phyug la gdams/ des lce sgom nag po/ des skal ldan yo so la gdams/ bshad pa dang phyag len gyi chos rnams rgyas so/ /de
nas sgrub brgyud kyi gdams pa rnams ni/ dam pa sangs rgyas las brgyud pa/ bka' babs rnam gsum ste/ snying po

rma so kam gsum du grags pa dang / rje btsun seng ge las brgyud pa nas zha ma lcam sring dang / zhang dgon pa ba la/ gsang sngags lam skor ba dang / dam pa rin po che nas rgyud
pa/ a ma lab kyi sgron ma la sher phyin gcod kyi gdams pa/ sras rgyud blos nas nyams rgyud gnyis la sgrub po mang du byon/ rje btsun chen po mi la'i thugs kyi sras bzhi
ni gung thang gi rdo rje grags pa/ lcem lung gi ngan rdzong ras pa/ rta mo'i 'bri sgom/ mdo phra'i se ban/ phrom zhu yas kyi dar ma dbang phyug zhi ba 'od/ gnal ba nyi
sgom bsod nams rin chen/ sngags skyes lhan gcig sgron me/ sgrub pa ba bdun ni/ ras pa sangs rgyas skyabs/ ras pa rtsa yu ba/ ras pa rdo rje dbang / gshen sgom ras pa/ rong
chung ras pa/ 'khar chung ras pa/ gyen sgom ras pa dang bdun no/ /thugs zin drug ni/ dwags po lha rje/ ling gor cha ru/ 'od stong dge 'dun/ skyo stan shag gu/ dam pa
rgyags phug pa/ 'bri than bkra shis/ slob ma grub thob pho bco brgyad byung / grub thob ma dgu byung / rje btsun chen po'i thugs sras kyi dam pa rje dwags po rin po che la/
slob ma ston sgom sgrub pa po sum brgya lhag pa zhig byung / dbon po dwags po sgom tshul la/ zhang g.yu brag pa/ de las rtogs ldan mang du byung ba ni/ tshal pa skor zer/
rje dus gsum mkhyen pa ste/ grub thob dbu se las/ song brag pa khams pa/ shangs kyi rmog cog pa dang / dge slong la yag pa dang / 'ol ka chos g.yung / de'i slob ma sgyer
sgom zhig po/ de'i slob ma khams sgom/ chu bzang ba/ dmar sgom ma mdzod ma ba/ 'u brag pa/ rje dwags po'i sras mchog phag mo grub pa la/ slob ma mthar thug bzhi ni/ shes
rab kyi mthar thug stag lung pa/ bsod nams kyi mthar thug 'bri gung pa'o/ /gzhan yang sgrub pa dang rtogs pa ldan pa mang du byung ngo / /rtogs ldan mi nyag sgom rin/
grub thob nya rang se bo/ g.ya' bzang pa/ skal ldan ye shes seng ge/ khro bu ba rgyal mtshan rin chen kun ldan/ gtsang pa ras chung / gtsang pa jo sras/ rtogs ldan gtsang
pa rgya sgur/ byang chub sems dpa' skor sgom la sogs pa mang po dar bar mdzad do/ /de dag gi slob bu/ yang slob/ slob ma pa rnams la dwags po bka' brgyud du grags so/ /rje
btsun dam pa dmar por grags pa'i grub thob byon/ de la slob ma chung gsum dang brgyad tshan gsum la sogs pa byon/ sprang po'i ded dpon mdzad de 'gro ba mang po grol bar
mdzad do/ /de dang dus mtshungs par sbas shAkya brtson 'grus la slob ma rdza phor ra'i brgyud pa/ bka' babs bzhi dang / gdung 'dzin brgyad dang / thugs sras bzhi dang
/ nye ba'i sras brgyad ces pa byung / dus de tsa na zar stag sna'i zhang po rgya 'thing las rnal 'byor smyon tsho dang / rtsi ri'i 'o la 'ba' su las rnal 'byor byar med dang
/ ru mtshams kyi rgyal ba sro kha 'thams las me chu go log pa dang / dbus kyi she mo rgya lcam las/ glong nag po rgya 'dzam/ de la 'phur tsho zhes zer te/ shangs kyi
rnal 'byor stag tsho dang / rji lung gi mgos tshos kha bskangs pa 'di rnams la/ rnal 'byor nag po drug zer/ khong rang gis sgrub brgyud bzang por byed/ lo paN gyi rjes su
'breng ba rnams ni khong ngi de rnams rdol chos su byed/ gzhan yang bod yul 'dir mkhas pa/ bzang ba/ grub thob/

'khrul zhig rtogs ldan ji snyed byon na yang / rnam thar rnams bris na spro ba skye bar 'gyur mod kyi/ bsam gyis mi khyab pas 'dir spros na ye ge mang bar 'jigs pas ma bris
so/ /bstan pa phyi dar gyi lo rgyus zhabs su btags pa'o/ /rgyal po ngo bo nges tshig dang / /dbye ba mtshan nyid bsdus don lnga / /ngo bo spyod tshul gzhan las 'phags/ /nges
tshig dbang po'i bdag po dang / /rgyal po zhes byar gcig pas te/ /dpa' zhing rang gi yul 'khor bsrung / /gzhan rnams zil gyis gnon pa mtshan nyid yin/ /bsdu na rnam
pa gnyis yin te/ /'jig rten dag las 'das pa dang / /ma 'das rgyal po rnam pa gnyis/ /'das pa slob dang mi slob gnyis/ /slob pa sa bcur gnas pa yin/ /mi slob sangs rgyas rnams
la grags/ /ci 'byor 'jig rten las rgyal phyir/ /ma 'das rgyal po bem rig gnyis/ /rig pa mi ma yin pa dang / /mi'i rgyal po rnam pa gnyis/ /mi ma yin pa'i rgyal po dang
/ /mdor na lha gnas man chod nas/ /yi dwags dmyal ba yan chad du/ /dbang byed thams cad rgyal po yin/ /mi'i rgyal po zer lags kyang / /gling gzhan gsum na so so'i sder/
/dbang bskur rgyal por bshad pa ste/ /'dzam gling 'di'i rgyal por mang / /mi rigs sum brgya drug cu la/ /dbang byed rje dang mtshungs par bshad/ /de dag brjod kyis mi rdzogs
pa/ /yongs su grags pa'i rgyal po gsum/ /gdung rgyud bskos dang glo bur gsum/ /gdung rgyud mang pos bkur ba pa/ /kha gcig 'di ltar gsum du 'byed/ /bskal pa dang po'i
rgyal po lnga/ /de nas 'khor los sgyur rgyal bzhi/ /de yan chad la gdung rgyud zer/ /mdor na mang pos bkur ba nas/ /ngar du 'khor lo can bzhi nas/ /shAkya rigs yan chad
kun yin te/ /sgra gcan 'dzin gyi gdung chad nas/ /srid pa'i skye rgyun chad par bshad/ /bskos pa'i rgyal po sde bzhi ni/ /rgya gar chos kyi rgyal por gcig /rgya nag gtsug
lag rgyal por gnyis/ /stag gzig nor gyi rgyal por gsum/ /ge sar dmag gi rgyal por bzhi/ /de bzhi'i ming dang bskos lugs dang / /ston pa gang gis byas pa dang / /chos lugs
las spyod zas nor gos/ /sgra rnams mi mthun so sor yod/ bskos pala'i rgyal po phyogs bzhi po/ /rgya gar chos kyi rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /byin rlabs bum pa glang po'i sna
la bzhag /de yis su la dbang bskur de la bsko/ /rgya nag gtsug lag rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /shel gyi skas btsugs su thar de la bsko/ /ge sar dmag gi rgyal por bsko ba ni/
/phyogs bzhir dpag chen bzhi yis mda' 'phangs pas/ /mda' bzhi dus gcig sus zin de la bsko/ /stag gzig nor gyi rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /rin chen gling nas nor bu sus lon de
la bsko/ /rgya gar rgyal po sngon sbyangs las 'phro can/ /sangs rgyas chos kyi snod du rung bas na/ /rgyal ba shAkya tub pas ston pa mdzad/ /rgya nag gtsug lag dpyad kyis
'dul gzigs nas/ /mkhyen rab bdag po 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis/ /gab rtse sum brgya drug cu'i ston pa mdzad/ /ge sar dmag gi rgyal pos 'dul gzigs nas/ /'phags pa nor 'dzin
sku sprul ston pa mdzad/ /rgya gar chos kyi rgyal pos ma rig mun pa sel/ /rgya nag gtsug lag rgyal pos legs nyes me long ston/ /stag gzig nor gyi rgyal pos dbul ba'i sdug
bsngal sel/ /ge sar dmag gi rgyal pos phyi'i dgra dpung 'joms/ /glo bur bod kyi rgyal po yin/ /spyir na bod

kyi rgyal khams na/ /dbang byed rig rim pa bcu gnyis kyis/ /tha ma rgyal phran bcu gnyis kyis/ /sil ma bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis dang / /rgyal phran drug cu rtsa bzhi sogs/ /dbye
ba mang du yod gyur kyang / /bka' drin can gyi rgyal po med/ /glo bur spur rgyal btsad po yin/ /mdor bsdus kyang sa nas cung zad bstan/ /'di la spyad lugs rnam pa gsum/
/bon po'i yi ge lha dge can/ /gnam nas babs zhes bsgrags pa'i lugs/ /rje nyid gsungs pa phyag rgya can/ /rgya gar rgyal phran rgyud par 'dod/ /de nas gleng pa'i zhib rtsing
gsum/ /rkang rkyang pa gcig rgyud rtsi ba yin/ /de ming za gzhug rgan rabs can/ /khug pa yum sgam smos pa la/ /'dab ma dgu rtseg can zhes bya/ /yun po rgyas bshad yin
pal/ /zing po sna tshogs can du grags/ /de la rkyang pa brtsis pa la/ /rje rgyal gnya' khri btsan po'i sras mu khri btsan po/ /de'i sras ding khri btsan po/ /de'i sras so
khri btsan po/ /de'i sras khri ye btsan po bya ba yin/ /de'i sras khri yer bya ba yin/ /de la grim gum btsan po 'khrungs/ /de tsho gnam gyi khri bdun yin/ /gri gum btsan
po'i sras gsum la/ /che dag gnya' sha khri nyang po spyugs/ /nyang rgyal thams cad de nas gyes/ /'bring po nya bya khri spu bor spyugs/ /kha cig 'di la stod btang steng
zer/ /gdung la ru las skyes kyis de spyan drangs/ /spu lde gung rgyal bya bar grags/ /spu rgyal btsan por de nas grags/ /de'i rgyal sras sho legs dang / /de sho legs dang
phu ru legs/ /'bring shar legs shes bya ba dang / /i sho rno legs i sho legs/ /de rnams rim bzhin chig rgyud yin/ /de la legs drug de ltar zer/ /i sho legs kyi rgyal sras
la/ /gza' nam zin te bya ba yin/ /de'i sras lde 'phrul po dang / /de'i sras lde snol nam/ de'i rgyal sras lde rgyal te/ /de dag sde bzhi rgyal po zer/ /dgu rtseg can na
lde brgyad zer/ /lde brgyad po'i sras ni/ /to re long btsan bya ba yin/ /de'i sras khri btsan rnam nal yin/ /de'i sras khri btsan rgyal dpung btsan/ /de'i sras thog rje
thog btsan yin/ /de'i sras tho tho gnyan btsan yin/ /de lnga btsan lnga dag tu bshad/ /tho tho gnyan zhal rgyal sras ni/ /'dus nas zla bo btsan de'i sras/ /'brong gnyen lde'u
bya ba yin/ /de'i sras stag gu gnyan gzigs yin/ /de'i sras gnam ri long btsan yin/ /de'i sras srong btsan sgam po yin/ /de'i sras gung srong gung btsan yin/ /de'i sras
mang srong mang btsan yin/ /de'i sras 'dus song mang po rje/ /de'i sras khri lda btsan la/ /khri srong lde btsan 'khrungs pa yin/ /da'ei sras che dag mu ne btsan po yin/
/yum gyis gsol drangs grongs pa yin/ /'bring po mu re btsan po yin/ /sna nam bsad pas mtha' ru spyugs/ /chung dag sad ne btsan po yin/ /dgu rtseg can nas sras bzhir 'dod/
/sad ne btsan po'i sras gsum la/ /che dag ral pa can gyi gdung nas chad/ /chung dag gtsang ma mon du spyugs/ /'bring po glang dar sras gnyis la/ /yum brtan 'od srungs
smos pa gnyis/ /yum brtan rgyud pa dbu rur chad/ /'od srungs la ni dpal mgon btsan/ /de la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa la/ /che shos skyid lde nyi ma mgon/ /spu rang stod du
gshegs pa yin/ /mnga' bdag rtse lde la sogs yin/ /chung dag bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal/

/de'i sras bkra shis brtsegs pa mgon/ /de'i sras kho re/ de'i sras srong nges rim par ro/ /byung tshul mkha' ltar rgya che bsam yas pa/ /bdag blo'i sbrang bus mtha' rtogs mi
nus kyang / /mkhas pa'i gsung gi 'dab gshog la brten nas/ /yin lugs byung tshul nam mkha'i phyogs de mthong / /mkha' la rlung ltar 'dzin chags kun las grol/ /zla ba nya
ltar yon tan gsal la rdzogs/ /sa chen ji bzhin yon tan malus gzhi/ /snga rabs 'das pa'i rnam thar 'di la dad/ /nor bu rin chen rin thang med pa yang / /blun po rnams la
rdo dang mtshungs zhes grags/ /skal med ngan pa'i spyod la goms rnams kyis/ /byung tshul 'di la cir yang mthong mi 'gyur/ /sa la gser dang shing la tsan dan dang / /rta la
