cang shes mi la 'khor los bsgyur/ /mchog tu gyur cing dkon pa ji lta bar//lo rgyus 'di mchog 'di la mos pa dkon/ /yon tan rgya mtsho thub bstan rin chen mdzod/ /thugs rje
nyi ma 'gro ba kun la snyom/ /lo rgyus rin chen mkhas pa kun gyi rgyan/ /brgyud ldan skyes mchog dam pa rnams la yang / /dad gus sems kyis zhabs la spyi bos 'dud/ /ma
dag skye bo kun spyod 'dam las brgal/ /sangs rgyas dgyes pa'i lha spyod dpal gyis mdzes/ /rigs ldan bung ba'i tshogs rnams tshims mdzad pa/ /byang chub 'di ni gsal ba'i me
tog yin/ /yon tan rgya mtsho'i lo rgyus me tog pad mos blangs/ /shes rab lag pas dran pa'i skud pa la/ /tshig sdeb rin chen me tog 'phreng ba 'di/ /rang sems dad pa'i mgo
la tod du bcings/ /'di bkod dge ba dri med kun tu dag /rnam thar rin chen 'phreng ba de bzhin du/ /rgyal sras 'dus pa'i chos kyi dga' ston la/ /rnam mkhyen rgyal ba'i
drung du 'tshog par shog / dang po bka' bsdu ba gsum gyi yon bdag chen po gsum gyis mdzad pa nas/ gzhan yang / rgya gar dang / kha phye dang / o rgyan dang / li yul dang
/ khu sen dang / bal yul dang / rgya nag dang / 'jang yul dang / mi nyag yul la sogs pa rnams su'ang / chos dang ldan pa'i rgyal po/ rgyal po ma skyes dgra dang / chos rgyal
mya ngan med pa dang / chos rgyal gzugs can snying po dang / chos rgyal ka ni ka la sogs pa mang pos/ rang rang gi yul du dam pa'i chos dar zhing rgyas par byas so/ /de
bzhin gshegs pas nges par lung bstan pa/ /byang phyogs kha ba can gyi ljongs 'di ru/ /'dul dka'i skye bo dpag med srid las sgrol/ /rigs gsum mgon dang byams mgon 'phags
la sogs/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi/ /thugs rje'i rnam 'phrul bod kyi rgyal po ni/ /mes dbon rnam bzhi la sogs rim pas byon/ /'das dang ma 'ongs kun
tu khyab pa yis/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rnam thar bsam mi khyab/ /byang chub sems dpa'i rnam thar bsams pa/ /nyan thos rang rgyal rnams kyi rnam thar bsam yas so/ /dgra bcom
rgyun du zhugs kyi rdzu 'phrul dpag yas so/ /rig pa 'dzin pa rnams kyi mthu stobs dpag tu med/ /gang zag khyad par 'phags pa'i bsod nams bsam las 'das/ /rkang gnyis gtso
bo de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang la gang 'dul de la der ston pa/ /thub pa chen po'i drung du rnam par sprul/ /'gro drug mun sel 'gro ba 'dren mdzad pa/ /mgon po spyan ras
gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha dbang brgya byin tshangs pa chen po dang / dbang phyug chen pos kyang ni 'gro

ba 'dul/ /mdzad pa mtha' yas khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal blon byang chub sems dpa'i rnam thar 'di/ /mgo rtsa bsgrigs pa 'di rnams gang gis byas/ /lho brag dpal gyi dgon
par gcig pu ru/ /sems can kun la brtse ba'i thugs rje can/ /bdud ratsi zhig po zhes pa'i 'khrul zig dam pa dang / 'jig rten mgon po rin po che/ /rgyal ba'i sras po mthu
bo chos ye yis/ /yang yang bskul ma btab pala'i ngor byas nas/ /bka' gter mang po ji snyed legs gzigs nas/ /nyang ban nyi ma 'od zer bsam pa dwangs pas byas/ /rang bzo ra
chod ras gcod spangs te yi ger bkod/ /de yang rgyal po chems kyi yi ge 'di yang / mthong ba dang / thos pa dang / rnyed par bka' dka' bas te/ ji ltar bka' dka' na/ sngon
bsod nams bsags pa'i gang zag ma yin pas mi thos/ /dad pa yang mi skye/ skal ba dman pas mi go/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro mas lung bstan pa ni/ dpal ldan a ti shas ra sa 'phrul
snang gi gdung bar nas rnyed pa rgyal po ranams kyis mdzad pa'i bka' rtsis chen po dang / btsun mo rnams kyis mdzad pa'i dar dkar gsal ba'i me long dang / blon po rnams
kyis mdzad pa'i zla ba'i 'dod 'jo rnams dang / yang jo bo rjes/ bsam yas arya pa lo'i gling nas dang / gra pa mngon shes can gyis bton pa dang / la ston gnyag ston grub
thob dngos grub kyis thugs rje chen po'i gtsang kang rta mgrin gyi 'og nas bton pa dang / nyang ral pa can kho bos bsam yas dang / khra 'brug dang / mkho 'thing lha khang
nas bton pa'i gter yig dang / dus phyi dar gyi lo rgyus rnams dang / bod dang sngags dang mtshan nyid grwa sa kun la mkhas pa rnams kyi snyan du grags pa'i gsung dang
/ gtam rgyud ma nor ba dang / rgyal rabs gsang ba chos lugs dang / sgrag pa bon lugs/ rkyang pa/ khug pa/ sbags sbas pa gsum/ rgyal blon gab pa/ yun po gser skas dgu pa/
zings po sna tshogs can/ de rnams kyi don dang ston pa'i gsung rab las byung ba dang / bla ma dam pa rnams kyi bka' lung dang / rgyal po'i gsung rab las byung ba dang /
bla ma dam pa rnams kyi bka' lung dang / rgyal po'i bka' chems/ so so skye bo'i bden pa'i ngag smra ba rnams/ 'dul ba dang / bstan bcos dri ma med pa las byung ba dang /
de rnams kyi nang nas bsdus te/ nges don gtan la phab/ lhad ma bcug sgro ma btags/ skur ba ma btab/ gra chag zur nyams su ma btang / bka' mdo rgyud rnams dang / bstan bcos
man ngag kun nas gtan la legs par phab ste bsdebs pa lags so/ /'gal 'phrul nyes pa'i dri ma mi bdog pas/ /'di la rtsod pa byed 'gyur mi dad na/ /log rtog phrag dog can
la bzod par gsol/ /lhag chad ma snyems dag nyes pa mchis srid na/ /chos kyi spyan ldan mkhas pa rnams dang ni/ /ye shes spyan ldan tshogs la bzod par gsol/ /bstan pa'i gsal
byed lags pas gzigs mo mdzod/ /rmongs pa brtol col ma smra mdo rgyud ltos/ /snga rabs makas pa rnams kyang de ltar gsungs/ /'phags pa'i sprul pa mnyam med 'gro ba'i dpal/
/chos kyi rgyal po 'gran zla med pa yis/ /sprul pa'i rgyal po mdzad pa yongs su grags/ /mi nub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan che po yi/ /yon tan mang po brjod palar ma nus
kyang / /rigs rgyud dbon sras rim pa zhib par bkod/ /kun dang thun mong ma

lags rtsis su mdzod/ /dkon na rin thang che ba bod kyi lugs/ /deng sang dus na gna' gtam rnying par rtsi/ /bka' dang mdo rgyud gong ma'i gsung la smad/ /gzu lum ra chod ras
gcod dam pa'i chos la smra/ /sdig dang sdug la dge ba'i rtsa bar re/ /kye ma 'khrul rtogs can la ji ltar bgyi/ /'on kyang bshes gnyen rnams kyi bka' drin gyis/ /theg chen
chos la nges shes skyes pas na/ /sems can don du 'di bris bsod nams kyis/ /kun kyang dge bar myur la sangs rgyas shog / chos 'byung gi lo rgyus mi 'dra ba mang du snang
yang / la la ngan smras/ la la zhe 'dod/ la la bsdus pa/ la la le tshe/ la la bcos ma yin te/ 'di ni sel med rnal ma yin/ legs par bzung la legs gyis/ /legs par slobs la
mkhas par mdzod/ /so so skye bos bkod rnams 'khrul ba srid/ /gzhung lugs rnal ma thogs pa shin tu dkon/ /man ngag kun la yod na mkhas pa su yis byed/ /yi ge gzhan la ma
ster blo la bzung la shod/ /bris nas snod du bcangs na bang mdzod nor bu yin/ /ya rabs rnams la dgos kyis thugs la zhog /bka' rtsis yi ge zhib par zhabs btags pa/ /dpe la
dog la bshad la yangs su mdzod/ /ngo mtshar che ba gzigs pa rnams kyis mdzod/ /bshes gnyen rnams la sde snod mang du thos/ /chos dang chos min 'byed pa'i blo gros yod/ /dam
tshigs legs srungs lta ba dag par rtogs/ /nang ban nyi ma'i 'od zer 'di skad smra/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa rin po che'i/ /shAkya seng ge'i gsung rab rnams/ /grub chen mkhas
pa kun gyis ni/ /rgya gar yul du gsal bar mdzad/ /de nas gangs ri'i khrod 'di ru/ /rigs gsum rnam sprul rgyal po ni/ /mes dbon rnam gsum bka' drin gyis/ /skad gnyis
smra ba rnams kyis bsgyurd/ dang po dag cing dar bar mdzad/ /de rjes glang dar bas bsnubs/ /de nas stod smad gnyis nas dar/ /byang sems ldan pas gsal byas kyang / /deng sang
longs spyod dar ba'i dus/ /dam chos rin chen nub la khad/ /de nyid gsal bar byed 'dod pas/ /bdag gis sbas pa bton/ /skal ldan gcig dang 'phrad 'gyur gsungs/ /chos lugs
ma nor bzung bar bya/ /legs par rtogs la mkhas pa yin/ /dri med dag pa'i dam chos la/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ /dgongs don zab mo 'grub par 'gyur/ /des na brtson
'grus chen po yis/ /bka' lung dri ma med pa la/ /dad ldan rnams kyis 'jug par rigs/ /thos bsam sgom gsum mthar ru phyung / /mkhas pa rnams kyis bshad pa 'di/ /nyams
su blang gi rmongs pa'i gdams ngag spongs/ /zhes so/ /mangga laM bha wantu/ /dge'o// //
